Surasuṁdarīcariyaṁ

by Dhanēsarō

suhasāmannapaïnnāsamayasamāraddhalōyakammassa

amaravaïvayaṇadhariō parikuḍilō kuntalakalāvō

kannāsannē sōhaï jassa avatthāṇapatthaṇatthaṁva

cittabbhantararuddhappavēsakandappadūuvva

ahavā

sōhaï jassa susaṅgayaübhayaṁsalulantakuntalakalāvā

muttī suvannavannā sakajjalaggavva dīvasihā

jassa paṇāmā pāvaï palayaṁ paürōpi vigghasaṅghāō

tassa risahassa paḍhamaṁ namāmi payapaṅkayaṁ payaō

ajiyāiṇō jiṇindē vandē jammaṁmi jēsimamarindā

rāgāiṇō vi sattū pañcattaṁ pāviyā samayaṁ

jammaṇasamayāṇantarasumērusiharābhisēyasamayammi

sakkandaṇakayakuviyappannāsaṇē kayapayattassa

rāgāivaïrisēṇavva jassa daṭṭhuṁ aṇannasāmatthaṁ

tharahariyā accatthaṁ sasilōccayasāyarā vasuhā

nimmalakamanahaniyarō paḍibimbiyapaṇayatihuaṇō jassa

uvvahaï jāyagavvō kēvalanāṇassa samasīsiṁ

jassa ya paṇāmamēttā nimmalakamaṇakkhapaḍiyapaḍibimbā

ēkkārasaguṇamuvalabbha appayaṁ harisiyā tiyasā

taṁ vandē jiṇayandaṁ dēvindanarindavindavandiyayaṁ

siddhatthanarindasuaṁ carimaṁ carimaṁ gaïṁ pattaṁ

dujjayaaṇaṅgamāyaṅgabhaṅgasāraṅgapuṅgavasaricchē

sāsayasivasuhasahiē siddhē sirasā namaṁsāmi 11

duddhaṁsadhantaviddhaṁsadhīrasiddhantadēsaē dhīrē

pañcavihāyāraraē sirasā vandāmi āyariē

visayasuhanippivāsē saṁsāracchēyakaraṇatallicchē

vandāmi uvajjhāē suttatthavisāraē sayayaṁ

pañcamahavvayaduvvahapavvayaüvvahaṇapaccalē sirasā

gharavāsapāsamukkē sāhū savvē namaṁsāmi

jīē kamakamalaṁ pāviūṇa pāvinti pāṇiṇō paramaṁ

nāṇaṁ annāṇā vi hu sā jayaï sarassaī dēvī

jāṇa pasāēṇa puṇa maēvi jaḍabuddhiṇā kahākaraṇē

līlāē payaṭṭijjaï, visēsaō tē gurū vandē

iya pujjapaṇaïkaraṇappaṇāsiyāsēsavigghasaṅghāō

vōcchaṁ saṁvēgakariṁ kahaṁ tu surasundariṁ nāma

annaṁ ca tassa kīraï paḍhamaṁ ciya patthaṇā khalajaṇassa

bīhēi kavijaṇō jassa mūsaō iva biḍālassa

ahavā sahāvaücciya dōsaggahaṇammi vāvaḍamaṇassa

abbhatthaṇāsaēhi vi na khalassa khalattaṇaṁ galaï

kuḍilattaṇaṁ na ujjhaï paricchiddagavēsaō ya dōjīhō

patthijjantō vi kavīhiṁ dujjaṇō sappasāricchō

abbhatthiō vi vaṅkō kalusiyahiyaō suvittaparihīṇō

candōvva dujjaṇō iha dōsāsaṅgē payāsēi

laliē va niṭṭhurē vā kavvē dōsō khalēhiṁ ghēttavvō

uṭṭhamuhāō ahavā nīharaï na jīrayaṁ kahavi

dujjaṇasahāē paḍiyaṁ nimmalakavvaṁ pi lahaï na païṭṭhaṁ

jalabinduvva sutattē āyasabhāṇammi pakkhittō

āsajja dujjaṇaṁ kavijaṇassa abbhatthaṇā taō vihalā

na hu sakkararasasittōvi cayaï kaḍuyattaṇaṁ nimbō

ahavā kahāpabandhō kīraï kiṁ dujjaṇāṇa saṅkāē?

jūyābhaēṇa parihāṇavimōyaṇaṁ handi! na hu juttaṁ

dujjaṇaasaṁmayaṁ pi hu kuṇaï kavī kavvamēttha kimajuttaṁ?

uluyāṇamabhāsantōvi diṇayarō kiṁ na uggamaï?

apatthiōvi suyaṇō kaīṇa kavvē guṇē payāsēi

dhavalēi jayaṁ sayalaṁ sabhāvaō cēva nisināhō

nindākārijaṇassa vi dōsaggāhī na sajjaṇō kahavi

kuṇaï suyandhaṁ vāsiṁ tacchijjantō vi malayaruhō

annaṁ ca havaï hu virūvayampi hu kavvaṁ suyaṇāṇa saṅgamē laṭṭhaṁ

sippipuḍammi paviṭṭhaṁ jalampi muttāhalaṁ hōi

abbhatthaṇārihāṁ jaṁ suyaṇā tō tē u patthimō iṇhiṁ

ēgaggamaṇā hōuṁ sāhijjantiṁ nisāmēha

ghōrē aṇōrapārē saṁsārē jōṇilakkhapaürammi

aïdulahaṁ laddhūṇaṁ maṇuyattaṁ bhaviyalōēṇa

dēvindacandanāgindavindamaṇuindavandiyajiṇēhiṁ

vajjariē ujjamiuṁ juttaṁ dhammammi suddhammi

sō antarārivijaē rōgaddōsā ya antarā sattū

tavvijae cciya sōkkhaṁ tēhiṁ jiyāṇaṁ puṇō dukkhaṁ

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē rāgaddēsāṇugayā jīvā pāvēnti vivihadukkhāiṁ

tamhā tavvijae cciya vibuhēhiṁ hōi jaïyavvaṁ

ēyatthasāhaṇaparā sōlasaparicchēyasaṅgayā laliyā

pāiyagāhāhiṁ kahā kīraï surasundarīnāmā

abuhajaṇabōhaṇaṁ taha dukkahalōyāṇa cittarañjaṇayaṁ

jugavaṁ ṇō sakkijjaï kavīhiṁ ubhayampi kāūṇa

jaō sālaṅkārēṇa ghaṇakkharēṇa rañjijjaē jaṇō vibuhō

payaḍatthalaliyakavvaṁ abuhāṇaṁ bōhaṇaṁ kuṇaï

dōṇha vi ēkkavaēcciya sakkijjaï rañjaṇaṁ na kāūṇaṁ

ēkkaṁ gēṇhantāṇaṁ avassa kira nāsaē bīyaṁ

niyagurukamappasāyā kāvi hu sattī u jaïvi maha atthi

uvamāsilēsarūpagavaṇṇagabahulammi kavvammi

tahavi hu tayaṁ na kīraï asamatthaṁ patthuammi jaṁ atthē

tō abuhabōhaṇatthaṁ payaḍatthā kīraē ēsā

kiñca sīsiṇimayahariyāē gurubhagiṇīē alandhavayaṇāē

sirikallāṇamaīē pavattiṇīē u vayaṇēṇa

pāraddhā jaṁ ēsā kavittagavvēṇa nō maē tēṇa

kīraïuttāṇatthā pāiyagāhāhiṁ laliyapayā

hu pajjattaṁ bahuṇā patthuyavigdhāvahēṇa vihalēṇa

vihavakulabāliyākayakaḍakkhavikkhēvasarisēṇaṁ

nisuṇaha ēgaggamaṇā hōumiyāṇiṁ kahaṁ kahijjantaṁ

aḍ̣dhāijjasaēhiṁ gāhāṇaṁ kayaparicchēyaṁ

atthēttha suvitthinnō uḍ̣dhāhōlōgamajjhayārammi

nāmēṇa tiriyalōgō vibuhāṇugaō sumēruvva

dīvō u atthi tatthavi vittharaō jōyaṇāṇa lakkhaṁ tu

jalahivalayāvagụ̄dhō jambuddīvō tti vikkhāō

tassa ya dāhiṇabhāgē bharahaṁ nāmēṇa atthi varakhēttaṁ

vēyaḍḍhanagavarēṇaṁ duhā vihattaṁ suvitthinnaṁ

aha dāhiṇaḍḍhabharahē gaṅgāsindhūṇa majjhayārammi

kappadumōvva dumāṇaṁ bahudēsāṇaṁ pahāṇayārō

dhannasamiddhilapāmararāsayasaṁsaddapūriyadiyantō

avikarahamahisarāsahanāṇāvihagōhaṇāinnō

païdiyahavahantāṇēyasāraṇīvisararēhirujjāṇō

puranagaragāmapaürō bahuriddhisamiddhasayalajaṇō

niccaṁ pamuiyalōō nāṇāvihaücchavēhiṁ avirahiō

bhayaḍamararahiyagāmō kurutti nāmēṇa varadēsō

aviya aṇavarayavahantāṇēyavaṇiyasatthōhavasimasayalapahō

jattha na najjaï pahi pahiṁ aḍavivasiṭhāṇayavisēsō

annaṁ ca tammi dēsē guṇāṇa bhavaṇammi ēyamacchariyaṁ

sōarahiōvi jaṁ suṇaï jaṇavaō lōyabhaṇiyāiṁ

aviya jattha ya gāmamahallā kararahiyā dhammavajjiyā muṇiṇō

dēsassa tassa saṁvaṇṇaṇammi kō ujjamaṁ kuṇaï?

tatthavi ya atthi vitthinnajalahivalayāṇukāriparihāē

parapurisālaṅghāē parikkhittaṁ bhamiramayarāē

paḍavakkhabhayuppāyaṇavisālasālēṇa parigayaṁ rammaṁ

ramaṇīyamagaratōraṇagōuradārēhiṁ parikinnaṁ

aïnīlabahalaüvavaṇavirāyamāṇāvasāṇabhāgēhiṁ

mattālambagavakkhayajuēhiṁ varacittajuttēhiṁ

nāṇabhūmijuēhiṁ pāsāēhiṁ tusāradhavalēhiṁ

tannayaravāsijaṇajasathūhēhivva niccamaïrammaṁ

taha avarāvaradēsāgaēṇa tannayaravāsiṇā cēva

vaṇiyakalāniuṇēṇaṁ païdiyahaṁ vaṇiyalōēṇa

kijjantavaṇijjēhiṁ virāyamāṇaṁ aṇēgahaṭṭēhiṁ

paripūriēhiṁ antō bahumullakiyāṇagasaēhiṁ

uttuṅgamagaratōraṇapavaṇuddhuyadhavaladhayavaḍaḍ̣dhēhiṁ

sudaṁradēvaülēhiṁ uvasōhiyasundarapaēsaṁ

taha paṇḍupaümasaṇḍōhamaṇḍiyāṇēyagurutarasarēhiṁ

sōvāṇapantisugamāvayāravāvīsahassēhiṁ

varatiyacaükkacaccaraārāmujjāṇadīhiyāīhiṁ

dēvāṇamavi kuṇantaṁ paē paē cittasaṁharaṇaṁ

sayalannapurapahāṇaṁ nayaraṁ sirihatthiṇāuraṁ nāma

nayaraguṇōhuvavēyaṁ saṅkāsaṁ amaranayarassa

jattha ya nivasaï lōō piyaṁvaō dhammakaraṇatallicchō

dakkhinnacāyabhōgēhiṁ saṅgaō taha kalākusalō

jattha ya purammi niccaṁ iō taō bahupaōyaṇaparēṇa

bhamirajaṇasamudaēṇaṁ dussañcārāō ratthāō

jattha ya kōḍipaḍāyāpacchāiyasayalagayaṇamaggammi

lōō gimhadiṇēsuvi ravikaratāvaṁ na yāṇēi

jattha ya purammi purisā gharabhittinihittamaṇimaūhēhiṁ

niccaṁ hayandhayārē gayampi rāiṁ na yāṇanti

rammattaṇaō jassa ya palōyaṇatthaṁva āgayā dēvā

kōugavakkhittamaṇā aṇamisanayaṇattaṇaṁ pattā

dhavalaharasiharaviraïyapavaṇapahallantavējayantīō

sannanti va raviṇō sārahissa aïuccagamaṇaṭṭhā

jattha ya purammi dīsaï pāyapahārō u raṅgabhūmīsu

daṇḍō u dhayavaḍāṇaṁ sīsacchēō juyārīṇa

kusumāṇa sirasi bandhō sāgacchēttēsu jīvakattaṇayā

taha paṇḍiyaparisāsu pattāṇaṁ handi! bhindaṇayā

aha ēkko cciya dōsō guṇāṇa bhavaṇammi tammi nayarammi

niddōsasāhuṇō jaṁ sayāvi dīsanti guttiṭhiyā

aha tammi purammi pahū pabhūyakariturayarayaṇabhaṇḍārō

jahabhaṇiyanīipālaṇaāṇandiyasayasajaṇacittō

niyabuddhisamudaēṇaṁ vasīkayāsēsasattusantāṇō

sampūriyatthisamudayamaṇapatthiyaatthavitthārō

daḍhakạdhiṇabhuyā 'parimiyaparakkamakkantasayalapaḍivakkhō

paḍivakkhabhāmiṇīvayaṇanaliṇasaṅkōyamaṇamayaṅkō

sūrōvva pihupayāvō sīhō iva akayaparabalāsaṅkō

uyahivva sugambhīrō candō iva jaṇamaṇāṇandō

ruvēṇa kāmadēvō buddhiē suragurussa sāricchō

nivasaï pamōyapattō rāyā siriamarakēutti

tassa ya tivaggasāraṁ rajjasiriṁ sammamaṇuhavantassa

vaccanti vāsarāi indassa va dēvalōgammi

aha annayā kayāivi atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō tassa

viṇayapaṇaüttamaṅgō paḍihārō bandhulō bhaṇaī

dēva! kusaggapurāō cittayarō cittakammapattaṭṭhō

nāmēṇa cittasēṇō samāgatō ciṭṭhaï duvārē

sō dēvapāyadaṁsaṇasuhakaṅkhī icchaē iha pavēsaṁ

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē amhaṁ dēvāēsō pamāṇanti

tattō raṇṇā bhaṇiyaṁ lahuṁ pavēsēhi tāhē sō vihiṇā

atthāṇammi paviṭṭhō kayaviṇaō rāiṇō puraō

uvaviṭṭhō bhūmīē rannā bhaṇiō kuō 'si taṁ bhadda!?

kēṇa va kajjēṇa ihaṁ samāgaō maha samīvammi?

tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō kusagganayarāu āgaō dēva!

cittagarō sāisayaṁ jāṇāmi ya cittakammamahaṁ

cittappiō ya dēvō summaï vattāsuṁ tēṇa ahamēttha

cittakalaṁ payaḍēuṁ samāgaō dēvapāsammi

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ kērisayaṁ cittakōsalaṁ tujjha?

daṁsēhi tāva majjhaṁ ālihiyaṁ kiñci vararuvaṁ

aha tēṇa kakkhadēsammi gōviyā cittapaṭṭiyā sahasā

payaḍīkāuṁ raṇṇō samappiyā hiṭṭhavayaṇēṇa

pasarantapayaḍapulaō rāyā pulōēi tattha ālihiyaṁ

nāṇāvannayakaliyaṁ pamāṇarēhāhiṁ suvisuddhaṁ

ahiṇavajjōvvaṇavararuvajuttamaccantamaṇaharāgāraṁ

ahiṇavasihiṇārambhaṁ kaṇṇāē ruvayaṁ pavaraṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ naranāhō cintaï ēsō hu cittakammammi

aïkusalō jaṁ lihiyaṁ aüvvaruvaṁ imaṁ rūvaṁ

tilōkkammivi mannē ērisarūvā na itthiyā atthi

cittakalāniuṇattā adiṭṭharūvā imā lihiyā

jaï puṇa katthavi hōjjā ērisaruvēṇa itthiyā kannā

tīē vi saṅgamō jaï tā rajjaṁ hōjja sakayatthaṁ

ēvaṁ cintēntassa ya vammahasaragōyarammi paḍiyassa

vīsariō sē appā cittē 'vakkhittacittassa

tattō khaṇantarāō saṁmīliyalōyaṇō amarakēū

sīhāsaṇāu paḍiō mucchāē paravasō sahasā

hā! hā! hatti bhaṇantā atthāṇagayā samuṭṭhiyā lōyā

vīyanti vīyaṇēhiṁ sīyalasalilēṇaṁ siñcanti

vayaṇē khivanti khippa kappūraṁ taha malēnti aṅgāiṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ cittasēṇō pahasiyavayaṇō daḍhaṁ jāō

rē! rē! kōvi hu pāvō ahimararūvēṇa āgaō ēsō

kammaṇagārī jēṇiha vimōhiō amha sāmitti

tālēha haṇaha vandhaha ēvaṁ bhaṇantēhiṁ aṅgarakkhēhiṁ

gahiō sō hammantō ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō

bhō! bhō! bhaddā! nāhaṁ duṭṭhō tā mā muhā kayatthēha

tattō ya tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kahaṁ na duṭṭhō tumaṁ pāva!?

kammaṇakayaṁ hi cittaṁ payaṁsiyaṁ kīsa rāiṇō tumaē?

taha mucchiyammi dēvē viyasiyavayaṇō ya kiṁ jāō?

tā kahasu kēṇa raṇṇō vahaṇatthaṁ pēsiō tumaṁ pāva!?

tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō akkhissaṁ tumha savvampi

rannō abbhudayatthaṁ samāgaō na uṇa duṭṭhabuddhīē

ēmāi bhaṇantōvi hu baddhō sō rāyapurisēhiṁ

ētthantarammi rāyā gayamucchō satthacēyaṇō jāō

aha naravaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ muñcaha bhō! cittagaramēyaṁ

ucchōḍiyabandhō sō rannā bhaṇiō ya bhadda! uvavisasu

āikkhasu maha saccaṁ kēṇa tumaṁ pēsiō ēttha?

tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō nisuṇasu naranāha! ēttha paramatthaṁ

cittagaravēsadhārī samāgaō jēṇa ahamēttha

atthēttha kusaggapuraṁ supasiddhaṁ cēva dēvapāyāṇaṁ

nayaraguṇōhuvavēyaṁ dhaṇadhannasamiddhajaṇakaliyaṁ

paṇaïjaṇapūriyāsō rāyā ghaṇavāhaṇotti tatthāsi

pāṇappiyā sē dēvī vasantasēṇatti nāmēṇa

tāṇa ya puttō naravāhaṇotti nāmēṇa ukkaḍapayāvō

kamalāvaïttināmā dhūyāaccantarūvavaī

aha annayā ya rāyā dāuṁ naravāhaṇassa niyarajjaṁ

kamalāvaī ya bhagiṇī aṇurūvavarassa dāyavvā

iya bhaṇiūṇa puttaṁ sugurusamīvammi jāyasaṁvēgō

saṁsārucchēyakaraṁ sāmannaṁ uvagaō vihiṇā

naravāhaṇōvi rāyā rajjaṁ pālēi paṇayapaḍivakkhaṁ

ciṭṭhaï kannantēuramajjhē kamalāvaï vi suhaṁ

ēttō ya tammi nayarē nivasaï vaṇiō u sāgarō nāma

rannō bālasavayaṁsō jiṇavayaṇē gāḍhamaṇurattō

sirimaïnāmā bhajjā aïppiyā tassa sīlasampannā

siridattō sē puttō sirikantā tahaya duhiyatti

sirikantā aṇudiyahaṁ vaccaī kamalāvaīē pāsammi

jāyā ya garuyapīī annōnnaṁ tāṇa dōṇhampi

itthījaṇajōgāō gahiyāō kalāō bālabhāvēvi

sagalakalāniuṇassa u pāsammi sumittasēṇassa

rāyaduhiyāē samayaṁ cittāīyāhi vivihakīlāhiṁ

sirikantā kīlēttā vigālasamayammi ēi gihaṁ

sirikantāē samayaṁ siṇēhasārāē rāyadhūyāē

vōlīṇō bahukālō nāṇāvihakīḍaṇarayāē

kamasō vaḍḍhantīō tiyasāṇa vi patthaṇijjarūvāō

pattāō paḍhamajōvvaṇamaṇaṅgasiṅgāraāvāsaṁ

aha annayā ya rāyā maïsāgarasāgarēhi sañjuttō

atthāṇamaṇḍavammī āsīṇō acchaī jāva

niyasahiyaṇasañjuttā tāva ya kamalāvaī tahiṁ āyā

bhūsaṇapasāhiaṅgī gēnduyakīlāē kīlantī

aha sā bhagiṇī rannā pīīē nivēsiyā niucchaṅgē

tattō daṭṭhuṁ tīē rūvaṁ taha jōvvaṇamudaggaṁ

bhaṇiō rannā mantī maïsāgara! taïya pavvayantēṇa

tāēṇa ahaṁ bhaṇiō bhagiṇī ṭhāṇammi dāyavvā

iṇhiṁ varassa uciyā jāyā ēsatti tā mahaṁ kahasu

kō aṇurūvō purisō imīē sukulappasūō ya?

maïsāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ dēvo cciya ēttha jāṇaē uciyaṁ

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ mē phuraī cittammi

kīraï sayaṁvarō iha hakkārijjantu savvarāyāṇō

jō cēva hiyayaïṭṭhō taṁ cēva varēī jēṇēsā

maïsāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaṁ dēvō āṇavēi taṁ kiccaṁ

navari sayaṁvarakaraṇaṁ sampaï uciyaṁ na kāuṁ jē

savvēvi nivā jaïyā āyattā honti ēganaravaïṇō

tadaṇunnāēṇa tayā sayaṁvarō hōi kāyavvō

ēgassa jaō varaṇē sēsāṇaṁ sō nivāragō hōi

sampaï puṇa rāyāṇō narinda! savvēvi ahamindā

tā tāṇamēgavaraṇē sēsā savvēvi sattuṇō honti

na ya sakkā saṅgāmē jiṇiuṁ savvēvi ēgēṇa

tā alamimiṇā naravara! viggahamūlēṇaṇatthabahulēṇa

kamalāvaīsayaṁvarakaraṇēṇa ēttha patthāvē

tattō raṇṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kassēsā tarihi bhadda! dāyavvā

kō va imīē iṭṭhō maṇassa iha kaha ṇu nāyavvaṁ?

jassa va tassa va rannō dāyavvā na ya maē niyayabhagiṇī

dinnā hōi sudinnā jassa, imā tassa dāyavvā

ēvaṁ ca jāva jampaï rāyā maïsāgarēṇa saha tattha

tāva ya duvārapālō paṇāmapaccuṭṭhiō bhaṇaï

aṭṭhaṅganimittaviū bhūyabhavissatthapayaḍaṇapaḍiṭṭhō

suṇaīnāmō ihaïṁ samāgaō dēva! nēmittī

sō dēvadaṁsaṇatthaṁ duvāradēsammi ciṭṭhaï iyāṇiṁ

iya sōuṁ naravaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ turiyaṁ pavēsēhiṁ

tayaṇantaraṁ ca sumaī nimmalasiyavasaṇasōhiyasarīrō

gōrōyaṇakayatilaō samāgaō rāiṇō puraō

āsīpayāṇapuvvaṁ dāuṁ duvvakkhaē narindassa

rannā kaōvayārō uciyāsaṇagammi uvaviṭṭhō

rannā paccayahēuṁ atīyavatthummi pucchiō ēsō

paccakkhaṁ piva savvaṁ sāhēi sō avitahaṁ jāva

tāhē pahasiyavayaṇō rāyā naravāhaṇō imaṁ bhaṇati

bhō sumaï! majjha bhagiṇī ēsā kamalāvaī kaṇṇā

ēīē kō bhattā hōhī maṇavallahutti vajjarasu

sumaī nirūviūṇaṁ nimittamēvaṁ samullavaï

naravara! cittē lihiyaṁ ēīē rūvayaṁ pulōēttā

mucchijjissaï jō iha hōhī bhattā imīē sō

sayalōrōhapahāṇā tassa ya hōhī imā mahādēvī

ētthattthē ya narēsara! mā kāhisi annahābhāvaṁ

ētthantarammi sāgarasēṭṭhī saṁlavaï sumaïnēmittiṁ

sirikantāē bhattā kō hōhī majjha dhūyāē?

vajjaraï taō sumaī kasiṇabhuyaṅgēṇa ḍasiyamēyaṁ jō

ujjīvissaï so cciya bhattā dhūyāē tē hōhī

ēvaṁ ca pucchiūṇaṁ uciyaṁ kāūṇa tassa uvayāraṁ

paṭṭhaviō naravaïṇā jahāgayaṁ paḍigaō sumaī

tattō ya bhaṇaï mantī sōhaṇamahuṇā narinda! sañjāyaṁ

tā iṇhiṁ tabbhaṇiē kāyavvō ujjamō hōi

bhaṇiyaṁ rannā kō iha sāisayaṁ lihaï cittakammanti

maïsāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ supasiddhō tāva iha nayarē

ēkko cciya kamalāvaïujjhāyasumittasēṇanāmassa

taṇaō u cittasēṇō aïkusalō cittakammammi

rannā bhaṇiyaṁ sigghaṁ vāharaha tayanti takkhaṇēṇa ahaṁ

vāhariō sampattō bhaṇiō rannā sabahumāṇaṁ

kamalāvaīē rūvaṁ sigdhaṁ ālihasu cittaphalahīē

jaṁ āṇavēsi bhaṇiuṁ, sōhaṇavannēhi taṁ lihiyaṁ

dēkkhāliyaṁ ca rannō sāisayaṁ pēkkhiūṇa tō tuṭṭhō

bhaṇiō ahaṁ rannā ētthatthē taṁ siuciutti

cittagaravēsadhārī ēyaṁ ghēttūṇa savvarāīṇaṁ

daṁsēṇu jassa mucchā jāyaï ēyaṁ pulōēuṁ

sō maha sāhēavvō sigdhaṁ āgamma, jēṇa tassēva

mahayā uvayārēṇa dijjaï kamalāvaī ēsā

ēvaṁ raṇṇā bhaṇiō tattō paṇamittu tassa payakamalaṁ

kaïvayapariyaṇasahiō kusagganayarāu nīhariō

suggīvakittivaddhaṇapamuhāṇaṁ naravaīṇa mē ēsā

sandaṁsiyāu na puṇō jāyā iha atthasaṁsiddhī

ajja puṇō iha nayarē samāgaō dēva! tumha pāsammi

ēyaṁ niyacchiūṇaṁ mucchā jāyā ya tumhāṇaṁ

jāyaṁ maha sāmisamīhiyaṁ ti cinttittu tēṇa naranāha!

jāō harisō majjha sumariya nēmittiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ

ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ mucchāē tumha harisiō ahayaṁ

tā mā narinda! annahabhāvēṇa viyappasu mamanti

ii cittasēṇavayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ vigayaannaāsaṅkō

vajjaraï amarakēū vimhaïō cittarūvēṇa

kiṁ tīē kannāē ērisayaṁ atthi rūvasōhaggaṁ?

tā bhaṇaī cittasēṇō nimēsamēttaṁ imaṁ lihiyaṁ

kō sakkaï kusalōvi hu jahaṭṭhiyaṁ tīē rāyakannāē

nijjiyatiyasavilāsiṇīrūvaṁ rūvaṁ samālihiuṁ?

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisiyahiyaēṇa rāiṇā tassa

aṅgavilaggamasēsaṁ pasāiyaṁ kaḍayavatthāiṁ

tō bhaṇaï cittasēṇō āēsaṁ dēha dēva! amhāṇaṁ

naravāhaṇassa raṇṇō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ jēṇa sāhēmō

raṇṇaṇṇunnāō sō kamēṇa pattō kusagganayarammi

naravāhaṇassa rannō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō

aha tēṇavi niyabhagiṇī pabhūyadhaṇapariyaṇēṇa pariyariyā

paṭṭhaviyā hiṭṭhēṇaṁ sayaṁvarā amarakēussa

sirikantāisahijaṇaṁ ābhāsittā ya sayalaparivāraṁ

kamalāvaīvi caliyā harisavisāyāurā hiyaē

icchiyavaralābhēṇaṁ sāṇandā tahaya bandhuvirahēṇaṁ

kiñci sasōgā pattā kamēṇa sā hatthiṇapurammi

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ sōhaṇalaggammi gurupamōēṇaṁ

kamalāvaī u rannā pariṇīyā khattakulavihiṇā

pāṇāṇavi abbhahiyā pavarā antēurassa sayalassa

indassava indāṇī jāyā aha sā mahādēvī

tīē saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa rāiṇō tassa

nīīē sayalabhūmiṁ niyayaṁ parivālayantassa

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ suhasamudayamasamamaṇuhavantassa

vibuhapahussava tiyasālayammi addiṭṭhadukkhassa

tammi ya purē pasiddhō pavarō paürāṇa āsi dhaṇadhammō

sēṭṭhī nivassa iṭṭhō pattaṭṭhō savvasatthēsu

nīsēsaatthivittharapatthiyaabbhahiyadinnavaradāṇō

ajjayapajjayajaṇayajjiyāē lacchīē 'laṅkariō

jiṇasamayasatthavittharaviyakkhaṇō mōkkhamaggatallicchō

jiṇasāhupūyaṇaraō sāhammiyavacchalō dhaṇiyaṁ

avahasiyatiyasasundarirūvāisayā paīvayā dakkhā

bhajjā maṇōramanāmā tassa ya pāṇappiyā dhaṇiyaṁ

tāṇaṁ tivaggasāraṁ visayasuhaṁ sammamaṇuhavantāṇaṁ

niyakulamaṇḍaṇabhūō jāō aha dāraō ēkkō

vattē ya bārasāhē ammāpīīhiṁ niyayakulavihiṇā

dhaṇadēvotti ya sammaṁ nāmaṁ nivvattiyaṁ tassa

aha pañcadhāikayavivihalālaṇō dāraō sa vaḍḍhantō

pattō kumārabhāvaṁ māupiuṇaṁ kayāṇandō

abbhahiyaaṭṭhavarisō sammaṁ abbhasiyasayalavijjassa

ujjhāyassuvaṇīō vinnāyakalākalāvassa

thēvēṇa vi kālēṇaṁ ahigamiyāō samatthavijjāō

sayalē kalākalāvē aha jāō sōvi pattaṭṭhō

tattō gahiyakalāvō samāṇiō niyagharammi dhaṇadēvō

piuṇā sē ujjhāō sa pūiō vatthamāīhiṁ

kamasō pavaḍḍhamāṇō dhaṇadēvō jōvvaṇaṁ samaṇupattō

nijjiyaaṇaṅgaruvō jāō varakāmiṇīdaïō

aha sō samāṇajōvvaṇarūvāisaēhiṁ varavayaṁsēhiṁ

pariyariō āhiṇḍaï īsaralīlaṁ viḍambantō

aha annayā kayāivi vayaṁsavisarēṇa parigaō ēsō

nayarāō nīhariō pattō ya maṇōramujjāṇē

diṭṭhō ya tattha ēgō purisō gurusōyaparigaō tēṇa

vāvītaḍōvaviṭṭhō aṁsujalōhaliyagaṇḍayalō

dhaṇadēvō taṁ daṭṭhuṁ purisaṁ uppannagaruyakāruṇṇō

āsannē gantūṇaṁ mahuragirāē imaṁ bhaṇati

kō si tumaṁ kattō vā kiṁ vā tē sōyakāraṇaṁ bhadda!?

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō sō purisō ēvamullavaï

kaha tammi vajjarijjaï dukkhaṁ gurudukkhapīḍiyamaṇēhiṁ

na kuṇaï jō paḍiyāraṁ na ya duhiō ahava jō hōi?

tahavi hu kahēmi sundara! mā vayaṇaṁ tujjha nipphalaṁ jāu

sīhaguhānāmēṇaṁ aïvisamā atthi pallitti

tīē ya supaïṭṭhō pallivaī tassa bhāriyā lacchī

tīē puttō jāō jayasēṇō jaṇamaṇāṇandō

tassa ya bālaggahō ahayaṁ nāmēṇa dēvasammotti

kīlāmi ya jayasēṇaṁ tattha ahaṁ vivihakīlāhiṁ

aha annayā ya bāhiṁ viṇiggaō gēṇhiūṇa jayasēṇaṁ

purisēhiṁ dōhi diṭṭhō tattha ahaṁ jōgirūvēhiṁ

sambhāsiūṇa puvviṁ dinnō maha tēhiṁ pavaratambōlō

tammi samāṇiyamittē maïsaṁmōhō mahaṁ jāō

tattō kumarasamēō tēsimaṇumaggamēva laggō haṁ

jāṇāmi nēva kiñcivi vimōhiō tēhiṁ pāvēhiṁ

tēhi samētō ahayaṁ vayāmi jā kittiyampi bhūbhāgaṁ

tāva ya tisiēṇa maē ēgammi uvavaṇaniguñjē

bahuvihataruphalakalusaṁ pīyaṁ nīraṁ tu tappabhāvēṇa

jāō satthasarīrō vicintiyaṁ tāhi mē ēyaṁ

rayaṇīi gahiya kumaraṁ nāsissamimāṇa pāvapurisāṇaṁ

iya cintiya caliō haṁ alakkhiō cēva saha tēhiṁ

pattāē rayaṇīē nisuyā annōnnamullavēmāṇā

ēēṇa bālaēṇaṁ sijjhissaï jakkhiṇī amhaṁ

tugīyapavvayammī pattā huṁṇiūṇa bālayaṁ ēyaṁ

siddhāē jakkhiṇīē pāvissāmō nihiṁ taṁ tu

iya tēsiṁ sōūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ, bhayavēvirō daḍhaṁ jāō

suttēsu tēsu ghēttuṁ jayasēṇaṁ tāhi naṭṭhō haṁ

kahakahavi hu nāsantō gavēsamāṇēhiṁ tēhiṁ haṁ pattō

bandhittu taō vasabhē samāruhēttā ihāṇīō

ajja puṇō iha nayarē sampattō sattamāu divasāu

tanhāchuhābhibhūō mukkō haṁ ēttha ujjāṇē

tā bhadda! imaṁ gurusōyakāraṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ maē tumha

jaï atthi kāvi sattī tā rakkhaha bālayaṁ taṁ tu

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ sampaï ciṭṭhanti kattha tē purisā?

sō bhaṇaï gahiyakumarō ēgō naggōhahēṭṭhammi

bīō purē paviṭṭhō surāikajjēṇa sampayaṁ cēva

iya bhaṇiē dhaṇadēvō jōgiyapāsē gaō turiyaṁ

bhaṇiō ya tēṇa ēsō ēyaṁ maha dēsu bālayaṁ bhadda!

ahayaṁ suvannalakkhaṁ tuha dēmi, na ēttha sandēhō

tō jōgiēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jāva na sō ēi duiyaō jōgī

tāva maha dēsu lakkhaṁ jēṇa imaṁ dēmi tuha bālaṁ

tattō dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ samappiyaṁ aṅgulīyayaṁ tassa

dīṇāralakkhamullaṁ mukkō ya imēṇa jayasēṇō

ghēttūṇa aṅgulīyaṁ sigghayaraṁ jōgiō taō naṭṭhō

ghēttūṇa ya jayasēṇaṁ dhaṇadēvō dēvasammassa

pāsammi samallīṇō bhaṇiō ēsō ya ginha kumaratti

tattō ya dēvasammō pahasiyavayaṇō imaṁ bhaṇaï

taṁ sāmī taṁ bandhū taṁ ciya maha jīyadāyagō suyaṇu!

kiṁ kiṁ na kayaṁ tumaē jīyaṁ kumarassa dintēṇa?

maha sāmiyassa dinnaṁ, jīyaṁ jaṁ pāṇavallahō puttō

pāviṭṭhaduṭṭhajōgiyakayantavayaṇāu nīhariō

tattō dhavadēvēṇaṁ nīō gēhammi bhōiō sammaṁ

satthassa mēliūṇaṁ paṭṭhaviō niyayaṭhāṇammi

ēsō puṇa vuttantō vitthariō tattha puravarē sahasā

aïcāī dhaṇadēvō dēi dhaṇaṁ lakkhagannēhiṁ

tā jattha jattha dīsaï dhaṇadēvō niyavayaṁsapariyariō

annōnnaṁ puralōō tattha imaṁ vivihamullavaï

ēsō sō dhaṇadēvō cāī bhōgī ya taha kalākusalō

atthijaṇapatthiō jō varisaï lakkhēhiṁ dhannotti

annē puṇa macchariṇō bhaṇanti niyacāyagavviyā tattha

kiṁ salahijjaï ēsō niyapiulacchīē khayakālō?

taṁ dāṇamiha pasassaṁ taṁ cēva ya pōrusassa vuḍ̣dhikaraṁ

jaṁ niyaparakkamēṇaṁ viḍhaviya vilasijjaï jahicchaṁ

jaṁ puṇa ajjayapajjayajaṇayajjiyaatthamajjhaō dāṇaṁ

paramatthaō kalaṅkaṁ tayaṁ tu purisābhimāṇīṇaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ca bappaviḍhaviya davvēṇaṁ kō na viḍ̣dhiraṁ kuṇaï

saïviḍhavaṇavilāsaṇayaṁ jaṇayaï viralaṁ suyaṁ nārī

ēyaṁ jaṇappavāyaṁ nisuṇittā cintaī u dhaṇadēvō

saccaṁ bhaṇanti ēē na hu juttaṁ majjha ērisayaṁ

tā paradēsaṁ gantu viḍhavittā bhūribhūipabbhāraṁ

vilasāmi jahicchāē dīṇā 'ṇāhāṇa avisaṅkō

iya cintiya dhaṇadēvō māupiūṇaṁ sagāsamāgamma

viṇayapaṇaüttamaṅgō kayañjalī bhaṇiumāḍhattō

tubbhēhiṁ aṇunnāō gantūṇaṁ tāya! annadēsammi

viḍhavāmi bhūridavvaṁ iya icchā sampayaṁ majjha

tā aṇujāṇaü tāō pujjantu maṇōrahā imē majjha

gacchāmi annadēsaṁ vaṇijjabuddhīē sayamēva

bhaṇiyaṁ jaṇaṇīē taō gamaṇavayaṇampi dussahaṁ putta!

acchaü tā dūre cciya puṇa gamaṇaṁ annadēsammi

annaṁ ca atthi lacchī tuha jaṇaēṇāvi ajjiyā putta!

jīē vilasantōvi hu antaṁ kāuṁ na sattō si

aviya jaṇaēṇa ya tuha puttaya! atthuppattīē kāraṇaṁ jaṁ jaṁ

taṁ savvaṁ kāraviyaṁ kiṁ kajjaṁ tuha vaṇijjēṇa?

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ jāvajjavi ammi! bālaō puttō

tāva niyajaṇaṇisihiṇē pharisantō lahaï sōhampi

vōlīṇabālabhāvō chippaï pāvēṇa taṁ karēmāṇō

taha piulacchī jaṇaṇivva hōi susamatthaputtāṇaṁ

susamatthō vi hu jō jaṇayaajjiyaṁ sampayaṁ nisēvēi

sō ammi! tāva lōē mamaṁva uvahāsaṁ lahaï

iya bhaṇiuṁ dhaṇadēvō aṁsujalupphuṇṇalōyaṇō sahasā

mukkalaha iha bhaṇantō paḍiō jaṇaṇīē calasēṇu

tō dhaṇadhammō sēṭṭhī nāuṁ avasāṇa- (ya) kāraṇaṁ tassa

vajjaraï puttaṁ! kō tujjha vañchiē kuṇaï vigghanti?

jaṇaēṇaṁ jaṇaṇī puttaviōgaṁ aṇicchamāṇīvi

kahakahavi hu saṇṭhaviyā vinnāyasuyāvamāṇēṇa

ēvaṁ sō dhaṇadēvō māyāvittēhiṁ abbhaṇunnāō

paradēsagamaṇajōgaṁ gahiūṇa caüvvihaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ

aṭṭhāhiyamahimāō kārāvēttā jiṇindabhavaṇēsu

sampūiya sāhujaṇaṁ saṁmāṇiya māṇaṇijjajaṇaṁ

sayalammi tammi nayarē kāriya āghōsaṇaṁ jaṇē miliē

nēmittiyaāiṭṭhē suhadivasē vihiyamaṅgallē

gahiūṇa pavarasaüṇaṁ aṅgīkāuṁ kusaggavaranayaraṁ

hiyabandhuvaṇiyasahiō nīhariō niyayanayarāō

ēvaṁ sō dhaṇadēvō saṁvāhiyasahapayaṭṭajaṇaniyarō

lahulahupayāṇaēhiṁ vaccaï saha garuyasatthēṇa

tattō 'ṇuvāsaraṁ sō satthō vasimaṁ aïkkamēūṇa

aha kamasō sampattō ēkkaṁ aïbhīsaṇaṁ aḍaviṁ

jattha adīsantāṇavi ghaṇapattalapaürapāyavattaṇaō

kūiyasarasaṁsavaṇā gammaï vihagāṇa atthittaṁ

annaṁ ta jīē lōyā nīipahāṇassa puhaïpālassa

nayarīē iva na kuṇanti kahavi ummagasañcaraṇaṁ

viyaḍāḍavīē tīē majjhaṁmajjhēṇa vayaï sō satthō

niyakōlāhalapaḍiravapaḍipūriyajunnataruvivarō

tuṅgataruniyarasāhappasāhasañchannaambarattaṇaō

savvampi vahaï diyahaṁ alaggaravikiraṇasantāvō

kavikaguyugarutaravōkkārasavaṇasahasuttasantabahuvasahō

uttasiyavasahavālaṇanimittapamukkahakkārō

hakkārasaddapaḍiravasaṁsavaṇuttāsiyāṇa sayarāhaṁ

āyannantō disi disi ghūyāṇaṁ bhūrihuṅkārē

vasahakaṇṭhapalambiraghaṇṭiyā-raṇiyapūriyabhūritarambarō

visakhurukkhayarēṇunirantarō, vayaï tattha sa vāṇiyasatthaō

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsō ēttha samappaï aḍavipavēsassa vannaṇō nāma

surasundarināmāē kahāē paḍhamō paricchēō

aha annavāsarammī kamēṇa bahuvōliyāē aḍavīē

gahiya jalāsayamēgaṁ aha sō āvāsiō satthō

aha tammi satthalōē ulladdiyasayalavasahaniyarammi

jalaïndhaṇāiaṭṭhā iō taō pariyaḍantammi

pamukkēsu disi disi caraṇatthaṁ savvavasahamahisēsu

pāraddhēsu ya takkālamuciyakiccēsu lōēṇa

nāūṇa paṇihivasaō bhōyaṇakajjammi āulaṁ satthaṁ

satthammi tammi paḍiyā jhaḍitti bhillāṇa dhāḍitti

aviya

navamuggavannaaḍḍaṇaḍhakkiyaājāṇubhīsaṇasarīrā

masirāsī iva kālā kuviyakayantōvva duppicchā

kharabībhacchasarīrā palāsapattēhiṁ vihiyasēharayā

guñjāphalaratacchā ubbhaṅkharakēsamapabbhārā

sanaddhabaddhakavayā paṭṭhipaēsā 'vaṇaddhatōṇīrā

kannāyaḍḍhiyadhaṇuhapaṭṭhadīsantabhallōḍā

kēvi asivaggahatthā kēvi hu karagahiyalaüḍayā avarē

gumphaṇaphēraṇasuṅkāraēhiṁ jīyaṁ va avaṇēntā

dhiṭṭhāniṭṭhurahiyayā disō disiṁ ‘māri māri’ bhaṇamāṇā

annāyā ēva kuōvi jjhatti bhillā samāvaḍiyā

paḍiēsu taō tēsuṁ satthō savvō vi āulībhūō

bhillāṇa paürabhāvā vakkhēvā satthapurisāṇa

aha tammi saraṇarahiē lhasijjantē samatthasatthammi

dappaparipūriyaṅgā hakkiya jampanti kēvi narā

rē! rē! pisāyarūvā! katthiṇhiṁ jāha diṭṭhipahapaḍiyā

payaḍaha savvaṁ jaï atthi tumhamiha pōrisaṁ kimpi

kēvi puṇa bhīruhiyayā varayā dasaṇaüḍagahiyaaṅguliṇō

hā! hā! rakkhaha rakkhaha ēvaṁ kaluṇāiṁ jampanti

kēvi hu luṇṭijjantā iō taō taha pahammamāṇā ya

kīvā palāyaṇaṭṭhā tattha gavēsanti chiddāṇi

kēvi kahakahavi pāviyachiddā gāḍhaṁ ca khasaphasēmāṇā

saṇiyaṁ saṇiyaṁ ōsakkiūṇa līyanti gahaṇēsu

kēvi hu vēviradēhā sịdhilīkayakacchabandhaṇā dhaṇiyaṁ

pamukkapurisayārā aṅgīkayadīṇajaṇacēṭṭhā

paricattasayalalajjā kahakahamavi mōkkhaṇaṁ vimaggantā

tēsiṁ ciya pāvāṇaṁ, kuṇanti bahucāḍukammāṇi

kēvi hu mayamiva bhūpaṭṭhisaṇṭhiyaṁ appayaṁ payaṁsanti

kēvi hu chuhanti gaṇṭhiṁ mahīē pakkhāṇi jōēttā

jēvi hu iō taō indhaṇāiaṭṭhā gayāsi satthāō

tēvi hu kalayalasaddaṁ sōuṁ vaccanti dūrayaraṁ

rē! lēha haṇaha bandhaha māraha vayaṇāiṁ bharaha dhūlīē

summanti tattha satthē disi disi ēvaṁvihā saddā

ēyāvasarammi taō pāsittu iō taō vilumpantaṁ

bhillēhiṁ satthalōyaṁ kaïvayaniyapurisapariyariō

uppāēntō tēsiṁ āgiīē cēva cittasaṅkhōhaṁ

vasunandayakhaggakarō dhaṇadēvō ēvamullavaï

rē! rē! pāvā! jaï atthi tumha iha kāvi dappakaṇḍūī

tā havaha majjha puraō sahasā taṁ jēṇa avaṇēmi

mā bhaṇaha jaṁ na bhaṇiyaṁ ēsa kasavaṭṭaō supurisāṇa

na hi niyajuvaïsalahiyā purisā purisattaṇamuvēnti

hā! dhī! dhī! ēyassa u rē! duṭṭhā! tumha purisagārassa

nāsantalōyapaṭṭhīdhāvaṇaüvaladdhāpasarassa

ēvaṁ ca nisāmittā dōccaṁ taccaṁ samullavantassa

dhaṇadēvassullāvē suhaḍāṇavi bhūribhayajaṇagē

rē! rē! lēha imassavi phēḍēmō dhīrayaṁ kirāḍassa

ēvaṁ samullavantā valiyā tē jhatti tayabhimuhaṁ

pattā ya āhasantā dhaṇadēvassantiyaṁ samantā tē

tikkhāsikōntatōmarabhallīhi ya pahariuṁ laggā

dhaṇadēvōvi asaṅkō tahā payaṭṭēsu tēsu bhillēsu

tāṇamuramōḍiūṇaṁ kuṇaï niyapōrisaṁ payaḍaṁ

jaha jaha tē bhillanarā dēnti pahārē daḍhaṁ dayāhīṇā

dhaṇadēvō uṇa taha taha abbhasiyakalō pavañcēi

aviya pharaēṇa kēvi hu iō taō kēvi kāyakaraṇēṇaṁ

kēvi hu dūrāucciya ēntē khaggābhidhāēṇa

kahakahavi hu bhillēhiṁ gahiō pharaēhiṁ uṭṭhahēūṇa

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēhiṁ rē! rē! ēsō satthāhivō vaṇiō

tā bandhiūṇa ēyaṁ akkhayadēhaṁ tu pallināhassa

appēmō jēṇēsō dēi vaṇiō dhaṇaṁ bahuyaṁ

tattō ya tēhiṁ gantuṁ pallīvaïṇō samappiō ēsō

ētthantarammi diṭṭhō dhaṇadēvō dēvasammēṇa

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiō sadukkhamēvaṁ tu pallināhassa

hā! hā! sāmiya! ēsō mahāṇubhāvō sa dhaṇadēvō

jēṇa tayā tuha taṇaō jōgiyagahiōvi mōiō āsi

dāuṁ suvannalakkhaṁ nikkāraṇavacchalēṇaṁ tu

jayasēṇakumarajīviyadāyā dhaṇadhammasēṭṭhiputtō sō

paramuvayārī sāmiya! kahaṇu ahannēhiṁ vihiutti?

iya dēvasammabhaṇiyaṁ sōuṁ sambhantalōyaṇō sahasā

aha bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō muñcaha muñcaha mahābhāgaṁ

pāsaṭṭhiyapurisēhiṁ takkhaṇamucchōḍiyā ya sē bandhā

pallīvaïṇā tāhē avagụ̄dhō sāyaraṁ ēsō

tattō vihiyapaṇāmō takkālamuciyammi āsaṇē dinnē

pāsaṭṭhiyapurisēhiṁ, uvaviṭṭhō tattha dhaṇadēvō

tattō ya dīhadīhaṁ nīsasiya visāyagabbhiṇaṁ ēvaṁ

lajjāvaṇamiyavayaṇō pallivaī bhaṇiumāḍhattō

paramuvagāritti tumaṁ uvēcca kilahōsi amha daṭṭhavō

navaraṁ gihāgayassavi sāgayamēvaṁvihaṁ vihiyaṁ!

jāyaï avagāraphalō vihiō pāvāṇaṁ ahava uvayārō

sappassa jahā dinnaṁ duddhampi visattaṇamuvēi

pāvō ahaṁ kayagdhō suyajīviyadāyagassa jēṇajja

gihamāgayassa ēyaṁ ahammakammaṁ samāyariyaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ kīsa imaṁ vahaha guruvisāyanti

annāṇaṁ avarajjhaï, kō dōsō ēttha tumhāṇaṁ?

daṭṭhuṁ aṇannasarisaṁ bhillavaī tassa vayaṇavinnāṇaṁ

rūvaṁ taha suyaṇattaṁ puṇōvi aïrañjiō bhaṇaï

pēcchaha ēgammi narē kēttiyaguṇasamudaō samaṁ vasaï?

bahurayaṇā hu vasumaī saccō lōyappavāō 'yaṁ

dhī! dhī! maha purisattaṁ dhī! dhī! maha ērisāē vittīē

niyakulakalaṅkabhūyassa majjha dhī! purisajammēṇa

dhī! majjha jīviēṇa kukammanirayassa dhammarahiyassa

ēyārisapurisāṇaṁ luṇṭaṇakammammi nirayassa

ēttiyamēttēṇaṁ ciya dhannō 'haṁ jaṁ mahāṇubhāvassa

akkhayadēhassa imassa daṁsaṇaṁ jhatti sañjāyaṁ

jaï puṇa hōjja vivattī samayaṁ bhillēhiṁ jujjhamāṇassa

tā kaha majjha aünnassa hōjja pāvassa nitthārō?

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ appāṇaṁ nindiūṇa tō bhaṇaï

bhō! bhō! bhillā satthē jaṁ gahiyaṁ ēttha tumhēhiṁ

taṁ savvampi samappaha imassa dhaṇadēvanāmavaṇiyassa

tēhiṁ taṇamajjāyaṁ samappiyaṁ tassa taṁ savvaṁ

tattō sabālavuḍ̣dhē miliē lōgammi bhayavimukkammi

vajjaraï suppaïṭṭhō dhaṇadēvaṁ nēhagabbhamiṇaṁ

ēttō gāuyamēttē sīhaguhā nāma atthi mē pallī

tīē lahumāgacchaha ajja maha pāhuṇā hōha

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti tāhē sō satthō

dhaṇadēvamaggalaggō sīhaguhaṁ jhatti sampattō

āvāsiyassa tattō vasimāsannammi satthalōyassa

pallīvaïṇā nīō dhaṇadēvō niyayagahēmmi

abbhaṅgiūṇa vihiṇā sugandhatēllēhiṁ pavarajuvaīhiṁ

addhāṇaparissamanāsagēṇa varavāriṇā nhaviō

ghaṇasārasārasirikhaṇḍacacciō tāhē pallināhēṇa

sahiō pavarāhāraṁ bhōttūṇa samuṭṭhiō kamasō

kappūrapūrasahiē tambōlē āyarēṇa sē dinnē

vajjaraï dhaṇadēvō suhāsaṇatthō imaṁ vayaṇaṁ

ēsā hu tāva pallī āvāsō nigdhiṇassa lōyassa

tubbhēvi tassa pahuṇō aṇannasōjjannadayakaliyā

ēsō na sammajōgō ahivaïbhiccāṇa maha ṭhiyaṁ cittē

jaṁ sōyasaccadakkhinnavajjiyāṇaṁ imaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

bhillāṇaṁ nāhāvi hu jaṁ ērisaguṇagaṇēṇa sañjuttā

ēyaṁ maṇammi bhāvaï mahantamacchērayaṁ majjha

asarisasōjannajuyā tumhē ēyāē vasaha pallīē

uttamanarāvi hōuṁ sāhaha maha kēṇa kajjēṇa?

tō bhaṇaï supaïṭṭhō kiṁ kahiēṇaṁ imēṇa dhaṇadēva!

vañcaṇamavamāṇaṁ ciya maïjuttō nō pagāsējjā

tahavi hu bhaṇāmi mā hōu tujjha abbhatthaṇā imā vihalā

ēgaggamaṇō hōuṁ sāhijjantaṁ nisāmēhi

niccaṁ pamuiyanaranāriputragāmāvalīē ramaṇīō

bahudivasavannaṇijjō aṅgō nāmēṇa dēsō 'tthi

tammi ya puraṁ purāṇaṁ pavaraṁ suranayarasarisariddhillaṁ

bhayaḍamarakaravimukkaṁ siddhatthapuranti vikkhāyaṁ

tammi ya mayandhariukaraḍikaraḍanibbhēyaṇammi pattaṭṭhō

kambunnayasuggīvō suggīvō nāma naranāhō

sayalōrōhapahāṇā sundarasaradindubimbasamavayaṇā

buddhīē aṇannasamā kamalā nāmēṇa sē dēvī

tīē saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa taha ya rajjadhuraṁ

puvvabhavapunnapāyavasamappiyaṁ pālayantassa

vaccantēsu diṇēsuṁ tīē dēvīē aha ahaṁ puttō

jāō kayaṁ ca nāmaṁ vihiṇā maha suppaïṭṭhotti

lālijjantō pañcahiṁ dhāīhiṁ kamēṇa vaḍḍhamāṇō 'haṁ

sañjāō pañcavarisō māupiūṇaṁ kayāṇandō

ētthantarammi gimhē santāviyamahiyalē vaïkkantē

nivvaviyamahīvị̄dhō rasantasālūrasaṅghāō

pavahantabahalavāhiṇikhalahalasaṁsaddabahiriyadigantō

gajjantagahirajalaharadaṁsaṇanaccantasihinivahō

papphullaphullasōhiyanīvōhavirāyamāṇavaṇaniyarō

mucakundakuḍayasandiyarayagabbhiṇavāiyasamīrō

puliṇapaïṭṭhiyabālayakayavāluyadēulēhiṁ ramaṇīō

karisayajaṇapārambhiyahalaüttayacacciyabaïllō

harisavasahasirapāmara disi disi cabbhattabhūrikēyārō

pattō vāsārattō kaddamadullaṅghamaggillō

ēyārisammi navapāusammi pattammi annadivasammi

naranāhō suggīvō vihiṇā kayabhōyaṇō santō

candaṇacacciyadēhō parihiyamiusaṇhanimmaladugūlō

tambōlavaggahatthō samāgatō dēvibhavaṇammi

sattatalē pāsāē ārụ̄dhō uvarimāē bhūmīē

dēvīē kayaviṇaō maharihasējjāē āsīṇō

khaṇamēgamacchiūṇaṁ parihāsakahāhimpiyayamāē saha

siyavasaṇacchāiyāē kōmalatūlīē pāsuttō

tatō ya sajalajalaharagañjiyasaddēṇa naṭṭhaniddō sō

uṭṭhittuṁ saṁniviṭṭhō nijjūhagasaṇṭhiyamasūrē

addhāsaṇē niviṭṭhā kamaladēvīvi tāhē narapahuṇō

vajjaraï taō rāyā harisavasullasiyarōmañcō

maha (naha) saṅgamagaruyasamullasantamaṇaharapaōharā jhatti

pēccha piē! sañjāyā tujjha saricchā kubēradisā

taralattaṁ nayaṇāṇaṁ kuḍilattaṁ sutaṇu! tujjha kēsāṇaṁ

aṇukaraï pēccha vijjū ghaṇamajjhē cigicigāyantī

annaṁ ca piya! pēcchasu paribbhamantēhiṁ indagōvēhiṁ

najjaï pāusalacchī pacunniyā mahīyalē paḍiyā

pāusanarindanavasaṅgamammi jāyammi bhūmimahilāē

hariyaṅkuracchalēṇaṁ pēcchasu rōmañcaō jāō

niṭṭhura karapasarēṇaṁ imēṇa santāviā imā puhaī

iya rōsēṇava ruddhō ghaṇēhiṁ sūrassa karapasarō

maha āgamēvi piyavirahiyāṇa mahilāṇa kiṁ na phuṭṭāiṁ

hiyayāiṁ sāmarisaṁ vijjujjōēṇa jōēi

nāuṁ maha āgamaṇaṁ tahavi hu kiṁ calliyā piyā mōttuṁ

gajjantō rōsēṇava pahiyāṇaṁ dalaï hiyayāiṁ

dhavalabalāyādạ̄dhō vijjulayācavaladīhajīhālō

kasaṇaśarīrō dhāvaï pahiyāṇaṁ pāusapisāō

pēccha suracāvaniggayadhārābāṇēhiṁ virahihiyayāiṁ

vindhantō uvahasaïva pañcasaraṁ pañcasarasahiyaṁ

ētthantarammi dēvī naranāhaṁ bhaṇaï harisitā santī

sēsaüūṇa naravara! abbhahiō pāusō ēsō

mōttūṇa virahiṇijaṇaṁ suhaō jaṁ ēsa kāmuyajaṇassa

pāmaravacchataṇōsahipamuhāṇaṁ tahaya jīvāṇaṁ

aha bhaṇaï puhaïnāhō īsiṁ hasēūṇa, dēvi! taṁ saccaṁ

āhīṇaṁ sañjāyaṁ jaṁ summaï ēttha lōgammi

dhāyā purisā pēcchanti āyārā dhāyacaṁ disāvalayaṁ

taha dēvi! tumaṁ suhiyā savvaṁ suhiyanti mannēsi

savvēvi dēvi! uuṇō saünnalōyassa honti suhahēū

punnavihūṇāṇa puṇō pāusasamaōvi duhahēū

ō! pēccha pēccha sundari! addhasamārammi jarakuḍīrammi

ōghasarasayavirāiyavirāiyaḍimbhasamūhē ruyantammi

niyayaghariṇīē bāḍhaṁ cōijjantō puṇō puṇō varaō

āvaraṇarahiyadēhō hammantō vāridhārāhiṁ

uddhusiyarōmakūvō sīyalaanilēṇa saṅkuiyagattō

ēsō dariddapurisō kahakahavi samāraï kuḍīraṁ

ōlambiyakannajuyaṁ hammantaṁ guruyavāridhārāhiṁ

ōluggabhaggadēulakōṇagayaṁ rāsabhaṁ niyasu

taha pēccha imaṁ sundari! suṇahaṁ cullīē sunnagēhammi

sīēṇa kuṇukuṇantaṁ kharakharakhaḍḍaṁ khaṇēmāṇaṁ

taha pēccha jarabaïllā jalaharadhārāvalīhi hammantā

īriyāsamiuvva muṇī vaccanti mahiṁ palōēntā

sēvāliyabhūmitalē phillusamāṇā ya thāmathāmammi

hatthagayalaṭṭhikhaṇḍā bhikkhaṁ pariyaḍaï jararōrō

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï dēvīē tāva kañcuī jhatti

pāyavaḍaṇuṭṭhiō aha vasudattō bhaṇiumāḍhattō

dēvēṇa jō u puvviṁ paṭṭhaviō āsi campanayarīē

sirikittivammarannō dūō dāmōdarō nāma

sō dēvapāyadaṁsaṇasuhakaṅkhī āgaō duvārammi

ciṭṭhaï, ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē dēvō pamāṇanti taṁ sōccā

diṭṭhīē āpucchiya dēviṁ sahasatti uṭṭhiō rāyā

atthāṇamaṇḍavassa u āsannō jāva sampattō

tāva ya vijjucamukkāraṇantaraṁ caṇḍacaḍaḍasaṁsaddō

āsannō sañjāō bhēsiyanaranārisaṅghāō

tayaṇantaraṁ ca mahāhāravasaṁmīsaṁ samuṭṭhiyaṁ saddaṁ

dēvīgihammi sōuṁ sahasā valiō mahīnāhō

vajjaraï dēvidhāvī ruyamāṇī dhagdharēṇa saddēṇa

naravara! muṭṭhā muṭṭhā dēvī vijjūē daddhatti

daṭṭhūṇa bhūmipaḍiyaṁ dēvīdēhaṁ jiēṇa paricattaṁ

hā! hā! hatti bhaṇantō rāyā mucchāvasaṁ pattō

daṭṭhūṇa bhūmipaḍiyaṁ naranāhaṁ mucchiyaṁ vigayacēṭṭhaṁ

bhūritarō sañjātō pariyaṇaakkandasaddōvi

pāsaṭṭhiyapurisēhiṁ sīyalapavaṇāiyammi vihiyammi

rāyāvi vigayamucchō vilaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattō

hā vallahi! hā sāmiṇi! hā jīviyadāyagē! visālacchi!

hā maha hiyayanivāsiṇi! hā! kattha gayā mamaṁ mōttuṁ?

hā gōradēṁhi! hā pihupaōharē! hā sukōmalasarīrē!

hā kaha nigghiṇavihiṇā tuha uvariṁ pāḍiyā vijjū?

ghaṇasāraghusiṇacaccaṇaüciyasarīrammi kaha ṇu hayavihiṇā

vijjūnivāō vihiō majjha aünnēhiṁ pāvēṇa?

hā dēvi tujjha virahē nāranārīsaṅkulaṁ imaṁ nayaraṁ

uvvasiṁyanayarasarisaṁ aḍavisamāṇaṁ ca paḍihāi

kila dēvi! taṁ bhaṇantī tuha virahē acchiuṁ na sakkēmi

taṁ kaha ahaṁ ahannō tumaē sahasā pariccatō

hā! kiṁ na kimpi jampasi kiṁvā taṁ suyaṇu! majjha ruṭṭhā si

kiṁva maē avaraddhaṁ sundari! taṁ majjha sāhēsu?

taṁ ciya maha vallahiyā nēhō maha natthi annaïtthīsu

tujjha kaē paricattō sayalō ōrōhanārijaṇō

tahavi tumaṁ kiṁ sundarī! nibbhararattassa dēsi nālāvaṁ?

tā pasiya pasiya sāmiṇi! uṭṭhiya maha dēsu paḍivayaṇaṁ

ēmāi jāva vilavaï vivihaṁ rāyā sakaluṇasaddēṇa

tāva ahaṁ sampattō rōvantō tattha dhaṇadēva!

ucchaṅgē viṇivēsiya mamaṁ taō gāḍhakaluṇasaddēṇa

taṁ cēva palavamāṇō sudīharaṁ ruvaï bālōvva

ētthantarammi mantī sumaīnāmō bhaṇaï naranāha

dēva! alaṁ runnēṇa mayakiccaṁ kuṇaha dēvīē

bhaṇaï taō naranāhō candaṇadārūṇi bāhiṁ nīṇēha

dēvīē jēṇa samayaṁ ahampi aggīē vissāmi

tō bhaṇaï sumaïmantī kāyarajaṇacēṭṭhiēṇa kiṁ imiṇā

maraṇa 'jjhavasāaiṇaṁ, avalambasu dhīra! dhīrattaṁ

maraṇēṇa tujjha naravara! dēsō savvōvi hōi jaṁ gammō

paḍivakkhanaravarāṇaṁ bālō taha supaïṭṭhotti

dēvāṇaṁ bambhaṇāṇa ya ligīṇaṁ taha pāgayajaṇassa

dhammakiriyāō savvā vahanti dēvē dharantammi

mahilāmēttassa kaē na hu juttaṁ tumha uttamanarāṇa

asamañjasamāyariuṁ vinnāyajagassabhāvāṇaṁ

aviya niruvakkamakāyassavi usabhajiṇindassa āidēvassa

maraṇaṁ jāyaṁ jaïyā kā gaṇaṇā annamaṇuēsu?

nijjiyapaḍivakkhassavi chakkhaṇḍamahīsarassa bharahassa

jaïyā jāyaṁ maraṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā annamaṇuēsu

garuyaparakkamanijjiyariubalapāikkaccakkakayarakkhā

sōṇḍīrā naravaïṇō sōmajasā ' 'iccajasapamuhā

jaï tāva tē ya nihāyā pāvakayantēṇa nigghiṇamaṇēṇa

anivāriyapasarēṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā annalōyammi?

jēsimpi ya tittīsaṁ āuyamudahīṇa pavaradēvāṇaṁ

tēsimpi hōi cavaṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā annasattēsu?

bhavaṇavaïvāṇamantarajōisiyāṇaṁ vimaṇavāsīṇaṁ

jaï nāma hōi cavaṇaṁ kā gaṇaṇā maṇuyalōyammi?

sō kōvi natthi jīvō tilōyamajjhammi jō vasaṁ na gaō

maccussa pāvamaïṇō mōttuṁ siddhē suhasamiddhē

iya kālakavaliyaṁ pēcchiūṇa sayalampi tihuaṇaṁ dēva!

jāyammi dēvimaraṇē kiṁ sōgaṁ kuṇaha vihalaṁ tu?

jujjaï kāuṁ sōgō maraṇaṁ jaï hōjja tīē ēkkāē

sāhāraṇammi maraṇē kō sōgō kiṁva runnēṇa?

aïtaṇutaṇaggasaṅgayajalalavatullammi jīviyavvammi

niddāsaṅgē jaṁ puṇa uṭṭhijjaï taṁ mahacchariyaṁ

iya lōyassa sarūvaṁ kuviyakayantassa ērisaṁ daṭṭhuṁ

dēvimaraṇammi naravara! na hu juttaṁ sōgakaraṇanti

ēvaṁ ca bahuvigappaṁ bhaṇiō sō sumaïṇā naravarindō

takkāluciyaṁ savvaṁ maïkiccaṁ kuṇaï dēvīē

kaïvayadiṇāiṁ paricattalōyasambhāvaṇāivāvārō

gahagahiō iva ciṭṭhaï rāyā dēvīē sōgēṇa

sumaïmuhēhiṁ tāvaya nāṇāvihasōyamōyaṇapaḍūhiṁ

bōhijjantō girāhiṁ jāō kālēṇa gayasōgō

nāūṇa aṭṭhavarisaṁ mamaṁ taō garuyaputtanēhēṇa

saṅgahiya uvajjhāyaṁ gāhēi kalāṇasandōhaṁ

gahiē kalākalāvē gāmasahassaṁ tayā mahaṁ dinnaṁ

maha daṁsaṇēṇa rāyā sāhāraï dēvivirahampi

aha annayā kayāivi atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō jhatti

paṇamiya duvāravālō vajjaraï sūhavō ēvaṁ

campāpurīō sāmiya! mahantaō kittidhammanaravaïṇō

dēvassa daṁsaṇatthaṁ ciṭṭhaï paḍihārabhūmīē

sigghaṁ pavēsasutti ya bhaṇiē sō rāiṇā aṇunnāō

āgamma vihiyaviṇaō uvaviṭṭhō uciyaṭhāṇammi

tambōlāipayacchaṇapuvvaṁ sō rāiṇā samullaviō

āgamakāraṇaṁ bhō! sāhasu tō bhaṇiumāḍhattō

campāē puravarīē supasiddhō cēva dēvapāyāṇaṁ

vitthāriyavimalakittī rāyā sirikittidhammō 'tthi

nijjiyasurindasundarirūvātisayā samatthamahilāṇa

abbhahiyā sē dēvī kittimaī lōyavikkhāyā

tīya dhūyā sōhaggarūvaviṇṇāṇagāravagdhaviyā

pāyālakannayasamā kaṇayavaī nāma varakannā

sampattajōvvaṇā sā ābharaṇavibhūsiyā piusayāsē

paṭṭhaviyā māūē taduciyavaradāṇaaṭṭhāē

āgamma pāyapaḍiyā piuṇā sā saharisaṁ niucchaṅgē

viṇivēsiya avagụ̄dhā bhaṇiyā ya imaṁ tu sā kannā

putti! niyahiyayaïṭṭhaṁ sāmantamahantayāṇa majjhammi

sāhasu jēṇa tuhaṁ sō kijjaï bhattā, kimannēṇaṁ?

ēvaṁ piuṇā bhaṇiyā lajjāē ahōmuhī ṭhiyā bālā

puṇaruttaṁ puṭṭhāvi hu na kiñci paḍiuttaraṁ dēi

tō cintiuṁ payattō ēyā lajjāluyā imā varaī

na hu sakkaï vajjariuṁ ēsō maha tāya! iṭṭhotti

tā cintēmi sayaṁ ciya aṇurūvamimīē pavarabhattāraṁ

vinnāṇarūvasampayakaliyaṁ varavaṁsaüppannaṁ

khaṇamēgamacchiūṇaṁ rāyā cintāurō bhaṇaï tattō

putti! tuha rūvasarisō bhattā laddhō maē iṇhiṁ

siddhatthapurē rāyā suggīvō nāma maha paraṁ mittaṁ

tassa tumaṁ gaccha lahuṁ sayaṁvarā, ēttha kiṁ bahuṇā?

ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiyamēttē sā kannā dēva! tumha nāmēṇa

nisuēṇaṁ ciya jāyā harisavasullasiyarōmañcā

nāūṇa tīē bhāvaṁ rāyā sampēkkhiuṇa maha vayaṇaṁ

vajjaraï, taṁ mahābala! vaccasu siddhatthanayarammi

ghēttuṁ sayaṁvaramimaṁ kaṇagavaïṁ bhūribhūisañjuttaṁ

kaïvayabalasañjuttō sōhaṇatihikaraṇanakkhatō

jaṁ āṇavēsi bhaṇiuṁ tattō haṁ taṁ gahīya sañcaliō

jāva ya kamēṇa ēttō jōyaṇamēttammi sampattō

ajja rayaṇīvirāmē kaïvayaturaēhiṁ vēgavantēhiṁ

uggiliya āgaō huṁ tumhāṇa piyaṁ nivēēmi

dēva! mahamēyamāgamaṇakāraṇaṁ pucchiyaṁ hi jaṁ tumaē

ēvaṁ cavatthiyammi sampaï dēvō pamāṇanti

harisāūriyahiyaō aha rāyā bhaṇaï pariyaṇaṁ niyayaṁ

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ nayarē kannaṁ pavēsēha

tō pariyaṇēṇa sammaṁ tahatti sampāḍiyammi vayaṇammi

sōhaṇalaggē rannā pariṇīyā tattha kaṇagavaī

sā rannō kaṇagavaī kālēṇa aīva vallahā jāyā

maha māūē ṭhāṇē vihiyā aha paṭṭabaddhā sā

aïvallahampi vīsaraï māṇūsaṁ dēsakālaantariyaṁ

vallīsamaṁ hi pimmaṁ jaṁ āsannaṁ tahiṁ caḍaï

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ maha piuṇō tīē gāḍharattassa

sịdhilīkayasēsōrōharamaṇigamaṇāicēṭṭhassa

aha annayā kayāivi kaṇagavaīē suō samuppannō

surahotti vihiyanāmō pattō sō kumarabhāvammi

annadiyahammi ēyaṁ ēgantē bhaṇaï kaṇagavaī dēvī

juvarāyapaē kiṁ navi ahisiccaï dēva! mē puttō

tō bhaṇaï naravarindō jēṭṭhē puttammi suppaïṭṭhammi

vijjantē na hu juttaṁ juvarāyaṁ ṭhāviuṁ surahaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvīē taō jēṭṭhaṭṭhavaṇē nihōḍaü kō ṇu?

jaï tujjha ahaṁ daïyā tā surahaṁ kuṇasu juyarāyaṁ

tāhē rannā bhaṇiyaṁ suṭṭhuṁ piyā taṁ sulōyaṇē! majjha

kintu imassa 'ṇurattā sāmantamahantayā savvē

taha ēsō susamatthō ēvaṁ vihiē vihējja taṁ kimpi

avamāṇiō hu jēṇaṁ mamāvi rajjaṁ avaharējjā

tō bhaṇaï hasiya dēvī ērisasattēṇa kaha tumaṁ vihiṇā

piyayama! rāyā vihiō navari kirāḍō kaō hontō?

jēṇēva suppaïṭṭhō ērisaō ukkaḍō payāvēṇa

tēṇēva imaṁ sigghaṁ kaṭṭhaharē khivasu jattēṇa

tattō ya majjha puttaṁ juvarāyaṁ ṭhāviuṁ payattēṇa

acchasu vigayāsaṅkō rajjaṁ ca mamaṁ ca māṇantō

ēvaṁ dēvīvayaṇaṁ sōuṁ paḍiuttaraṁ adāūṇaṁ

rāyā samuṭṭhiūṇaṁ atthāṇē gantumuvaviṭṭhō

ēyaṁ ca dēvivayaṇaṁ sūhaviyānāmiyāē cēḍīē

pacchannē sōūṇaṁ savvaṁ dhaṇadēva! maha siṭṭhaṁ

taṁ sōuṁ maha vigappō cittē ēyārisō samuppannō

kiṁ kaṇagavaīē vuttō karējja ēvaṁ piyā majjha?

ahavā na gaṇanti puvvanēhaṁ na ya nīiṁ nēya lōyaavavāyaṁ

na ya bhāviāvayāō purisā mahilāṇa āyattā

tā jā na kimpi annaṁ dēvīvayaṇāō maha piyā kuṇaï

tāva ahiṭṭhēmi sayaṁ rajjaṁ, piyaraṁ viṇāsēttā

ahava na ēyaṁ juttaṁ vivēyajuttassa majjha kāuṁ jē

tā bandhiūṇa piyaraṁ kaṭṭhaharagayaṁ aṇucarāmi

kiṁvā kaṇagavaïṁ ciya saha surahēṇaṁ nayāmi jamavayaṇē

kiṁvā kaṭṭhaharammi dōnnivi ghēttēmi bandhaüṁ?

ahavā kiṁ maha imiṇā pēkkhāmō tāva jaṁ piyā kuṇaï

adiṭṭhapāṇiyammi na hu juttaṁ pāṇahummuyaṇaṁ

aha rāyā maha uvariṁ diṇē diṇē piyayamāē bhannantō

jāō sịdhilasiṇēhō kannavisaṁ jaṁ mahantavisaṁ

sahasatti annadiyahē kimpi misaṁ dāviūṇa maha rannā

hariyaṁ gāmasahassaṁ dinnaṁ lahukhēḍayaṁ ēkkaṁ

sañjāyaamarisēṇaṁ tāhē maē cintiyaṁ durāyāraṁ

mārēūṇa ēyaṁ rajjamahiṭṭhēmi, kiṁ bahuṇā?

ahavā na puvvapurisēhiṁ majjhaṁ vaṁsē kayaṁ imaṁ pāvaṁ

tamahampi kaha karōmī asārarajjassa kajjēṇa?

mahilāvayaṇēṇa imō rāgandhō kuṇaï, kuṇaü annāyaṁ

maha puṇa vivēyajuttassa handi! na hu ērisaṁ juttaṁ

tā kiṁ karēmi iṇhiṁ avamāṇaṁ tāva dūsahaṁ piuṇō

appavahōvi na juttō dēsaccāō paraṁ juttō

gantūṇamannadēsaṁ tamhā sēvāmi annanaranāhaṁ

huṁ tampi hu nahu juttaṁ avamāṇapayaṁ hi sēvatti

suggīvanarindasuō juyarāyā āsi ēsa riddhijuō

sampaï puṇa vaṇṭhōiva kaha sēvaṁ kuṇaï bhiccāṇa?

ēmāivayaṇavittharavajjaraṇasamujjaēṇa lōēṇaṁ

daṁsijjantō riūṇa kahaṁ gēhēsuṁ paribhamissaṁ?

tamhā kaïvayaniyapurisaparigaō akayaannajaṇasēvō

gantuṁ ciṭṭhāmi ahaṁ kammivi paccantadēsammi

jā jīvaï ēsa piyā ēyammi mayammi puṇa jahā juttaṁ

taïya cciya kāhāmō kiṁ iṇhiṁ tīē cintāē?

ēvaṁ viṇicchiyamaī kaïvayapiyapariyaṇēṇa pariyariō

sāmantamantipuranāyagēhiṁ rannā ya annāō

nīhariō tattō haṁ kamēṇa aha pāviuṁ imaṁ palliṁ

sīhaguhaṁ nāmēṇa acchiumēīē pāraddhaṁ

miliyā majjha aṇēgē bhillā cōrā kukammanirayā ya

tēhiṁ parivāriō haṁ sampaï pallīvaī jāō

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ tumhāṇaṁ kaha ṇu ēttha āvāsō

uttamanarāṇa pāviṭṭhalōyajōgāē pallīē?

ēyaṁ saṅkhēvēṇaṁ kahiyamavatthāṇakāraṇaṁ ēttha

taṁ tuha dhaṇadēva! maē garuyasiṇēhēṇa savvampi

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ avvō! jaṇaōpi ērisaṁ kuṇaï

avamāṇaṁ puttāṇaṁ dhī! dhī! saṁsāravāsassa

so cciya kajjavasēṇaṁ vallahaō hōi ēttha saṁsārē

kāraṇavasēṇa sōvi hu riuvva vēsō jaṇō hōi

paramatthaō na kōvi hu piō va sattū va atthi lōgammi

naï māyā nēya piyā sakajjavasaō jaṇō savvō

puttōvi sattusarisō dīsaï niyakāraṇē apujjantē

piuṇā suviṇīōvi hu dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa

taṁ ciya kumāra! mahappā taṁ ciya pasamassa laddhaparamatthō

taṁ ciya vivēyajuttō tumae cciya maṇḍiyā vasuhā

piuṇā 'vamāṇiōvi hu annaṁ asamañjasaṁ akāūṇaṁ

santammi balē tahavi hu dēsaccāō kaō jēṇa

ēmāivayaṇavittharaavarōpparavaḍḍhamāṇanēhāṇaṁ

tāṇaṁ pañca va satta va vōlīṇā vāsarā jāva

tāvaya samatthasatthaṁ daṭhṭhūṇaṁ gamaṇaücchugībhūyaṁ

dhaṇadēvō āpucchaï gamaṇatthaṁ suppaïṭṭhaṁ taṁ

tumha viōgō dūsahō ēsō satthō samucchugībhūō

taṁ kumārō! amha jāyaṁ ēttha taḍī ēttha vagghotti

ēēṇaṁ ciya nēcchanti sāhavō sajjaṇēhiṁ saṁsaggiṁ

jamhā viōgavihuriyahiyayassa na ōsahaṁ annaṁ

jahavi hu vahaï na jīhā ērisavayaṇē samullavijjantē

tahavi hu bhaṇāmi muñcasu gacchāmō sampayaṁ amhē

tā kimpi cintiūṇaṁ khaṇantaraṁ dīhara ca nīsasiuṁ

vajjaraï suppaïṭṭhō savisāyaṁ ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ

amhārisēhiṁ gihamāgayāṇa tumhārisāṇaṁ suyaṇāṇaṁ

kō uvayārō kīraü ērisaṭhāṇē vasantēhiṁ?

tahavi hu bhaṇāmi kiñcivi kāyavvō nēva patthaṇābhaṅgō

jēṇa parakajjasāhaṇanirayā khalu sajjaṇā honti

tattō phurantanimmalama ūhavicchu riyadasadisā ' 'bhōgō

ēkkōvi aṇēgaguṇō pavaramaṇī tassa uvaṇīō

daṭṭhuṁ divvamaṇiṁ taṁ dīsantāṇēyalakkhaṇaṁ vimalaṁ

viyasiyalōyaṇajualō aha dhaṇadēvō imaṁ bhaṇaï

ērisapavaramaṇīṇaṁ maṇussakhēttammi sambhavō natthi

navaraṁ jaï suralōgē havējja na hu annakhēttammi

ēvaṁ viṇicchiyammivi tahavi hu kōūhalaṁ mahaṁ hiyaē

tō bhaṇasu kaha ṇu jāyā sampattī tumha ēyassa?

tō bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō sammaṁ hi viṇicchiyaṁ tumē bhadda!

māṇusakhēttasamutthō na hōi ēsō maṇī tāva

kintu suralōgajāō ēsō sampāviō jahamhēhiṁ

taṁ ēgamaṇō hōu jaï kōugamatthi tō suṇasu

puvvaṁ ēgammi diṇē pabhāyasamayammi gahiyakōdaṇḍā

caliō kaïvayaniyapurisaparigaō migavahaṭṭhāē

uttaradisāmuhō haṁ gāumēttammi bhūmibhāgammi

ghaṇapattalataruvarasaṅkulami viyarāmi jāva vaṇē

tāva ya nisuō saddō dūsahagurudukkhasūyaō kaluṇō

āgāsē mahilāē saghaggharaṁ rōyamāṇīē

hā! kaha majjha nimittē piyayama! atigaruyaāvayaṁ pattō?

hā! ajjaütta! iṇhiṁ tuha virahē natthi maha jīyaṁ

tadaṇantaraṁ ca kēṇavi hakkiya aïniṭṭhuraṁ samullaviyaṁ

kattō maha vasagāē sāhārō tujjha ēēṇa?

taṁ sōūṇaṁ majjhaṁ maṇammi kōūhalaṁ samuppannaṁ

jāva ya dōṇṇi va tiṇṇi va vaccāmi payāiṁ tā nisuō

ēgammi vaṇaniguñjē adissamāṇassa kassavi narassa

gurudukkhasūyaṇaparō mandō nitthaṇaṇasaṁsaddō

tattō mahantakōūhalēṇa tattōmuhō ahaṁ caliō

pēcchāmi sambalitaruṁ saralaṁ uttuṅgamaïgaruyaṁ

daṁsaṇamēttuppāiyaaïgaruyabhaēhiṁ rattanēttēhiṁ

kasiṇasarīrasamubmūyabhūripahābhariyagayaṇēhiṁ

nimmalamaṇivalayasamucchalantakantīē payaḍavayaṇēhiṁ

gururōsavasaviyambhiyaphāraphaṇāghōrabhuyagēhiṁ

dīharalalantajīhāsahassavipphuraṇabhīijaṇagēhiṁ

asarisaamarisavasavippamukkaphuṅkārasaddēhiṁ

aïgaruyapannagēhiṁ samantaō vẹ̄dhiyō aṇēgēhiṁ

ēgō divvāgārō purisō diṭṭhō ahē tassa

aïdūsahaviyaṇāvasavimukkapuṇaruttamandahuṅkāraṁ

ākaṇṭhavẹ̄dhiyaṁ taṁ daṭṭhuṁ purisaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ

dhī! dhī! hayavihiṇō vilasiyassa asamikkhiyassa ēyassa

ēyārisēvi purisē ērisadukkhaṁ karēntassa

ēmāi maē paridēviyammi bhaṇiyaṁ imaṁ taō tēṇaṁ

alamimiṇā tē paridēviēṇa suṇa tāva maha vayaṇaṁ

ciṭṭhaï cūḍāē mahaṁ majjhē baddhō phurantakiraṇillō

divvō maṇīṇa pavarō maṇī bhuyaṅgōhaviddavaṇō

jassa pabhāvēṇa imē ḍasiumaṇāvi hu cayanti nō ḍasiuṁ

ghōravisāvi hu sappā sappanti na baddhavayaṇavva

taṁ ghēttūṇaṁ varamaṇiṁ siñcasu salilēṇa tēṇa tō pacchā

acchōḍēsu bhuyaṅgē aṅgavilaggē mahamaṇēgē

āmanti bhaṇantēṇaṁ tavvayaṇaṁ sāyaraṁ kayaṁ savvaṁ

acchōḍiyā jalēṇaṁ jhatti vilīṇā aha bhuyaṅgā

aviya maṇisalilēṇaṁ sittā khaṇēṇa savvēvi pāviyā vilayaṁ

kharajālāvalijalaṇōvatāviyā mayaṇapiṇḍavva

aha sō paṇaṭṭhaviyaṇō sīyalataruchāhiyāē uvaviṭṭhō

mahapurisakayasukōmalakisalayasañchaṇṇasantharaē

ābhaṭṭhō paḍhamaṁ ca tēṇa ahayaṁ kattō tumaṁ āgatō,

kiṁvā nāma kahiṁ kulammi vimalē jāō si, kō tē piyā?

ēvaṁ bhō dhaṇadēva! tēṇa taïyā puṭṭhē maē sāhiyā

puvvuttā sayalāvi tujjha kahiyā jā sā paüttī tahiṁ

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsō ēttha samappaï vijjāharamōyaṇotti nāmēṇa

surasundarināmāē kahāē bīō paricchēō

aha sōvi maē puṭṭhō kēṇa tumaṁ ērisāē ghōrāē

khittō si āvayāē kēṇa va kajjēṇa bhadda! muhā

ēvaṁ ca pucchiō sō sadukkhamaïdīharaṁ ca nīsasiuṁ

cittabbhantaragurudukkhasūyagaṁ mōttu aṁsujalaṁ

aha sō bhaṇaï subhaṇiō saṁsārē rōgamōhiyamaṇāṇaṁ

sulahāō āvayāō jīvāṇa adīhadaṁsīṇaṁ

saṁsārasāgarammī paribbhamantāṇa bhadda! jīvāṇaṁ

na hu cōjjamāvayāhiṁ anijantiyakaraṇavaggāṇaṁ

puvvakayakammadōsā dukkhaṁ savvampi jāyaï jiyāṇaṁ

avarāhēsu guṇēsu ya nimittamētaṁ parō hōi

paramatthaō na kēṇaï suhaṁ va dukkhaṁ va kīraï narassa

puvvakayamēva kammaṁ suhaduhajaṇaṇammi tallicchaṁ

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō

tahavi hu visēsakāraṇaviyāṇaṇē amhaïcchatti

aha bhaṇaï bhō sundara! jaï ēvaṁ suṭṭhu tumha nibbandhō

tā ēgamaṇō hōuṁ sāhijjantaṁ nisāmēhi

atthētha bharahakhēttē vikkhāō khēyarāvalīgammō

tuṅgōvva ruppapuñjō dasadisipasarantakantillō

jharajharajharantanijjharahuṅkāraravēhiṁ bahiriyadiyantō

mayarandapāṇalampaḍaalivalayavirāyamāṇavaṇō

vahamāṇavāhiṇīṇaṁ disidisisuvvantakhalaharāsaddō

ṭhāṇē ṭhāṇē vijjāharōrupurapantisōhillō

vijjāpasāhaṇujjayavijjāharasaṁniruddhaēgantō

varasiddhāyayaṇēhiṁ parimaṇḍiya cūliyāsiharō

siddhāyayaṇapariṭṭhiyajiṇabimbaccaṇanimittamintīhiṁ

vivihavibuhāvalīṁhiṁ viṇāyamāṇambarā ' 'bhōgō

kayalīharaṭṭhiēhiṁ païmajjhaṇhaṁ vaṇē vaṇē bahusō

kantābiijjavijjāharēhiṁ kijjantasaṅgīō

aïmahurabhāraīē ṭhāṇē ṭhāṇammi cāraṇamuṇīhiṁ

pāraddhadēsaṇēhiṁ paḍibōhijjantajantugaṇō

puvvāvarasāgarapāviēṇa hōūṇa majjhadēsammi

pisuṇēṇava jēṇa kaō dubbhāvō bharahavāsassa

suvisāladakkhiṇuttaravibhattasẹ̄dhīdugēṇa sōhillō

āsiyasavviḍ̣dhīō vēyaḍ̣dhō nāma sēlotti

tatthatthi dakkhiṇāē sẹ̄dhīē khayaralōyapaḍipunnaṁ

bhamirakhayaraṅgaṇāgaṇanēurajhaṅkāraravamuhalaṁ

uttuṅgamagaratōraṇaasamāṇaduvāradēsasōhēhiṁ

niccaṁ virāyamāṇaṁ vijjāharabhavaṇavandēhiṁ

sayalataïlōkkalacchīniyanilayaṁ rayaṇasañcayaṁ nāma

nagaraṁ nayaraguṇaḍḍhaṁ pamudiyanaranārīsaṅghāyaṁ

tammi ya purammi bahuvihavijjāharasayasahassasaṅkinnē

parivasaï guṇanihāṇō pavaṇagaī nāma varakhayarō

vinnāṇaviṇayajuttā païṇō accantavacchalasahāvā

niyaparimalajiyabaülā baülavaī nāma sē bhajjā

tīē saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa tassa kālēṇa

ahamēgaēva puttō uppannō kayamaṇāṇandō

jammadiṇe cciya puranaracittacamukkārakārayaṁ majjha

vaddhāvaṇayaṁ piuṇā kāraviyamasamaharisēṇaṁ

kamasō ya bārasāhē vōlīṇē majjha jaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ

guratuṭṭhīē païṭṭhiyamahihāṇaṁ cittavēgotti

vōlīṇēsu ya kaïvayavarisēsu ahaṁ mahantabuddhissa

ajjhāvayassa suhatihirikkhammi samappiō piuṇā

tattō akālahīṇaṁ tahavihaajjhāvayappabhāvēṇa

niyamaïsāmatthēṇa ya gahiyāō kalāō sayalāō

niyakulakamāgayāō piuṇā vijjāō majjha dinnāō

nahagāmiṇipamuhāō jahavihiṇā sāhiyavvāō

daṁsiyamayaṇaviyāraṁ mahilājaṇahiyayamōhaṇamudāraṁ

aha kamasō sampattō ahayaṁ navajōvvaṇārambhaṁ

annammi diṇammi ahaṁ samāṇajōvvaṇavayaṁsapariyariō

pattō aṇēyatarusaṇḍamaṇḍiyaṁ maṇaharujjāṇaṁ

pāraddhavivihakīlā ciṭṭhāmō jā khaṇantaraṁ tattha

tāva ya gayaṇē diṭṭhā divvavimāṇāṇa riñchōlī

pasarantapavararayaṇōrudittivicchuriyanahayalā ' 'bhōyā

uttaradisā payaṭṭā surasundarī gēyasōhillā

taṁ daṭṭhu maē bhaṇiyaṁ kattha imō handi! dēvasandōhō

caliō calantakuṇḍalamuttāhaladhavalagaṇḍayalō?

īsi hasiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ majjha vayaṁsēṇa bandhudattēṇa

supasiddhamēva ēyaṁ vēyaḍḍhanagē vasantāṇaṁ

jiṇavandaṇatthamētthaṁ siddhāyayaṇēsu ēi suranivahō

niccampi vayaṁsa! aō pasiddhavatthummi kā pucchā?

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu nisuṇēsu

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ na ēti niccaṁ surā ēttha

ajja puṇō savimāṇā savviḍ̣dhīē mahantaharisēṇaṁ

dīsanti jaṁ vayantā tēṇa maē pucchiyaṁ mitta!

aha bhaṇaï bandhudattō khaṇantaraṁ cintiūṇa savitakkaṁ

huṁ nāyaṁ pāraddhā siddhāyayaṇēsu jattāō

pasarantasurahimalayāniluddhurō jēṇa vaṭṭaï vasantō

kisalaïyasayalataruvaravirāyamāṇōruvaṇaniyarō

aviya vāyantamalayamāruyacalantapattalavisālasāhāhiṁ

naccantiva taruṇō paharisēṇa mahumāsaāgamaṇē

kusumā ' 'mōyā ' 'yaḍ̣dhiyaaliulajhaṅkāragahirasaddēṇa

gāyantiva taruniyarā vasantamāsāgamē tuṭṭhā

mayarandapiñjarāō visaṭṭasugandhakusumavayaṇāō

vaṇarāīō hasantiva vasantamāsāgamaṁ daṭṭhuṁ

daṭṭhūṇava taruniyaraṁ mahusamaē bahalapattalacchāyaṁ

avamāṇiō palāsō kasiṇamuhō jhatti sañjāō

acchaü tā phalakālē phullimaṁsamaēvi kālimā vayaṇē

iya kaliuṁva palāsō cattō pattēhiṁ kiviṇōvva

daṭṭhūṇa vaṇasamiddhiṁ palāsaviḍavēhiṁ maüliyaṁ vayaṇaṁ

annēvi hu appattā parariddhiṁ nēya visahanti

aviya pāviyavasantamāsō vaṇammi nissēsapīyalōhiyaō

piyavirahiyapahiyāṇaṁ bhayajaṇaō kiṁsuyapisāō

annaṁ ca pañcasaralōddhaēṇaṁ mahumāsabiijjaēṇa dayarahiyaṁ

hammantīō gāḍhaṁ daṭṭhūṇava pahiyamahilāō

hasiyaṁva majjhasaṇṭhiyakalayaṇṭhikaēṇa kūiyaravēṇa

payaḍiyamañjarigurudantapantiyaṁ cūyaviḍavēhiṁ

daṭṭhūṇa pahiyanivahaṁ nihayaṁ mahumāsalōddhayanarēṇa

ōṇayamuhīō kusumaṁsuēhiṁ rōyantiva layāō

mayapahiyāṇa jalantiva ṭhāṇē ṭhāṇē mahantacīyāō

ghaṇakiṁsuyacchalēṇaṁ aliravamisimisiyasaddāō

nijjharataḍēsu taruṇō pavaṇapahallantajalanibuḍḍēhiṁ

sāhākarēhiṁ dēntiva jalañjaliṁ jattha pahiyāṇaṁ

kiñca ghaṇakiṁsuyanavaraṅgayavirāiyā baddhapavaramayaṇahalā

pāḍalakusumā sōhaī vasantalacchī navavahuvva

annaṁ ca buhasahiōvi hu sūrō kavvasattō vasantamāhappā

uvabhuñjiūṇa mīṇaṁ sampaï mēsassa ukkotti

tā ērisē vasantē disidisipasarantaparahuyāsaddē

vitthariyacaccarīravamuhariyaüjjāṇabhūbhāgē

vilasanti kāmuyajaṇā andōlijjanti taruṇajuvaīō

vittharaï paḍahayaravō piyanti varavāruṇiṁ taruṇā

sāhīṇapiyayamāṇaṁ taruṇīṇaṁ vallahammi mahumāsē

dhammaparāyaṇalōēṇa ēttha kīranti jattāō

jiṇabimbāṇaṁ bhattīē tēṇa ēē samāgayā dēvā

savvāyarēṇa vēyaḍḍhasiddhakūḍēsu jattatthaṁ

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ jaï ēvaṁ tō vayaṁsa! amhēvi

gantūṇa siddhakūḍē sāsayasavvannupaḍimāō

bhattīē paṇamiūṇaṁ karēsu niyamāṇusattaṇaṁ sahalaṁ

pēcchāmō jiṇajattaṁ suyakhayarōhēṇa kijjantaṁ

aha savvēhivi bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti suṭṭhu tē bhaṇiyaṁ

ētthantarammi pattō maha dhāisuō balō nāma

āgamma tēma bhaṇiyaṁ piuṇā tē cittavēga! saṁlattaṁ

ēsō hu rayaṇasañcayavatthavvō sayalakhayarajaṇō

nhāō vilittadēhō suhanēvatthō mahāvibhūīē

caliō jiṇajattāē āsannē siddhakūḍammi

tēṇa samaṁ amhēvi hu caliyā tā sigghamēva āgaccha

kayaṇhāṇāivihāṇā jēṇa samaṁ cēva gacchāmō

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ niyagēhē āgaō piusamīvē

tēvi ya majjha vayaṁsā niyaniyagēhēsu sampattā

kayaṇhāṇāivihāṇō saha piuṇā tāhē pavaṇagaïṇā haṁ

takkāluciyaṁ savvaṁ gahiūṇaṁ dhūvapupphāiṁ

nāgarajaṇēṇa sahiō uppaïō khaggasāmalaṁ gayaṇaṁ

gacchantēṇa kamēṇaṁ diṭṭhaṁ bhavaṇaṁ jiṇindassa

vāyantamaüyamāruyamandandōlantadhayavaḍagēhiṁ

sannaṁva karēmāṇaṁ āgamaṇatthaṁ jaṇōhassa

dunduhimaündamaddalatilimāpamuhēṇa tūrasaddēṇa

hakkārantēva jaṇaṁ jattāsamaē jiṇindassa

tattō kamēṇa pattā disi disi naccantaaccharāniyaraṁ

maṇaharagēyajhuṇīē āṇandiyabhaviyasandōhaṁ

nāṇāvihavatthēhiṁ kayaüllōyaṁ maṇōharāyāraṁ

vicchittīē lambiyanimmalavarahāraōcūlaṁ

viraïyaghaṇaphullaharaṁ vicittalambantatāriyāinnaṁ

pavarapaḍimaṇḍavēṇaṁ ucchāiyaaṅgaṇābhōyaṁ

nīsalataḍḍiyacandāyaēhiṁ maṇḍiyacaükkiyādēsaṁ

phullamayapavaratōraṇasōhiyamajjhaṁ jiṇindagihaṁ

tassa ya duvāradēsē nimmalajalapūriyāē vāvīē

kāuṇa pāyasōyaṁ niyayavayaṁsēhiṁ parivariō

jiṇabhavaṇaduvāraṭṭhiyaüccalliyaphullamāliyōhassa

pupphāiṁ gēṇhantō antō vihiṇā paviṭṭhō haṁ

pūiya jiṇindabimbē kāuṁ cīivandaṇaṁ jahāvihiṇā

bāhiṁ nīhariō haṁ uvaviṭṭhō khayaramajjhammi

vattē jiṇamajjaṇaē iō taō tattha sañcarantō haṁ

avarōpparadaṁsiyakōugēhiṁ sahiō vayaṁsēhiṁ

katthaï vilāsiṇijaṇaṁ pēcchantō naccamāṇayaṁ vivihaṁ

katthaï kavivaranivahaṁ jiṇacariyaṁ ahiṇavēmāṇaṁ

vīṇāravasaṁvaliyaṁ katthavi gīyajjhuṇiṁ nisāmēntō

viraïyavivihāyāraṁ katthavi ya baliṁ palōēntō

katthaï taruṇanarēhiṁ dijjantaṁ rāsayaṁ suṇēmāṇō

surasundarīhiṁ katthaï gijjantaṁ dhavalasaṅghāyaṁ

ēvaṁ ca jāva kōūhalēṇa avarāvarēsu ṭhāṇēsu

hiṇḍāmi tattha bhavaṇē līlāē samaṁ vayaṁsēhiṁ

tāva maha māulasuō saharisamāgamma sāiyaṁ dāuṁ

vajjaraï bhāṇuvēgō pabhūyakālāō diṭṭhō si

kusalaṁ ca pavaṇagaïṇō piubhagiṇīē ya baülavaïyāē?

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ kusalaṁ savvēsi, annaṁ ca

ētthēva āgayāi imāiṁ ciṭṭhanti bhadda! jiṇabhavaṇē

ammāpiūṇa mūlaṁ samāgaō tēṇa sahiō haṁ

sāyaramavagụ̄dhō sō tēhiṁ paüttiṁ ca pucchiō bhaṇaï

kusalaṁ maha jaṇagāṇaṁ nāgamaṇaṁ kāraṇāvēkkhaṁ

aha sō maē pabhaṇiō vittappāyā imā hu jiṇajattā

sampaï puṇa amhāṇaṁ āgacchasu pāhuṇō tāva

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu nisuṇēsu

maha cittabhāṇupiuṇā lahumāgacchējja iti bhaṇiyaṁ

tā cittavēga! sampaï taṁ ciya nagarammi ēhi mahataṇaē

ukkaṇṭhiō pagāmaṁ jaṁ acchaï tumha māulaō

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō ammāpīīhiṁ abbhaṇunnāō

bhāusamēō pattō nagaramahaṁ kuñjarāvattaṁ

tahiṁya ca cittabhāṇū maṁ daṭṭhūṁ suṭṭhu harisiō bhaṇaï

sundaramāyariyaṁ tē jamāgaō amha pāhuṇaō

niyayapaüttiṁ savvaṁ kahiuṁ kayabhōyaṇāivāvārō

pattāē rayaṇīē pāsuttō pavarasayaṇīē

tattha ya pabhāyasamaē lavamāṇē tambacūlaniurambē

diṭṭhō adiṭṭhapuvvō ēsō sumiṇō maē taïyā

kila dhavalaphullamālaṁ maṇōharaṁ daṭṭhu taggahaṭṭhāē

caliō haṁ na ya sakkēmi gēṇhiuṁ taṁ jayā kahavi

kēṇavi mittēṇa taō samappiyā āyarēṇa mē gahiyā

ōlambissaṁ galaē kila niyaē tāva sā jhatti

paḍiyā maha hatthāō katthavi ya gayatti nēya jāṇāmi

tāhē mahantadukkhaṁ tavvirahē majjha sañjāyaṁ

sukkāvi maē ēsā puṇōvi amilāṇakusumiyā vihiyā

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ kēṇavi kaṇṭhē viṇivēsiyā majjha

tāva paḍupaṭahajhallarikāhalabhambhāmaündasaddālaṁ

sōuṁ tūrassa ravaṁ jhatti paṇaṭṭhā mahaṁ niddā

tō harisavisāyaḍḍhaṁ daṭṭhuṁ sumiṇaṁ vicintiyaṁ hiyaē

kiṁ nāma majjha sūyaï adiṭṭhapuvvaṁ imaṁ sumiṇaṁ?

kā handi! imā mālā vijjā va sampayā va maha hōjjā

dinnā kēṇavi naṭṭhā puṇaravi laddhā, na yāṇāmi

ēvaṁ aṇicchiyatthō suviṇasarūvassa uṭṭhiō ahayaṁ

kāuṁ pabhāyakiccaṁ aha sahiō bhāṇuvēgēṇa

ārụ̄dhō pāsāē uvarimabhūmīē cittasālāē

maṇirayaṇakōṭṭimammī uvaviṭṭhō mattavāraṇaē

aha taṁ pabhāyadiṭṭhaṁ siṭṭhaṁ suviṇaṁ tu bhāṇuvēgassa

nicchaïuṁ nō sakkaï sōvi hu suviṇassa sabbhāvaṁ

cintittā suviṇaphalaṁ vigappasaṅkappakhittaniyacittā

jā ciṭṭhāmō amhē khaṇantaraṁ tattha ṭhāṇammi

tāva ya varanēvatthō mahagghaābharamabhūsiyasarīrō

savvō vi nayaralōō gantuṁ katthavi payaṭṭōti

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ sabālavuḍ̣dhō imō jaṇō kattha

kayaüvasōhō vaccaï sāhasu bhō bhāṇuvēgamha?

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa nisuṇasu ajjaṁ jaṁ mayaṇatērasī bhadda!

mayarandujjāṇaṭhiyassa tēṇa jattāē mayaṇassa

ēsō naranārigaṇō pūyatthaṁ tassa vaccaï pamōyā

amhēvi hu gacchāmō pēcchāmō kusumasarajattaṁ

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti dōvi sañcaliyā

kayasiṅgārā payaō pattā ya kamēṇa ujjāṇaṁ

kīlantakāmiṇīyaṇaraṇantanēuraravēṇa taruniyarō

mayaṇamahūsavatuṭṭhō gāyaï iva caccariṁ jattha

malayānilahallāviyasāhāhiṁ vighummamāṇayā dhaṇiyaṁ

kōilakayakalakōlāhalēhiṁ aphuḍakravārālāvā

āyambiranavakisilayaāyambamuhā mahīruhā jattha

āsāiyamahumāsā mattā iva saccavijjanti

suvisaṭṭakusumasōhantamañjarīpuñjaraïyasēharayā

jōhārēntativa pavaṇōṇayāhiṁ sāhāhiṁ paürajaṇaṁ

tammi ya pavarujjāṇē ghaṇataruvaramaṇḍiē suramaṇīē

daṁsaṇamēttupāiyamayaṇē mayarandanāmammi

nāṇānēvatthēṇaṁ nāyaralōēṇa parigayā jāva

pavisāmō tā diṭṭhaṁ dūrāō mayaṇadēvaharaṁ

raïjuttamayaṇapūyaṇanimittamittēṇa paüralōēṇa

paḍipunnaṁ suvilāsaṁ uttuṅgaṁ tuṅgapāgāraṁ

uddāmavajjantaaccantavaramaddalaṁ mattavarakāmiṇīsaṅghakayagundalaṁ

caccarīsaddaakkhittakāmuyajaṇaṁ paḍahiyāsaddanaccantabahuvāmaṇaṁ

piyayamāsattanararuddhakayalīharaṁ dōliyārūḍhapurabāliyāsundaraṁ

saviḍavēsājaṇāraddhajalakīḍayaṁ salilasampāyakayakaddamuppīlayaṁ

taṁ majjhē pavisittā daṭṭhūṇa raīē sañjuyaṁ mayaṇaṁ

niggantūṇaṁ dōṇṇivi uvaviṭṭhā bāravēīē

nāṇavihakīlāhiṁ kīlantaṁ purajaṇaṁ pulōēntō

jāva khaṇantaramēgaṁ kumara! ahaṁ tattha acchāmi

tāvāsannammi dumē andōlintī sahīṇa majjhagayā

diṭṭhā aüvvarūvā juvaī navajōvvaṇārambhā

pīṇunnayaghaṇasihiṇucchalantahārāvalīē kayasōhā

uttattakaṇayavannā maṇikuḍaṁlamaṇḍiyakavōlā

amayamaïyavva vihiṇā vihiyā kayalōyalōyaṇāṇandā

daṁsaṇamēttēṇaṁ ciya palhāyantī jaṇamaṇāiṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ cintiyaṁ mē kā ēsā handi! maṇaharasaruvā

kiṁ nāgakannagēsā avaïnnā, ahava vaṇalacchī?

kiṁvā suralōgāō pabbhaṭṭhā tiyasasundarī ēsā

kiṁvā mayaṇaviutta hōjja raī gahiyadēhatti?

ēvaṁ vigappamāṇō aṇamisanayaṇēhiṁ taṁ pulōēntō

tīēvi pulōiō haṁ sasiṇiddhaavaṅgadiṭṭhīē

puṭṭhō ya bhāṇuvēgō kā ēsā kassa vāvi mahilatti?

īsīsivihasiuṇaṁ aha bhaṇiyaṁ bhāṇuvēgēṇaṁ

ēīē saṅkahāē na hu kajjaṁ kiñci uṭṭhimō tāva

ēsā huṁ vaṅkavaṅkaṁ jōyaï tuha saṁmuhaṁ jēṇa

aṅgēsu nivaḍamāṇā diṭṭhī ēvaṁvihāṇa mahilāṇa

dēhaṁ kuṇaï asatthaṁ avassa hiyayaṁ avaharējjā

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ parihāsaparō si amhē ēmēva

pucchāmō kōugēṇaṁ taṁ puṇa annaṁ viappēsi

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō imammi nayarammi atthi payaḍajasō

khayarō amiyagaī tassa bhāriyā cittamālatti

ēsā ēgā dhūyā tāṇaṁ jāyā aṇōvamaguṇaḍ̣dhā

nāmēṇa kaṇagamālā vinnāṇasamanniyā kannā

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ kā ēsā mayaṇapūyaṇaṁ kuṇaï?

ēsāvi kā sahīē puraō vattaṁ kahēmāṇī?

kō va imō avalambaï galaē vēsāē taruṇaō purisō?

ēmāi maē puṭṭhō hasiūṇa taō imaṁ bhaṇaï

ēvaṁvihapucchāhiṁ kīsa tuma suyaṇu! maṁ payārēsa?

kō junnamajjariṁ kañjiēṇa paviyāriuṁ taraï?

na hu suyaṇu! paḍhamapucchaṁ ērisapucchāhiṁ chāiüṁ tarasi

kiḍaēhiṁ payattēṇavi chāijjaï kaha ṇu paccūsō?

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō lajjāē ahōmuhō ṭhiō ahayaṁ

taṁ daṭṭhu bhāṇuvēgō ṭhiō alakkhōvva hōūṇaṁ

lajjāē tassamaē vālijjantīvi annaōhuttaṁ

maḍḍāē tahavi nivaḍaï maha diṭṭhī tīē muhakamalē

aṇurāyatantibaddhā diṭṭhī jaṇasaṅkulēvi maggami

sariūṇa saṇiya-saṇiyaṁ jattha piyaṁ tattha alliyaï

sahijaṇapacchannēhiṁ puṇō puṇō taraladiṭṭhipāēhiṁ

bhaddavayamēhavijjūē vilasiyaṁ tīē vijiyanti

tō tīē taralapamhaladiṭṭhībāṇēhiṁ jajjarē hiyaē

majjha paviṭṭhā pañcavi kusumasarā mayaṇapavimukkā

ētthantarammitīē sahinivahō niyagihēsu sañcaliō

sāvi hu bālā caliyā puṇō puṇō maṁ pulōēntī

valiyaggīvaṁ tīē sasiṇiddhaavaṅgadiṭṭhidōrēṇa

āyaḍ̣dhiya pacchannaṁ maha hiyayaṁ jhatti avahariyaṁ

nāuṁvaharijjantaṁ maha hiyayaṁ tīē payavilaggāiṁ

kūyanti nēūrāiṁ puṇō puṇō kụdhiyapurisōvva

mayaṇattā sā jantī aṇamisanayaṇēhiṁ pulaïyā tāva

jāvujjāṇatarūhiṁ antariyā diṭṭhimaggāō

vōlīṇadaṁsaṇāē tīē maha māṇasammi santāvō

duvvisahō sañjāō samayaṁ aïdīhasāsēhiṁ

aha bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō gacchāmō niyagihammi amhēvi

ēvanti maē bhaṇiē samāgayā dōvi gēhammi

tattō ahamārụ̄dhō uvarimabhūmīē tattha sayaṇīē

pāsuttō uvaviṭṭhō maha pāsē bhāṇuvēgōvi

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō kīsa tumaṁ dummaṇōvva sañjāō?

muñcasi visāyagabbhē sudīharē kīsa nīsāsē?

kiṁ kuṇasi aṅgabhaṅgaṁ dīhaṁ nīsasiya mukkahuṅkārō

bhaṭhṭhaṭṭiyacaṇagō viva sayaṇīē kīsa taḍaphaḍasi?

kiṅkimpi cintiūṇaṁ aṇimittaṁ cēva kīsa taṁ hasasi?

niyayavigappavasēṇaṁ kīsa puṇō dummaṇō hōsi?

nāṇārasasaṅkinnaṁ nāḍayakavvaṁ ahiṇavēmāṇō

kiṁ ciṭṭhasi na ya sāhasi sabbhāvaṁ kiñci amhāṇaṁ?

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bahusō pucchijjantēṇa kumara! mē bhaṇiyaṁ

jāṇāmi nēva kiṁ puṇa maha dēhaṁ gāḍhamassatthaṁ?

hasiūṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ puvvaṁ ciya sāhiyaṁ maē tujjha

ēvaṁvihamahilāṇaṁ na sundaraṁ daṁsaṇaṁ hōi

tā tīē cakkhudōsā ēsō savvōvi tujjha santāvō

dāvijjaï sā hatthaṁ paṭṭhīē jēṇa hōi suhaṁ

nīsasiya maē bhaṇiyaṁ sandēhō jīviyassavi ya amhaṁ

taṁ puṇa suhiō bhāō ya parihāsaṁ kīsa nō kuṇasi?

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō sabbhāvavivajjiyassa purisassa

annāyammi sarūvē kiṁ kāuṁ sakkimō amhē?

tāhi maē vajjariyaṁ sāhijjaï tassa jō na yāṇāi

taṁ puṇa jāṇantōvi hu aliyaṁ ciya pucchisi mamanti

ēmāivayaṇavittharavajjaraṇaparāyaṇāṇa amhāṇaṁ

cūyalayā gihadāsī āgantūṇaṁ imaṁ bhaṇaï

acchaï duvāradēsē samāgayā tumha daṁsaṇanimittaṁ

sōmalayā nāmēṇaṁ varadhāī kaṇagamālāē

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō lahuṁ pavēsēha ēva bhaṇiyammi

aha sacciya sōmalayā samāgayā amha pāsammi

kayaüvayārā tāhē uvaviṭṭhā bhaṇaï sāyaraṁ vayaṇaṁ

ēgantaṁ kuṇaha taō cūyalayā pēsiyā tattō

bhaṇiyaṁ sōmalayāē saraṇāgayavacchalā jaō suyaṇā

paritāyaha paritāyaha mamaṁ taō bhīmavasaṇāō

harisāūriyahiyaēṇa tāhē ēvaṁvihaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ

kattō bhaddē! vasaṇaṁ, sā bhaṇaī kusumabāṇāō

īsīsi vihasiūṇaṁ vajjariyaṁ tāhi bhāṇuvēgēṇa

kaḍakaḍiyasavvasandhiṁ gayalāyannaṁ tuha śarīraṁ

ninnaṭṭhadantapantiṁ siyakēsahasantasīsasōhillaṁ

dūrapalambiravalivalayasahiyasihiṇēhiṁ bībhacchaṁ

daṭṭhūṇa bhīyabhīō dūraṁ dūrēṇa vaccaï aṇaṅgō

tattō kaha tujjha bhayaṁ jarāē jajjariyadēhāē?

sōmalayāē bhaṇiyaṁ mā maṁ uvahasasu suṇasu vattantaṁ

jaha kusumabāṇavihiyaṁ paramparāē maha bhayanti

ujjāṇāu kīliya samāgayā niyagihē kaṇagamālā

vicchāyavayaṇasōhā viḍappagahiyā sasikalavva

tattō ya maē puṭhṭhā kīsa tumaṁ putti! vimaṇadummaṇiyā?

na ya tīē kiñci siṭṭhaṁ sudīharaṁ navari nīsasiuṁ

aṁsujalapūriyāiṁ nayaṇāiṁ kayāiṁ dīṇavayaṇāē

tattō ya maē puṭṭhā tīē sahī haṁsiyā nāma

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ambē! ujjāṇa ajja pāviyā amhē

pūiya mayaṇaṁ bāhiṁ nīsariyā jāva tā diṭṭhō

kōugavakkhittamaṇō uvaviṭṭhō bhāṇuvēgapāsammi

paccakkhōvva aṇaṅgō ēgō taruṇō mahābhāgō

taṁ daṭṭhūṇaṁ ēsā jāyā nipphandalōyaṇā sahasā

āsattā tavvayaṇē ālēkkhagayavva niccēṭṭhā

savvaṅgiō imīē aṇimisadiṭṭhīē jōiō sa yuvā

na ya tēṇa imā diṭṭhā kōugavakkhittacittēṇa

tō tassa nayaṇagōyaramapāvamāṇā salajjamuhakamalā

dōhaggadūsiyaṁ piva attāṇaṁ mannamāṇavva

kiṅkimpi cintiūṇaṁ bhaṇaï sahīō! imammi cūyadumē

kīlāmō tāva khaṇaṁ bandhiya andōlayaṁ amhē

ēvaṁ tāhiṁ bhaṇiē tahēva sampāḍiyammi ēsāvi

gurusaddēṇa sahīō āsannāōvi vāharaï

jaï ēsō maha saddaṁ sōūṇaṁ saṁmuhaṁ palōējjā

hōjjāmi tā kayatthā ii āsāē taḍijjantī

taṁ pēkkhiūṇa ya maē parihāsavasēṇa jampiyaṁ ēyaṁ

āsannampi sahijaṇaṁ uccuccaṁ kīsa vāharasi?

kōugavakkhittamaṇō ēsō tuha dēi nēya paḍivayaṇaṁ

taṁ vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ savilakkhā kiñci sañjāyā

ētthantarammi diṭṭhā tēṇa juvāṇēṇa 'ṇaṅgarūvēṇa

sajjhasaharisēhiṁ imā tāhi aüvvaṁ rasaṁ pattā

tēṇālōiyamēttā sōhaggasamanniyaṁ ca appāṇaṁ

jīviyamavi sakayatthaṁ mannantā pulaïyasarīrā

avaruṇḍaï sahinivahaṁ uccaṁ saṁlavaï hasaï animittaṁ

pāyaṅguṭṭhēṇa mahiṁ vilihaï kēsē ya sañjamaï

ēmāiṁ saviyāraṁ cēṭṭhantā kīliūṇa khaṇamēgaṁ

mayaṇasaravihuriyaṅgī ihāgayā ērisā jāyā

ēvaṁ ca haṁsiyāē bhaṇiyammi puṇōvi sā maē puṭṭhā

kō sō purisō haṁsiṇi!, kahiyaṁ savvampi maha tīē

sōhaṇaṭhāṇē rāgō puttīē, cintiuṁ gayā pāsē

tīē diṭṭhā ya maē sayaṇīyagayā kaṇagamālā

āpaṇḍuramuhakamalā sudīhasāsēhiṁ sōsiyasarīrā

kahakahavi hu niyajīyaṁ mahayā kicchēṇa dhārantī

piyavirahajalaṇajālāvalīhiṁ santāviyāē varaīē

hārō candaṇapaṅkō mummurasarisōvva paḍihāi

cīyavva muṇālāiṁ naliṇīdalāimpi jālatullāiṁ

aṅgārarāsisarisā paḍihāsaï haṁsatūlīvi

puṭṭhā na dēi vayaṇaṁ ālavaï na sahijaṇaṁ siṇiddhampi

jhāṇōvagayā varajōgiṇivva jāyā vigayacēṭṭhā

piyavirahapisāēṇaṁ gahiya gayacēyaṇāvi hu sahīhiṁ

āsāsijjaü varaī sundara! tuha nāmamantēhiṁ

piyavirahapīḍiyaṁ taṁ tuḍigayaniyajīviyaṁ muṇēūṇaṁ

taddukkhadukkhiyā haṁ samāgayā tumha pāsammi

ēvaṁ kusumasarāō aïgaruyaṁ āgayaṁ mahaṁ vasaṇaṁ

jaṁ tīē dukkhiyāē ahampi aïdukkhiyā cēva

tā suyaṇu! kaṇagamālā jā sā nīsāsasōsiyasarīrā

āsāsijjaü varaī jāva na sāsā samappanti

lahu kuṇasu kiñcuvāyaṁ jāva na nīsaraï jīviyaṁ tīē

gayajīviyāē pacchā kiṅkāhī lāvayarasēṇa?

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ taïyā aha rāyaütta! mē bhaṇiyaṁ

ēyampi na jāṇāmō kā ēsā kaṇagamālatti

tā puccha bhāṇuvēgaṁ patthuyavatthummi gahiyaparamatthaṁ

amhē puṇa pāhuṇayā ayāṇuyā ēttha vatthumi

aha bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō amhēvi hu nēva jāṇimō kiñci

tō bhaṇaï sōmalayā sāsūyaṁ ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ

hariūṇa tīē hiyayaṁ diṭṭhibāṇēhiṁ pahariyaṁ aṅgē

tuḍigayajīyaṁ kāuṁ taṁ sampaï ayāṇuō jāō

kaṇṭhagayajīviyāsā tuha virahē maraï natthi sandēhō

ayaṇattaṁ avalambiyaṁ taṁ ciṭṭhasi niddaō bhadda!

annaṁ ca

jō jattha jaṇō nivasaï rakkhaï sō āyarēṇa taṁ gēhaṁ

tīē maṇammi vasantō kiṁ niddaya! taṁ maṇaṁ dahasi?

hariūṇa tīē hiyayaṁ sampaï cōrōvva ninhavēmāṇō

na hu chuṭṭasi suyaṇu! tumaṁ kiñci uvāyaṁ vicintēsu

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ amma! taṁ cēva sāhasu uvāyaṁ

ēvaṁ cavatthiyammi jaṁ juttaṁ amha kāuṁ jē

bhaṇiyaṁ sōmalayāē cittaṁ pattaṁ va paccayanimittaṁ

paṭṭhavasu jēṇa cittaṁ sandhīraï sā tayaṁ daṭṭhuṁ

tattō ya maē lihiyā pattē naliṇīō tīē paümammi

mōttūṇa sēsakusumē nilīyamāṇō alī lihiō

hiṭṭhē ya tassa lihiyā ēsā gāhā uvvunnayarasēṇa

niyabhāvasūyaṇaparā pacchannatthā tayā kumara!

taha kahavi pariṭṭhaviyaṁ aliṇō naliṇīē parimalaṁ hiyaē

lōyaṇuppayaṇaṁ jaha tassa kēvalaṁ saṁsakusumēsu

taṁ ca bahu pattamajjhē kāuṁ tō pēsiō satambōlō

cūyalayāē hatthē dōvi gayā tīē pāsammi

tattō khaṇantarāō cūyalayā āgayā imaṁ bhaṇaï

ēttō viṇiggayā haṁ pattā ya kamēṇa taggēhē

mattavva mucchiyā iva giliyā iva suyaṇu! gurupisāēṇa

diṭṭhā u kaṇagamālā visamamavatthantaraṁ pattā

tīē sahīhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ samāgayā cittavēgadūitti

aha sā tuha nāmakkharaāyannaṇaladdhabuddhiyā

jhatti niviṭṭhā tattō pāsiya maṁ lajjiyāva maṇayanti

tāhē samappiō sē tambōlō saharisaṁ gahiō

gahiyatthāē bhaṇiyaṁ kēṇēsō pēsiō mha tambōlō?

mē bhaṇiyaṁ taha sundari! maṇōharēṇaṁ piyayamēṇaṁ

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ kannā ahanti kaha majjha piyayamō bhaddē!?

mē bhaṇiyaṁ naṇu hōhī aha sā aphuḍakkharaṁ bhaṇaï

kaha māmi! aünnāē ēttiyamēttāṇi majjha punnāṇi

jaṁ sō bhattā hōhī daṁsaṇamittampi aïdulahaṁ

ēttiyamēttaṁ bhaṇiuṁ aṁsujalupphuṇṇalōyaṇā jhatti

nīsāsamōttūṇaṁ gayacēṭṭhā sā puṇō jāyā

tattō sahīhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sāhējjasu tassa nigghiṇamaṇassa

jahadiṭṭhaṁ hi sarūvaṁ imīē aïgaruyapēmmāē

annaṁ ca jaha kahavi tāva vōlaï rayaṇī kusalēṇa tā pabhāyammi

ujjāṇammi gayāē dāyavvaṁ daṁsaṇamimīē

taddaṁsaṇēṇa jīvaï na annahā ēsa nicchaō amha

ēvaṁ bahuhā bhaṇiyā samāgayā tumha pāsammi

ēvaṁ cūyalayāē bhaṇiyaṁ sōūṇa tīē vuttantaṁ

duguṇatarō mē jāō tavvirahē garuyayasantāvō

jaï marihī sā bālā kahavi hu guruvirahatāviyā handi!

ēēṇa nimittēṇaṁ tā majjhavi āgayaṁ maraṇaṁ

ahavā siṇēhajuttā jaï sā tā kīsa majjha paḍivayaṇaṁ

navi dinnaṁ tā mannē mandasiṇēhā u maha uvariṁ

jaïvi hu sā ninnēhā tahavi maṇaṁ majjha tīē virahammi

pajaliyajalaṇasamujjalajālāliddhaṁva paḍihāi

nayaṇēhiṁ pulaïyā sā tāiṁ ciya dahaü ēsa piyavirahō

hiyaēṇa kimavaraddhaṁ jēṇa tayaṁ niddayaṁ dahaï?

annēṇa kayaṁ annō na bhuñjaē aliyamērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ

sā diṭṭhā nayaṇēhiṁ jāō hiyayassa santāvō

rōvantu nāma taṁ jaṇamapēcchamāṇāṇi daḍḍhanayaṇāṇi

taṁ hiyaya! kiṁ vimūrasi sāhīṇē cintiyavvammi?

nayaṇēhiṁ jōiyā sā hiyaēṇa kaō ya gurayapaḍibandhō

sarisēvi hu avarāhē virahō hiyayaṁ daḍhaṁ dahaï

ētthantarammi sūrō bhamiūṇaṁ bhuvaṇamaṇḍalamasēsaṁ

atthagirimatthayatthō jāō addhāṇakhinnōvva

niṭṭhurakarēhiṁ bhuvaṇaṁ imēṇa santāviyanti rōsēṇa

najjaïva atthagiriṇā sīsāō ̣dhāliō sūrō

nāūṇa sūrapaḍaṇaṁ aṇulaggā uvari atthasēlassa

rōsēṇa rattamuhā samāgayā jhatti aha sañjhā

tayaṇantaramandhāriyadisivalayā navari āgayā rayaṇī

payaḍiyatārayanivahā kōsiyahuṅkārabhīsaṇayā

tāva ya khaṇantarāō ninnāsiyabahalatimirasaṅghāō

māṇiṇimāṇummahaṇō vitthariō sasikaranihāō

mayalañchaṇapavaṇēṇaṁ gāḍhaṁ sandhukkiō viōyaggī

santāviuṁ payattō maha hiyayaṁ tāhē sayaguṇiyaṁ

aha cintiuṁ payattō amayamaō summaī imō candō

navaraṁ tavvirahē ajja vijjupuñjōvamō jāō

hē hiyaya! kīsa ujjhasi uvvēyaṁ kīsa kuṇasi accatthaṁ?

dullahajaṇammi rāgaṁ paḍhamaṁ ciya kīsa taṁ kuṇasi?

annaṁ ca jō kira karēi nēhaṁ tassēva ya hiyaya! racciuṁ juttaṁ

dūraṭṭhiōvi jō dahaï māṇasaṁ tammi kō rāgō?

so cciya vubbhaï hiyaē so cciya aïniṭṭhurō dahaï dēhaṁ

kassa kahijjaï vattā saraṇāō bhayammi ubbhūē?

kiṁ mannē hōjja diyahaṁ jammī laggējja majjha hatthammi

maṇanivvavaṇō tīē kamalōyarakōmalō hatthō

acchaü tā dūre cciya pāṇiggahaṇāiyaṁ tu saha tīē

amhāṇa maṇōdaïyaṁ daṁsaṇamavi dullahaṁ mannē

kiṁ majjha jīviēṇaṁ kiṁvā maha handi! maṇuyajammēṇa

jō virahadukkhasamaṇaṁ tīē vayaṇaṁ na pēcchāmi?

ahavā cūyalayāē bhaṇiēṇaṁ bhavissaī pabhāyammi

tīē saha daṁsaṇayaṁ aṇukūlō jaï vihī hōhī

guruvirahajalaṇajālāvalīhiṁ santāviyassa hiyayassa

annō natthi uvāō piyadaṁsaṇaōsahaṁ mōttuṁ

ēmāivigappēhiṁ paṇaṭṭhaṇiddassa majjha sā rayaṇī

caüjāmāvi hu taïyā jāmasahassōvamā jāyā

asarisadūsahasantāvatāviyaṁ kahavi māṇasaṁ majjha

phuḍamāṇampi na phuṭṭaṁ mannē taddaṁsaṇāsāē

sīyalakaraniyarēṇavi santāvaṁ phēḍiuṁ maha asattō

aha lajjiuvva candō atthagiriṁ pāviō tattō

paccūsagayavarummūliyāē uḍḍīṇasasivihaṅgāē

rayaṇilayāē galantiva kusumāiṁ tārayanihēṇa?

aha indadisā sahasā kēsuyasuyatuṇḍasacchahā jāyā

āsannasūramaṇḍalavajjaraṇatthaṁva lōyassa

paḍibōhiyakamalavaṇō pasariyakharakiraṇapūriyadiyantō

mēliyarahaṅgajuyalō tadaṇantaramuggaō sūrō

ētthantarammi ahayampi samuṭṭhiūṇa kiccaṁ pabhāyataṇayaṁ kariuṁ payattō

bhō suppaïṭṭha! taïyā daïyāi hōhī sandaṁsaṇamha ii pahiṭṭhamaṇō pagāmaṁ

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï virahē sūruggamotti supasiddhō

surasundarināmāē kahāē taïō paricchēō 950

aha bhāō bhāṇuvēgō samāgaō pahasiō mamaṁ bhaṇaï

gammaü ujjāṇammi cūyalayāvayaṇamaṇusariuṁ

harisāūriyahiyaēṇa tāhi ēvanti japamāṇēṇaṁ

takkāluciyaṁ jāva ya kāyavvaṁ kāumāradvaṁ

ētthantarammi nisuō maṅgalatūrassa gahiranigghōsō

puṭṭhō ya maē bhāyā kattha imaṁ vajjaē tūraṁ?

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō sammaṁ jāṇē na kāraṇaṁ ēttha

navaraṁ amiyagaïgihē bhāvijjaï ēsa tūraravō

aha cintiyaṁ maē kiṁ āsannapiyāsamāgamassāvi

abbhahiō santāvō phuraï ya vāmaṁ tahā nayaṇaṁ?

tā bhaviyavvaṁ kēṇavi ēttha naṇu kāraṇēṇa tāhē maē

cūyalayā vāhariyā samāgayā aha imaṁ bhaṇiyā

kattha imō tūraravō kēṇava kajjēṇa sammamuvalabbha

āgantūṇaṁ bhaddē! sigghaṁ ciya kahasu amhāṇaṁ

gantūṇaṁ cūyalayā khaṇantarāō samāgayā dhaṇiyaṁ

vicchāyavayaṇakamalā puṭṭhā ya maē imaṁ bhaṇaï

ēttō viṇiggayāē amiyagaïgihassa dāradēsammi

bhūrijaṇasaṅkulammī maē na laddhō pavēsōvi

tattō ya bandhudattō patthuyavatthummi pucchiyā bhaṇaï

varaṇammi ēsa bhaddē! mahōcchavō kaṇagamālāē

sirigandhavāhaṇasuō gaṅgāvattammi khayaranayarammi

nahavāhaṇotti summaï tassa viinnā kaṇayamālā

ēvaṁ viyāṇiūṇaṁ samāgayā ēttha tumha pāsammi

kannakaḍuyampi tumhaṁ sāhijjaï mandābhāgāē

tīē vayaṇaṁ sōuṁ dhasatti gurumōggarēṇa pahaō haṁ

mucchānimīliyacchō paḍiō bhūmiē gayacēṭhṭhō

ghaṇasārasāragōsīsamīsasalilēṇa tāhi saṁsittō

sukumālatālaviṇṭayasīyalapavaṇēṇa gayamucchō

paricintiuṁ payattō pēcchaha duvvihiyavilāsiyaṁ vihiṇō

piyasaṅgamaṇōrahabhaṁsaṇammi ujjuttacittassa

ahavā annaha paricintijjaï saharisakaṇḍujjaēṇa hiyaēṇa

pariṇamaï annahacciya kajjārambhō vihivasēṇa

kattha imā kattha ahaṁ annōnnaṁ kattha garuyaaṇurāgō

navaraṁ hayāsavihiṇā savvaṁ ciya annahā vihiyaṁ

puvvampi hu jaï buddhī ērisayā āsi tujjha rē divva!

tā kaha maha paḍhamaṁ ciya tīē saha daṁsaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ?

kāūma daṁsaṇaṁ garūyarāyasahiyaṁ hayāsa! rē! divva!

annattha taṁ mayacchiṁ jōḍēntō ki naṁ lajjihisi?

aviya nayaṇāṇa paḍaü vajjaṁ ahavā vajjassa vaḍḍilaṁ kimpi

amuṇiyajaṇēvi diṭṭhē aṇubandhaṁ jāṇi kuvvanti

khaṇapariciyadullahalōyakāraṇē kīsa! taṁ mihasi?

muñcasu garuyavisāyaṁ vivarīō hayavihī jēṇa

ērisaduvissahēvi hu sañjāē hiyayaṁ garuyadukkhammi

vajjaghaḍiyaṁva mannē jaṁ navi sayasikkaraṁ jāsi

ēmāibahuvigappaṁ cintēmāṇassa garuyasōgassa

tavvirahadūmiyamāṇasassa taïyā mahaṁ kumara!

uvaviṭṭhā maṁ daṭṭhuṁ suṭṭhuṁ visāyāuraṁ taïyā

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē ajjavi kiṁ āsā kāvi atthi amhāṇa

tuha virahē gayacēṭṭhaṁ daṭṭhūṇaṁ tāva kaṇagamālaṁ tu

āsāsiyāvi varaī tuha saṅgamapāvamāṇā u

gāyaï hasaï ya vēvaïrōvaï ya khaṇēṇa uttasaï

suhasajjhaṁ cēva imaṁ mā putti! visāyamuvvahasu

amukūlamiṇaṁ jāyaṁ mā cintasu annahā vacchē!

niyadhūyāē paüttī savvāvi hu tassa akkhāyā

taṁ sōuṁ amiyagaī sāmamuhō takkhaṇēṇa sañjāō

bhaṇaï ahō! aïgarūyaṁ samāgayaṁ amha vasaṇanti

tō bhaṇaï cittamālā piyayama! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ nu vasaṇassa?

tattō ya amiyagaïṇā vajjariyaṁ piyayamē! suṇasu

sirigandhavāhaṇassa ō pāsammi gaō ahaṁ taïyā

sambhāsiēṇa ya taō nivēiyaṁ rāyakajjaṁ sē

ētthantarammi sundari! paḍihāranivēiō aṇunnāō

atthāṇammi paviṭṭhō ēgō vijjāharakumārō

vihiyapaṇāmō rannō pāraddhō ērisaṁ sa vajjariuṁ

vijjāharāṇa rāyā vēyaḍ̣dhē āsi jō dēva!

saṁsiddhasayalavijjō sasurāsuramaṇuyalōyavikkhāō

suravāhaṇotti nāmaṁ vijjāharacakkavaṭṭitti

dhūyāē kō bhattā hōhī maṇavallahotti ēyāē

cintāē maha hiyayaṁ bhayavaṁ! niccapi akkhaliyaṁ

ēvaṁ ca pucchiēṇaṁ kēvaliṇā suyaṇu! ērisaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

mā bhadda! kuṇa visāyaṁ thōva ciya ēttha vatthummi

guṇakaliyaṁ pālissaï vijjāharacakkavaṭṭittaṁ

hōhī sayalantēuralalāmabhūyā mahādēvī

aha rannā haṁ bhaṇiō bahumāṇajuyaṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ

jaṁ ēsā lōgaṭṭhiī tēṇamhē ērisaṁ bhaṇimō

niyayapaē ṭhaviuṇaṁ sēvāmō tāyapayajuyalaṁ

tattō maēvi bhaṇiyaṁ ētthatthē natthi kiñci vattavvaṁ

kēvaligirāvi saccā jaṁ kijjaï ērisē vihiē

tumha suyaṁ mōttūṇaṁ vēyaḍḍhagirimmi hōjja kō annō

vijjāṇa cakkavaṭṭī jassa piyā hōjja maha dhūyā?

niyanayarēsañjuttiṁ vivāhakajjassa kārēmi

ēīē aṇurāō sañjāō cittavēgammi

tā jaï maṇō 'ṇukūlaṁ sampāḍissaṁ na ēkkadhūyāē

ēīyavi, tā sundarī! kiñca maē jīviēṇanti?

uvayārēṇaṁ mahayā vimaggiyā rāiṇā suyanimittaṁ

sirigandhavāhaṇēṇaṁ maēvi dinnā imā tassa

taṁ ca iyāṇiṁ annahakāuṁ cāijjaē na jaṁ suyaṇu!

ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ mē bhaṇiyaṁ āgayaṁ vasaṇaṁ

ēvaṁ piyayamavayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ cittavēga! sañjāyā

maha sāmiṇīvi vicchāyavayaṇiyā cittamālatti

tattō tīē bhaṇiyaṁ maha cittē phuraï ērisaṁ tāva

paricayaï kaṇagamālā tavvirahē jīviyamavassaṁ

kahakahavi maē jaṁ sā tappāvaṇasuyagēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ

puvviṁ sadhīraviyā ēyaṁ puṇa annahā jāyaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ca amiyagaïṇā ēvaṁ hi ṭhiē karēmi kiṁ suyaṇu!

jaï tāva na dēmi imaṁ tō rāyā rūsaï avassaṁ

kēvalivayaṇā rannō aïgaruō ēttha āyarō jāō

tēṇa imāi adāṇē aïgaruyaṁ hōi maha khūṇaṁ

ruṭṭhēṇa tēṇa vēyaḍḍhanagavarē jaṁ na hōi āvāsō

aïthōvaṁ ciya ēyaṁ, annampi virūvayaṁ hōi

tāva varaṁ sayamēva ya samappiyānēhaviddhīē

tā tassāvi amhāṇavi pāṇāṇavi saṁsaō hōi

tā sundari! na hu kajjaṁ annēhiṁ ēttha bahuvigappēhiṁ

taha bhaṇasu kaṇagamālaṁ jaha ujjhaï tammi aṇurāyaṁ

ēvaṁ ca amiyagaïṇā bhaṇiyāē tāhi cittamālāē

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ cēva ya ittha gahiyaparamatthā

nahavāhaṇaṁ pasaṁsiya abbhahiyaguṇaṁhiṁ, nindiūṇannaṁ

taha kuṇasu jahā icchaï vīvāhaṁ ēyataṇaēṇa

sōuṁ paüttimēyaṁ mannē jīyaṁ pariccayaï

viyalantasakajjalanayaṇasalilasāmaliyagaṇḍayalā

tattō aïgurusōgaṁ ruyamāṇiṁ picchiūṇa niyadaïyaṁ

kiṁ maha thōvaṁ dukkhaṁ navaraṁ na caēmi annahākāuṁ

tadaṇunnāē ya jaō sayaṁvarāīvi kīranti

nijjiyaaṇaṅgaruvē diṭhṭhē uṇa tammi hōhihī rāgō

gantūṇa kaṇagamālaṁ suniuṇavayaṇēhiṁ bhaṇasu taṁ suyaṇu!

ēyammi vaïyarammi jaha amhaṁ hōi na hu vasaṇaṁ

ēvaṁ ca amiyagaïṇā bhaṇiyāē tāhi cittamālāē

bhaṇiyā haṁ sōmalaē! piyayamavayaṇaṁ lahuṁ kuṇasu

tattō tahatti bhaṇiu samuṭṭhiyā jāva tāhi mē puṭṭhā

candaṇanāmā cēḍī katthacchaï kaṇagamālatti?

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēsā uvarimabhūmīō uttirēūṇa

gihaüjjāṇābhimuhā gacchaï vicchāyamuhakamalā

taṁ sōūṇa vigappō uppannō maha maṇammi ērisaō

nūṇaṁ alakkhiyāē piuvayaṇaṁ tīē nisuyanti

tēṇēva imā mannē jāyā vicchāvayaṇiyā bālā

tā jāva ēttha gantuṁ virūvamāyaraï navi kiñci

tā sigdhaṁ ciya gantu nivāraṇē tīē ujjamāmitti

ēvaṁ vicintayantī aṇumaggēṇēva caliyā haṁ

pattā ya gharujjāṇē iō taō taggēvasaṇanimittaṁ

jā pariyaḍāmi ahayaṁ ghaṇataruyarasaṅkaḍillammi

ghaṇapattalakayalīharamaṇōharē tattha ēgadēsammi

pattalatamālatarutalahēṭṭhaniviṭṭhā maē diṭṭhā

tattō vicintiyaṁ mē kiṁ mannē niyagihaṁ pamōttūṇa

ēgāgiṇī hu ēsā samāgayā ēttha ujjāṇē?

tā ēīi adiṭṭhā pacchannaṭhiyā niēmi jaṁ kuṇati
