ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ tuṇhikkā kayalithambhaantariyā

khaṇamēgaṁ jā ciṭṭhāmi tattha tā suṇasu jaṁ jāyaṁ

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tu kaṇagamālāē

ajjavi kimittha bahuṇā vigappasaṅkappajālēṇa?

suciraṁ vicintiūṇavi tēṇa jaṇēṇaṁ na saṅgamō tāva

punnarahiyāē majjhaṁ hayavihiṇō vilasiyavasēṇa

acchaü saṅgamasōkkhaṁ daṁsaṇaāsāvi dullahā jāyā

jāē tassa viōgē phuṭṭantaṁ dhāriyaṁ hiyayaṁ

tā kā ajjavi āsā jēṇa tumaṁ hiyaya! phuṭṭasi na jhatti

khaṇamittadiṭṭhavallahaviōyavajjēṇa daliyampi?

na ya piuvayaṇaṁ sōuṁ icchiyajaṇavirahakārayaṁ hiyaṁ

vajjaghaḍiyaṁva mannē jaṁ navi sayasikkaraṁ jāsi

ammāē tāyassavi vallahiyā haṁ ti iya maraṭṭō jō

hiyayammi āsi majjhaṁ sōvi hu iṇhiṁ palīṇotti

suhasajjhaṁ ciya ēyaṁ kajjaṁ mā putti! kuṇa visāyanti

ēvaṁvihavayaṇēhiṁ payāriyā jēṇa ambāē

jassuvari tujjha icchā dāyavvā tassa taṁ maē putti!

iyaniyavayaṇaṁ tāēṇa sampayaṁ annahā vihiyaṁ

vinnāyamahasarūvō ō annahā jaï karēi tāōvi

maha vañchiyasampattīē sambhavō tā kahaṁ hōu?

ēvaṁ viyāṇiūṇavi hiyaya! tumaṁ kīsa muñcasi na āsaṁ

tajjaṇasaṅgamavisayaṁ jēṇajjavi jīviyaṁ dharasi?

ahavā na kōvi dōsō pahuparavasaciṭṭhiyassa tāyassa

summaï jaṇammi payaḍaṁ kaṭṭhō khalu bhiccabhāvotti

jaïvi hu vijiyāṇaṅgō ruvēṇaṁ jaïvi sampayākaliō

jaïvi hu uttamavaṁsō sakkhā sakkandaṇō jaïvi

tahavi na bhāvaï annō purisō taṁ hiyayavallahaṁ mōttuṁ

jaï ēsa nicchaō hiyaya! tujjha tā kiṁ vilambēṇa?

ēsō sō patthāvō aïdulahō pāviotti kaliūṇaṁ

ujjama vicintiyatthē hōu avigdhēṇa sampattī

ēvaṁ hi kaē tāyasya dēi dōsaṁ na kimpi rāyāvi

dūsahaviōyadukkhassa hōi ēvaṁ ca vōcchēō

ēmāibahuvigappā bhaṇiūṇaṁ cittavēga! sā bālā

kayamaraṇajjhavasāyā ārụdhā aha tamālammi

daṭṭhūṇa sāhasantīē navari dēhaṁ pakampiyaṁ majjhaṁ

na vahaï vāyā kahavi hu thakkāō savvasandhīō

tattō ya kaṇagamālā āruhiūṇaṁ tamālasāhāē

bandhiya niuttarīyaṁ bandhaï niyakandharābhōē

aha pabhaṇiuṁ payattā ammē! jaṁ kiñci bālabhāvāō

pabhiiṁ kilēsiyā taṁ taṁ khamiyavvaṁ mahaṁ saṁvvaṁ

tāya! tumampi hu maha khamasu sampayaṁ paṇayaparavasāi maē

puvviṁ kilēsiō jaṁ paralōyaṁ patthiyā ahayaṁ

jaṇaṇīsamahiyanēhē! sōmalaē! khama kilēsiyā jaṁ si

susiṇiddhasahīsandōha! khamasu jaṁ kiñci avaraddhaṁ

khaṇamittadiṭṭha! vallaha! hiyayabbhantarapaviṭṭha! nisuṇēsu

patthēmi kiñci sāmiya! pāṇaccāyaṁ karēmāṇī

tuha saṅgamarahiyāē ēsō jammō hu tāva vōlīṇō

annabhavē puṇa sāmiya! taṁ ciya maha vallahō hujjā

annaṁ bhaṇāmi sāmiya! jaïvi hu aïniṭṭhuraṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ

tahavi hu tuha āvayāvāraṇatthamēsō mha nibbandhō

nīsara maha hiyayāō ruddhē kaṇṭhammi pāsaēṇahavā

sakkēsi na nīsariu sāmiya! maha pāṇavallahaya!

mannē ca kiñci laddhaṁ hayavihiṇā maraṇakāraṇaṁ annaṁ

maha tēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ tumaē saha daṁsaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ

vaṇadēvayāō! nisuṇaha tumha pasāyāō annajammēvi

sō khaṇadiṭṭhō lōgō daïō maha hōjja, nannotti

ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ tīē mukkō appā ahōmuhō jhatti

ētthantarammi gayaṇē samuṭṭhiyā ērisā vāyā

mā mā sāhasamēyaṁ āyara bhaddē! samucchugā hōuṁ

sō cēva tujjha bhattā hōhī naṇu cittavēgotti

tatthēva laggadivasē pāṇiggahaṇaṁ bhavissaī tēṇaṁ

aha sundari! ētthatthē mā kiñcivi kuṇa visāyanti

vayaṇāṇantaramēva hi tuṭṭō sē pāsaō, taō ahayaṁ

tavvayaṇagaliyasajjhasasatthasarīrā gayā pāsē

tattō salajjavayaṇā bhaṇiyā ya maē na putti! tuha juttaṁ

ērisamāyariuṁ jaṇaṇijaṇagamāīṇaduhajaṇayaṁ

tattō ya tīi bhaṇiyaṁ ambē! amhārisāṇa kiṁ anna

ēvaṁ hi gaē kāuṁ juttaṁ maraṇaṁ pamōttūṇaṁ?

jaō vari maraṇaṁ mā virahō virahō aïdūsahō 'mha paḍihāi

vari ēkkaṁ ciya maraṇaṁ jēṇa samappanti dukkhāiṁ

tattō ya maē tīsē kahiō savvōvi puvvavuttantō

bhaṇiyā ya putti! sampaï kiṁ tuha paḍihāsaē kāuṁ?

aha tīē vajjariyaṁ lajjaṁ mōttuṁ bhaṇāmi ēyaṁ tu

navi majjha karē laggaï annō purisō ihaṁ jammē

hasiūṇa maē bhaṇiyaṁ dēvayavayaṇāu siddhamēyanti

kintu kaha tujjha jaṇaō chuṭṭissaï gandhavāhaṇaō?

ētthantarammi puṇaravi gayaṇē vāyā samuṭṭhiyā ēsā

mā! kuṇaha bahuvigappē maha vayaṇaṁ tāva nisuṇēha

gantūṇaṁ sōmalayā sāhaü jaṇayassa ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ

bhaṇiyā bahuppagāraṁ bhaṇaï taō kaṇagamālēvaṁ

jaṁ cēva kuṇaï tāō taṁ cēva majjha bahumayaṁ savvaṁ

jaï hōi sundaraṁ iha tāyassavi kīraï tayanti

tattō avigappaṁ sē varaṇāiṁ paḍicchiyavvanti

ēvaṁ hi kaē kamasō hōhī iṭṭhatthasampattī

iya dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ cittavēga! amhāṇaṁ

sañjātō gurutōsō tatō ya maē imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

maṇavañchiyavatthummī mā kīraü putti! kāvi āsaṅkā

kavaḍēṇavi tēṇa tumaṁ mannasu niyajaṇayavayaṇanti

ēvaṁ ca dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ annassa nēva kahiyavvaṁ

mā vinnāyasarūvō virūvamāyaraï sō rāya

ēyammi kaē payaḍē lōyapavāyāu nāyaparamatthō

rāyā 'vassaṁ tuha vallahassa āyaraï asuhanti

tō bhaṇaï kaṇagamālā ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō

tā ambē! patthuyatthē ujjama kiṁ ēttha bahuēṇa?

tattō ya maē gantuṁ siṭṭhaṁ ēyaṁ tu cittamālāē

bhaṇiyā bahuppagāraṁ tuha dhūyā bhaṇaï ēvaṁ tu

jaṁ kiñci bhaṇaï tāō jaṁ ciya iha bahumayaṁ tu ambāē

jaṁ cēva ya saguṇataraṁ maēvi taṁ cēva kāyavvaṁ

jaha abbhudaō tāyassa hōi, jaha hōi nāvayā kayāvi

taha cēva ya kāyavvaṁ maēvi, kiṁ ēttha annēṇa?

tattō ya cittamālā tavvayaṇaṁ kahaï niyayadaïyassa

taṁ sōuṁ amiyagaī harisiyavayaṇō imaṁ bhaṇaï

sundaramaṇuṭṭhiyaṁ handi! majjha dhūyāē jaṇayabhattāē

dakkhinnavayaṇavinnāmapagarisō daṁsiō ēvaṁ

tattō pabhāyasamaē rāyāmaccēhiṁ varaṇayaṁ tīsē

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ vihiyaṁ kayajaṇayaāṇandaṁ

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē tuha maṇanivvuihēuṁ tīē vayaṇēṇa āgayā ahayaṁ

kahaṇatthaṁ patthuyavatthuvittharassēttha tuha pāsē

tā mā sundara! varaṇayasavaṇāō dummaṇō tumaṁ hōsu

jaṁ dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ aliyaṁ na ya havaï ēyaṁ tu

ēvaṁ ca kaṇagamālābhāṇaï na nāha! taṁ pamōttūṇa

annassa karō laggaï maha hatthē ittha jammammi

dēvayavayaṇaṁ jaï saccayaṁ tā dharēmi niyapāṇā

tadabhāvē puṇa saraṇaṁ maraṇaṁ maha nicchaō ēsō

bhō suppaïṭhṭha! ēvaṁ sōmalayāvayaṇasavaṇaō taïyā

jāyaṁ maṇayaṁ maha māṇasassa satthattaṇaṁ tattō

ēvaṁ vicintiyaṁ mē kēvaliṇā jēṇa ērisaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

puvvabhavanēhabaddhā hōhī bhajjatti, tā ēyaṁ

sambhavaï nūṇa amhaṁ avarōppadaṁsaṇāō aïgaruō

aṇurāō jāō jaṁ summaï lōyappavāō ya

jāisarāiṁ mannē imāiṁ nayaṇāiṁ sayalalōyassa

viyasanti piyē diṭṭhē avvō! maülinti vēsammi

tā bhaviyavvaṁ imiṇā navaraṁ aïdugghaḍamha paḍihāi

jaṁ sā rāyasuēṇaṁ variyā kaha majja hōhitti?

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ tambōlapayāṇapuvvayaṁ bhaṇiyā

jaṁ kiñci ēttha hōhī dīsissaï taṁ sayaṁ ambē!

bhaṇiyaṁ sōmalayāē ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō

tattō vihiyapaṇāmā uṭṭhiyasaṭṭhāṇamaṇupattā

aha bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō puvviṁ diṭṭhassa tassa sumiṇassa

lēsēṇa kōvi atthō 'vadhāriō tāva taṁ suṇasu

ēsā hu kaṇagamālā mālā hōhitti, tīē jō rāgō

taggahaṇaṁ taṁ jāṇasu varaṇaṁ puṇa tīē apattī

ēttiyamēttō atthō paripphuḍō tāva jāṇiō hu maē

sēsampi hu avvattaṁ viyāṇiyaṁ kiñci taṁ suṇasu

kōvi uvāēṇa imaṁ appissaï tujjha sā puṇō kahavi

bhaṭṭhā tuha hatthāō pāvissaï āvaï garuiṁ

tattō rakkhiya kōvi hu ̣dhōissaï tujjha tēṇa pajjantō

suviṇassa sundarō iya viṇicchiō suviṇasabbhāvō

taṁ sōuṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ sammaṁ hi viṇicchiyaṁ tumē suyaṇu!

ghaḍaï jaō ēsatthō navaraṁ aïdugghaḍō lāhō

tō bhaṇaï bhāṇuvēgō vatthuṁ na taṁ atthi ēttha lōgammi

aṇukūlassa u vihiṇō jaṁ mannē dugghaḍaṁ hōi

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ païdiyahaṁ takkahāviṇōēṇa

tappāvaṇaāsāē vōlīṇā vāsarā kaïvi

āsannamāgayaṁ aha laggadiṇaṁ tāhi khayarapariyariō

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ bandhujaṇasamanniō tattha

vīvāhatthaṁ tīē nahavāhaṇakhayararāyaaṅgaruhō

sampattō aha pattā kamēṇa sā pañcamitihīvi

tattō 'varaṇhasamaē majjha vigappō maṇammi uppannō

avvō! kiṁ taṁ aliyaṁ hōhī iha dēvayāvayaṇaṁ?

ahava na dīsaï kiñcivi aṇurūvaṁ tassa tēṇa mannāmi

sōmalayāvajjariyaṁ savvamalīgaṁ hi sañjāyaṁ

ēmāibahuvigappaṁ cintēntō raṇaraṇēṇa gahiō haṁ

katthavi dhiimalahantō nīhariō tāō nayarāō

pattō ya tamujjāṇaṁ saccaviyā jattha sā maē puvviṁ

andōlaṇataruhiṭṭhē gantumahaṁ tāhi uvaviṭṭhō

aha cintiuṁ payattō iṇhiṁ kiṁ majjha kāumuciyaṁ tu

parahatthaṁ sampattā tāva piyā maha niyantassa

dēvayavayaṇāsāē nēva uvāōvi cintiō kōvi

iṇhiṁ puṇa nō sakkaṁ kimpi uvāyantaraṁ kāuṁ

ēsōvi hu aṇurāgō ēvampi gaē na tuṭṭaē kahavi

païsamayaṁ ca pavaḍḍhaï santāvō virahasañjaṇiō

aviya dullahalambhammi jaṇē jassiha purisassa hōi aṇurāgō

chillarayapāṇiēṇava aṇudiyahaṁ tēṇa susiyavvaṁ

garuyapiyasaṅgamāsābhaṁsasamucchaliyaraṇaraṇāinnaṁ

na ya jāṇē kahava imaṁ niyahiyayaṁ saṇṭhavāmitti?

tā kiṁ karēmiṁ iṇhiṁ ahavā kiṁ ēttha bahuvigappēhiṁ

guruvirahadukkhasamaṇō pāṇaccāō paraṁ juttō

jaïvi na jujjaï ēsō vivēyajuttāṇa uttamanarāṇa

tīē virahē tahavi hu sakkēmi na jīviyaṁ dhariuṁ

tā ētthēva taruvarē tīē andōlaṇēṇa supavittē

ubandhiya appāṇaṁ pāṇaccāyaṁ karēmitti

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ ārụdhō tammi taruvarē ahayaṁ

dāuṁ galaē pāsaṁ aha ēvaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattō

rē divva! annajanmē dullahalambhammi māṇasē nēhaṁ

mā maha karijja ēsā hu patthaṇā tuha maē vihiyā

annaṁ ca kēvaliṇō taṁ vayaṇaṁ, sā vāyā dēviyāvi, taṁ suviṇaṁ

āsānibandhaṇaṁ majjha divva! savvaṁ kayaṁ aliyaṁ

ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa maē mukkō appā ahōmuhō jhati

tāhē gạ̄dhībhūē pāsammi sarīrabhārēṇa

rūddhaṁ galayaṁ ākuñciyāō dhamaṇīō pasariyā viyaṇā

bhaggaṁ lōyaṇajuyalaṁ ruddhō pavaṇassa sañcārō

uvvēlliyamaṅgēhiṁ jāyaṁ udaraṁ ca pavaṇapaḍihatthaṁ

karaṇāiṁ ghāiyāiṁ jāyā aha vēyaṇā mandā

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ viyaṇāparimandaïndiēṇa maē

ētthantarammi nisuō saddō apaṇaṭṭhacittēṇa

mā sāhasa mā sāhasamēyaṁ kāurisajaṇasamāiṇṇaṁ

āyariya dēvadullahaniyaruvaṁ bhadda! nāsēsu

ētthantarammi kēṇavi lambantaṁ ukkhivittu maha dēhaṁ

lahu cchindiūṇa pāsaṁ vihiō miusīyalō pavaṇō

tattō tusārasīyalasāraminīracchaḍāhiṁ saṁsittō

ulhāsiūṇa hiyayaṁ aṅgaṁ saṁvāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

mucchānimīliyacchō savvaṁ suviṇaṁva taṁ vimannantō

kōmalakisalayaraïē sattharaē sōviō tēṇa

puṇaruttapavaṇakaraṇāiyāhiṁ nāṇāvihāhiṁ ciṭṭhāhiṁ

gayavēyaṇēṇa tattō khaṇantarā cēyaṇā laddhā

ummīliyalōyaṇajuyalaēṇa diṭhṭhō visiṭṭhasaṇṭhāṇō

navajōvvaṇō juvāṇō paccakkhaṁ pañcabāṇōvva

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa kiṁ bhadda! bāhaē, daṁsiyaṁ maē galayaṁ

aha saṁvāhaṇavihiṇā tampi hu satthaṁ kayaṁ tēṇa

vigayasayalapīḍō satthadēhō tayā haṁ, kisalayaraïyammī sattharē saṁniviṭṭhō

virahavihuriyaṅgō dīhanīsāsakhinnō ahilasiyapaya-tthā 'sāhaṇuvvinnacittō

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï pāsagaparimōyaṇotti nāmēṇa

surasundarināmāē kahāē turiō paricchēō 1000

aha sō daṭhṭhūṇa mamaṁ viddāṇamuhaṁ galantanayaṇillaṁ

karayalanimiyakavōlaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō

sundara! tuha sarisāṇaṁ uttamapurisāṇa jujjaï na kāuṁ

ahamajaṇasamāinnō appavahō kugaïsañjaṇaṇō

annaṁ ca kō si tumaṁ kassa kaō kēṇa va kajjēṇa ēyamāyariyaṁ?

kīsa sasōgō sundara! aviralathūlaṁsuai muyasi?

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ tattō ya maē tayā imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

kiṁ kahiyāē imāē vihalāē suyaṇu! vattāē?

kahiēṇa jēṇa labbhaï kōvi guṇō, tamiha sāhiuṁ juttaṁ

annaha puṇa tusakhaṇḍaṇasarisēṇaṁ kiṁ nu kahiēṇaṁ?

aviya vōlīṇapāyakajjē sāhārō kōvi natthi kahiēṇa

gayapāṇiyammi pālīi bandhaṇaṁ kaṁ guṇaṁ lahaü?

dussahadukkhasamucchēyaṇammi ujjuttamāṇasassa tumē

kīsa kayaṁ maha vigdhaṁ pāṇaccāyaṁ karēntassa?

tā mā kāhisi iṇhimpi majjha vigghanti, tāhi sō bhaṇaï

mā bhadda! kuṇasu ēvaṁ sāhasu maha kāraṇa tāva

vinnāyammi sarūvē jēṇa uvāōvi labbhaē kōvi

tattō ya maē kahiyā nīsēsā puvvavattā sē

ullambaṇaavasāṇā taṁ sōuṁ suppaïṭṭha! tēṇāhaṁ

bhaṇiō juvaīē kaē na hu juttaṁ uttamanarāṇa

ērisamāyariuṁ bhō! visēsaō tumha nīikusalāṇa

jīvantā jēṇa narā kallāṇaparaṁ paramuvinti

kiñca dhannō si tumaṁ jassatthi tāva annōnnavayaṇasañcārō

taha dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ āsāē nibandhaṇaṁ atthi

taha ēganagaravāsō avarōpparabhāvajaṇaṇasaṅgabbhō

tā kīsa kuṇasi sōyaṁ, dhannō taṁ punnavantō ya

maha puṇa punnavihūṇassa kahavi taddaṁsaṇammi jā āsā

tīēvi hu dāliddaṁ tahavi hu dhārēmi niyapāṇē

kittiyamittaṁ dukkhaṁ hontē vayaṇakkamammi tuha bhadda!?

jaṁ maha maṇadaïyāē ṭhāṇāiṁ ayāṇamāṇassa

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ sāhasu maha tāva niyayavuttantaṁ

ṭhāṇampi nēya jāṇasi kaha ṇu tumaṁ niyadaïyāē?

kammi purē tuha vāsō kēṇava kajjēṇa āgaō ēttha?

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēgamaṇō bhō! nisāmēhi

ētthēva atthi sēlē bahuvijjāharapurōhaparikaliē

suvibhattatiyacaükkaṁ nāṇāujjāṇaramaṇīyaṁ

suvisālasālakaliyaṁ sakkandaṇapuravarassa sāricchaṁ

uttarasẹ̄dhīē puraṁ pavaraṁ suranandaṇaṁ nāma

sāhīṇasayalavijjō vijjāharaniyarapaṇayapayakamalō

kamaladalatullanayaṇō nayaṇamaṇāṇandaṇō sūrō

sūrōvva nihayatēyassitēyanivahō akhaṇḍiyapayāvō

dappiṭṭhavaïrivāraṇanivāraṇē sīhapōyasamō

vijjāharāṇa rāyā supasiddhō cēva savvakhayarāṇa

pasarantavimalakittī āsī haricandanāmotti

sarasiruhasarisavayaṇā nīluppaladalavisālavaranayaṇā

kamalōyararuidēhā rayaṇavaī nāma sē mahilā

sayalōrōhapahāṇāē tīē pāṇappiyāē dēvīē

samayaṁ tivaggasāraṁ visayasuhaṁ aṇuhavantassa

dēvakumārasaricchō aha tīē dāraō samuppannō

uciyasamaē ya tēhiṁ pahañjaṇō nāma sē vihiyaṁ

dhūyā ya bandhusundarināmā asamāṇaruvalāvannā

dōnnivi tāiṁ kamasō pattāiṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ

aha annayā kayāivi avarōpparanēhagaruyabhāvāṇaṁ

ēgantammi ṭhiyāṇaṁ ullāvō tēsiṁ sañjāō

bhaṇiyaṁ pahañjaṇēṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ tuha hōi kiñcijamavaccaṁ

dhūyā vā taṇaō vā taṁ maha taṇayassa dāyavvaṁ

aviya tujjha mahaṁ vā jaṁ hōjja kimpi iha paḍhamagaṁ tu ḍimbharuyaṁ

avarōpparasambandhō tāṇaṁ amhēhiṁ kāyavvō

tā bandhusundarīē tahatti bahu manniyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ

garuyasahōyarasabbhāvanēhaakkhittacittāē

ēttō ya atthinayaraṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarāē sẹ̄dhīē

savvōuyataruvaṇasaṇḍamaṇḍiyaṁ camaracañcanti

tattha ya khayaranarīsō bhāṇugaï nāma atullasāmatthō

nijjiyaaṇaṅgaruvō kāmiṇijaṇamāṇasāṇandō

haricandakhayarapavarēṇa niyasuyā bandhusundarī tassa

dinnā varapīīē vivāhiā sāyaraṁ tēṇa

tīi sutaṇūi samayaṁ aṇuhavamāṇō u garuyapīīē

pañcapayārē visaē bhāṇugaī bhuñjaï rajjaṁ

vaccantēsu diṇēsuṁ tīē dēvīē dāriyā jāyā

ujjōiyadisivalayā u cittalēhatti nāmēṇa

tayaṇantaraṁ ca dēvī sundarasuviṇēhiṁ sūiya taṇayaṁ

sūyā suhatihirikkhē cittagaï nāma sē vihiyaṁ

haricandōvi hu rāyā cāraṇasamaṇassa sumuhanāmassa

payamūlē sōūṇaṁ jiṇadhammaṁ siddhisuhahēuṁ

niyayapaē ṭhaviūṇaṁ pahañjaṇaṁ niyasuyaṁ viṇikkhantō

saṁsāravāsabhīō nivvinnō kāmabhōgāṇa

sāmannaṁ kāūṇaṁ payamūlē cāraṇassa sumuhassa

niṭṭhaviyakammajālō, antagaḍō kēvalī jāō

jō pahañjaṇōvi hu vijjāharanaravaī payāvillō

bhuñjaï jaṇayaviiṇṇaṁ rajjaṁ gayasayalaāsaṅkō

tassaya sayalantēurapavarāō dunni aggamahisīō

kalahaṁsī mañjūsā uttamavaṁsappasūyāō

kalahaṁsīē jāō puttō jalaṇappahotti nāmēṇa

mañjūsāē lahuō puttō kaṇagappahō nāmō

niyayasahōyaravayaṇaṁ sumarantī bandhusundarī dēvī

nāūṇa cittalēhaṁ niyadhūyaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ pattaṁ

aha taṁ bhāuyavayaṇaṁ sāhaï daïyassa bhāṇugaïṇō sā

tattō ya bhāṇugaïṇā niyadhūyā cittalēhā sā

dinnā khayarapahañjaṇasuyassa jēṭṭhassa rūvajutassa

jalaṇapahassa, tēṇavi pariṇīyā paramapīīē

suranandaṇammi nayarē nīyā aha tīē nēhasahiyāē

saha visaē bhuñjantō ciṭṭhaï dēvōvva diyalōē

aha annayā kayāivi khayarāhivaī pahañjaṇō daṭṭhuṁ

gayaṇē sasaṅkadhavalaṁ dēvaülagōrayaṁ gēhaṁ

aha cintiuṁ payattō maṇōharō handi! ēsa āgārō

ēyāgiīē tā haṁ kārēmi jiṇālayaṁ rammaṁ

maṇikuṭṭimammi tattō ālihiuṁ ujjaō jayā rāyā

tāva ya jhatti vilīṇō pavaṇahaō jalaharō savvō

daṭhṭhūṇaṁ taṁ vilīṇaṁ khaṇēṇa rāyā vicintaē ēvaṁ

ēvaṁvihā narāṇaṁ lacchīō cavalarūvāō

jaha ēsō abbhalavō khaṇēṇa diṭṭhō puṇō paṇaṭṭhotti

taha savvēvi payatthā khaṇamittāṇandasañjaṇaṇā

rūvaṁ ca jīviyaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ ca savvēvi bandhusambandhā

ēvamaṇiccā avvō! dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa

paccakkhaṁ hi aṇiccaṁ nāūṇavi jaṁ thiraṁva mannanti

visayā ' 'sattā sattā, ēyaṁ avivēyasāmatthaṁ

nāūṇavi jiṇavayaṇaṁ ārambhapariggahēsu vaṭṭanti

kāmāsattā jaṁ puṇa ahō! mahāmōhamāhappaṁ

tā 'laṁ mama rajjēṇaṁ saṁsāranivāsahēubhūēṇa

jāṇiyajiṇindavayaṇassa handi! gurudukkhamūlēṇa

tā sāvajjaṁ vajjiya pavvajjāujjamaṁ karēmi lahuṁ

kiṁ maha imiṇā duggaïnibandhaṇāsārarajjēṇa?

annaṁ ca majjha vaṁsē rajjaṁ dāūṇa niyayaputtāṇa

bahavē kayasāmannā rāyāṇō pāviyā sugaïṁ

tavvaṁsapasūēṇa maēvi kāyavvayaṁ imaṁ tamhā

iya cintiūṇa rāyā saṁsaï saṁnihiyakhayarāṇaṁ

ētthantarē sughōsō caünāṇī cāraṇō muṇī tattha

virahantō sampattō bhaviyāṇa vibōhaṇaṭṭhāē

rāyā pahañjaṇō aha suyassa jalaṇappahassa aha rajjaṁ

dāūṇa tahā kaṇagappahassa pannattivaravijjaṁ

tattō ya viṇikkhantō sughōsasāhussa pāyamūlammi

avahāya rāyalacchiṁ pahañjaṇō khayararāyatti

jalaṇappahōvi bhuñjaï rāyasiriṁ khayaraniyaraparikinnō

sayalōrōhapahāṇāi cittalēhāi samayanti

kaṇagappahōvi sāhiya vijjaṁ pannattināmiyaṁ vihiṇā

vijjāpabhāvasañjāyagaruyasāmatthavitthārō

ujjhiya niyavaṁsakamaṁ aṇavikkhiya ayasapaḍahayaṁ lōē

bahumanniya avivēyaṁ aviyāriya dōggaïgamaṇaṁ

aṇavēkkhiya gurubhāvaṁ aṅgīkāūṇa taha adakkhinnaṁ

rāyasirilōluēṇaṁ vijjābaladappabhariēṇa

jalaṇappahassa jiṭṭhassa bhāuṇō piuvidinnarajjapayaṁ

uddāliyaṁ tu kaṇagappahēṇa vijjāpabhāvāō

tattō ahiṭṭhiyaṁ taṁ rajjaṁ savvampi uggatēēṇa

sāmāiṇā savvō vasīkaō khayaraniurambō

nīsāriō sabhūmīō tāhi jalaṇappahō kaṇiṭṭhēṇa

nayarammi camaracañcē samāgaō sasurapāsammi

bahumāṇapuvvayaṁ sō pavēsiō niyapurammi sasurēṇa

bhāṇugaïrāiṇā aha samayaṁ ciya cittalēhāē

aha paramapamōēṇaṁ tahiṁ vasantassa suranayarammi

bhō cittavēga! tassa u vōlīṇā vāsarā kaïvi

aha annayā kayāivi jalaṇapahō sālaēṇa sañjuttō

cittagaïnāmaēṇaṁ nīhariō tāō nayarāō

pēcchantō bahuvihaüvavaṇāṁi ramaṇīyatarusaṇāhāiṁ

bhāraṇḍacakkamaṇḍiyapasannajaladīhiyānivahaṁ

pasariyasiyabhāsāiṁ pēcchantō girivarassa siharāiṁ

kinnaramihuṇasusaṅgakayalīharavihiyasōhammi

aïkalakūiyakalayaṇṭhilaṭṭhakōlāhalābhiramaṇīē

paribhamirabhamaraniurambagaruyajhaṅkāramahurammi

ēgammi vaṇaniguñjē phalabharaviṇamantadumasayāinnē

pattō sakōugēṇaṁ samayaṁ ciya cittagaïṇā u

vāyantamaüyamāruyahallantasupallavōhasōhillaṁ

pēcchaï rattāsōyaṁ mahuyarigaṇavihiyahalabōlaṁ

tassa ya ahē niviṭṭhō kañcaṇapaümammi muṇivarō diṭṭhō

vijjāharanarakinnarasuravisarēṇaṁ namijjantō

uppannavimalakēvalanāṇō aha suravarēhiṁ thuvvantō

āsannē uṇa jalaṇappahēṇa sō paccabhinnāō

sō ēsō majjha piyā pahañjaṇō nāma muṇivarō ēvaṁ

siṭṭhammi cittagaïṇō tattō tē dōvi harisēṇa

ti païkkhiṇiuṁ sammaṁ harisavasuṭṭhantabahalarōmañcā

paṇamiyakēvalicalaṇā viṇiviṭṭhā dharaṇivaṭṭhammi

nijjiyasanīrajīmūyaghōsagambhīrabhāraīē taō

tīi parisāi bhayavaṁ pāraddhō dēsaṇaṁ kāuṁ

aviya gayakalahakannacavalā lacchī maṇuyāṇamāumaṇiccaṁ

jōvvaṇamavi maṇuyāṇaṁ sahasatti jarā abhiddavaï

rōgasayapīḍiyaṁ tampi jōvvaṇaṁ jāi jīvalōgammi

iṭṭhaviyōgā 'ṇiṭṭhappaōgadukkhēhiṁ kēsiñci

aïparimiyammi cavalē rōgajarāsōgavāhipaürammi

jīvāṇa jōvvaṇē ērisammi kō nāma paḍibandhō?

visayā kugaïnimittaṁ uvabhuttā tucchagā tahā tēvi

virasā saï avasāṇē tēsu taō kō va paḍibandhō?

iya saṁsārē sāraṁ jaṁ kira paḍihāsaē vivajjāsā

tampi hu duhasayahēutti jāṇiuṁ kuṇaha jiṇadhammaṁ

jaṁ dulahā sāmaggī ēsā tubbhēhiṁ bhavasamuddammi

pattā apattapuvvā tā mā taṁ nipphalaṁ nēha

ēsā hu puṇō dulahā jāīlakkhōhasaṅkulabhavammi

hiṇḍantāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ na ya annaṁ jiṇamayaṁ mōttuṁ

tamhā jiṇēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ dikkhaṁ ghēttūṇa sañjamaṁ kāuṁ

ujjhiya tō saṁsāra pāvaha siddhīē pavarasuhaṁ

ēvaṁ muṇiṇā dhammammi sāhiē kēvi tattha pavvaïyā

jāyā uvāsayā taha annē sammaṁ pavannatti

ētthantarammi paṇamiya jalaṇapahō vinnavēi niyapiyaraṁ

bhayavaṁ! puṇaravi rajjaṁ kiṁ taṁ maha hōjja nō ahavā?

aha kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ hōhī, taṁ kaïya, pucchiyamaṇēṇa

tō bhaṇaï muṇivarindō kēvalavinnāyaparamatthō

bhāṇugaïdinnarōhiṇivijjāē sāhiyāē tē bhadda!

hōhī puṇaravi khayarāhivattaṇaṁ natthi sandēhō

ēvaṁ muṇiṇā bhaṇiē pahasiyavayaṇēhiṁ vandiō bhayavaṁ

ētthantarammi parisā jahāgayaṁ paḍigayā savvā

tattō tē dōvi jaṇā samāgayā jhatti niyayanayarammi

cittagaïṇā ya kahiyaṁ kēvalivayaṇaṁ tu niyapiuṇō

tattō ya bhāṇugaïṇā sōhaṇarikkhammi rōhiṇī vijjā

jāmāuyataṇayāṇaṁ dōṇhavi samayaṁ vidinnati

bhaṇiyā ya puvvasēvaṁ karajāvavihāṇaō kuṇaha sammaṁ

vasimammi ṭhiyā samayaṁ chammāsaṁ jāva tō pacchā

uttarasēvā uggā kāyavvā ēgagēhiṁ aḍavīē

bīēṇa puṇō uttarasāhagarūvēṇa hōyavvaṁ

annaṁ ca bhīsaṇāsuvi vibhīsiyāsuṁ maṇaṁ na dāyavvaṁ

punnē sattamamāsē dēssaï aha daṁsaṇaṁ vijjā

ēvaṁ rannā bhaṇiyā dōnnivi paṇamittu tassa payakamalaṁ

pāraddhā taṁ kāuṁ chammāsā jāva punnatti

aha sattammi māsē gantuṁ aḍavīē tavvihī savvō

jalaṇappahēṇa puvviṁ pāraddhō jāvahōmāī

vasunandayakhaggakarō cittagaī tassa rakkhaō jāō

sōvi hu aṇannacittō pāraddhō taṁ vihiṁ kāuṁ

annadivasammi turiyaṁ āgacchantī pakampamāṇataṇū

diṭṭhā u cittalēhā bhayabhīyā tammi ṭhāṇammi

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ niyabhagiṇiṁ cittagaī bhaṇaï kattha taṁ bhaddē!

āyā subhīsaṇāē ēkkallā ēttha aḍavīē?

kassa va bhaēṇa gāḍhaṁ kampasi taṁ bhagiṇi! tāhi sā bhaṇaï

nayarāu niggayā haṁ pariyariyā dāsacēḍīhiṁ

pattā ujjāṇammī tattha maē pūiō kusumabāṇō

niyagihamāgacchantī vimōhiyā jhatti kēṇāvi

mōttūṇaṁ pariyaṇaṁ taṁ palāyamāṇī samāgayā ēttha

aḍavīē tāva maē diṭṭhō kaṇagappahō sahasā

pāvēṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ iccha mamaṁ tāhi gāḍhakuddhāē

akkōsiō sa bahuhā niṭṭhuravayaṇēhiṁ mē tāhē

uggīriūṇa khaggaṁ bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa icchasu mamanti

aha navi, tō tē sīsaṁ chindāmi imēṇa khaggēṇa

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiyā palāyamāṇī bhaēṇa kampantī

pattā tumha samīvē rakkha mamaṁ tāō pāvāō

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇiṁ taṁ sahasā āgamma giṇhiuṁ hatthē

uppaïō kaṇagapahō tamāladalasāmalaṁ gayaṇaṁ

hā! rakkha rakkha bhāuya! hā vallaha! kuṇasu maha parittattiṁ

ēmāi vilavamāṇiṁ hīrantiṁ daṭṭhu niyabhagiṇiṁ

niyakulakalaṅkakāraya! kattha mamaṁ jīsi diṭṭhipahapaḍiō?

purisō bhava ēsa tuhaṁ sīsacchēyaṁ karēmitti

ēmāi vāharantō cittagaī gahiyanisiyakaravālō

aṇumaggēṇuppaïō bhagiṇiē vimōyaṇaṭṭhāē

aha taṁ vimōhayantō kaṇagapahō āgaō niyanayarē

cittagaīvi khayarō aṇumaggaṁ tassa sampattō

tattō vimōhaṇīē vijjāē mōhiūṇa cinttagaïṁ

suranandaṇē paviṭṭhō kaṇagapahō niyayanayarammi

aha sō mōhiyacittō cittagaī tattha vāhirujjāṇē

vīsariyabhagiṇiharaṇō avayariō kōuhallēṇa

daṭṭhuṁ jaṇasandōhaṁ usabhajiṇindassa pavarabhavaṇammi

jattāsamaē miliyaṁ vicittanēvatthasacchāyaṁ

pavisiya jiṇindabhavaṇaṁ vandiya bhattīi paḍhamajiṇanāhaṁ

uvaviṭṭhō cittagaī vijjāharaniyaramajjhammi

pattō khaṇantarāō jalaṇappahapēsiō narō ēgō

pucchantō cittagaïṁ damaghōsō nāma jiṇabhavaṇē

daṭṭhūṇa ya cittagaïṁ paṇamiya nēūṇa tāhi ēgantē

damaghōsō bhaṇaï taō bhagiṇīē vimōyaṇaṭṭhāē

uppaïō tāva tumaṁ, jalaṇapahō picchiumpi taṁ savvaṁ

akkhuhiyamaṇō sammaṁ navi caliō niyayakiriyāō

niccalacittaṁ daṭṭhuṁ jalaṇapahaṁ mantajāvavāvāraṁ

aha sā rōhiṇivijjā paccakkhā jhatti sañjāyā

bhaṇiyaṁ tīē puttaya! aṇannasarisaṁ hi suṭṭhu dhīrattaṁ

tā siddhā tujjha ahaṁ bhaṇasu ya jaṁ majjha kāyavvaṁ?

bhaṇiyaṁ jalappahēṇaṁ avahariyā majjha bhāriyā jā sā

kaṇagappahēṇaṁ, taṁ tāva sigghamāṇēha maha pāsaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ vijjāi taō suṇasu imaṁ tāva vaïyaraṁ putta!

kēvalivayaṇāīō savvōvi hu vaïyarō tassa

pannattīē kahiō tattō sō āgaō tuha samīvē

khōhaṇahēuṁ savvaṁ māyāē kayaṁ imaṁ tēṇa

tuha mahilā niyagēhē acchaï niruvaddavā suhēṇaṁ tu

cittagaī puṇa tēṇaṁ vimōhiō mōhaṇipabhāvā

suranandaṇammi nayarē jiṇindabhavaṇammi acchaï niviṭṭhō

tā mā kāhisi kiñcivi ētthatthē putta! uvvēvaṁ

ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ vijjā adaṁsaṇaṁ jhatti uvagayā tāhē

ahayaṁ jalaṇapahēṇaṁ paṭṭhaviō tumha pāsammi

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō damaghōsēṇaṁ amūḍhacittō sō

cittagaī sañjāō caliō saha tēṇa niyaṭhāṇaṁ

ētthantarammi nhavaṇē vittappāyammi jiṇavarindassa

pavisaï nayarē lōgō nāṇāvihavāhaṇārụ̄dhō

aviya kōvi hu sibiyārụ̄dhō ārụ̄dhō rahavarēsu cittēsu

hayagayaassatarēsuṁ ḍōliyajugēsu vivihēsu

ētthantarammi hatthī kaṇagappahasantiō mahākāō

mayamattō ummiṭṭhō nīhariō tāō nayarāō

bhañjantō gihadārē uḍ̣dhōsēntō varaṇḍaē bahusō

mārintō jaṇaniyaraṁ acchōlintō rahē vivihē

aha taṁ kayantasarisaṁ uḍ̣dhīkayagurukaraṁ sughōramuhaṁ

daṭṭhuṁ naṭṭhō lōō disō disiṁ maraṇabhayabhīō

sōvi hu pavahaṇanivahaṁ bhañjantō dantapāyaghāēhiṁ

ucchōlintō suṇḍāi hiṇḍaē savvaō tattha

kōūhalēṇa gayaṇē pariṭṭhiō pulōiüṁ payattō sō

cittagaī mattakariṁ kayantavayaṇaṁva duppicchaṁ

ētthantarammi ēgammi rahavarē paḍhamajōvvaṇārambhā

juvaī aṇannarūvā bahuvihavarabhūsaṇāinnā

ummaggapayaṭṭēhiṁ jaccaturaṅgēhiṁ hatthitaṭṭhēhiṁ

bhaggammi rahē bhūmīi nivaḍiyā vigayajīyavva

navanīluppalasacchahavisālalōlantalōyaṇā varaī

sambhaggakannakuṇḍalaviluliyavarakuntalakalāvā

vicchinnakaṇayakhiṅkhiṇiniyarapalambantamēhalādāmā

īsīsihārapacchannathaṇaharā galiyasirakusumā

vihaḍiyaaṅgayajuyalā nivaḍiyakaḍayā paṇaṭṭhagēvijjā

tuṭṭaguṇahāraviyaliyamuttāhalasōhiyasarīrā

sambhagganēurajuyā musumūriyarayaṇamāliyāniyarā

bhūmitalaluliyadēhā aha diṭṭhā tēṇa sā kariṇā

tattō ujjhiyahatthō tīi vahaṭṭhāi karivarō caliō

taṁ daṭṭhu pariyarēṇa garuō hāhāravō vihiō

susiliṭṭhaaṅguvaṅgaṁ aha taṁ paḍipunnacandasamavayaṇaṁ

karagijjhamajjhabhāgaṁ viyaḍaniyambatthaliṁ juvaïṁ

daṭṭhumpi samāsannaṁ nāgaṁ, gantuṁ acāyamāṇiṁ tu

maraṇabhayāō gāḍhaṁ vēvantasarīrayaṁ khuddhaṁ

tāyāramapikkhantiṁ sataralatāraṁ disō niyacchantiṁ

daṭṭhūṇaṁ citagaī gayaṇatthō cintaē ēvaṁ

hā! hā! kāmanihāṇaṁ mahilārayaṇaṁ viṇassaï laggaṁ

ōyariūṇaṁ gayaṇāu tāhi aṅkammi sā gahiā

ghittūṇa sayaṁ sahasā ṭhāṇē niruvaddavammi nēūṇa

sīyalataruchāyāē nivēsiyā kuṭṭimucchaṅgē

tattō ya uttarīyamiupavaṇā ' 'sāsiyāē sō tīē

lajjāsajjhasamaüliyanayaṇēhiṁ pulōiō tattō

ciyapariciyaṁva daṭṭhuṁ taṁ taruṇaṁ garuyanēhasabbhāvā

amaēṇava saṁsittā jāyā aha viyasiyakavōlā

cittagaīvi ya tīē daṭhṭhūṇa aṇōvamaṁ tayaṁ rūvaṁ

tavvayaṇanisiyanipphandalōyaṇō ciṭṭhaī jāva

tāva ya tīē dhāī kaïvayajuvaīhiṁ parigayā jhatti

āgantuṁ uvaviṭṭhā bhaṇaï tayaṁ mahuravāṇīē

parakajjakaraṇanirayā havanti kira sajjaṇatti saccaviyaṁ

kannagamēyaṁ mōyantaēṇa tumaē gaïndāō

tā nikkāraṇavacchala! tujjha pabhāvāō jīviyā ēsā

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ abhinandiya sā puṇō bhaṇaï

gacchāmi amha gēhaṁ ussūraṁ vaṭṭaē jaō iṇhiṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ca cittagaïṇā ēvaṁ kuṇahatti tattō ya

niyanayarābhimuhāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ caliyāṇa tīē kannāē

cittagaïkarayalaō muddārayaṇaṁ lahuṁ gahiyaṁ

niyayakarasaṇṭhiyaṁ puṇa samappiyaṁ tassa tāṇa pacchannaṁ

aha sā sajjhasavēviradēhā gantuṁ payaṭṭatti

valiyaggīvaṁ tīē aïguruaṇurāyapisuṇadiṭṭīē

nijjhāiō tahāsō jaha jāō kusumasaravisaō

aha sā sahiyaṇasahiyā kamēṇa niyapuravaraṁ paviṭṭhatti

cittagaīvi ya tīē jōvvaṇarūvēhiṁ hayahiyaō

cittalihiuvva jāō khaṇantaraṁ vigayaannavāvārō

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ damaghōsō saviṇayamēvaṁ samullavaï

attha girisiharamaṇusaraï diṇayarō ēsa viyaliyapayāvō

tā gammaü niyaṭhāṇē kumāra! kimiṇā vilambēṇa?

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ kāuṁ āgārasaṁvaraṁ bhaṇaï

ēvaṁ karēmu navaraṁ kāraṇamēyaṁ vilambassa

maha hatthāō paḍiyaṁ muddārayaṇaṁ tu ēttha katthavi ya

taṁ gavisiuṁ pabhāē jhaḍatti ahamāgamissāmi

taṁ puṇa gacchasu sigdhaṁ kahējja jalaṇappahassa vuttantaṁ

īsi hasiūṇa taō damaghōsō ēvamullavaï 166

paccakkhammivi diṭṭhē kumāra! kiṁ ēttha vaṅkabhaṇiēēhiṁ?

kiṁ navi diṭṭhā kannā tuha hatthā taṁ pagiṇhantī

tā kavaḍaṁ mōttūṇaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ cēva sāhiuṁ juttaṁ

kannāē mūlasuddhiṁ uvalabhiuṁ āgamissāmi

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiō cittagaī vihasiūṇa vajjaraï

sammaṁ viyāṇiyaṁ tē maṇōgayaṁ majjha damaghōsa!

aha sō kayappaṇāmō uppaïō pāviō niyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

cittagaīvi paviṭṭhō jugāijiṇamandirē rammē

vandiyajiṇindabimbō jiṇaüggahavajjiyammi ēgantē

gantūṇaṁ uvaviṭṭhō samāgayā tāva rayaṇīvi

aha cintiuṁ payattō kiṁ mannē tīi majjha hatthāō

gahiuṁ muddārayaṇaṁ kiṁvā maha ̣dhōiyaṁ niyayaṁ?

kaṇa ṇu maē nāyavvaṁ tīē kulaṁ kahava sā varēyavvā

jaï sā havijja mahilā havijja tō jīviyaṁ sahalaṁ

tārisarūvajuyāē samayaṁ iha visayasēvaṇaṁ juttaṁ

tadabhāvē visayāsā viḍambaṇā majjha pajihāi

sō ya kayatthō purisō laggijjā jassa karayalē bālā

rambhāgabbhasukōmalabāhulayā haṁsagaïgamaṇā

dhannō hamittiēṇaṁ gahiyā aṅkammi sā maē sutaṇū

avagūhiyā ya gāḍhaṁ jaṁ na maē vañciō taṁ tu

puṇaravi havijja jattā hatthibhaē bhūminivaḍiyā taha sā

ghittūṇa jēṇa sahasā avayāsējjā tayaṁ gāḍhaṁ

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ vicitayantassa taggayamaṇassa

niddāē samaṁ rāī khayaṁ gayā, uggaō sūrō

aha sō pahāyasamaē vihiṇā vandittu jiṇavaraṁ paḍhamaṁ

caliō kannā kulaharaviyāṇaṇatthaṁ purābhimuhō

pattō ya puraṁ picchaï jaṇarahiyaṁ sunnasayaladhavalaharaṁ

puralacchivippamukkaṁ uvvasiyaṁ aḍavipaḍiruvaṁ

aha picchiūṇa taṁ sō vimhiyahiyaō maṇēṇa cintēi

kattō hanta! akaṇḍē puramēyaṁ uvvasaṁ jāyaṁ?

kiṁ hōjja indayālaṁ ahavā saccaṁ hi uvvasaṁ ēyaṁ

kiṁ kuviēṇa surēṇaṁ avahariyamimāō ṭhāṇāō

ahavā bhayāō kassavi naṭṭhō lōgō imāō nayarāō

ēvaṁ vicintayantō cittagaī pavisaī jāva

tāvaya samuhamintō ēgō purisō pulōiō tēṇa

uvayārapuvvayaṁ sō mahuragirāē imaṁ bhaṇiō

bhaddamuha! kiṁnimittaṁ uvvasiyaṁ puravaraṁ imaṁ sahasā

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sāhijjantaṁ nisāmēhi

tāva supasiddhamēyaṁ vijjāpannattigavviō sūrō

pālaï puravaramēyaṁ kaṇagapahō khayararāyatti

jalaṇappahassa jēṭṭhassa bhāuṇō piuvidinnarajjapayaṁ

uddāliūṇa jēṇiha ahiṭṭhiyaṁ appaṇā cēva

nīsāriō ya bhāyā jiṭṭhō sasurassa sō gaō nayarē

ēsōvi imammi purē acchaï rajjaṁ aṇuhavantō

sasurēṇa bhāṇugaïṇā kila vijjā rōhiṇī u sē dinnā

sō sāhiuṁ payattō siṭṭhaṁ ca imassa vijjāē

tattō tavvigghaṭṭhā rāyā kaṇagappahō gaō tattha

na ya khōbhiō sa tēṇaṁ maṇēṇa bhīō taō ēsō

niyanayarābhimuhēṇaṁ āgacchantēṇa annacittēṇa

kahavi hu pamāyavasaō jiṇabhavaṇaṁ laṅghiyamaṇēṇa

puvvaṁ dharaṇindēṇaṁ ēsō samaō kaō nahayarāṇa

jiṇabhavaṇasāhupaḍimāṇaṁ laṅghaṇaṁ ēttha jō kāhī

tassa khayarāhamassa ō vijjācchēō bhavissaī sahasā

ēvaṁ vēyaḍḍhanagē aïvidiyaṁ sayalakhayarāṇa

tattō imassa rannō jinabhavaṇaṁ laṅghiyanti ruṭṭhēṇa

dharaṇēṇa takkhaṇicciya vijjācchēō kaō bhadda!

jalaṇappahassa vijjā siddhatti viyāṇiūṇa kaṇagapahō

vijjārahiō ihayaṁ ṭhāumasattōti aha naṭṭhō

gaṅgāvattammi gaō bhayabhīō dakkhiṇāē sẹ̄dhīē

sirigandhavāhaṇassa ō saraṇaṁ saha nāivaggēṇaṁ

nāūṇa vaïyaramiṇaṁ khuhiō savvōvi nāyarō lōgō

pahurahiō bhayabhīō avarōpparamēvamullavaï

amhāṇa pahū naṭṭhō na ya sakkaï vāsiuṁ puraṁ ēyaṁ

tēṇa viṇā tā amhaṁ na juttamiha acchiuṁ iṇhiṁ

kō kuṇaï amha rakkhaṁ ēttha vasantāṇa nāharahiyāṇa

savvēsiṁ tēṇa uciyaṁ puramēyaṁ ujjhiuṁ sigghaṁ

ēvaṁ viṇicchiyammī nayaramahantēhiṁ mantakusalēhiṁ

savvōvi jaṇō naṭṭhō jāyaṁ aha sunnayaṁ nayaraṁ

āsajja kāraṇamiṇaṁ uvvasiyaṁ tēṇa puravaraṁ ēyaṁ

cittagaī bhaṇaï taō kattha gaō sō jaṇa bhadda!?

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kōvi jaṇō gayaṇavallahē nayarē

kōvi gaō vijayapurē kōvi hu iha vējayantammi

sattuñjayammi kōvi hu ariñjaē kōvi taha gaō lōō

annō nandaṇanayarē avarō vimalammi nayarammi

rahanēurammi kōvi hu āṇandapurammi arijaē kōvi

sagaḍāmuhammi kōvi hu purīē taha vējayantīē

kōvi hu rayaṇapurammi sirinayarē rayaṇasañcayaṁ kōvi

nayarammi jalāvattē kōvi gaō saṅkhanābhammi

avarāvaranayarēsuṁ paḍivakkhasamāsaēṇa puralōō

savvōvi hu vikkhiriō sattuyapuñjōvva vāyahaō

ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa narō vihiyapaṇāmō sa gantumāraddhō

cittagaīvi ya tāhē sōccā tavvayaṇaṁ sahasā

pahaüvva mōggarēṇaṁ giliō iva rakkhasēṇa khuhiēṇa

vajjēṇa tāḍiō iva dukkhaṁ aïdūsahaṁ pattō

aha cintiuṁ payattō daṭṭhavvā kattha sā maē bālā

maha hiyayakayāṇandā ēvaṁ vihiyammi hayavihiṇā?

itthavi nayarē tīē kulakōḍisamāulammi viulammi

daṁsaṇamavi aïdulahaṁ aviyāṇiyakulaharāē u

iṇhiṁ puṇa nāṇāvihanayarēsuṁ pavasiyammi lōyammi

daïyāē paüttīyavi viyāṇaṇē sambhavō natthi

tā kiṁ karēmi iṇhiṁ hayavihiṇā vihaḍiyammi ēyammi

labbhijja kaha paüttī kahavā maha daṁsaṇaṁ hōjjā?

kō pucchijjaü nāmaṁ kō maha sāhijja kulaharaṁ tīē?

jattha gayā mama daïyā akkhijjā puravaraṁ kō taṁ?

kahava tuḍijōgaō sā diṭṭhā amhēhiṁ hayavihiniōgā

iṇhiṁ puṇa daṭṭhavvā kō jāṇaï katthava navatti?

tīē nāmakkharāiṁ virahapisāyassa mantabhūyāiṁ

suigōyaraṁ gayāiṁ na majjha hā! kattha vaccāmi?

hā! hiyaya! kāsa jhūrasi nibbandhaṁ muñca tammi lōyammi

ajjavi kā tuha āsā ṭhāṇampi ayāṇamāṇassa

aviya jaï ḍajjhasi tā ḍajjhasu kuṭṭasi hē hiyaya! na hu nivārēmi

daïyāē jaṁ paüttīvi dullahā sampayaṁ jāyā

ahavā kiṁ imiṇā cintiēṇa aïgaruyavisāyagabbhēṇa

avalambiya dhīrattaṁ kiñci uvāyaṁ vicintēmi

jēṇa uvāyapayaṭṭā purisā pāvinti icchiyaṁ atthaṁ

summaï lōyammi jaō labbhaï suviṇaṁ suyantēhiṁ

ēsō ya iha uvāō bhamāmi savvēsu khayaranayarēsu

mā kahaya kōvi katthavi tīē paüttimpi sāhijjā

dāsijja ahava sakkhā paribbhamantēhi kammivi purammi

candamuhī sā bālā, tahā ya aïsundaraṁ cēva

ēvaṁ viṇicchiyatthō sō haṁ bhō cittavēga! cittagaī

daïyāviōyagurudukkhavajjaniddaliyamaṇasēlō

paricattabandhuvaggō aha guruaṇurāyaparavasō tattō

ēgāgī vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarasẹ̄dhīē nayarēsu

savvēsuvi paribhamiō na ya laddhā tīē katthavi paüttī

tattō ya dakkhiṇāē sēṇīē āgaō ahayaṁ

tatthavi purēsu kēsuvi āhiṇḍiya icchiyaṁ apāvintō

ajja puṇō iha pattō tuha nayaraṁ kuñjarāvattē

ēyammi ya ujjāṇē maha pavissantassa sōhaṇō saüṇō

sañjāō taha phuriyā dāhiṇabāhū tahā nayaṇaṁ

tattō viyappiyaṁ mē avassamajjēva hōhiī tīē

daïyāē daṁsaṇaṁ, ahava kiñci aïsōhaṇaṁ annaṁ

ēvaṁ vicintayantō pattō haṁ ēttha kayaligēhammi

kāūṇa pāyasōyaṁ uvaviṭṭhō kuṭṭimucchaṅgē

tāva ya khaṇantarāō samāgayā suyaṇu! majjha niddatti

sōūṇa tujjha saddaṁ jhatti pabuddhō ahaṁ tattō

kēṇa imaṁ ullaviyanti cintiuṁ jā disāō pulaēmi

tāva ya tumaṁ hi diṭṭhō palambamāṇō tarulayāē

hā! hā! aṇaṅgarūvō kaha ṇu juvāṇō viṇassaē laggō?

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ hāhāsaddaṁ karēmāṇō

pattō tujjha samīvē chinnō aha pāsaō maē sahasā

bhō cittavēga! sēsaṁ paccakkhaṁ cēva tuha savvaṁ

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ kaha ṇu tumaṁ bhadda! niyayadaïyāē

ṭhāṇampi nēya jāṇasi taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

tō dulahaṁ maṇuyattaṁ daṭṭhūṇaṁ rūvajōvvaṇasamēyaṁ

mahilāmittassa kaē na hu maraṇaṁ hōi kāyavvaṁ

bhō cittavēga! jaïvi hu piyavirahē dūsahaṁ havaï dukkhaṁ

uttamakulappasūyāṇa tahavi ēyaṁ na juttanti

jāṇāmi ahampi imaṁ maṇavallahamāṇusassa virahammi

naraē nēraïyassava uppajjaï dāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ

tahavi hu na hōi juttō appavahō kintu kōvi hu uvāō

cintēyavvō jaha sā pāvijjaï hiyayavallahiyā

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ vajjariē tēṇa cittagaïṇā ō

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ ēvaṁ hi maē samullaviyaṁ

vōlīṇā tīi kahā na hu iṇhiṁ atthi kōvi uvāō

ajjēva ya rayaṇīē jaṁ hōhī tīi vivāhō

cittagaī bhaṇaï taō ēkkōvi ya tīē pāvaṇōvāō

maha phuraï māṇasammī jaï tuha paḍihāsaē suyaṇu!

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē kō sō tattō sō bhaṇaï bhadda! nisuṇēsu

kila ēsō kulāyārō dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīē khayarāṇa

kannāvivāhasamaē ēkallā pūyaē kusumabāṇaṁ

niyakulakamāgayaṁ aha pariṇijjaï sā taō pacchā

taṁ kamamaṇupālintī sā ēhī mayaṇapūyaṇanimittaṁ

amhē puṇa dōvi jaṇā puvvaṁ ciya ittha pavisāmō

aha tīē āgayāē nēvatthaṁ tīē santayaṁ ahayaṁ

ghittūṇa itthirūvō gacchissaṁ varayapāsammi

ghitūṇa kaṇagamālaṁ taṁ puṇa nāsijja takkhaṇā cēva

ahayampi uvāēṇaṁ nāsissaṁ laddhapatthāvō

ēvaṁ hi kaē tīē sampattī atthi, nannahā bhadda!

taha dēvayāē vayaṇaṁ hōjjā ēvaṁ ca saccanti

kiñca purisēṇa purisayārō kāyavvō tāva icchiyatthammi

vihiṇō niōgaō puṇa havaï hu kajjassa nipphattī

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa kahiē uciē uvāē āgāmiyaṁ garuyadukkhamacintiūṇa

bhō suppaïṭṭha! vayaṇaṁ paḍivannayaṁ sē tivvāṇurāgaparimōhiyamāṇasēṇa

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi kaṇagamālāpāvaṇaüvaēsasūyagō bhaṇiō

surasundarīkahāē pañcamaō varaṁ paricchēō 1250

itthantarammi sūrō bhamiūṇaṁ gayaṇamaṇḍalamasēsaṁ

avarasamuddaṁ pattō pahakhinnō majjaṁṇatthavaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ca cittagaïṇā annāyā ēva ēttha pavisāmō

mayaṇassa gihē sampaï patthuaatthassa hēummi

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ hōutti uṭṭhiyā dōvi

ucciṇiya kaïvayāiṁ pupphāiṁ tattha ujjāṇē

pavisiya mayaṇassa gihē pūiya mayaṇaṁ ca ēvamullaviyaṁ

bhayavaṁ! tuha ppasāyā sampajjaō icchiyaṁ amha

ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa taō dōvi nilukkā aṇaṅgapaṭṭhīē

rayaṇīē jāmamittē bōlīṇē, kiñciahiyammi

bahupariyaṇapariyariyā gijjantā pavaramaṅgalasaēhiṁ

vajjantēṇa ya vivihaṁ nāṇāvihatūranivahēṇa

niyasahiyaṇēṇa sahiyā ārụ̄dhā uttimāē sibiyāē

kayamaṅgalōvayārā siyabhūsaṇabhūsiyasarīrā

siyavasaṇapāuyaṅgī ābaddhasugandhakusumaāmēlā

pattā ō kaṇagamālā dārē aha kāmagēhassa

uttinnā siviyāō pūyaṇaüvagaraṇayaṁ gahēūṇa

dhariūṇa dāradēsē sayalaṁ niyapariyaṇaṁ tāhē

ēgāgiṇī paviṭṭhā mayaraddhayabimbapūyaṇanimittaṁ

pavisittu bhavaṇadāraṁ aggaliyaṁ tāē bālāē

sampūiūṇa kāmaṁ aha sā nivaḍēvi tassa calaṇēsu

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ galantathūlaṁsunayaṇillā

lahusaddēṇaṁ ēyaṁ sōvālambhaṁ sagaggaraṁ bhaṇaï

nijjiyasuramaṇuōvi hu paharasi itthīṇa kiṁ bhayavaṁ!?

jaï majjha tammi lōē bhayavaṁ! garuō kaō hu aṇurāō

tā kīsa taṁ pamōttuṁ ghaḍasi mamaṁ annalōēṇaṁ?

annaṁ ca summanti ittha lōē pañcēva silīmuhā ō kila tujjha

navaraṁ mamaṁ paḍuccā sahassabāṇōvva taṁ jāō

jaï jāva majjha paharasi paharasu kō taṁ nivārēi bhayavaṁ!

navaraṁ taha maha paharasu kayantabhavaṇē jaha vayāmi

tumaē puṇa taha pahayā jaha na mayā nēya jīviyā ahayaṁ

tā kiṁ bhaṇāmi iṇhiṁ saraṇammi samāgayā tujjha?

daḍḍhassa huyavahēṇaṁ sō cēva jahōsahaṁ tu lōyassa

tumaē pīḍiyadēhā taha saraṇaṁ tujjha allīṇā

jaï majjha tumaṁ tuṭṭhō dēhi varaṁ patthiō maē ēyaṁ

mā maha havijja ērisaviḍambaṇā annajammēvi

tāva imō maha jammō piyajaṇaāsāē vōliō ahalō

taṁ ciya daïyaṁ dijjasu bhayavaṁ! maha annajammēvi

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇaṁ tāhi kaṇagamālāē

vialantathūlaaṁsuyapavāhasaṁsittasihiṇāē

nāṇāviharayaṇaviṇimmiyammi pasarantavimalakiraṇammi

gabbhaharadāranihiē rammē aha tōraṇē tīē

baddhō niuttarīēṇa pāsaō tāhi sā puṇō bhaṇaï

ēsā marāmi sampaï kusumāuha! tujjha puraō haṁ

mā maha bhaṇijja kōvi hu vihiyamajuttanti kaṇagamālāē

ēttiyamittaṁ kālaṁ vimāliyaṁ jēṇa āsāē

iṇhiṁ puṇa na hu sakkā kāuṁ bhaṅgaṁ tu niyapaïnnāē

taṁ mōttuṁ hiyayadaïyaṁ na laggaē maha karē annō

annaṁ ca dēvayāō! aliyaṁ jampanti nēya kaïyāvi

tampi hu annaha jāyaṁ majjha aünnēhiṁ pāvāē

ahava kavaḍēṇa kēṇavi pisāyarūvēṇa vañciyā taïyā

nahavāhaṇabhattēṇaṁ ahavā khayarēṇa kēṇāvi

tā sampayaṁmi mā hōjja majjha abhivañchiyatthavāghāō

bhayavaṁ! tuha ppasāyā sijjhaü maraṇaṁ avigghēṇa

piyavirahagaruyamōggarajajjariyamaṇāē majjha pāvāē

maraṇaṁ hōjja na hōjja va ajjavi āsaṅkaē hiyayaṁ?

piyavirahadukkhasamaṇaṁ labbhaï maraṇampi garuyapunnēhiṁ

taṁ jaï havijja iṇhiṁ sukayatthā hōjja tā ahayaṁ

ēvaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tīē mukkō appā ahōmuhō jhatti

turiyaṁ gantūṇa maē chinnō aha pāsaō tīē

gahiūṇa tayaṁ aṅkē tāhē saṇiyaṁ maē imaṁ bhaṇiyā

nijjiyasurāsurindō tuṭṭhō tuha suyaṇu! raïnāhō

asarisasāhasaāvajjiēṇa mayaraddhaēṇa tuha suyaṇu!

ēyammi cēva jammē uvaṇīō sō jaṇō ēsō

kijjaü kaṇṭhaggahaṇaṁ gāḍhaṁ ukkaṇṭhiō jaṇō tujjha

ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā bālā lajjāē ahōmuhī jāyā

cittagaīvi ya tāhē samāgaō tammi cēva ṭhāṇammi

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ varamittō ēsa maha suyaṇu!

tujjha viōē sundari! appavahē ujjaō ahamimēṇa

viṇivāriō akāraṇavacchallajuēṇa dhīrēṇa

tuha pāvaṇē uvāō ēsō maha sāhiō imēṇēva

ēēṇa sahāēṇaṁ sijjhissaï icchiyaṁ amha

kannāsahāvasulahaṁ ujjhittā sajjhasaṁ suyaṇu! tamhā

niyanēvatthaṁ savvaṁ jhatti samuppēsu ēyassa

kāūṇa tujjha rūvaṁ jēṇa imō suyaṇu! vaccaē bāhiṁ

pariyaṇavimōhaṇaṭṭhā parakajjasamujjaō dhīrō

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiyā saharisahiyayā karēi taṁ savvaṁ

aha dōvi nilukkāiṁ puṇaravi mayaṇassa paṭṭhīē

cittagaīvi ya tīē nīsēsaṁ nivisiūṇa nēvatthaṁ

ugdhāḍiuṁ duvāraṁ ārụ̄dhō jhatti siviyāē

aha tammi gaï lōē nīsaddaṁ jāṇiūṇa taṁ bhavaṇaṁ

bhaṇiyā ya maē ēsā sundari! kiṁ iṇhi kāyavvaṁ?

ōṇayaṁmuhīē tīē sajjhasavasakampamāṇagattāē

kahakahavi hu ullaviō khalantaavvattavāṇīē

guruvirahapīḍiyāē piyayama! taṁ pāviō tuḍivasēṇa

kuṇasu sayaṁ jaṁ juttaṁ saraṇammi samāgayā tujjha

ēvaṁ tīē bhaṇiē gandhavvavihīē sā maē bālā

pariṇīyā taṁ mayaṇaṁ dēvaṁ kāūṇa sakkhiṇayaṁ

avaṇittu kamēṇa taō sajjhasamēīi vivihavayaṇēhiṁ

khaṇamēgaṁ ramiūṇaṁ suttō āliṅgiūṇa tayaṁ

niddāvigamē ya maē vajjariyaṁ suyaṇu! vaccimō iṇhiṁ

ērisamāyariūṇaṁ na hu juttaṁ acchiuṁ ēttha

dīhaṁ nīsasiēṇaṁ aha bhaṇiyaṁ tīī hiyayadaïyāē

hā ajjaütta! juttaṁ kamapattaṁ āsi maha maraṇaṁ

majjha nimittē pāvisi sāmiya! jaṁ garuyaāvaïṁ iṇhiṁ

nahavāhaṇō payaṇḍō vijjābaladappiō tahaya

nāsantāṇavi amhaṁ na nāha! saraṇaṁ tu vijjaē kiñci

tā tuha vaïriṇirūvā jāyā paramatthaō ahayaṁ

tuhavirahatāviyāē na āsi maha sāmi! tārisaṁ dukkhaṁ

jaṁ tuha nāha! vivattiṁ sambhāviya iṇhi sañjāyaṁ

laddhōvi nāha! kahavi hu majjha aünnāē hōsi na hu iṇhiṁ

punnarahiyāṇa ahavā pattampi hu vihaḍaē sahasā

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ avalambiūṇa maha kaṇṭhē

gurudukkhanibbharāē runnaṁ aha tīē bālāē

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ sundari! kiṁ sōyamasarisaṁ vahasi?

laddhaṁ jaṁ lahiavvaṁ iṇhiṁ jaṁ hōu taṁ hōu

tuha saṅgamarahiyāṇaṁ maraṇaṁ jaï hōjja, hōjja tā dukkhaṁ

iṇhiṁ puṇamha sundari! maraṇēvi hu natthi dukkhanti

kiñca ēsō acintiōvi hu jaha jāō saṅgamō saha tumāē

taha cēva mā kayāvi hu annampi hu sōhaṇaṁ hōjjā

kīraü tāva uvāō ahalō jaï hōi hōu, kō dōsō?

mañcayavaḍiyāṇa puṇō tahaṭṭhiyā cēva bhūmitti

nahavāhaṇakhayaraṁ taṁ daṭṭūṇa maē imaṁ kayaṁ suyaṇu!

bhaviyavvayāē diṭṭhaṁ hōjjā jaṁ kiñcimaha uciyaṁ

abbhuvagayaṁ hi maraṇaṁ nāsijjaü tahavi tāō khayarāō

jalacavvaṇujjayāṇaṁ mā kahavi hu ēi gulaōvi

tā suyaṇu! muñca sōyaṁ vaccāmō rayaṇasañcaē tāva

kālōciyaṁ ca pacchā diṭṭhaṁ diṭṭhaṁ karissāmō

tattō ya tīē samayaṁ nīhariō paṇamiūṇa raïnāhaṁ

aha tīē kaṇṭhalaggō uppaïō gayaṇamaggammi

rāgandhayāramōhiyanarāṇa daṭṭhuṁva tārisaṁ cariyaṁ

dūraṁ nāsiyatimirō aha sahasā uggaō sūrō

tattō ya tīē bhaṇiyaṁ sāmiya! gāḍhaṁ pivāsiyā ahayaṁ

sūsaï galayaṁ ajjavi kēdūrē amha taṁ nayaraṁ?

dūrē ajjavi nayaraṁ sundari! ittha vaṇanikuñjammi

ōyarimō jaṁ hōhī ittha jalaṁ ēva mē bhaṇiē

tattō dōvi jaṇāiṁ avaïnnāiṁ vaṇammi rammammi

sīyalajalapaḍipunnaṁ aha diṭṭhaṁ tattha nijjharaṇaṁ

pāūṇa jalaṁ aha sā pattalataruchāhiyāē uvaviṭṭhā

kāuṁ sarīracintaṁ ahamavi tatthēva āyāō

bhō suppaïṭṭha! ēvaṁ khaṇantaraṁ vīsamāmi jā tattha

tāva ya nisuō saddō āsannē kēligēhammi

jāyā satthasarīrā sundari! vaccāmu iṇhiṁ niyaṭhāṇaṁ

ēyaṁ saddaṁ sōuṁ ēsa vigappō mahuppannō

nūṇaṁ cittagaïssa ya ēsō saddō na hōi annassa

ēyammi vaṇaniguñjē ahavā kō sambhavō tassa?

ēvaṁ viñcintiyammī kayalīgēhāō tāō guvilāō

taruṇamahilāsamēō cittagaī jhatti nīhariō

tattō gantūṇa maē saharisamāliṅgiō sanēhēṇaṁ

ahamavi tēṇaṁ, tattō uvaviṭṭhā dōvi tatthēva

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyō nīhariēṇaṁ tu mayaṇagēhāō

kiṁ mitta! tumē vihiyaṁ vimōhiō pariyaṇō kahavā?

kahava tumaṁ nicchuṭṭō kā vā ēsā maṇōharāgārā

mahilā, kattha va pattā, sāhasu maha savvamēyanti?

cittagaī bhaṇaï taō nisuṇasu bhō cittavēga! ēgamaṇō

kāūṇa kaṇagamālārūvamahaṁ tāva nīhariō

ārụ̄dhō sibiyāē pattō ya kamēṇa varasamīvammi

vijjāharigaṇagijjantavivihavaramaṅgaluppīlō

laggē samāgayammī gahiō maha karayalō saharisēṇa

nahavāhaṇēṇa, tattō kamēṇa vattō ya vīvāhō

nahavāhaṇassa puraō naṭṭaṁ vivihaṅgahārasōhillaṁ

pāraddhaṁ vāravilāsiṇīhiṁ varagēyasaṁvaliyaṁ

ētthantarammi ēgā juvaī āgamma karayalaṁ niyayaṁ

muddārayaṇasamēyaṁ daṁsaï maha sajjhasupphuṇṇā

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ cintiyaṁ mē ēsā sā majjha santiyā muddā

hatthibhayamōiyāē jā gahiyā tīē kannāē

aïguruyaṁ aṅguṭṭhiṁ maṇayaṁ ōsāriuṁ maē tattō

avalōiyā ya ēsā sahasā aha paccabhinnāyā

ēsā sā maha daïyā hatthibhaē jā vimōiyā taïyā

vihiṇō niōgaō kaha jāyā haggāvaṇāpacchaṁ

pēccha aïdugghaḍampi hu sahasā kaha majjha daṁsaṇaṁ jāyaṁ?

aṇukūlō ahava vihī kiṁvā taṁ jaṁ navi karēi?

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ nidaṁsiō niyakarō maē tīē

puvvaṁ samappiyāē tīē muddāē sañjuttō

kannē hōu tīē āsannasahīya sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

avaniddaēṇa dukkhaï sīsaṁ kira kaṇagamālāē

tā ēsā khaṇamēgaṁ asōgavaṇiyāi suvaï laggatti

tumhē ēttha ṭhiyāō jahāsuhaṁ cēva acchāha

vattē puṇa pēkkhaṇaē jāṇāvijjāu amha sigghanti

ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ tīē uṭṭhaviō cittavēga! ahaṁ

tattō tīē samayaṁ pavaragharujjāṇatilayabhūyāē

viyasantasurahimañjarimayarandāmōyasuhayāē

pattō ramaṇīyāē asōgavaṇiyāē saharisaṁ tīē

dinnammī āsaṇammī uvaviṭṭhō, sāvi maha puraō

aha sā sajjhasabhariyā jāhē na caēi kiñci vajjariuṁ

tāhē niyayapaüttī savvāvi hu cittavēga! maē

puvvaṁ jā tuha kahiyā tīēvi hu sā maē samāsēṇa

kahiyā ya jāva itthaṁ itthīrūvēṇa āyāō

sundari! tujjha viōgē gurudukkhaṁ māṇasaṁ maē pattaṁ

bhamiō tujjha nimittē savvēsuvi khayaranayarēsu

tā lajjaṁ mōttūṇaṁ sāhasu kiṁ tujjha nāmadhēyanti

kammi kulē tuha jammō kiṁvā nāmaṁ tu tē piuṇō?

kahavi purē iha pattā pabhūyalōyassa majjhayārammī

itthīrūvōvi ahaṁ vinnāō suyaṇu! kaha tumaē?

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiyā kahavi hu ujjhittu sajjhasaṁ bālā

maṇayaṁ khalantavayaṇā aha ēvaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattā

āyannasu maṇavallaha! kahēmi savvampi jaṁ tumē puṭṭhaṁ

tumha supasiddhamēva hi nayaraṁ suranandaṇaṁ tāva

tatthāsi suvikkhāō pahañjaṇō nāma khayararāyatti

tassa ya pavarō mantī aïkusalō nīisatthēsu

pahuṇō ya daḍhaṁ bhattō buddhīē caüvvihāē sampannō

rannō vissāsapayaṁ āsi purā mēhanāutti

tassa ya ghariṇī pavarā païvvayā rūvasaṁvayākaliyā

uttamakulappasūyā indumaī nāma āsitti

tīē saha visayasōkkhaṁ nisēvamāṇassa mēhanāyassa

jāō suō surūvō nāmēṇaṁ asaṇivēgotti

abbhasiyakalāniyarō sāhiyavijjō guṇāṇa āvāsō

jaṇayāṇa kayāṇandō kamasō sō jōvvaṇaṁ pattō

ēttō ya dakkhiṇāē imīē sẹ̄dhīē kuñjarāvattē

ēyammi cēva nayarē candagaī āsi varakhayarō

tassa ya maṇavallahiyā mahilā nāmēṇa mayaṇarēhatti

kālēṇa tāṇa puttō amiyagaī nāma sañjāō

dhūyā campayagōrā campayamālatti tadaṇusañjāyā

pattā ya jōvvaṇaṁ sā vijjāharakumaramaṇaharaṇaṁ

aha sā campagamālā variyā suranandaṇammi nayarammi

mantisuyaasaṇivēgassa, sāyaraṁ tēṇa pariṇīyā

nīyā niyaē nayarē saha tīē sō visālanayaṇāē

parapīīē jutō bhuñjaï māṇussaē bhōgē

aha annayā kayāivi mantipayaṁ dēvi asaṇivēgassa

niyataṇayassa tattō virattacittō mahāsattō

rannā pahañjaṇēṇaṁ sahiō sañjāyagaruyasaṁvēgō

suguruṇa pāyamūlē pavvaïō mēhanāō sō

khayarō vi asaṇivēgō campagamālāē hiyayadaïyāē

samayaṁ gihavāsaphalaṁ aṇuhavaī visayasōkkhanti

aha campagamālāē kamēṇa puttā ō pañca uppannā

tāṇaṁ piyayama! nisuṇasu kamēṇa ēyāiṁ nāmāiṁ

vajjagaī vāugaī candō taha candaṇō susīhō ya

pañcaṇhaṁ puttāṇaṁ uvariṁ dhūyā ahaṁ jāyā

jammadiṇē maha piuṇā suyajammamahūsavāō avmahiō

kārāviō saharisaṁ mahōcchavō garuyanēhēṇa

vattē ya bārasāhē nāmaṁ tu piyaṅgumañjarī majjha

vihiyaṁ kamēṇa ahayaṁ dēhōvacaēṇa vaḍḍhantā

jaṇayāṇa kayāṇandā lālijjantā ya dhāipaṇagēṇa

pattā kumāribhāvaṁ kayapariyaṇalōyaṇāṇandā

juvaījaṇajōggāō naṭṭāīyā kalāō sayalāō

gahiyāō kamēṇa taō pattā haṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ

susiṇiddhasahīsahiyā ramāmi vivihāsu tattha kīlāsu

varacittapattachijjayanaccaṇagandhavvavīṇāsu

tattha ya piyayama! ahayaṁ sahāvaō purisavēsiṇī jāyā

varayā ya majjha bahavē inti tahiṁ khayarapavarāṇa

vararūvakalāriddhīō tēsiṁ, jaṇaōvi majjha sāhēi

na ya katthavi maha īcchā jāyaï tō tē nivārēi

jō jō āvaï varaō taṁ taṁ nēcchāmi jāvaya ahaṁ tu

tāhē ya asaṇivēgō majjha piyā sōyamāvannō

jaṭṭhūṇaṁ taṁ sasōgaṁ campagamālā u bhaṇaï niyadaïyaṁ

kīsasasōgō sāmiya! dīsasi cintāurō dhaṇiyaṁ?

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ maha dhūyā tāva jōvvaṇaṁ pattā

na ya icchaï kimpi varaṁ sundari! garuī imā cintā

dhūyā jōvvaṇapattā vararahiyā kulaharammi vasamāṇā

taṁ kimpi kuṇaï kajjaṁ lahaï kulaṁ maïlaṇaṁ jēṇa

kō hōjja varō dhūyāē handi! maṇaïcchiutti cintāē

sudaṁri! na ēi niddā rayaṇīēvi maha pasuttassa

ēyaṁ nisamma vayaṇaṁ campagamālāvi tāhi mē jaṇaṇī

majjha nimittē sundara! jāyā sōgāurā dhaṇiyaṁ

annadiṇammi piyasahī pabhāyasamayammi dhāriṇīnāmā

sujjāpahassa dhūyā samāgayā majjha pāsammi

bhaṇaï ya kimajja piyasahi! hiyavva vikkiyavva vunnavva

dīsasi annamaṇā viva viddāṇamuhā sasōgillā

ciraāgayāvi piyasahi! kīsa na sambhāsiyā ahaṁ tumaē?

tā bhaṇasu sōgakāraṇamēyaṁ jaṁ tujjha sañjāyaṁ?

ēvaṁ ca piyasahīē bhaṇiyāē maē tayā samullaviyaṁ

sammamuvalakkhiyaṁ tē dhāriṇi! nisuṇēsu vuttanttaṁ

tujjhēhiṁ samaṁ piyasahi! kīlittā tā viyālasamayammi

nāṇāvihakīlāhiṁ samāgayā niyayagēhammi

uvarimabhūmīi taō nāṇāmaṇirayaṇahēmamaïyammi

pallaṅkē pāsuttā pavarāē haṁsatūlīē

aha aḍḍharattasamaē dunduhisaddaṁ suṇittu paḍibuddhā

picchāmi gayaṇamaggaṁ divvavimāṇēhiṁ saṅkinnaṁ

daṭṭhūṇa dēvanivahaṁ ujjōiyagayaṇamaṇḍalaṁ tattha

surasundarigaṇasahiyaṁ cinttā mē ērisā jāyā

katthērisāiṁ mannē divvavimāṇāiṁ diṭṭhapuvvāiṁ

ēvaṁvihā ya dēvā dēvīō kattha diṭṭhāō

ēvaṁ viñcintayantī piyasahi! mucchāvasaṁ ahaṁ pattā

mucchāviramē tattō jāīsaraṇaṁ samuppannaṁ

sambhariyā puvvabhavā dōnni maē maṇuyadēvasambaddhā

jaha taṁ nisuṇasu dhāriṇi! savvampi hu vajjarijjantaṁ

jambuddīvē dīvē suragiriṇō uttarammi pāsammi

ēravayaṁ varakhittaṁ ihatthi tēlōkkavikkhāyaṁ

tammi ya majjhimakhaṇḍē āriyakhittammi āsi varanayaraṁ

amarapurasarisarūvaṁ paḍivakkhanarindaduggammaṁ

tihuaṇalacchīnilayaṁ ibbhasahassōvasēviyaṁ viulaṁ

ākālasuppaïṭṭhaṁ nāmēṇavi suppaïṭṭhanti

uvahasiyadhaṇayavihavō uvayāraraō ya sayalalōyassa

dēvagurupūyaṇaraō vacchallayarō ya bandhūṇaṁ

dakkhinnadayākaliō aggāṇī sayalavaṇiyasatthassa

haridattō nāmēṇaṁ ibmō parivasaï aha tattha

nijjiyaraïsōhaggā sīlavaī mahurabhāsiṇī dakkhā

pāṇapiyā viṇayavaī viṇayavaī bhāriyā tassa

pañcapayārē visaē tīē samaṁ tasya aṇuhavantassa

jāō pahāṇaputtō vasudattō nāma suprasiddhō

tatō viṇayavaīē kamēṇa dhūyāō tinni jāyāō

nijjiyasurindasundarirūvāisaēṇa kaliyāō

jēṭṭhā sulōyaṇatti ya bīyā kannā aṇaṅgavaīnāmā

vasuvaïnāmā taïyā tilōyaacchērayabbhūyā

kamasō vaḍḍhantīō taruṇajaṇummāyakārayaṁ rammaṁ

aha tāō pattāō tinnivi navajōvvaṇārambhaṁ

kannā sulōyaṇā sā pariṇīyā mēhalāvaïpurīē

sāgaradattasuēṇaṁ subandhunāmēṇa vaṇiēṇa

vijayavaīnayarīē suēṇa dhaṇabhūisatthavāhassa

dhaṇavāhaṇanāmēṇaṁ vivāhiyā 'ṇaṅgavaïkannā

sāvi hu vasumaïkannā nayarīē mēhalāvaīē ō

dhaṇavaïṇā pariṇīyā taṇaēṇa samuddadattassa

aha sō dhaṇavaïvaṇiō kalāsu kusalō aṇaṅgapaḍirūvō

samayaṁ tu vasumaīē bhuñjaï māṇussaē bhōē

vaḍḍhantasiṇēhāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ annōnnarattacitāṇaṁ

navajōvvaṇāṇa sarasaṁ visayasuhaṁ sēvamāṇāṇaṁ

gurujaṇaviṇayarayāṇaṁ avarōpparavirahadukkharahiyāṇaṁ

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ āṇandiyabandhuvaggāṇaṁ

aha annayā kayāivi pavarē hammiyatalammi pāsuttō

dhaṇavaïvaṇiō tīē vasumaïdaïyāē sañjuttō

nimmalasasikaraüjjōiyāē rayaṇīē pacchimē jāmē

niddākhaē vibuddhā muddhā sā vasumaī varaī

niyasayaṇīyapasuttaṁ parapurisaṁ pikkhiūṇa bhayabhīyā

sā pavaṇahayā taṇutarulayavva aha kampiyā sahasā

cintaï sā miyanayaṇā kattha gaō majjha niyayanāhō sō

dukkhapavēsammi gihē ēsō purisō kaha paviṭṭhō?

kiṁvā sō maṇadaïō havijja nihaō imēṇa pāvēṇa

sōcciya daïō annō paḍihāsaï kiṁ vivajjāsā?

ahavā na hōi ēsō maha daïō tāva nicchaō ēsa

ēsa aüvvō kōvi hu dīsaï divvāṇukāritti

taha suvaï suvīsatthō pavisittā paragihammi jaṁ ēsō

taṁ nūṇaṁ bhaviyavvaṁ kēṇāvi hu kāraṇēṇittha

jaï ēsa annapurisō daïō vā tahavi iṇhi maha juttaṁ

niyasāsuyāē sigghaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ cēva sāhēuṁ

jaï puṇa ēyaṁ na kahēmi kahavi niyasāsuyāē vuttantaṁ

ājammampi kalakaṁ sudūsahaṁ hōi tā majjha

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ uttariyā hammiyāō sā bālā

pattā ya sāsuyāē sudaṁsaṇāē samīvammi

sā saṇiyaṁ uṭṭhaviyā bhaṇaï kimāgamaṇakāraṇaṁ suṇhē!

tattō ya vasumaīē jahaṭṭhiyaṁ sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ sudaṁsaṇāē na sambhavō atthi ittha annassa

niddāvasaō hōjjā tuha jāō vibbhamō ēsō

bhaṇiyaṁ ca vasumaīē amba! sayaṁ cēva tā nirūvēsu

ēvaṁ tīē bhaṇiyā sudaṁsaṇā lahuṁ gayā tattha

sammaṁ nirūviō sō niddāē pasuttaō tahiṁ purisō

nāyaṁ sudaṁsaṇāē jaha ēsa na hōi maha puttō

tattō sudaṁsaṇāē pōkkariyaṁ dīharēṇa saddēṇa

dhāvaha dhāvaha lōyā! ēsa aüvvō narō kōvi

amha gharammi paviṭṭhō jārō cōrōvva nūṇa hōūṇa

ēvaṁ sudaṁsaṇāē vihiyaṁ sōūṇa halabōlaṁ

rē! lēha lēha dhāvaha kattha gaō kattha acchaï nilukkō

ēmāi vāharantō samuṭṭhiō pariyaṇō savvō

miliō ya bhūrilōgō kiṁ kiṁ ēyanti ēva jampantō

siṭṭhī samuddadattō bhaṇaï piē! kēṇa musiyā si?

sōvi hu sayaṇīyāō samuṭṭhiō kalayalaṁ nisāmittaṁ

vajjaraï kēṇa ambē! musiyā, jaṁ ēvamullavasi?

na hu ittha kōvi dīsaï duṭṭhamaī kīsa ambi! uvviggā?

ēvaṁ tu tēṇa bhaṇiyā sudaṁsaṇā ēvamullavaï

kō si tumaṁ kassa suō kīsa gihaṁ majjha āgaō pāva!?

hā! dhiṭṭha! kiṁnimittaṁ ambitti mamaṁ samullavasi?

kīsa maha puttasējjāē ittha suttōsi naṭṭhamajjāya!

kattha kaō mē puttō dhaṇavaïnāmō hayāsa! tumē?

ēvaṁ ca tīi niṭṭhuravayaṇāṇi nisamma vimhiō cittē

sō purisō niyadēhaṁ puṇō puṇō aha pulōēi

ālōiūṇa suiraṁ niyadēhaṁ jāva sāmalamuhō sō

uppaïyamaṇō tāhē ālōyaï nahayalaṁ sahasā

buḍa buḍa iya avvattaṁ jāvaṁ dintōvva pavaravijjāē

ullalaï ya puṇaruttaṁ daddura iva bhūmipaṭṭhammi

jāō khaṇēṇa dīṇō khayarakumārōvva naṭṭha varavijjō

gāḍhaṁ vēviradēhō mụ̄dhōvva hiuvva sañjāō

aha taṁ tārisarūvaṁ purisaṁ daṭṭhūṁ sudaṁsaṇā bhaṇaï

pāviṭṭha! kiṁ na sāhasi kattha kaō maha suō tumaē?

sōvi ahōmuhavayaṇō hōūṇa ṭhiō na jampaī jāva

tāhē sō jaṇanivahō vivihaṁ ullaviumāḍhattō

ēsō ibbhagharammī samāgaō cōriyāē dhaṇaluddhō

annē bhaṇanti cōrō jaï tā sējjāē kiṁ suttō?

tā ēsa vasumaīē kaēṇa paradāriyāē āyāō

annē bhaṇanti jārō jaï tā ambitti kiṁ bhaṇaï?

tā ēsa dhaṇavaïcciya vihiō kēṇāvi annaruvēṇa

dēvēṇa dāṇavēṇa va kēlīē piēṇa mannāmō

annē bhaṇanti bhūō ēsa pisāuvva āgaō ēttha

amhāṇa chalaṇahēuṁ ērisaruvēṇa duṭṭhappā

bhō bhō na ēvamēyaṁ bhaṇanti annē u kintu nisuṇēha

vasumaïyāē sīlaṁ parikkhiuṁ āgaō tiyasō

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ parōpparaṁ jā jaṇō samullavaï

tāva ya piyasahi! dhāriṇi! nisuṇasu jaṁ tattha sañjāyaṁ

kēūrahāraaṅgayavirāyamāṇō maṇōharasarīrō

sahasā payaḍībhūō bhāsuradittī tahiṁ tiyasō

dēvēṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇaha ēyassa vaïyaraṁ bhaddā!

aviyāṇiyaparamatthā karēha kiṁ bahuvihavigappē!

ēsō hu pāvakārī sumaṅgalō nāma nahayarō āsi

sāhiyabahuvihavijjō vijjāharanayarasupasiddhō

aha annayā kayāivi bhamamāṇō icchiēsu nayarēsu

ēsō ittha puraē samāgaō jōvvaṇummattō

hammiyatalamārụdhā ṇhāṇuttinnā hu vasumaī ēsā

gayaṇaṭṭhiēṇa diṭṭhā imēṇa suiraṁ ca nijjāyā

daṭṭhuṁ imīē rūvaṁ khuhiyaṁ aha māṇasaṁ tu ēyassa

kāuṁ dhaṇavaïruvaṁ avayariō ittha gēhammi

aviyāṇiyaparamatthā bhuttā aha vasumaī imēṇāvi

surayammi rañjiyamaṇō cintaï ēvaṁ mahāpāvō

dhaṇavaïrūvēṇa ṭhiō annāō ēttha sayalalōēṇa

ēīē varataṇūē samayaṁ sēvāmi surayasuhaṁ

vijjāharīhiṁ kiṁvā maha kajjaṁ kiṁva annajuvaīhiṁ

sōhagganihāṇāē pattāē imāē mahilāē?

ēvaṁ vicintiuṇaṁ avahariō dhaṇavaī imēṇaṁ tu

nēūṇa bharahakhittē mukkō u viṇīyanayarīē

pacchāiya niyaruvaṁ dhaṇavaïruvaṁ vihittu vijjāē

vasumaïsurayāsattō ēsō sō ciṭhṭhaī ēttha

sōvi hu dhaṇavaïvaṇiō viṇīyanayarīē pāviō varaō

daṭṭhuṁ aüvvanayariṁ vimhiyahiyaō viñcitēi

kā ēsā varanayarī kattha va sā mēhalāvaī nayarī

kiṁ kēṇa va avahariō pēcchāmi va sumiṇayaṁ ēyaṁ?

ēvaṁ vicintayantō bāhiṁ nayarīē jāva paribhamaī

tāvaya pavarujjāṇē samōsạdhō kēvalī diṭṭhō

siriusahanāhajiṇavaravaṁsapasūō tilōyavikkhāō

nāmēṇaṁ daṇḍaviraō rāyarisī muṇigaṇasamēō

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ jāyatōsō kāūṇa payāhiṇaṁ tu tikkhuttō

paṇamiya kēvalicalaṇē uvaviṭṭhō uciyadēsammi

nāūṇa ya patthāvaṁ vihiyapaṇāmēṇa tēṇa saṁlattaṁ

kēṇa ahaṁ avahariō bhavayaṁ! kiṁvā imaṁ khittaṁ?

kā vā ēsā nayarī ēvaṁ puṭṭhēṇa bhagavayā tassa

dhaṇavaïṇō puvvuttaṁ savvampi hu sāhiyaṁ taïyā

vinnāyasaruvō sō bhajjāpiimāivandhuparihīṇō

gurusōgasamāvannō kēvaliṇā ērisaṁ bhaṇiō

mā bhadda! kuṇasu sōyaṁ ērisaō cēva ēsa saṁsārō

iṭṭhaviōgā 'ṇiṭṭhappaōgadukkhēhiṁ saṅkinnō

ēyammi vasantāṇaṁ jīvāṇaṁ visayamōhiyamaṇāṇaṁ

sañjōgavippaōgā aṇantasō bhadda! jāyanti

paramatthaō ya dukkhaṁ jāyaï niyaduṭṭhakammuṇā jaṇiyaṁ

havaï hu nimittamittaṁ sēsaṁ puṇa bajjhaatthammi

tā tēṇa nahayarēṇaṁ na majjhaparamatthaō kayaṁ dukkhaṁ

kintu niyakammajaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ bhāvēsu niyacittē

aviya ‘‘pattharēṇāhaō kīvō pattharaṁ ḍakkumicchaī

migāriō saraṁ pappa saruppattiṁ vimaggaī’’

tā bhadda! jiṇāṇāē kammasamucchēyaṇammi ujjamasu

tattō vilīṇakammō pāvihisi na ērisaṁ dukkhaṁ

iya kēvaliyā bhaṇiō paḍibuddhō dhaṇavaī imaṁ bhaṇaï

icchāmō aṇusaṭṭhiṁ pavvajjaṁ dēha mē bhayavaṁ!

kēvaliṇā sē dinnā pavvajjā savvapāvamalaharaṇī

aha jāō sō samaṇō sāmannaguṇēhiṁ uvavēō

puvvasayasahassāiṁ tīsaṁ kāūṇa uggatavacaraṇaṁ

tēmāsiṁya ca kāūṇa aṇasaṇaṁ cattadēhō sō

uvavaṇṇō īsāṇē accharagaṇasaṅkulē vimāṇammi

candajjuṇābhihāṇē dēvō candajjuṇō nāma

ōhinnāṇēṇa taō nāūṇaṁ sayalaniyayavuttantaṁ

sō haṁ bhō bhō bhaddā! samāgaō ēttha nayarīē

vasumaïkaṇṭhavilaggō sayaṇīyagaō pasuttaō diṭṭhō

pacchāiyaniyarūvō dhaṇavaïrūvēṇa ēsa ṭhiō

jāō ya majjha kōvō tavvasaō cintiyaṁ maē ēyaṁ

mārēmi imaṁ pāvaṁ maha daïyāē saha pasuttaṁ

jaṇaṇijaṇayāṇa ahavā jāṇāvittā ya sayalalōyassa

ēyassa duṭṭhacariyaṁ kāhāmi viṇiggahaṁ pacchā

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ avahariyāō imassa pāvassa

savvāō vijjāō jāō ya imō sabhāvatthō

tattō ya vasumaīē sahasā niddā maē khayaṁ nīyā

ēīē vibuddhāē nāyaṁ jaha ēsa parapurisō

gantūṇa sāsuyāē siṭṭhā vattā imīi savvāvi

tattō sudaṁsaṇāē daṭhṭhūṇa imaṁ kaō rōlō

paḍibuddhēṇa imēṇavi tēṇiha ambā sudaṁsaṇā bhaṇiyā

sōuṁ niṭṭhuravayaṇaṁ palōiyaṁ niyayadēhaṁ tu

daṭhṭhūṇa puvvarūvaṁ niyadēhaṁ vimhiō imō cittē

maha vijjāē pabhāvō avahariō kēṇa ajjatti?

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ uppaïumaṇēṇa tāhi ēēṇa

niyavijjā sambhariyā pavarā nahagāmiṇī nāma

tahavi hu uppaïūṇaṁ jāhē na caēi tāhi vinnāyaṁ

kuviēṇa majjha kēṇavi vijjācchēō kaō 'vassaṁ

tēṇēva sabhāvatthō jāō na caēmi gayaṇamuppaïuṁ

ēvaṁ vigappayantō ēsō dīṇattaṇaṁ pattō

ēvaṁ piyasahi! dhāriṇi! sōuṁ tiyasassa bhāsiyaṁ tassa

sēṭṭhī samuddadattō sudaṁsaṇā sāvi sē bhajjā

āliṅgiya taṁ dēvaṁ aïgurusuyadukkhadaliyahiyayāiṁ

dīharasarēṇa dōṇṇivi karuṇaṁ rōttu pavattāiṁ

taha tēhiṁ tattha runnaṁ karuṇapalāvēhiṁ nēhabhariēhiṁ

jaha sō samāgayajaṇō savvōvi hu rōviuṁ laggō

sōūṇa runnasaddaṁ gihammi nayaravatthavvō

savvōvi hu saṁmiliō sabālavuḍ̣dhō jaṇō tattha

nāūṇa ya vuttantaṁ savvaṁ annunnavajjarijjantaṁ

akkōsanti bahuvihaṁ sumaṅgalaṁ nayaranārīō

ēyassa paḍaü vijjū suttō mā ēsa bujjhaü pāvō

niddōsōvi dhaṇavaī avahariō jēṇa pāvēṇa

hā! pāva! kiṁ na āsī khayarīō tuha sarūvajuttāō

muddhāē vasumaīē jēṇa tumē khaṇḍiyaṁ sīlaṁ?

tā pāva! iṇhi pāvasu aṇajjakajjammi niraya! nillajja!

niyaduccēṭṭhiyasarisaṁ ihaparalōē phalaṁ kaḍuyaṁ

ēyaṁ na hōi jōggaṁ nāmaṁ ēyassa duṭṭhacariyassa!

pāvō amaṅgalō ēsa jēṇa ēyaṁ kayaṁ pāvaṁ

kannakaḍuēhiṁ ēvaṁ asabbhavayaṇēhiṁ tēṇa lōēṇaṁ

akkōsiō sa bahuhā sudīṇavayaṇō tahiṁ varaō

tēṇēva dēvēṇa tahiṁ māyāvittāiṁ rōvamāṇāiṁ

aṇusāsiyāiṁ sammaṁ tuṇhikkāiṁ tu jāyāiṁ

tattō surēṇa bhaṇiyā muñcantī thūlaaṁsuyapavāhaṁ

bhaddē! vasumaï! iṇhiṁ kō tuha hiyayassa ucchāhō?

aha tīē vajjariyaṁ lajjāē samōṇamantavayaṇāē

jaṁ kiñci tuma sāmiya! āisasi tahiṁ samucchāhō

bhaṇiyaṁ surēṇa sundari! jaï ēvaṁ tā karēsu pavvajjaṁ

jiṇavarabhaṇiyaṁ dhammaṁ kammamahākandakōddālaṁ

jaïvi hu sundari! tumaē ayāṇamāṇāē ēyamāyariyaṁ

tahavi hu imassa ōsahaṁ hōu pavvajjā

tattō ya vasumaīē tahatti bahu manniyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ

mahaīē vibhūīē niyabandhavaaṇumayā tāhē

tatthēva ya nayarīē suhammanāmassa pavarasūrissa

mayahariyāē bahuvihasāhuṇigaṇasēviyakamāē

candajasānāmāē samappiyā suravarēṇa sayamēva

tīēvi ya āgamavihiṇā dinnā dikkhā vasumaīē

sōvi sumaṅgalakhayarō gururōsēṇāvi tēṇa dēvēṇa

daṭṭhūṇa dīṇavayaṇō na māriyō kahavi hu dayāē

nēūṇa māṇusuttaragirissa paraō sa ujjhiō varaō

aha sō tiyasō pattō niyayavimāṇammi vēgēṇa

sāvi hu vasumaïajjā samiīguttīsu sammamuvaüttā

sajjhāyajjhāṇajuttā ujjuttā viṇayakaraṇammi

puvvasayasahassāiṁ bahūṇi kāūṇa pavarasāmannaṁ

saṁlēhaṇāē sammaṁ jhōsittā niyayadēhaṁ tu

aṇurāyavasā taṁ ciya jhāyantī suravaraṁ niē hiyaē

kayaaṇasaṇā vasumaī kālaṁ kāūṇa uvavannā

īsāṇanāmammi biijjakappē candajjuṇē divvavimāṇayammi

dēvassa candajjuṇanāmagassa candappahā nāma pahāṇadēvī

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï vasumaïsuralōyapāvaṇō nāma

surasundarināmāē kahāē chaṭṭhō paricchēō

aha puvvasaṅgaēṇaṁ samayaṁ candajjuṇēṇa dēvēṇa

gạ̄dhāṇurāyarattā bhuñjaï diyalōgasōkkhāiṁ

candappahadēvīē suralōē suravarēṇa tēṇa samaṁ

bōlīṇō bahukālō divvasuhaṁ aṇuhavantīē

aha annayā kayāivi vicchāyaṁ picchiūṇa niyadaïyaṁ

bhayabhīyā sā dēvī taṁ dēvaṁ ēvamullavaï

sāmiya! kīsa sasaṅkō araïparaddhōvva dīsasi tumanti

taha kanta! ruivivajjiyadēhō dīṇōva kiṁ iṇhiṁ?

sukkaï kīsa akamhā kusumasamūhō sirammi sañjamiō?

vasaṇāṇi tujjha sāmiya! sāmalavannāṇi kiṁ ahuṇā?

tharaharaï kīsa diṭṭhī kāmammi ya sịdhilaāyarō iṇhiṁ

mōḍasi ya kīsa aṅgaṁ puṇō puṇō, dēva! vajjarasu?

aha candajjuṇadēvō ēvaṁ puṭṭhō piyāē vajjaraï

kiṁ na yāṇasi sundari! jēṇa mamaṁ pucchasi imaṁ tu?

dēvassa cavaṇasamaē imāṇi jāyanti suyaṇu! liṅgāṇi!

tā majjhavi cuisamaō āsannō vaṭṭaï iyāṇiṁ

ēvaṁ nisamma vayaṇaṁ dēvī aïvallahassa dēvassa

upannagaruyasōyā dukkhaṁ naraōvamaṁ pattā

aha annayā kayāivi sō dēvō tīi picchamāṇīē

kharatarapavaṇasamuddhayadīvōvva adaṁsaṇībhūō

daṭṭhūṇa cuyaṁ dēvaṁ dēvī candappahā sudukkhattā

mucchāviramē karuṇaṁ vilaviumēvaṁ samāraddhā

hā! nāha! pāṇavallaha! mōttūṇa mamaṁ gaō kahiṁ dēva!

tumaē rahiyā sāmiya! kaṁ saraṇamahaṁ pavajjāmi?

khaṇalavamēttampi tumaṁ viṇā maē nēva nāha! acchantō

mōttūṇa mamaṁ iṇhiṁ kattha gaō lōyaṇāṇanda!

taṁ cēva majjha saraṇaṁ taṁ nāhō jīviyaṁ tumaṁ dēva!

tumaē mukkā sāmiya! bhaṇa iṇhiṁ kattha vaccāmi?

hā! kattha gaō vallaha! ēttha aṇāhaṁ mamaṁ pamōttūṇaṁ

kō maha saraṇaṁ iṇhiṁ sāmiya! tumaē pamukkāē?

sō cēva dēvalōgō dēvasahassōvasōhiō rammō

tuha virahiyāē iṇhiṁ bhāvaï naraōvamō majjha

taṁ ciya imaṁ vimāṇaṁ rammaṁ maṇikaṇagarayaṇavicchuriyaṁ

tumaē mukkaṁ bhāvaï ghaḍiyālayasacchahaṁ nāha!

kiṅkaravaggōpi imō cāḍukarō viṇayakaraṇatallicchō

paramāhammiyasarisō bhāsaï tuha nāha! virahammi

puṁnāganāgacampayanamērumandārarēhiraṁ rammaṁ

ujjāṇaṁ tuha virahē asipattavaṇaṁva paḍihāi

varamajjaṇavāvīō nimpalajalapūriyāō rammāō

bhāsanti tujjha virahē vēyaraṇinaīē tullāō

dhannāō nārīō jāō mayaṁ aṇusaranti bhattāraṁ

ēyammi dēvabhāvē kattō ēyārisaṁ majjha?

ēmāi palavamāṇā sā dēvī haṇaï niyaya hatthēhiṁ

aṅgāiṁ sudukkhattā kandantī karuṇasaddēṇa

mucchijjaï puṇaruttaṁ nīsāhārā ya paḍaï bhūmīē

sampattacēyaṇā sā puṇaravi ēvaṁ samullavaï

hā! nāha! kiṁ na pēcchasi vilavantiṁ jaṁ na dēsi ullāvaṁ

kiṁ vā ruṭṭhō vallaha! kiṁ avaraddhaṁ maē tujjha?

paṇayakuviyāē sāmiya! cāḍusahassāṇi majjha kuvvantō

iṇhiṁ kīsa akaṇḍē vilavantiṁ muñcasi mamaṁ tu?

hā! nāha! kiṁ na yāṇasi aïguruaṇurāyamōhiyā ēsā

maha virahē kaha hōhī jēṇa akaṇḍē tumē mukkā?

ēvaṁ bahuppagāraṁ piyayamavirahammi kandamāṇā sā

jāyā ummūliyakamaliṇivva vicchāyamuhakamalā

daṭṭhūṇa garuyasōyaṁ gurudukkhasamōhayaṁ tayaṁ dēviṁ

tīē niddhavayaṁsā sayampabhā ēvamullavaï

jāṇiyajiṇavayaṇāvi hu saṁsārasarūvayaṁ suṇēūṇa

iyaramahilavva piyasahi! vilavasi kiṁ ērisaṁ bahuhā?

piyasahi! na hu sāhārō bahuṇāvi hu vilaviēṇa jaṁ atthi

tā kiṁ chāliyagalathaṇasamēṇa vihalēṇa runnēṇa?

jaï vilavasi sayahuttaṁ piṭṭasi dēhaṁ karēsi gurusōyaṁ

tahavi hu na ēi daïō kālakayantēṇa jō nīō

tō ēyaṁ nāūṇaṁ nēhaṁ sịdhilēsu muñca gurusōgaṁ

ujjama jiṇindadhammē ēvaṁvihadukkhasamaṇammi

sō tavasañjamarūvō dēvabhavē natthi vaṭṭamāṇāē

sammattasuddhihēuṁ sundari! tā ujjamaṁ kuṇasu

gantūṇa vidēhēsuṁ vandasu tilōkkabandhavajiṇindē

kēvaliṇō taha sāhū sañjamakaraṇujjaē dhīrē

sāsayajiṇabhavaṇaṭṭhiyajiṇindabimbāṇi paramabhattīē

kulasēladīvapavvayaṭhiyāṇi gantūṇa paṇamēsu

ēvaṁ visuddhasammattasañjuyā pāviūṇa maṇuyattaṁ

laddhuṁ jiṇavaradikkhaṁ hayakammā vayasi siddhīē

ēvaṁvihadukkhāiṁ tattha gayā nēva pāvisi avassaṁ

jaramaraṇarōgasōgēhiṁ vajjiyā hōsi ākālaṁ

ēvaṁ sayampabhāē bhaṇiyā candappahā tahiṁ dēvī

mōttuṇa daïyasōgaṁ samāgayā ēttha lōyammi

sahiyā sayampabhāē vandittā jiṇavarindabimbāiṁ

nandīsarammi tāhē samāgayā ēttha bharahammi

tattha ya pēcchaï nayarē rāyagihē pavarabāhirūjjāṇē

samaṇagaṇasēviyakamaṁ sasurāsuramaṇuyapariyariyaṁ

dhammaṁ vāgaramāṇaṁ suhaṅkaraṁ nāma kēvaliṁ tāhē

gayaṇāō ōyariyā sā dēvī piyasahisamēyā

vandiya suhaṅkaraṁ taṁ suhaṁ karantaṁ tu bhaviyasattāṇaṁ

sēsampi samaṇasaṅghaṁ uvaviṭṭhā uciyadēsammi

aha sō bhayavaṁ tīē sadēvamaṇuyāsurāiparisāē

gambhīrabhāraīē ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō

aïdulahō maṇuyabhavō sukuluppattī jiṇindadhammō ya

pattammi tammi ujjamaha savvahā mā pamāēha

karagahiyasalilasarisaṁ khaṇē khaṇē jhijjaē imaṁ āuṁ

tamhā jiṇavaradhammē mā hu pamāyaṁ kuṇaha tumhē

kusasūiaggasaṅgayajalalavatullammi jīviyavvammi

ujjamaha bhāvasāraṁ aïvisamā jēṇa kammagaī

jamhā pamāyamūlaṁ dukkhaṁ savvampi ēttha saṁsārē

caüsuvi gaīsu niyamā tēṇa imō hōi mōttavvō

ēsō jammanimittaṁ rōgajarāmaraṇadukkhasayahēū

ēyavasagā ya sattā bhamanti bhavasāgarē ghōrē

mōttuṇa tā pamāyaṁ karēha varaüjjamaṁ jiṇindassa

dhammammi taggayamaṇā saṁsārasamuddabōhitthē

paramatthabandhubhūē imammi dhammammi ujjamaṁ kuṇaha

niddhūyasavvapāvā pāvaha tō mōkkhasōkkhāiṁ

nāuṁ kahantaraṁ sā dēvī candappahā imaṁ bhaṇaï

bhayavaṁ! katthuvavannō daïō candajjuṇō majjha?

maha kittiyaṁ ca āuṁ iō cuyāē ya kattha maha jammō?

daïēṇa tēṇa hōjja navā daṁsaṇaṁ majjha?

ēvaṁ ca pucchiō sō bahumāṇajuyāē tīē dēvīē

bhayavaṁ suhaṅkarō aha ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō

bhaddē! sō tuha daïō iha cēva ya bhārahammi vāsammi

vēyaḍḍhapavvayavarē uttarasẹ̄dhīē rammāē

nayarammi camaracañcē bhāṇugaīnāmayassa khayarassa

piyajāyākucchīē uppannō puttabhāvēṇa

paliōvamāṇi aṭṭha ō tuha āu āsi samudiyaṁ maddē!

iṇhiṁ tu vāsalakkhaṁ avasēsaṁ ciṭṭhaē āuṁ

punnammi vāsalakkhē caïūṇa tumampi tīi sẹ̄dhīē

suranandaṇammi nayarē khayarassa ō asaṇivēgassa

dhūyā hōhisi bhaddē! pavarā u piyaṅgumañjarīnāmā

puvvadaïēṇa samayaṁ tattha ya tuha daṁsaṇaṁ hōhī

tattō ya bhaṇaï dēvī nāyavvō sō maē kahaṁ bhayavaṁ!

kahavā pāṇiggahaṇaṁ hōhī maha tēṇa samayampi?

aha kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu jattāē jiṇavarindassa

ummiṭṭhakarivarāō mōissaï jō tumaṁ bhaddē!

sō cēva ya nāyavvō ēsō sō puvvavallahō majjha

puṇaravi visēsadaṁsaṇamēvaṁ tuha hōhihī tēṇa

tuha māuladhūyāē pāṇiggahaṇammi kaṇagamālāē

kāuṁ tīē rūvaṁ ēhī sō mittakajjēṇa

jō tattha kaṇagamālārūvō hōhī sa puvvadaïutti

nāyavvō nīsaṅkaṁ bhaddē! candappabhē! tumaē

tayaṇantaraṁ ca hōhī pāṇiggahaṇampi tēṇa saha tujjha

jāīsaraṇēṇa tumaṁ sumarissasi maha imaṁ vayaṇaṁ

ēvaṁ piyasahi! dhāriṇi! kēvalivayaṇaṁ nisamma sā dēvī

jāyā harisiyahiyayā kēvaliṇō namiya payakamalaṁ

tattō uppaïyā sā sāsayajiṇacēiyāiṁ savvāiṁ

vandittā titthayarē mahāvidēhēsu savvēvi

saṭṭhāṇaṁ sampattā taṁ ciya dēvaṁ maṇēṇa cintēntī

aha annayā kayāivi sāvi cuyā āuyakhayammi

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē jā sā vasumaī ajjā dēvī candappahā ya suralōē

sā haṁ piyaṅgumañjarināmā iha suyaṇu! sañjāyā

daṭhṭhūṇa dēvanivahaṁ jāīsaraṇammi ajja uppannē

sambhariō sō dēvō pāṇappiō āsi jō saggē

cirapariciyassa piyasahi! gāḍhaṁ ukkaṇṭhiyā ahaṁ iṇhiṁ

tassaṅgamaïcchāi samucchugaṁ iṇhi maha cittaṁ

taṁ kaïya diṇaṁ hōhī jammi sasiṇēhaniddhadiṭṭhīē

puvvabhavanēhabaddhaṁ pēcchissaṁ vallahaṁ tamahaṁ?

kaha sō mē daṭṭhavvō sigghaṁ kaha tēṇa saṅgamō hōhī

ēvaṁvihacintāē jāyā sōgāurā ahayaṁ

taṁ ciya citantīē 'vakkhittamaṇāi āgayāvi tumaṁ

piyasahi! nō saccaviyā tēṇa na sambhāsiyā bhaddē!

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ jāyaṁ kiṁ sōgakāraṇaṁ tujjha

piyasahi! dhāriṇi! taṁ tuha nīsēsaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

aha dhāriṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ kēvalivayaṇaṁ na annahā bhaddē!

tā kīsa kuṇasi sōyaṁ ēvaṁ ēēṇa hōyavvaṁ?

hasiūṇa maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō

navaraṁ aïukkaṇṭhā tuvaraï maha māṇasaṁ suyaṇu!

ētthantarammi piyayama! campagamālā samāgayā jaṇaṇī

bhaṇaï lahu putti! majjasu bhuñjasu kuṇa pavarasiṅgāraṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē kiṁ ammi! kāraṇaṁ jaṁ aïppagē cēva

jāyā bhōyaṇavēlā, ammāē taō imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

ujjāṇē jiṇabhavaṇē hōhī ṇhavaṇaṁ jugādidēvassa

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ atthamaṇaṁ jāva sūrassa

tattha ya puravatthavvō vaccaï ṇhavaṇassa pēkkhaō lōgō

amhēvi gamissāmō pariyaṇasahiyāiṁ tatthēva

tēṇēva kāraṇēṇaṁ pabhāyasamayammi bhōyaṇaṁ siddhaṁ

tā hōsu lahuṁ paüṇā jiṇabhavaṇē jēṇa vaccāmō

ēvaṁ niyajaṇaṇīē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa uṭṭhiyā jhatti

kayabhōyaṇāicēṭṭhā ārụ̄dhā sandaṇē pavarē

niyapariyaṇapariyariyā gayā ya ujjāṇabhūsaṇē tattha

jiṇamandirammi sammaṁ pūittā vandiō bhayavaṁ

diṭṭhaṁ jiṇinda ṇhavaṇaṁ kīrantaṁ bhattijuttakhayarēhiṁ

vittappāyē nhavaṇē niyapariyaṇasañjuyā ahayaṁ

ārụ̄dhā rahapavarē valiyā nayarassa abhimuhā jāva

ummiṭṭhō nayarāō nīhariō karivarō tāva

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ saṁmuhamintaṁ turayā maha rahavarassa uttaṭṭhā

ummaggēṇa payaṭṭhā bhaggō sō sandaṇō tāhē

bhūmīē ahaṁ paḍiyā mucchāē vigayacēyaṇā jāyā

tēṇa paraṁ jaṁ jāyaṁ piyayama! tamahaṁ na jāṇāmi

navaraṁ diṭṭhō si tumaṁ vīyantō niyayaüttarīēṇa

daṭṭhūṇa tumaṁ jāō garuō hiyayammi āṇandō

tattō majjha vigappō piyayama! ēsō maṇammi sañjāō

ēyaṁ taṁ sañjāyaṁ kēvaliṇā jaṁ tayāiṭṭhaṁ

puvvabhavasaṅgaō sō tā nūṇaṁ ēsa vallahō majjha

ramaï ya imammi diṭṭhī maṇaṁ ca āṇandamuvvahaï

amaēṇava saṁsittaṁ diṭṭhammi imammi maha sarīrampi

viyasiyanayaṇō ēsōvi dīsaē sāṇurāgōvva

tā maha pāṇapiō sō avassamēsotti jāva cintēmi

tāva ya pariyaṇasahiyā samāgayā tattha maha dhāī

abhinandiūṇa tīē āpuṭṭhō tāhiṁ piyayama! tumanti

vaccamō niyanayarē ussūraṁ vaṭṭaē jēṇa

ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ caliyā tattō ya maē vicintiyaṁ ēyaṁ

punnēhiṁ piō diṭṭhō iṇhiṁ na caēmi chaḍḍēuṁ

ēyassa vayaṇapaṅkayapalōyaṇaṁ mōttu maha imā diṭṭhī

paṅkanibuḍḍā dubbalagāivva na sakkaē gantuṁ

aviya ēvaṁvihē muhuttē nayaṇajuyaṁ milaï kassavi jaṇassa

hatthivva pakakhuttō dukkhuttāraṁ daḍhaṁ hōi

ēsā vi majjha dhāī caliyā ēyaṁ pamōttu maṇadaïyaṁ

lajjāē vajjariuṁ ahampi sakkēmi nō kimpi

tā majjha imaṁ juttaṁ giṇhāmi imassa kiñci ābharaṇaṁ

taṁ ciya palōiūṇaṁ jēṇa maṇaṁ nivvuiṁ kuṇaï

maṇavallahēṇa ēēṇa virahiyā niyamihammi sampattā

taṁ cēva pulaïūṇaṁ sandhīrissāmi niyahiyayaṁ

annaṁ ca kila ēsa itthirūvō pāṇiggahaṇammi kaṇagamālāē

ēhī, tattha ya hōhī puṇōvi kila daṁsaṇaṁ imiṇā

iya taïyā kēvaliyā āiṭṭhaṁ majjha tēṇa ēyassa

taṁ cēva ya ābharaṇaṁ sābhinnāṇaṁ tahiṁ hōhī

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ muddārayaṇaṁ tu tumha hatthāō

gahiyaṁ vallaha! taïyā niyayā ya samappiyā muddā

piyakaraphāsapavittaṁ parihittā tampi gurupamōēṇa

caliyā valantagīvā sapariyaṇā nayarasaṁmuhiyā

aha dhāriṇināmāē kannē hōūṇa majjha ullaviyaṁ

ēyaṁ kēvalivayaṇaṁ nivvaḍiyaṁ tāva ikkaṁ tu

tā ēsa dēvajīvō puvviṁ jō āsi tujjha vallahaō

ēvaṁ tīē bhaṇiē sarōsamēvaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ

huṁ huṁ diṭṭhā si tumaṁ dhāriṇi! avasarasu diṭṭhimaggāō

ēvaṁvihamaṇibaddhaṁ jā jampasi amha puraütti

iṇhiṁ na vallahō kiṁ puvvaṁ jaṁ āsi majjha vallahaō

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō kayañjalī dhāriṇī bhaṇaï

piyasahi! khama avarāhaṁ savvamasaccaṁ imaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ

jaha puvvaṁ taha ahuṇāvi vallahō cēva tuha ēsō

kiṁ puṇa bhaṇāmi saccaṁ jaï daïō kīsa ujjhiuṁ caliyā?

tā mā piyasahi! rūsasu ghaḍaï ciya maha imaṁ vayaṇaṁ

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ sahāsavayaṇāi tīi sañjuttā

pattā gihammi kamasō atthamiō tāva sūrōvi

aha tīē dhāriṇīē jāisaraṇāisayalavuttantō

kahiō maha māūē taṁ sōūṁ harisiyā ēsā

tīēvi savvaṁ kahiyaṁ maha piuṇō asaṇivēganāmassa

tattō ya harisiēṇa vajjariyaṁ tēṇa ēvaṁ tu

āsi maha garuyacintā dhūyā jaṁ purisavēsiṇī jāyā

na ya icchaï kiñci varaṁ kahamēyamahaṁ karissāmi?

sundaramēyaṁ jāyaṁ jāīsaraṇaṁ imīē jaṁ jāyaṁ

amhaṁ ciya abbhudaō abbhudaō ubbhinnē pāṇiyaṁ paḍiyaṁ

annaṁ ca purisēhiṁ majjha siṭṭhaṁ hatthibhaē jēṇa mōiyā ēsā

sō bhāṇumaïputtō cittagaī nāma varakumarō

tassēva dēmi ēyaṁ jaï icchā atthi tammi ēāē?

tattō campagamālā harisiyacittā imaṁ bhaṇaï

jōgo cciya sō kumarō imāi pavarāi majjha dhūyāē

ēīēvi sañjāō aïguruō tammi aṇurāō

kintu nisuṇēsu sāmiya! rannō kaṇagappahassa ēyassa

bhāṇugaïṇō ya raṇṇō parōpparaṁ garuyavēranti

jalaṇappahakajjēṇaṁ, suppasiddhaṁ cēva tumha ēyanti

tā kaha ēhī ihaïṁ cittagaī pāṇigahaṇatthaṁ? ,

dhūyā saṁyavarā jaï pēsijjaï tammi cēva nayarammi

ēvaṁ na hōi piyayama! āṇandō majjha hiyayassa

jaō ēsā ēkkā dhūyā vallahiyā tā imīē vīvāhaṁ

jaha navi pēcchāmi ahaṁ tā kiṁ maha jīviēṇanti?

ēvaṁ campagamālā maha jaṇaṇī jāva tattha ullavaï

tāva ya candaṇanāmō maha bhāyā āgaō bhaṇaï

kiṁ acchaha vīsatthā tumhē iha tāya! nivvicintatti

ēyaṁ nayaraṁ tāva ya savvampi hu āulībhūyaṁ

tattō bhaṇiyaṁ piuṇā kēṇa va kajjēṇa putta! jāṇāsi?

aha candaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ iya vattā tāva nayarammi

kila kaṇagappaharannō jiṇabhavaṇē landhiyammi kuddhēṇa

vijjāṇaṁ avahārō vihiō dharaṇindanāmēṇa

jalaṇappahassa siddhā rōhiṇināmā kila 'jja vijjatti

tassa ya bhayāu naṭṭhō rāyā kaṇagappahō tāva

sirigandhavāhaṇassa u khayarappahāṇassa sō gaō saraṇaṁ

tavvirahē puramēyaṁ sayalampi hu āulībhūyaṁ

jalaṇappahabhayabhīyā savvēvi hu nāyarā palāyanti

mōttūṇa imaṁ nayaraṁ vayanti avarāvarapurēsu

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē amhampi tāya! iṇhiṁ visēsaō hōi nāsiyavvanti

kaṇagappahassa rannō pavarō mantī jaō tāō

ēvaṁ ca puttavayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ tāhi asaṇiyavēgēṇa

āṇattā niyapurisā sañjatti kuṇaha gamaṇatthaṁ

vijjāē varavimāṇaṁ viuvviyaṁ tāhiṁ majjha jaṇaēṇa

ārōviyaṁ ca savvaṁ gharasāraṁ tattha purisēhiṁ

ēvaṁ ca majjha piyayama! dhāriṇīnāmāē sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

ahamavi tammi vimāṇē ārụ̄dhā pariyaṇēṇa samaṁ

tattō ya taṁ vimāṇaṁ uppaïyaṁ khaggasāmalaṁ gayaṇaṁ

vēgēṇa ya sampattaṁ gaṅgāvattammi nayarammi

kaṇagappahassa rannō āvāsē tattha taṁ samōinnaṁ

aha gandhavāhaṇēṇavi uciyapavittī kayā tassa

ēvaṁ gaṅgāvattē kaïvayadivasāṇi jāva acchāmi

hiyaēṇa cintayantī piyayama! tuha daṁsaṇōvāyaṁ

aviya pēcchissaṁ kaïya ahaṁ kaïyā maha tēṇa saṅgamō hōhī

kaïyā vīvāhadiṇaṁ hōhī taṁ kaṇagamālāē?

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ cintēmāṇī ahōnisaṁ tattha

rayaṇīēvi nō niddaṁ lahāmi tuha nāha! virahammi

annadivasammi bhāyā campagamālāē majjha jaṇaṇīē

amiyagaī tattha purē samāgaō rāyakajjēṇa

daṭṭhūṇa asaṇivēgaṁ aha sō sañjāyapaharisō bhaṇaï

sirigandhavāhaṇēṇaṁ rannā bahumāṇapuvvaṁ tu

nahavāhaṇassa kajjē vimaggiyā ajja kaṇagamālatti

saharisavayaṇēṇa maēvi tassa dinnā imā bhadda!

ēīē pañcamīē vivāhalaggaṁ nirūviṁya tīē

niyabandhavajuttēṇaṁ āgantavvaṁ tahiṁ tumaē

aha bhaṇaï asaṇivēgō sayamēva ya tattha gantumuciyamha

tumha vayaṇāō sampaï visēsaō hōi gantavvaṁ

kintu nisuṇēsu kāraṇamamhaṁ gamaṇaṁ na hōi jaha uciyaṁ

kaṇagappahassa raṇṇō vaṭṭaï visamā dasā jēṇa

ēkkaṁ vijjāchēō rajjabbhaṁsō ya niyapuriccāō

tā tammi sasōgammi kaha gamaṇaṁ hōi maha uciyaṁ?

jē duhiyammi na duhiyā āvayapattē biijjayā nēva

pahuṇō na tē u bhiccā dhuttā paramatthaō nēyā

ētthatthē tā sampaï nibbandhō tē na hōi kāyavvō

tuha bhagiṇī puṇa ēhī laggadiṇē āulā jaïvi

amiyagaī bhaṇaï taō pēsēhi piyaṅgumañjariṁ tāva

ēīē kaṇagamālā acchaï ukkaṇṭhiyā jēṇa

tattō jaṇaēṇa ahaṁ paṭṭhaviyā māulēṇa saha ēttha

pattā ya kamēṇa ihaṁ miliyā tō kaṇagamālāē

ēvaṁ piyayama! ahayaṁ māulayagihammi ēttha āyāyā

cintēmi kaïya hōhī laggadiṇaṁ majjha puṇṇēhiṁ?

jattha maē daṭṭhavvō sō hu jaṇō jīviyāō abbhahiō

ēvaṁ cintētīē samāgayā pañcamī ēsā

jāva ya kamēṇa vattē pāṇiggahaṇammi tāhē pikkhaṇaē

nahavāhaṇassa puraō pāraddhē cintiyaṁ hi maē

ēsā hu kaṇagamālā sahijaṇamajjhammi dīsaï niviṭṭhā

sō maha maṇavallahaō na kōvi iha dīsaē tā kiṁ?

kēvaliṇō taṁ vayaṇaṁ hōjjā aliyaṁ tu maha aünnēhiṁ

nahi nahi, avaradīsāē avi uggamaï ravī kahavi

payalijja va mērugirī palayaṁ gacchējja udahiṇō savvē

na ya kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyā bhāvā iha annahā honti

tā kiṁ nu kaṇagamālā ahavā sō hiyayavallahō majjha?

daṁsiya muddārayaṇaṁ karēmi nīsaṅkiyaṁ ēyaṁ

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ samāgayā tāhi tujjha pāsammi

muddārayaṇasamēō niyayakarō daṁsiō tāhē

tattō piyayama! tumaē muddāsahiyammi daṁsiē hatthē

ēsō sō maha daïutti paccaō jhatti upannō

pēccha kaha ēsa ēvaṁ kāūṇavi vigayasayalaāsaṅkō

ciṭṭhaï, kiṁ navi bīhaï nahavāhaṇarāyaüttassa?

kiñci uvāyaṁ tāhiṁ karēmi ēyassa mōyaṇaṭṭhāē

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ vañciya taṁ sahiyaṇaṁ savvaṁ

kavaḍēṇa maē sāmiya! samāṇiō iha asōgavaṇiyaē

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

aviya jaïvi hu kannā piyayama! sajjhasabhariyā na sakkaē kahavi

maṇavallahassa puraō ēkkampi hu vayaṇamullaviuṁ

tahavi maē savisēsaṁ ṇiyacariyaṁ sāhiyaṁ imaṁ jamhā

jāīsaraṇaguṇēṇaṁ pariciya iva bhāsasi tumanti

bhō cittavēga! ēvaṁ tīē vayaṇaṁ nisamma sahasatti

mucchāviramē majjhavi jāīsaraṇaṁ samuppannaṁ

sambhariyaṁ savvampi hu maēvi puvvōiyaṁ niyañcariyaṁ

aha tīē saṁlattaṁ piyayama! kiṁ iṇhi kāyavvaṁ?

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ viyāṇiyaṁ kulaharaṁ tu tē suyaṇu!

tā vacca tumaṁ gēhaṁ ahamavi ittō palāissaṁ

paḍiyā hu kaṇagamālā maḍḍāē majjha ēttha vāvīē

kalayalapuvvaṁ ēvaṁ sāhijjasu sayalalōyassa

ēvaṁ kaē na kassa vi āsaṅkā hōi cittavēgammi

nāhavāhaṇāō ēvaṁ vimōiō hōi varamittō

annaṁ ca nisuyaṁ ca maē sundari! suranandaṇapuravarammi āgamma

jalaṇappahēṇa puṇaravi ahiṭṭhiyaṁ niyayarajjanti

vaḍiyaṁ ca puravaraṁ taṁ rannā saṁmāṇiō ya puralōō

tā tattha ahaṁ gantuṁ āṇāvissāmi tuha jaṇagaṁ

jalaṇappahōvi rāyā pēkkhissaï puvvagaüravēṇēva

tattha tumaṁ pariṇissaṁ ammāpīīṇaṇunnāyā (nnāō?)

ēvaṁ ca kaē vallahi! salāhaṇijjaṁ tu hōi savvampi

annaha puṇa vihiyammi ubhayakulaṁ maïliyaṁ hōi

tattō ya tīē bhaṇiyaṁ jamiha tumaṁ kiñci āṇavēsi maē

taṁ savvaṁ kāyavvaṁ navaraṁ piya! suṇasu vinnattiṁ

jīviyasandēhēṇaṁ kahavi maē ajja nāha! sampattō

mōttūṇa tumaṁ iṇhiṁ katthavi sakkēmi nō gantuṁ

tāvacciya maha jīyaṁ jāva tumaṁ nayaṇagōyarē vasasi

tuha daṁsaṇarahiyā puṇa jhatti ya pāṇēhiṁ muñcāmi

jampi nimisanti nayaṇā ēttiyamēttampi dūsahaṁ mannē

kiṁ puṇa jaṁ bahudivasē tuha virahē nāha! acchissaṁ?

tā nāha! jattha vaccasi aṇugantavvaṁ maēvi tatthēva

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē kajjē jaṁ kāyavvaṁ tayaṁ bhaṇasu

annaṁ ca saṭṭhāṇē pattāē pāṇiggahaṇaṁ bhavissaī majjha

ēvaṁvihaāsāē sagihaṁ vaccāmi jaï nāha!

ēttō ya majjha jaṇaō bhaṇiōvi hu jaï na vaccaī kahavi

jalaṇappahēṇa rannā, kaṇagapahaṁ mōttu niyanayarē

bhīsaṇabhuyagēhiṁ khaṇēṇa vẹ̄dhiyaṁ uggavisaviyārēhiṁ

savvaṅgēsu baddhō sarāgajīvōvva kammēhiṁ

tattō mahantaviyaṇā pāubbhūyā mamaṁ taō dēhaṁ

gayaṇāō nivaḍiō haṁ bhuyaṅgabhārēṇa bhūmīē

viyaṇāē vibbhalaṅgō saṁvalitaruṇō imassa hiṭṭhammi

gayacēyaṇōvva jāō bhujaṅgasaṅghāyaübbaddhō

sāvi maha pāṇadaïyā garuyaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa āvayaṁ majjhaṁ

aïdukkhiyā varāī rōyantā ghaggharasarēṇa

hā ajjaütta! vallaha! ēya aṇatthassa kāriṇī ahayaṁ

hā pāviṭṭhā taïyā kiṁ na mayā mayaṇapacakkhaṁ

hā kaha majjhanimittē piyayama! aïgaruya āvayaṁ pattō

hā ajjaütta! iṇhiṁ tuha virahē natthi maha jīyaṁ

bhō bhō dhaṇadēva! imaṁ sōuṁ khayarassa bhāsiyaṁ tassa

ētthantarammi ya mahaṁ ēsa vigappō samuppannō

mahilāpalāvasaddō puvviṁ jō āsi iha maē nisuō

ēyadaïyāē nūṇaṁ sō hōhī kaṇagamālāē

tattō ya purisasaddō tayaṇantaramēva jō maē nisuō

nahavāhaṇassa hōhī sō saddō ēyasattassa

ahavā kiṁ maē imiṇā vicintiēṇaṁ tu tāva nisuṇēmi

jaṁ kiñci kahaï ēsō niyacariyaṁ cittavēgotti

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ tattō dhaṇadēva! suṇiumāḍhattō

tavvayaṇamahaṁ savvaṁ aha sō ēvaṁ samullavaï

bhō suppaïṭṭha ēvaṁ vilavantā bahuvihaṁ sudukkhattā

nahavāhaṇēṇa nīyā majjha piyā kaṇagamālatti

ahayampi taō dūsahavisaharakayavēyaṇāē vēvantō

daïyā viōyagurudukkhatāviō jāva ciṭṭhāmi

bhō suppaïṭṭha! tāva ya tumampi iha āgaō paēsammi

tumaē maṇinīrēṇaṁ ēsō mēllāviō ahayaṁ

tā bhō tumaē dinnaṁ maha jīyaṁ ēttha natthi sandēhō

maṇiṇō ya pabhāvāō na ya ḍakkō duṭṭhasappēhiṁ

annaha kaha maha jīyaṁ havijjaguruvēyaṇā paraddhassa

kīṇāsavayaṇasacchahabhīsaṇabhuyagēhiṁ gahiyassa

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ kēṇa tumaṁ ērisāē mahaīē

khittō si āvayāē taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

iya bhō dhaṇadēva! tayā sōuṁ khayarassa bhāsiyaṁ tassa

tattō ya maē ēyaṁ vicintiyaṁ niyayacittammi

pēccha narā vibuhāvi hu aṇurāyaparavasā visayagiddhā

pāvinti āvayāō vivihāō ētthaṁ saṁsārē

acchaü tā paralōgē ihēva pāvinti garuyadukkhāiṁ

rāgavimōhiyacittā kajjākajjaṁ ayāṇantā

sārīramāṇasāṇaṁ dūsahadukkhāṇa kāraṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ

iha paralōē ghōrō rāgo cciya sayalajīvāṇaṁ

rāgandhā iha jīvā dullahalōyammi gāḍhamaṇurattā

jaṁ vēinti asāyaṁ kattō taṁ handi! naraēvi?

vallahaviōyataviyā asamañjasaciṭṭhiyāiṁ kuṇamāṇā

naraē nēraïyā iva niccaṁ ciya dukkhiyā honti

vahabandhamāraṇāiṁ lahanti rāgēṇa mōhiyā jīvā

vaccantti duggaīē sahanti vivihāiṁ dukkhāiṁ

rāgō hi dukkharūvō rāgō ciya sayalaāvayāhēū

rāgaparaddhā jīvā bhamanti bhavasāgarē ghōrē

tāva ciya paramasuhaṁ jāva na rāgō maṇammi uccharaï

handi! sarāgammi maṇē dukkhasahassāiṁ pavisanti

ēmāi cintiūṇaṁ dhaṇadēva! maē imaṁ tu vajjariyaṁ

bhō cittavēga! iṇhiṁ mā kīraü kōvi sōgotti

jaṁ ēsō saṁsārō ērisadukkhāṇa niyayaāvāsō

pattāē āvayāē tēṇa visāō na kāyavvō

jaramaraṇarōgavallahaviōgabahulammi ēttha saṁsārē

jamhā sakammajaṇiyaṁ jāyaï jīvāṇa dukkhanti

tō bhaṇaï cittavēgō bhadda! visāō na kōvi maha annō

ēkacciya maha cintā kuṇaï maṇē dūsahaṁ dukkhaṁ

sā kaha varaī hōhī nīyā nahavāhaṇēṇa ruyamāṇī

jīvaï va navā iṇhiṁ daṭṭhuṁ maha tārisamavatthaṁ?

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï sō khayarō majjha bhadda! dhaṇadēva!

ētthantaraṁmmi nisuṇasu jō vuttantō tahiṁ jāō

ēkkō kamaladala 'cchō pihuvacchō suravarō tahiṁ sahasā

ōinnō gayaṇāō ujjōintō disāvalayaṁ

daṭṭhuṁ samāgayaṁ taṁ viyasiyavayaṇō ya cittavēgō sō

abbhuṭṭhiūṇa paṇamaï taṁ dēvaṁ paramaviṇaēṇa

aha sō suhāsaṇatthō tiyasō saṁlavaï bhadda! tuha kusalaṁ?

maṇiṇō ya pabhāvāō nitthinnā āvayā viulā!

tō bhaṇaï cittavēgō tumha pabhāvāō sampayaṁ kusalaṁ

tā sampaï maha sāhasu mahantakōūhalaṁ ittha

puvvabhavē sambandhō tumaē saha āsi kō mamaṁ dēva!?

kēṇa va kajjēṇa tumaṁ āsi gaō ucchugō taïyā?

tattō ya bhaṇaï tiyasō imēṇa kajjēṇa āgaō suyaṇu!

sā ēgamaṇō hōuṁ sāhijjantaṁ nisāmēhi

jambuddīvē ihaïṁ ēravaē atthi āriē dēsē

vijayavaī nāmēṇaṁ nayarī suranayarisaṅkāsā

tīēvi suvikkhāō dhaṇabhūī nāma āsi satthāhō

dakkhinnadayājuttō ujjuttō jaïṇadhammammi

candōvva kalānilaō gayavva niccaṁ payaṭṭavaradāṇō

aṇuyattiyamittō vāsarōvva buhalōyamaṇaïṭṭhō

tassa ya pasantarūvā païvvayā saccasīladayajuttā

bhajjā sundaradēhā sundarināmā suvikkhāyā

vimalaṁ sāvagadhammaṁ sammaṁ aha tāṇa pālayantāṇaṁ

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ susāhujaṇabhattijuttāṇaṁ

aha annayā kayāivi pahāṇa suviṇēhiṁ sūiyaṁ taṇayaṁ

sā sundarī pasūyā pabhūyasuhalakkhaṇāinnaṁ

nijjiyaaṇaṅgarūvaṁ tēēṇa ya diṇayarassa sāricchaṁ

sōmaṁ sasibimbaṁ piva jiṇindadhammaṁva suhajaṇayaṁ

aha tassa bārasāhē vōlīṇē niyayajaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ

garuyapamōēṇa kayaṁ vihiṇā nāmaṁ sudhammotti

dhaṇavāhaṇābhihāṇō bīō kālēṇa sē suō jāō

sōvi hu sudhammanāmō jāō aha aṭṭhavārisaō

tīē ya puravarīē viharantō annayā samōyariō

samaṇasayasēviyakamō sadaṁsaṇō nāma āyariō

appaḍibaddhavihārī caüdasa puvvī guṇāṇa āvāsō

puvvuttaradisibhāē avaṭṭhiō nandaṇujjāṇē

savvōpi nayaralōō viṇggiō sūrivandaṇanimittaṁ

dhaṇabhūīvi hu caliō bhattīē taṇayasañjuttō

ummukkavāhaṇō aha dūrāō vihiyaüttarāsaṅgō

tipayakkhiṇiūṇa guruṁ vandaï paramāē bhattīē

bhīmabhavōyahinivaḍantajantusantaraṇavarataraṇḍammi

dinnammi dhammalābhē guruṇā, sēsē muṇī namiuṁ

uvaviṭṭhō satthāhō mahivaṭṭhē purajaṇēṇa sañjuttō
