surīvi mōkkhamaggaṁ jiṇadhammaṁ kahiumāḍhattō

aviya sammaddaṁsaṇamūlō pañcamahavvayamahalladaḍhakhandhō

samiīguttītavasañjamāisāhāpasāhillō

vivihābhiggahagōcchō maṇaharasīlaṅgapattasōhillō

varaladdhikusumakaliō sagga 'pavaggāisuhaphalaō

cārittakapparukkhō vittharaō sāhiō jiṇāṇāē

duhatāvatāviyāṇaṁ jiyāṇa saraṇaṁ aṇannasamaṁ

cavalāiṁ indiyāiṁ dukkhanimittaṁ ca visayasaṅgōvi

kōhāiṇō kasāyā nibandhaṇaṁ dōggaïē u

ēkkasi kaō pamāō jīvaṁ pāḍēi bhavasamuddammi

bhīmō ya bhavō bahusō payāsiō tīē parisāē

sūrissa tassa vayaṇaṁ paramāmayasacchahaṁ nisāmittā

saṁviggā sā parisā jahāgayaṁ paḍigayā savvā

sōūṇa sudhammanāmō dhammamaī gurugiraṁ nisāmittā

saṁsārabhaüvviggō paṇamiya sūriṁ imaṁ bhaṇaï

icchāmi tumha mūlē niravajjaṁ giṇhiuṁ supavvajjaṁ

jaṇagēhiṁ aṇunnāō bhīō jarajammamaraṇāṇaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ guruṇā ya taō hōu avigdhaṁ tuhēttha vatthummi

ammāpiūhiṁ mukkō aha sō pavvāviō guruṇā

abbhasiyaduvihasikkhō sañjamatavaviṇayakaraṇaüjjuttō

vihiṇāgurupāmūlē ahijjiuṁ sō samāḍhattō

siggha mahāmaī sō jāō suttatthatadumabhayavihinnū

cuddasapuvvī gurusāhusammaō guṇagaṇāvāsō

nāūṇa jōgayaṁ sē suharikkhē sūriṇā niyapayammi

ahisittō sūrīvi ya saṁlihiyataṇū gaō mōkkhaṁ

samaṇagaṇasamparivuḍō suhammasūrīvi vivihadēsēsu

bōhintō bhaviyajaṇaṁ viharaï puragāmanagarēsu

dhaṇavāhaṇōvi kamasō vaḍḍhantō pañcadhāipariyariō

pattō kumarabhāvaṁ ahijjiō taha kalānivahaṁ

pattō ya jōvvaṇaṁ sō kāmiṇijaṇahiyayacōraṇasamatthaṁ

piuṇā ya tannimittaṁ variyā vararuvasampannā

sirisuppaïṭṭhanayarē dhūyā haridattapavaraïbbhassa

viṇayavaīsaṁmūyā 'ṇaṅgavaī nāma varakannā

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ pariṇīyā sōhaṇammi sā laggē

dhaṇavāhaṇēṇa tattō āṇīyā niyayanayarīē

aha sō tīē rattō jōvvaṇavararuvasōumallēsu

gāḍhaṁ visayāsattō gayaṁvi kālaṁ na yāṇāi

aha annayā sudhammō viharantō muṇivarō tahiṁ pattō

vijayavaīnayarīē vāsārattassa pārambhē

sāhūhiṁ tattha vasahī vimaggiyā tāhi satthavāhēṇa

dhaṇabhūiṇā vidinnā suvisuddhā jāṇasālāsu

niyapariyaṇēṇa sahiō satthāhō ēi gurusamīvammi

sāmāiyāijuttō saṁviggō suṇaï jiṇaghammaṁ

dhaṇavāhaṇō u daïyāsurayasuhāsattamāṇasō dhaṇiyaṁ

piuṇā bhaṇiōvi daḍhaṁ na ē (hō?)i guruvandaō kahavi

ahataṁ visayāsattaṁ gururāgaṁ dhammakaraṇaniravēkkhaṁ

paricattasēsakajjaṁ daṭṭhuṁ lahubhāyaraṁ guruṇō

jāyā ēsā cintā bhāyā mē rāgamōhiō varaō

jiṇavayaṇabāhiramaī indiyavisaēsu āsattō

dullahamavi maṇuyattaṁ pāvittā dhammavirahiō ēsō

gacchissaï narayammi ghōrāsu ya tiriyajōṇīsuṁ

kēṇāvi uvāēṇaṁ bōhēmi rāgamōhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ guruṇā saddāviō bhāyā

mahayā uvarōhēṇaṁ samāgaō vandiūṇa tō sūriṁ

uvaviṭṭhō sē puraō aha sūri bhaṇiumāḍhattō

pōggalapariyaṭṭēhiṁ bahūhiṁ sampāviūṇa maṇuyattaṁ

hārēsu mā muhāē visayāmisamōhiō bhadda!

visaēsu daḍhaṁ sattā sattā bandhanti asuhakammāiṁ

tavvasaō saṁsārē bhamanti ahamāsu jōṇīsu

vahabandhamāraṇāī nāṇāvihavēyaṇāō naraēsu

pāvinti visayagiddhā dūsahāō dīharaṁ kālaṁ

acchaü tā paralōē ihēva pāvinti guruyadukkhāiṁ

visayapasattā duddantaïndiyā dēhiṇō bahavē

mōttūṇa niyayajūhaṁ karēṇusuhasurayaphāsapaḍibaddhō

baddhō vārībandhē phāsēṇa gaō gaō nihaṇaṁ

rasaṇindiyammi luddhō viddhō galaēṇa macchaō nihaō

dhāṇindiyammi sattō pattō uragōvi maraṇaduhaṁ

ujjōiyasayaladisaṁ dīvasihaṁ pēcchiuṁ payaṅgōvi

taggahaṇaraō maraṇaṁ pattō naṇu cakkhudōsēṇa

gōrīsaddāsattō niccalataḍḍaviyakannajuyalillō

savaṇindiyadōsēṇaṁ miō maō vāhabāṇēṇa

ēkkikkindiyavasagā ēē savvēvi pāviyā nihaṇaṁ

pañcidiyavasagāṇaṁ narāṇa puṇa kā gaī hōjjā?

tā pañcidiyavasagō visayasuhaṁ sēviūṇa mā bhadda!

dhammōvajjaṇarahiō vaccasu ghōrammi narayammi

kijjaü dhammammi maī visayasuhaṁ ujjhiūṇa tā iṇhiṁ

sahalīkarēsu sundara! aïdulahaṁ maṇuyajammanti

ēyaṁ guruṇō vayaṇaṁ nisamma dhaṇavāhaṇō imaṁ bhaṇaï

icchāmi tumhavayaṇaṁ kiṁ puṇa nisuṇēha maha bhaṇiyaṁ

aïnēhaparā varaī khaṇamavi virahaṁ na sakkaē sọ̄dhuṁ

daïyā 'ṇaṅgavaī maha tēṇa na sakkēmi taṁ mōttuṁ

tubbhampi vandaṇatthaṁ āgamaṇaṁ tēṇa hōi na majjha

maha virahē sā varaī iṇhimpi hu acchaē kicchaṁ

tattō guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ cañcalacittāṇaṁ mahiliāṇa kaē

kō va sakannō purisō hārijjā appayaṁ bhad!

pavaṇuddhuyadhayacañcalacittāsuṁ mahiliāsu āsattō

jō dhammammi pamāyaï, sō kāurisō na sappapurisō

aviya antōvisabhariyāō maṇahararuvāō bajjhavittīē

guñjāphalasarisāō honti sabhāvēṇa mahilāō

saccadayasōyarahiyā akajjanirayāō sāhasadhaṇāō

bhayajaṇaṇīō, tāsuṁ kō va sakannō raïṁ kujjā?

rattāō haranti dhaṇaṁ pāṇēvi haranti taha virattāō

rāgēvi virāgēvi ya bhayaṅkarā duṭṭhajuvaīō

annaṁ cintēnti maṇē niyanti annaṁ dhaḍēnti annēṇa

calacittāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ kō nāma havijja vallahaō?

mārēnti paï jārassa kāraṇē tampi handi! annaṭṭhā

vīsāsanti ya annaṁ sabbhāvaṁ nēya payaḍēnti

kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ jāō ya haṇanti niyayaputtampi

kō nāma piō tāsiṁ havijja cavalāṇa mahilāṇa?

tā bhadda! ērisāṇaṁ taḍicchaḍāḍōvacavalahiyayāṇaṁ

mahilāṇa kaē kō iha havijja sịdhilāyarō dhammē?

iya gurubhaṇiyaṁ sōuṁ vihasiya dhaṇavāhaṇēṇa saṁlattaṁ

annāō juvaīō ēvaṁvihaduṭṭhacariyāō

maha mahilā puṇa saralā païvvayā saccasīladayajuttā

aṇurattā suviṇīyā thiranēhā gurujaṇē bhattā

sarisā sā kaha hōjjā asuddhacariyāṇa annamahilāṇa?

lōhaturaṅgāīṇaṁ dīsaï guru antaraṁ lōē

tattō guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ maṇōharā tujjha jaïvi sā mahilā

tahavi hu uvabhujjantā saraṇī sā narayanayarassa

jaha kimpāgaphalāiṁ bhuttāiṁ duhāvahāiṁ iha honti

taha itthīsurayasuhaṁ maṇaharamavi dōggaïṁ nēi

jaha visamīsaṁ sarasampi bhōyaṇaṁ jīviyaṁ haraï bhuttaṁ

taha sundarāvi ramaṇī ramiyā naṇu dōggaïṁ dēi

tā ujjhasu aṇurāyaṁ kugaïnimittāē niyayadaïyāē

pañcamahavvayajuttō hōsuṁ tumaṁ caraṇaniraütti

ēvaṁ divasē divasē saṁvēgakarēhiṁ mahuravayaṇēhiṁ

bōhijjantō maṇayaṁ jāō aha payaṇurāgō sō

annadiṇē ēgantē gurupuraō añjaliṁ karēūṇa

dhaṇavāhaṇō sa ēvaṁ vajjaraī paramasaṁviggō

tumhāṇamamayabhūē vayaṇē nisuēvi majjha hiyayāō

kiṁ nō sakkaï rāgō visaṁva duṭṭhassa sappassa?

bhayavaṁ! tāva na tuṭṭaï daïyāē uvari savvahā rāgō

navaraṁ karēmi ēkkaṁ jaï juttaṁ tumha paḍihāi

surayasuhanippivāsō dikkhaṁ giṇhāmi tumha pāmūlē

daïyāē samaṁ ahayaṁ daṁsaṇamittēṇa santuṭṭhō

ēvaṁ vavatthiyammi jaï jōggaṁ dēha majjha tō dikkhaṁ

tīē adaṁsaṇēṇaṁ sakkēmi na jīviyaṁ dhariuṁ

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇa ya sudhammasūri vicintaē ēvaṁ

pēcchaha aïdurantō rāgō kaha vilasaē lōē?

ēvampi tā dijjaü pavvajjā tāhi gahiyasuttatthō

sayamēva vivēgajuō ujjhissaï rāgasambandhaṁ

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ aṇaṅgavaïyāē sañjuō tāhē

dhaṇavāhaṇō sabhāyā guruṇā pavvāviō vihiṇā

candajasānāmāē mayahariyāē samappiyā sāvi

sāhuṇigaṇamajjhagayā sikkhaï varasāhuṇīkiriyaṁ

ēvaṁ ca tāṇa dōṇhavi parōpparaṁ jāva tuṭṭaï na rāgō

bahuṇāvi hu kālēṇaṁ suttattha visārayāṇampi

tāva ya guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ ēgantē bhāraīē mahurāē

ēyaṁ na juttamahuṇā uttamasattāṇa tumhāṇa

aviraïjuvaïjaṇēvi hu saviyārapalōyaṇammi sāhussa

pāyacchittaṁ garuyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ suttē jiṇindassa

jaṁ puṇa sāhuṇi visaē saviyārapalōyaṇaṁ tu sāhussa

taṁ bhadda! guruaṇatthassa kāraṇa vanniyaṁ samaē

iyaramahilājaṇēvi hu diṭṭhīpāō na hōi juttōti

kiṁ puṇa samaṇīvisaē abōhibīyassa mūlammi?

tā ujjhiya avivēyaṁ rāgaṁ avahatthiūṇa bhāvēṇa

pariharasu savvahacciya diṭṭhikusīlattaṇaṁ ēyaṁ

ēvaṁ guruṇā bhaṇiō saṁviggō sōvi cintaē ēvaṁ

aïrāgaparavasassa ō dhī!dhī! maha nivvivēyassa

jō haṁ paṇaṭṭhalajjō gayarāyapayammi vaṭṭamāṇōvi

sāhujaṇanindaṇijjaṁ rāgaṁ na caēmi chaḍḍēuṁ

laddhūṇavi niravajjaṁ pavvajjaṁ duṭṭharāgapaḍibaddhō

hōhāmi punnarahiō dīharasaṁsāraābhāgī

hī jīva! pāva! bhamihisi nārayatiriēsu dīharaṁ kālaṁ

avisayapayaṭṭarāgō laddhūṇavi dhammamaṇavajjaṁ

ēvaṁ bhāvēntassavi dhaṇavāhaṇasāhuṇō na uttaraï

aṇurāgō tavvisaē tāēvi ya tassa uvarimmi

ēvaṁ vaccaï kālō sañjamatavaviṇayakaraṇanirarayāṇaṁ

guruāṇāsampāḍaṇaparāṇa aha tāṇa dōṇhampi

aha annayā kayāivi bhagiṇīē vasumaīē sañjuttā

caliyā 'ṇaṅgavaī viyārabhūmiē bahiyāō

diṭṭhō ya tāhi ēgō mahilāsahiō narō u ummattō

dhūlirayadhūsaraṅgō jaracīvaracīriyāinnō

ugāyantō bahuhā naccantō ḍimbhasatthaparikinnō

taṁ duṭṭhumaṇaṅgavaī suiraṁ pulaēi taṁ juyalaṁ

tattō tīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhagiṇīē sulōyaṇāē aṇuharaï

ajjō! ēsā juvaī gahagahiyanarassa pāsatthā

bhaṇiyaṁ ca vasumaīē suiraṁ nijjhāiūṇa savisāyaṁ

sacciya ēsā amhaṁ bhagiṇī ō sulōyaṇā nāma

pariṇīyā āsi purā subandhuṇā mēhalāvaïpurīē

diṭṭhā kaṇagarahēṇaṁ kayāi aha rāyaüttēṇaṁ

antēurammi chụ̄dhā aïguruaṇurāyahariyahiyaēṇa

sayalōrōhapahāṇā jāyā aha tassa vallahiyā

ēyaṁ maha paccakkhaṁ savvampi hu sāsurē vasantīē

vittaṁ, tumaēvi suyaṁ ajjē! lōyappavāyāō

ēsō gahagahiyanarō dīsaï sarisō u rāyaüttassa

tā ēsō kaṇagarahō ēsāvi sulōyaṇā nūṇaṁ

bhaṇiyamaṇaṅgavaīē sambhāsēmō imaṁ tu niyabhagiṇiṁ

kiṁ amhē pariyāṇaï, ahavāvia bhambhalā ēsā

tattō gantuṁ dōhivi mahuraṁ ābhāsiyāvi sā jāhē

navi jāṇaï kiñci phuḍaṁ bōllaï ya bahuasambadhdhaṁ

tāhē dōvi jaṇāiṁ sudhammasūrissa pāyamūlammi

karuṇāparāhiṁ ajjāhiṁ tāhi nīyāiṁ savisāyaṁ

bhaṇiō ajjāhiṁ gurū ēsā amhāṇa jiṭṭhabhagiṇī ō

kiṁ hōi navā bhayavaṁ! jāyā ummattiyā kahavā?

bhaṇiyaṁ guruṇā tattō nāṇēṇa viyāṇiūṇa paramatthaṁ

sacciya sulōyaṇā sā kaṇagarahō ēsa juvarāyā

jōgō maïmōhakarō sīsē khittō imāṇa suttāṇa

ēkkāē savattīē īsāvasagāḍhakuddhāē

tassa vasēṇaṁ dōṇhavi maïsaṁmōhō imāṇaṁ sañjāō

rannā ya taō vijjā bahavē saddāviā tattha

na ya kēṇavi paüṇāiṁ kayāiṁ kālēṇa rakkhaganarāṇa

kahavi pamāyaparāṇaṁ nīhariyāiṁ imāiṁ tu

bhaṇiyaṁ ca vasumaīē bhayavaṁ! ēyāṇa mūḍhacittāṇaṁ

jaï pēcchaha uvayāraṁ, paḍijōgaṁ dēha cintēuṁ

tattō guruṇā tēsiṁ dinnō ummāyanāsaṇapaḍiṭṭhō

paḍijōgō, jāyāiṁ dōṇṇivi aha satthacittāiṁ

daṭṭhūṇa bhagiṇijuyalaṁ sulōyaṇā vimhiyā imaṁ bhaṇaï

kiṁ nāma imaṁ sumiṇaṁ kiṁvā maïvibbhamō ēsa?

sā kattha amha nayarī sā ya vibhūī ya tē alaṅkārā

kaha dhūlighūsarāiṁ iha mhi ( mhō? ) sampāviyāinti?

dōnnivi gahiyavayāō kattha va bhagiṇīō majjha ihaïṁ tu?

tā nūṇa indayālaṁ ēyaṁ ahavāvi sumiṇanti

tattō ya vasumaīē kahiyaṁ ummāyakāraṇaṁ savvaṁ

jāva ya gurumāhappā naṭṭhō tumhāṇa ummāō

jaïyā ya tumaṁ bhaddē! chụdhā antēurammi juvarannā

taïyacciya khayarēṇaṁ māyāi sumaṅgalēṇa ahaṁ

bhuttā pabhūyakālaṁ dhaṇavaïdēvēṇa bōhiyā tattō

jāyā candajasāē payamūlē suyaṇu! pavvaïyā

ēsāvi aṇaṅgavaī dhammaṁ sōūṇa bhavabhayuvviggā

niyabhattuṇā samēyā pavvaïyā ēttha gacchammi

tā suyaṇu! na suviṇamiṇaṁ saccaṁ ciya jaṁ imaṁ diṭṭhaṁ

ēsō sō amha guru sudhammanāmō mahāsattō

tattō dōvi jaṇāiṁ sudhammasūrissa paramaviṇaēṇaṁ

vandanti haririsāiṁ payakamalaṁ sayaladōsaharaṁ

tattō saṁvēyakariṁ guruṇō sōūṇa dēsaṇaṁ pavaraṁ

paḍibuddhāiṁ dōnnivi kamēṇa pavvāiyāinti

mayahariyāē pāsē bhagiṇījualēṇa sañjuyā tattō

sañjamaguruviṇayarayā sulōyaṇā kuṇaï vivihatavaṁ

ēvaṁ candajasāē payamūlē tāṇa acchamāṇāṇaṁ

tiṇhampi hu bhagiṇīṇaṁ vōlīṇā vāsarā bahavē

muṇiṇō kaṇagarahassa u dhaṇavāhaṇasāhuṇō ya sañjāō

bhō cittavēga! taïyā annōnnaṁ garuyanēhotti

pañcamahavvayajuttā samiīguttīsu sammamuvaüttā

nāṇāvihatavanirayā giṇhanti ya suttaatthāī

guruāṇāē nirayā dōnnivi pālēnti caraṇakaraṇāiṁ

ēvaṁ pabhūyakālō vōlīṇō tāva dōṇhampi

aha annayā kayāivi thōvaṁ niyaāuyaṁ muṇēūṇaṁ

sūrī saṁlihiyataṇū aṇasaṇavihiṇā maō sammaṁ

bīyammi dēvalōgē pavarē candajjuṇē vimāṇammi

jāō vimāṇasāmī dēvō u sasippabhō nāma

dhaṇavāhaṇōvi sāhū atuṭṭarāgō carittu sāmannaṁ

kālaṁ kāuṁ vihiṇā uppannō bīyakappammi

sāmāṇiyaṭhāṇammi dēvassa sasippahassa sō jāō

bhāsurasarīradhārī dēvō vijjuppahō nāma

sāvi hu aṇaṅgavaïyā avigayarāgā carittu sāmannaṁ

vijjuppahassa jāyā dēvī aha candarēhatti

sambhariya puvvavēraṁ bahūvasaggē karittu aïbhīmē

aggikumārasurēṇaṁ sumbandhujīvēṇa pāvēṇa

kaṇagarahō sō sāhū sulōyaṇāē samaṁ tu ajjāē

nihaō taṁ uvasaggaṁ visahantō sammabhāvēṇa

kālaṁ kāuṁ dōnnivi uvannāiṁ tu bīyakappammi

candajjuṇē vimāṇē sāmāṇiyadēvabhāvēṇa

kaṇagarahō ō vihuppahanāmō iyarā sayampabhā nāma

sāvi taïjjā bhagiṇī vasumaïyā āuyakhayammi

puvvadaïyassa jāyā candajjuṇanāmagassa dēvassa

tatthēva kila vimāṇē dēvī candappabhā nāma

ēvaṁ ēgavimāṇē divvasuhaṁ tāṇa aṇuhavantāṇaṁ

savvēsiṁ annōnnaṁ aïgaruyā āsi pīīō

paliōvamāṇi aṭṭha u divvasuhaṁ tattha aṇuhavēūṇaṁ

dēvō vijjuppahō sō caïūṇa imammi vēyaḍ̣dhē

dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīi purē ramaṇīē rayaṇasañcaē pavarē

pavaṇagaïkhayaraputtō uppannō baülavaïyāē

ēvaṁ ci ṭhiē jō dhaṇavāhaṇajīvō dēvō vijjuppahō ya diyalōē

sō ya tumaṁ iha sundara! uppannō cittavēgotti

dēvīvi candarēhā tattō āukkhaē cuyā santī

uppannā vēyaḍ̣dhē nayarē sirikuñjarāvattē

khayarassa amiyagaïṇō piyāē bhajjāē cittamālāē

kucchīē sambhūyā piyadhūyā kaṇagamālatti

bhō cittavēga! puvviṁ tubbhaṁ jō āsi rāgasambandhō

sāmannamuvagayāṇavi tassa phalaṁ ērisaṁ jāyaṁ

ruvaṁ balaṁ ca dittī riddhīvi ya āsi thēviyā tumha

dēvabhavē tuha āuṁ vimajjhimaṁ thavēyaṁ āsi

ētthavi māṇussa-bhavē avarōppara-daṁsaṇāō ārabbha

dusahaṁ viōya-dukkhaṁ sañjāyaṁ tumha dōṇhampi

tumaēcciya aṇubhūyaṁ viōyadukkhaṁ sudūsahaṁ jamiha

bhō cittavēga! kiṁvā kahiēṇaṁ tēṇa tuha puraō?

kāūṇavi sāmannaṁ sarāgabhāvō tumē na jaṁ cattō

tassa phalēṇaṁ ēsā dūsahā tuha āvayā jāyā

dēvabhavē tuha mittō candajjuṇanāmagō ya jō āsi

caïūṇa sōvi tattō cittagaī ēttha sañjāō

vasumaïnāmā ajjā dēvī candappahā ya diyalōē

sāvi ya piyaṅgumañjarināmā iha bhadra! uppannā

jaṁ puvvasaṅgaō sō cittagaī tēṇa tumha sañjāō

annōnnaṁ gurunēhō sundara! saïdaṁsaṇēṇampi

tēṇaṁ uvāyapuvvaṁ ghaḍiyā sā tujjha kaṇagamālāō

iṇhiṁ sakammvasaō jāō tuha tīi saha virahō

bhō cittavēga! bahuṇā kiṁvā bhaṇiēṇa ēttha annēṇa?

jaṁ cēva āsi puṭṭhaṁ taṁ ciya tuha tāva sāhēmi

kaṇagarahō sō sāhū aïppiō āsi tujjha annabhavē

tattō ya dēvalōē vihuppahō nāma jō dēvō

sō ya ahaṁ tuha vallahamittō ajjavi tattha vasāmi divammi

kāraṇamitthamimaṁ tu paḍucca mē aïsaṅgayaō si tumanti

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsō ēttha samappaï cirapariciyavannaṇotti nāmēṇa

surasundarikahāē aṭṭhamaō varaparicchēō

aha bhaṇaï cittavēgō suravara! maha kahasu kēṇa kajjēṇa

taïyā maṇiṁ samappiya kattha gaō āsi turiyagaī?

tō bhaṇaï surō sundara! nisuṇasu ēyampi vajjarijjantaṁ

ajja ahaṁ āṇattō sasippahēṇaṁ tu dēvēṇa

gaccha vihuppaha! khippaṁ jambūdvīvammi bharahakhēttammi

nayarē kusagganāmē dhaṇavāhaṇamuṇivarasamīvē

sō puvvavēriēṇaṁ diṭṭhō jhāṇammi saṇṭhiō tattha

taṁ daṭṭhu kuviō sō kāhī aïgaruyaüvasaggaṁ

tā tassa rakkhaṇaṭṭhā sigdhaṁ vaccāhi tammi nayarammi

ahamavi indāṇattiṁ samāṇiuṁ āgamissāmi

tattō tahatti bhaṇiuṁ vēgēṇa samāgaō ahaṁ ihaïṁ

tāvaya daïyāsahiō palāyamāṇō tumaṁ diṭiṭhō

ōhināṇēṇa maē nāyaṁ jaha ēsa sō hi vijjupahō

maha mittō nahavāhaṇabhayāurō vaccaē turiyaṁ

nahavāhaṇōvi ēsō paṭiṭhavilaggō imassa ēitti

tāhē karēmi kiñcivi uvagāraṁ puvvamittassa

ēvaṁ vicintiūṇaṁ tumha samīvammi āgaō ahayaṁ

taïyā ya maṇī divvō samappiō jīvarakkhaṭṭhā

tattō ya gaō turiyaṁ ghaṇavāhaṇamuṇivarassa pāsammi

diṭṭhō ya maē dēvō uvasaggaṁ tassa kuṇamāṇō

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē rē! rē! tiyasāhama! kattha vaccasē iṇhiṁ

dēvidavandiyāṇaṁ muṇīṇa ēvaṁ karēmāṇō?

uppāyantō pīḍaṁ muṇīṇa samasattumittavaggāṇaṁ

pāviṭṭha! kattha vaccasi diṭṭhīmaggammi maha paḍiō?

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiē bhavaṇavaī sō surō sasambhantō

naṭṭhō sahasā tāva ya sukkajjhāṇē paviṭṭhassa

muṇiṇō mōhāvagamā uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ varaṁ nāṇaṁ

kēvalimahimā vihiyā taō maē paramaviṇaēṇaṁ

sōuṁ dunduhisaddaṁ dēvā maṇuyā ya āgayā bahavē

kahiō tēsiṁ dhammō kēvaliṇā mōkkhasuhahēū

patthāvaṁ lahiūṇaṁ puṭṭhō sō kēvalī maē ēvaṁ

bhayavaṁ! kiṁ avaraddhaṁ imassa dēvassa tumhēhiṁ

jēṇēsō pāvamaī jīviyavavarōvaṇammi ujjuttō?

tō bhaṇaï muṇī nisuṇasu jaha vēraṁ āsi anna bhavē

dhāyaïsaṇḍavidēhē campānāmēṇa āsi varanayarī

tīē paümō rāyā juvarāyā samarakēutti

jiṇavayaṇabhāviyappā sahōyarā dōvi nēhasañjuttā

pālēnti dēsaviraïṁ rajjadhuraṁ taha ya nīīē

atthāṇamuvagayāṇaṁ nāhiyavāī samāgaō kavilō

vajjaraï natthi jīvō na ya savvannū na nēvvāṇaṁ

jiṇamayasatthatthaviyāṇaēṇa juvarāiṇā jiō vāē

diṭṭhantahēukāraṇanāṇāvihajuttinivahēṇa

juvarannō paḍivayaṇaṁ jāhē na caēi kimpi sō dāuṁ

tāhē mantimahattamasāmantāīhiṁ uvahasiō

jāō ya vilakkhō sō daḍhaṁ paüṭṭhō ya samarakēussa

kaha ṇu mahāyaṇamajjhē ēēṇaṁ dharisiō ahayaṁ?

ēvaṁ vicintayantō aïgururōsēṇa dhamadhamantō sō

atthāṇamaṇḍavāō nīhariō cintaē ēvaṁ

na ya kēṇaï puvvamahaṁ parāiō vāiṇā ihaṁ lōē

pāvēṇa imēṇa puṇō sabhāē majjhammi kaha vijiō?

tā rayaṇīē bhavaṇē imassa gantūṇa gahiyakaravālō

chindāmi uttimaṅgaṁ jēṇa maṇaṁ nivvuiṁ lahaï

rōddajjhāṇōvagaō ēvaṁ sō cintiūṇa rayaṇīē

gahiyāuhō paviṭṭhō vāsaharē samarakēussa

vaccōharabhitīē pacchannō acchaē palīṇō sō

kāūṇa gōsakiccaṁ samāgaō tattha juvarāyā

dīvayavaggakarēhiṁ narēhiṁ ujjhōiēṇa maggēṇaṁ

vaccōharagamaṇicchā aha jāyā rāyaüttasya

purisēhiṁ tattha diṭṭhō vaccōharasaṇṭhiō sa duṭṭhamaī

āyaḍḍhantō khaggaṁ gahiō baddhō ya sahasatti

juvarannā nāō sō nāhiyavāī sa ēsa kavilotti

nūṇaṁ vāyammi jiō majjha vahaṭṭhā iha paviṭṭhō

daṭhṭhūṇa dīṇavayaṇaṁ vēvantasarīrayaṁ tayaṁ kavilaṁ

paricattajīviyāsaṁ jāyā karuṇā kumārassa

bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa taō jīvantō tāva iṇhi mukkō si

mōttūṇa majjha dēsaṁ ṭhāēyavvaṁ tumē pāva!

iya bhaṇiō sō naṭṭhō gantūṇaṁ tāhi dūradēsammi

bhillajaṇāinnāē avaṭṭhiōbhillapallīē

aha annayā ya paümō puttaṁ ahisiñciūṇa rajjammi

juvarāiṇā samēō pavvaïō gurusamīvammi

dōnnivi guruṇā sahiyā viharantā bahuvihēsu dēsēsu

satthēṇa samaṁ caliyā rayaṇapuraṁ nāma varanayaraṁ

satthāō kahavi bhaṭṭhā dōnnivi aḍavīē mōhiyā muṇiṇō

sampattā pallīē pāṇayaaṭṭhā paviṭṭhā tē

diṭṭhā ya pariyaḍantā kavilēṇaṁ kahavi paccabhinnāyā

kuddhō ya daḍhaṁ ēsō daṭṭhūṇa muṇiṁ samarakēuṁ

cintēi tāhē kavilō imēṇa vāēvi nijjiō ahayaṁ

nivvisaō āṇattō taïyā ya imēṇa pāvēṇa

tā kavaḍēṇaṁ kēṇavi vaïrassantaṁ karēmi iṇhimpi

iya cintiūṇa vandaï tē muṇiṇō paramaviṇaēṇa

nīyā ya nijē gēhē visamīsaṁ bhattapāṇayaṁ dinnaṁ

bhaṇiyā ya viṇayapuvvaṁ bhayavaṁ! ētthēva bhuñjēha

addhāṇagamaṇakhinnā nivviyaṇē ēttha ēgadēsammi

bhuñjiya vīsamiuṁ tō pabhāyakālē vaējjāha

ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā tēṇaṁ suhabhāvā vīsamittu khaṇamēgaṁ

sajjhāyaṁ kāūṇaṁ pāraddhā bhōyaṇaṁ kāūṁ

saṁnihiyadēvayāē muṇiaṇukampāē tayaṁ visaṁ hariyaṁ

bhōttūṇa taō dōnnivi sajjhāyaṁ kāumāraddhā

cintēi taō kavilō hanta visēṇaṁ na kiṁ mayā ēē

nūṇaṁ mantabalēṇaṁ avahariyā hōjja visasattī

tā rayaṇīi avassaṁ mārēyavvō maē imō muṇḍō

jīvantammi imammi natthi mamaṁ jēṇa santōsō

pattāē rayaṇīē sajjhāyaṁ kaṭṭu sāhuṇō suttā

kavilōvi addharattē samāgaō sāhuvahaṇaṭṭhā

āyaḍ̣dhiūṇaṁ khaggaṁ jāva pahāraṁ karēi sāhussa

ruṭṭhāē dēvayāē pahaō sō tēṇa khaggēṇa

rōddajjhāṇōvagaō mariūṇa gaō biijjapuḍhavīē

muṇiṇōvi niraïyāraṁ sāmannaṁ kāuṁ bahukālaṁ

kālaṁ kāuṁ vihiṇā dōnnivi sōhammanāmakappammi

uppannā suhappunnā accharagaṇasaṅkulavimāṇē

tattō ya paümajīvō sāgaramēgaṁ tu āuyaṁ tattha

aṇuhaviūṇiha dīvē ēravaē vijayanayarīē

dhaṇabhūināmagassa ō jāō taṇaō sudhammanāmotti

kāūṇa ya sāmannaṁ uppannō bīyakappammi

candajjuṇē vimāṇē sasippahō nāma sō surō jāō

dō cēva sāgarāiṁ sampunnaṁ āuyaṁ tassa

bhadda! vihuppaha! sampaï vimāṇasāmī u sō surō tumha

jassāēsēṇa tumaṁ samāgaō maha samīvammi

sō samarakēujīvō sāgaramēgaṁ tu aṭṭhapaliēhiṁ

abbhahiyaṁ aṇubhaviuṁ dēvabhavē aha cuō tattō

ētthēva bharahakhēttē kusagganayarammi bhaddakittissa

rannō piyamahilāē subandhudattāē kucchīē

uppannō sō dēvō jāō ya kamēṇa dāraō tattō

ghaṇavāhaṇotti nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ sē uciyasamayammi

vaḍḍhantō ya kamēṇaṁ pattō aha jōvvaṇaṁ jaṇāṇandaṁ

ahisiñciya taṁ rajjē jāō samaṇō piyā tassa

sōvi bahupuvvalakkhē rajjaṁ parivāliūṇa sambuddhō

naravāhaṇaṁ tu puttaṁ rajjē ṭhaviūṇa pavvaïō

bhadda! vihuppaha! sō haṁ viharantō ajja iha purē pattō

aha ēgarāiyāē ṭhiō ya paḍimāē aha ēttha

sōvi hu kavilō naraē aṇuhaviuṁ dāruṇaṁ mahaṁ dukkhaṁ

sāgaramēgaṁ ahiyaṁ āuṁ bhōttūṇa uvvaṭṭō

jāō magahāvisaē ābhīrō sābhaḍotti nāmēṇa

kāūṇa ya bālatavaṁ bhavaṇavaī sō surō jāō

paramāhammiyadēvō uvaruddō nāma sō tahiṁ jāō

daṭṭhūṇa mamaṁ ihaïṁ samāgaō āsuruttotti

sumarantō taṁ vaïraṁ samāgaō tēṇa maha vahaṭhṭhāē

ēyaṁ vaïranimittaṁ samāsaō tuha maē siṭṭhaṁ

bhō cittavēga! tattō puṇaravi sō kēvalī maē puṭṭhō

bhayavaṁ! kēttiyamāuṁ katthaṁ va maha hōjja uppattī?

kō va piyā maha hōhī bōhissaï kō jiṇindadhammammi?

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiṁō bhayavaṁ! sō bhaṇiuṁmāḍhattō

ciṭṭhaï āugasēsaṁ ēgavīsaṁ vāsakōḍikōḍīō

tattō caïūṇa tumaṁ āukkhaē hatthiṇapurammi

siriamarakēurannō dēvīkamalāvaīē kucchimmi

bahuuvayāiyaladdhō uvavajjisi puttabhāvēṇa

jaṇaṇīi samaṁ tattha ya avahariō puvvavēriyasurēṇa

bhō cittavēga! khayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi

ēntēṇa maha samīvē divvamaṇī jassa ̣dhōiō tumaē

so cciya paramatthapiyā bhavissaï tammi jammammi

pāsammi suppaïṭṭhassa sūriṇō pāviūṇa gihidhammaṁ

aha laddhuṁ samaṇattaṁ kāhisi saṁsāravōcchēyaṁ

iya kēvaliṇā bhaṇiē tahatti bahu manniūṇa tavvayaṇaṁ

ti payakkhiṇiūṇa puṇō 'bhivandiō sō maē bhayavaṁ

tattō uppaïūṇaṁ samāgaō ēttha tuha samīvammi

jaṁ taṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ ēyaṁ

bhō cittavēga! sampaï kāyavvaṁ jaṁ maē tamāisasu

tō bhaṇaï cittavēgō suravara! nisuṇēsu maha vayaṇaṁ

nahavāhaṇēṇa nīyā jā sā maha bhāriyā sudukkhattā

tayavatthaṁ maṁ daṭṭhuṁ vilavantī kaluṇasaddēṇa

bhuyagōhavẹ̄dhiyassavi na tārisaṁ āsi majjha maṇadukkhaṁ

jaha tīē kaluṇarōvaṇavilāvasaddaṁ suṇantassa

sā kaha ciṭṭhaï sampaï na navatti majjha sāhēsu?

ōhinnāṇēṇa tumaṁ jāṇasi paccakkhamiva savvaṁ

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō dēvō vajjaraï bhadda! nisuṇēsu

sā tuha bhajjā nīyā gaṅgāvattammi ruyamāṇī

nahavāhaṇēṇa tattō chụ̄dhā antēurammi niyayammi

gurusōyapīḍiyāē kila ēvaṁ cintayantīē

sō maha daïō tāvaya bhīsaṇabhuyagēhiṁ gahiyasavvaṅgō

guruvēyaṇāē mannē hōhī pāṇēṇa paricattō

aha kahamavi jaï jīvaï tahavi hu maha tēṇa natthisañjōgō

vijjābalaahiēṇaṁ pāvēṇa imēṇa hariyāē

tā sampaï maha juttaṁ mariuṁ gurusōyadukkhataviyāē

suviṇēvi nēva annō purisō maha laggaē aṅgē

iya mantiūṇa tīē aïuggavisaṁ tu bhakkhiyaṁ sahasā

bhañjiya lōyaṇajuyalaṁ mahīyalē nivaḍiyā tattō

tadavatthaṁ taṁ daṭṭhuṁ hāhāsaddō samuṭṭhiō tattha

taṁ sōuṁ nahavāhaṇakhayarōvi samāgaō tattha

nāūṇa visaviyāraṁ mantē tantē paüñjaī vivihē

visanimmahaṇē maṇiṇō ābandhaī tīē aṅgammi

na ya tīē kōvi guṇō jāō visaghāriyāē bālāē

āhūyā aha bahavē visamantaviyāṇayā khayarā

savvāyaralaggēhivi tēhivi paüṇā na sakkiyā kāuṁ

tāhē mayatti kāuṁ mayakiccaṁ tīē kāūṇa

nīyā pēyavaṇammī nahavāhaṇapariyaṇēṇa sā bālā

cīyāē pakkhiviuṁ tattō uddīviō jalaṇō

ēttiyamēttaṁ sāhaï sō dēvō jāva cittavēgassa

dhaṇadēva! tāva nisuṇasu jaṁ saṁvittaṁ tahiṁ taïyā

sōuṁ daïyāmaraṇaṁ dūsahagurudukkhadaliyasavvaṅgō

vajjāsaṇibhinnō iva uggabhuyaṅgēṇa gasiuvva

gahiuvva rakkhasēṇaṁ pahaō iva mōggarēṇa garuēṇa

nīsasiya dīhadīhaṁ gurusōyāuriō khayarō

mucchānimīliyacchō dhasatti dharaṇīyalammi sō paḍiō

ninnaṭṭhasayalacēṭṭhō sañjāō vigayajīuvva

daṭhṭhūṇa cittavēgaṁ tadavatthaṁ tāhē tēṇa dēvēṇa

sīyalajalamāṇēttā sittō sō savvaaṅgēsu

vihiō ya maē pavaṇō sukōmalō niyayaüttarīēṇa

tattō khaṇantarāō laddhūṇavi cēyaṇaṁ kahavi

puṇaruttaṁ mucchijjaï aïguruaṇurāyamōhiō khayarō

aïvallahamahilāē maraṇaṁ sariūṇa dukkhattō

kahakahavi samāsatthō vihiō gurusōyapīḍiō tahavi

thūlaṁsuē muyantō ahōmuhō ciṭṭhaī jāva

tāva ya surēṇa bhaṇiō mahilāmēttasya kāraṇē kīsa

āyasijjaï appā ēvaṁvihasōyakaraṇēṇaṁ?

vibuhajaṇanindaṇijjaṁ asamañjasacēṭṭhiyaṁ pamōttūṇa

vatthusarūvaṁ sundara! bhāvēyavvaṁ payattēṇa

saṁsārammi aṇantē paribbhamantāṇa honti jīvāṇa

saṁyōgavippaōgā iṭṭhāṇiṭṭhēhiṁ sayahuttaṁ

nahu harisō sañjōgē nēvaṁ visāōvi iṭṭhavirahammi

kāyavvō buddhimayā saṁsārarūvayaṁ nāuṁ

kiñca puvvabhavē jō tumaē aṇurāgō nēva ujjhiō taïyā

samaṇattaṇēvi pattē tasya pabhāvāu saggēvi

riddhibalatēyahīṇō āsi tumaṁ taha ya ēttha jammammi

ēvaṁ viōyadukkhaṁ pattaṁ takkammadōsēṇa

tahavi hu ajjavi rāgaṁ tīē uvariṁ na muñcasē kīsa?

ēvaṁvihadukkhāṇaṁ ēso cciya kāraṇaṁ paramaṁ

aha bhaṇaï cittavēgō suravara! maha phuraï dāhiṇaṁ nayaṇaṁ

pahasiyamuhō ya dīsasi tumanti tā kahasu paramarttha

kiṁ jīvaï sā bālā saccaṁ ciya ahava sā mayā varaī?

jaï tāva tumaṁ mittō āsi mahaṁ annajammammi

daṁsijjaü sā sigghaṁ aha navi tā majjha jīviyaṁ natthi

lajjāmi bahu bhaṇantō ēsō ciya nicchaō majjha

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō dēvō vajjaraï bhadda! jaï ēvaṁ

tā piṭṭhaō nirūvasu jēṇa tayaṁ pēcchasē daïyaṁ

ēvaṁ surēṇa bhaṇiō valiyaggīvaṁ nirūvaī jāva

tāva ya vihūsiyaṅgī pēcchaï niyabhāriyaṁ sahasā

taṁ daṭṭhu cittavēgō sasaṅkiō niyamaṇammi vajjaraï

suravara! sāhasu saccaṁ hāsaṁ mōttūṇa maha iṇhiṁ

kiṁvā sacciya ēsā nahavāhaṇaavahiyā mahaṁ daïyā

maha āsāsaṇahēuṁ suramāyā aha tumē vihiyā?

jaï tāva visaṁ bhakkhiya maha virahē sā mayā sudukkhattā

tā kaha iha jīvantī sampattā akkhayasarīrī?

tattō ya bhaṇaï dēvō sacciya ēsā, na hōi suramāyā

avahariya sā maē ihāṇiyā tahaya nisuṇēsu

kēvalimahimaṁ kāuṁ āgacchantēṇa tuha samīvammi

ōhinnāṇēṇa maē diṭṭhā tuha bhāriyā ēsā

kayamaraṇajjhavasāṇā tattō ya maē vicintiyaṁ ēyaṁ

gahiūṇa imaṁ pacchā gacchissaṁ mittapāsammi

iya cintiya pattō haṁ gaṅgāvattammi tammi nayarammi

visavēyavihuriyaṅgī diṭṭhā ya maē imā tattha

hantūṇa mantasattiṁ savvēsiṁ thambhiyaṁ maē u visaṁ

tattō mayatti kaliuṁ mayakiccaṁ tīē kāūṇaṁ

nīyā pēyavaṇammī nahavāhaṇapariyaṇēṇa sā bālā

cīyāē pakkhiviuṁ jāhē ujjāliō jalaṇō

tāhē avahariya visaṁ dhēttūṇa imaṁ samāgaō ihaï

tujjha samīvē tāva ya ēsa vigappō mahaṁ jāō

sōuṁ imīi maraṇaṁ kiṁ mannē ēsa kuṇaï maha mittō

kiṁ daḍharāgō ajjavi ahavāvi hu payaṇurāgotti

iya cintiūṇa ēsā addissā suyaṇu! tuha maē vihiyā

nāūṇa nicchayaṁ tē iṇhiṁ puṇa payaḍiyā bhadda!

tā mā kuṇa āsaṅkaṁ sacciya ēsā u kaṇagamālatti

iya bhaṇiē sō khayarō pahasiyavayaṇō daḍhaṁ jāō

aha paṇamiya taṁ dēvaṁ kayañjalī bhaṇaï cittavēgō sō

aïnēhō dakkhinnaṁ ahō ṇu tē mittavacchallaṁ

paraüvayārarayā iha mahānubhāvā bhavanti payaīē

aṇuvakayāvi parēṇaṁ vaṭṭanti sayāvi uvayārē

tumaē dinnaṁ jīyaṁ maṇasantāvō tumē ya nivvaviō

aṇahasarīsā ēsā tumaē majjha uvaṇīyā

āulamaṇassa puvviṁ tumaē jaṁ kiñci majjha uvaïṭṭhaṁ

savvaṁ bhariyaghaḍassava taṁ maha pāsēṇa bōlīṇaṁ

tujjha pabhāvā suravara! jāō haṁ satthamāṇasō iṇhiṁ

kāyavvaṁ jaṁ kiñcivi sampaï āisasu taṁ savvaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa taō havaï hu dēvāṇa daṁsaṇamamōhaṁ

tō bhaṇasu bhadda! kiñciṁvi jēṇa tayaṁ tuha payacchāmi

tō bhaṇaï cittavēgō jaï ēvaṁ dēsu majjha taṁ kiñci

nahavāhaṇakhayarō jaha na sakkaē maṁ parābhaviuṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa taō mahilāsahiyassa pahariō jaṁ sō

vijjāharakayamēraṁ viṁladhiuṁ dappavāmụ̄dhō

tēṇēva kāraṇēṇaṁ vijjācchēō imassa sañjāō

tā sampaï asamatthō bhadda! tumaṁ sō parābhaviṁu

annaṁ ca

kila puvvavēriēṇaṁ avahariō jāyagaruyarōsēṇa

tō cittavēga! khayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi

iya taïyā kēvaliṇā bhāvibhavaṁ majjha sāhayantēṇa

āiṭṭhaṁ tā tumaē hōyavvaṁ khayaranāhēṇa

vēyaḍḍhadakkhiṇāē sẹ̄dhīē sayalakhayaranāhāṇaṁ

sāmiṁ karēmi sampaï tumanti, kiṁ ēttha annēṇa?

majjha pabhāvāō tuha savvāō cēva khayaravijjāō

hōhinti pạdhiyasiddhā ahiyāō annakhayarēhiṁ

paravijjāṇaṁ chēyaṁ mantāṇa ōsahīṇa ahalattaṁ

kāhisi icchāē tumaṁ khayarāṇaṁ vayaṇamattēṇaṁ

aïdappiyāvi khayarā āṇāniddēsakāriṇō savvē

hōhinti viṇayapaṇayā majjha pabhāvāō tuha bhadda!

tā iṇhiṁ gantūṇaṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē siddhakūḍasiharammi

sāsayajiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ mahimaṁ aṭṭhāhiaṁ kāuṁ

abbhatthiya dharaṇinda savvāō tujjha khayaravijjhāō

dāuṇa jahāvihiṇā gacchissaṁ tāhi saṭṭhāṇaṁ

ēvaṁ surēṇa bhaṇiō payajuyalaṁ paṇamiūṇa sē khayarō

suravara! mahāpasāō ēvaṁ hōutti vajjaraï

bahumāṇajuyaṁ tattō ābhāsittā mamaṁ tu sō khayarō

dhaṇadēva! maha samappiya maṇimēyaṁ gurupamōēṇa

dēvēṇa tēṇa sahiō saha mahilāē nahammi uppaïō

ahayampi taō tattō samāgaō niyayaṭhāṇammi

tā bhō dhaṇadēva! maē ēēṇa kamēṇa pāviō ēsa

bahupunnapāvaṇijjō maṇī maṇāṇandasañjaṇaṇō

diyalōyasamuppannō pavarō ēsō maṇī mahābhāga!

nissēsadōsasamaṇō visēsaō visasamūhassa

tā dhaṇadēva! mahāyasa! gēṇhasu ēyaṁ tumaṁ maṇiṁ divvaṁ

sayalaguṇēganihāṇaṁ maha aṇurōhēṇa, kiṁ bahuṇā

ēyaṁ nisamma vayaṇaṁ kusalō bhaṇiīsu bhaṇaï dhaṇadēvō

bhō rāyasuya! jamēyaṁ tumaē saha daṁsaṇaṁ majjha

jaṁ ca imaṁ accataṁ vayaṇaṁ sabbhāvagabbhiṇaṁ bhadda!

taṁ cēva majjha maṇisayasahassalakkhāṇa abbhahiyaṁ

aha bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō nisamma dhaṇadēvabhāsiyaṁ vayaṇaṁ

atthi ya ēyaṁ dhaṇadēva! kintu ahayampi ēyammi

gahiē divvamaṇimmī tumaē mannē kayatthamappāṇaṁ

tā bhō maha dhiihēuṁ kijjaü maṇigahaṇamaviyappaṁ

nāuṁ aïnibandhaṁ gahiō viṇiēṇa sō maṇī pavarō

aha bhaṇaï suppaïṭṭhō puṇaravi dhaṇadēvamāsajja

gantūṇa kusaggapurē niyattamāṇēṇa niyapurābhimuhaṁ

āgantavvaṁ ihaïṁ amhāṇa aṇuggahaṭṭhāē

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ hōu avigdhēṇa tāva samaō sō

jaṁ ēsō ciya maggō niyattamāṇāṇamamhāṇa

ēvaṁ kayasambhāsō rayaṇiṁ gamiūṇa tassa gēhammi

pattē pabhāyasamaē saṁvụ̄dhē sayalasatthammi

tavvēlasamuciyaṁ sō kāyavvaṁ kāuṁ niggaō tattō

niyapariyaṇasahiēṇaṁ pallīvaïṇā 'ṇugammantō

kahakahavi niyattēuṁ sasōyavayaṇaṁ tu pallīnāṁhaṁ taṁ

satthēṇa samaṁ caliō dhaṇadēvō vēsarārụ̄dhō

kālēṇa ya sampattō kusagganayarammi vaṇiyasañjuttō

ghēttuṁ mahagdhamullaṁ darisaṇayaṁ naravaïsamīvē

sampattō naravāhaṇarannā bahu manniō taō tēṇa

suṅkavaï sayalabhaṇḍaṁ pañcaülaṁ sakkhiṇaṁ kāuṁ

sāgarasēṭṭhissa taō bhavaṇēsu bhāḍaēṇa gahiēsu

uttāriyaṁ tu bhaṇḍaṁ savvampi niuttapurisēhiṁ

uttaraï ya païdiyahaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ taha ghēppaē ya paḍibhaṇḍaṁ

ēvaṁ ca kaïvi māsā vōlīṇā tattha nayarammi

sāgarasēṭṭhisuēṇaṁ siridattēṇa samaṁ tu ēyassa

sañjāyā gurupīī sambavahāraṁ karēntassa

aha annayā ya nīō niyayagihē bhōyaṇassa kajjēṇa

mahayā uvarōhēṇaṁ siridattēṇaṁ tu dhaṇadēvō

tattha ya gaēṇa diṭṭhā sirikantā pavararūvasampannā

bhagiṇī siridattassa u kannā navajōvvaṇārambhā

sā tāliyaṇṭahatthā vīēntī bhōyaṇaṁ karēntēṇa

saccaviyā paccaṅgaṁ abbhuvavannō taō ēsō

tīēva sasiṇēhaṁ avaṅgadiṭṭhīē pulaïō ēsō

aha cintaï dhaṇadēvō tīē rūvēṇa akkhittō

jaï tāva imā kannā, dēnti ya jaï mē vimaggiyā ēē

tā hōjja maha kayatthō daïyāē imāē maṇuyabhavō

kaha hōjja majjha ēsā maggāmi sayampi ahava annēṇa

jaï dāhinti na majjhaṁ vimaggiyā, hōjja lahuyattaṁ

ahavā samāṇajāī dhaṇavantō vasaṇavajjiō taha ya

ēsāvi jōvvaṇatthā tamhā dāhinti maha ēē

ēvaṁ vicintayantō kāūṇaṁ bhōyaṇaṁ tu dhaṇadēvō

siridattēṇa viinnē tambōlavilēvaṇāimmi

gēhāō nīhariō gantūṇaṁ niyayavāsaṭhāṇammi

sirikantāhayahiyaō pāsuttō pavarasayaṇīē

ēttō ya mayaṇavasagā sirikantā raṇaraṇēṇa abhibhūyā

gantūṇa gihujjāṇē pāsuttā kayaligēhammi

tatthayavakkhittamaṇā kasiṇabhuyaṅgēṇa bāhumūlammi

daṭṭhā dṭhṭhūṇa ahiṁ aīvabhayavēvirasarīrā

āgamma māumūlē ruyamāṇī bhaṇaï vēyaṇaparaṭṭhā

ammō! khaddhā khaddhā ahayaṁ gurukasiṇasappēṇa

pēlavasattattaṇaō ukkaḍayāē ya visaviyārassa

vēyaṇāē pabhūyattā sabhayattā itthibhāvassa

mīliyalōyalajuyalaṁ nīsāhārā dhasatti dharaṇīē

vihalandhalā nivaḍiyā jaṇaṇīē pēcchamāṇīē

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ sirimaïṇā sāgarasēṭṭhī tahēva siridattō

taha sayalapariyaṇō sō sahasati samāulībhūō

tāhē bahugāruḍiyā hakkārijjanti mantatantaviū

kīranti mantajāvā taha vaṭṭijjantī mūlīō

dhārēnti dhāraṇāō kēvi hu kannammi dinti sē jāvaṁ

kaluṇaṁ vilavaï jaṇaṇī sandhīraï sē piyā ēvaṁ

sundari! mā kuṇa sōyaṁ ēyaṁ nēmittiyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ

sampaï payaḍīhōhī daïē! jāmāuō tujjha

avisaṁvāī jaṁ sō sumaī nēmittiō tahā suyaṇu!

kamalāvaīē savvaṁ nivvaḍiyaṁ tēṇa āiṭṭhaṁ

ēvaṁ ca vaṭṭamāṇē jāhē na caïnti tattha gāruḍiyā

savvāyaralaggāvi hu visaviyaṇaṁ sē niyattēuṁ

tattō tīē visannō savvōvi hu pariyaṇō piyā bhāyā

cintēnti ya kiṁ hōhī aliyaṁ nēmittiyāiṭṭhaṁ?

puṇaravi ya tammi nayarē ḍiṇḍimasaddēṇa savvagāruḍiyā

vāhariyā na ya kēṇavi uṭṭhaviyā sappadaṭṭhā sā

ētthantarammi kēṇavi paōyaṇēṇaṁ samāgaō tattha

dhaṇadēvō aha pēcchaï samāulaṁ pariyaṇaṁ savvaṁ

aha daṭṭhuṁ siridattaṁ pucchaï kiṁ mitta! āulā tubbhē?

dīsaha viddāṇamuhā, aha siridattō imaṁ bhaṇaï

sirikantā maha bhagiṇī kannā sappēṇa ajja daṭṭhatti

na u jīvāvaï kōvi hu tēṇamhē āulā mitta!

annaṁ ca

nēmittiēṇa puvvaṁ āiṭṭhaṁ āsi sappaḍasiyaṁ jō

ujjīvissaï ēyaṁ hōhī ēyāē sō bhattā

ēyaṁ ca tassa vayaṇaṁ aliyappāyaṁ tu sampaïṁ jāyaṁ

jaṁ sā ahiṇā ḍakkā na ya kōvi hu taṁ samuṭṭhavaï

dhaṇadēva! taō amhaṁ sampaï tuṭṭā ō jīviyavvāsā

aïvallahabhagiṇīē tēṇamha sōgāulā dhaṇiyaṁ

iya sōuṁ dhaṇadēvō saharisacittō samullavaï ēvaṁ

mā kuṇa sōyaṁ sundara! na hōi aliyaṁ tayaṁ vayaṇaṁ

dē! picchāmō tāva ya tuha bhagiṇiṁ, tēṇa ēvamullaviē

nīō tīē samīvē dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï niyapurisaṁ

taṁ supaïṭṭhadinnaṁ āṇēsu maṇinti tāhē sō purisō

ghittuṁ lahu divvamaṇiṁ samāgaō tassa pāsammi

vimalasalilēṇa sittō divvamaṇī tāhē tēṇa nīrēṇa

abbhōkkhiyā salīlaṁ samuṭṭhiā suhapasuttavva

aviya

tīē taṁ dēhagayaṁ sappavisaṁ maṇijalēṇa saṁsittaṁ

sukkajjhāṇābhihayaṁ naṭṭhaṁ kammaṁva mōhaṇiyaṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ siridattō sāgarasiṭṭhī ya harisiyā dōvi

pisuṇanti tujjha ēsā dinnā dhaṇadēva! sirikantā

tattō sōhaṇalaggē pariṇīyā ucchavēṇa mahayā u

tīē sō aṇurattō visayasuhaṁ bhuñjaē tattha

jā tattha kaïvi māsē ciṭṭhaï sō tīē jōvvaṇāsattō

tāva ya savvaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ vikkīyaṁ tassa purisēhiṁ

paḍibhaṇḍaṁ pihu gahiyaṁ saṁvụ̄dhā sayalasatthiyā tāhē

dhaṇadēvō āpucchaï gamaṇatthaṁ sasuravaggaṁ taṁ

aha bhūridaviṇajuttā dāsīdāsāipariyaṇasamaggā

sirikantā niyapiuṇā paṭṭhaviyā bhattuṇā samayaṁ

puvvuddiṭṭhakamēṇaṁ dhaṇadēvō garuyasatthapariyariō

caliō niyanayarammi kusagganayarāu suhadivasē

aha kamasō sampattō sīhaguhāsannabhūpaēsammi

āvāsiyammi satthē dhaṇadēvō cintaē ēvaṁ

taïyā pallīvaïṇā bhaṇiō u ahaṁ avassamēntēṇa

āgantavvaṁ tumaē maha dhiihēunti tā iṇhiṁ

āsannā sā vaṭṭaï pallī tā sigghamēva gacchāmi

daṭhṭhūṇa suppaïṭṭhaṁ puṇaravi ihamāgamissāmi

iya cintiūṇa kaïvayapurisajuō vēsarīē ārụ̄dhō

sampattō aha pēcchaï sīhaguhaṁ savvaō daḍḍhaṁ

aviya

jālāluṅkhiyanivaḍiyagōmahisakaraṅkakaliyapērantaṁ

pērantasatthaviṇihayahayaruhirapavāhaduggandhaṁ

duggandhadharaṇinivaḍiyabhaḍamaṁsavasāpasattabahusuṇahaṁ

suṇahabhayaṁmukkamāṇusakaraṅkasivamukkaphēkkāraṁ

phēkkārasavaṇasantaṭṭhabhīruuḍḍīṇagiddhasisunivahaṁ

sisunivahahatthasandaḍḍhabhillajuvaīhiṁ duppicchaṁ

duppicchajalaṇajālāpaluṭṭhabhillōhabhavaṇabībhacchaṁ

bībhacchajalaṇakavaliyamayamāṇusasayasamāinnaṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ dhaṇadēvō ēvaṁ vajjaraï hā! kimēyanti

aïvisamāvi hu pallī kēṇa imā handi! daḍḍhatti?

ētthantarammi kēṇavi karaṅkamajjhaṭṭhiēṇa vajjariyaṁ

dhaṇadēva! ēhī ēttō ahayaṁ sō dēvasammotti

palicchinnacalaṇajuyalō gurupaharaṇaghāyajajjariyadēhō

gāḍhaṁ tisābhibhūō ajjavi ciṭṭhāmi jīvantō

taṁ sōuṁ dhaṇadēvō purisaṁ paṭṭhaviya pāṇiyanimittaṁ

aïguruvisāyajuttō pattō aha tasya pāsammi

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ sāhasu bhō! kēṇa vilasiyaṁ ēyaṁ

sō kattha suppaïṭṭhō aha sō saṇiyaṁ samullavaï

ēttō taïyammi diṇē siddhapurāō samāgaō purisō

ēgantammi ya siṭṭhaṁ tēṇa imaṁ pallināhassa

kumara! ahaṁ paṭṭhaviō tuhapiuvaramantisumaïnāmēṇa

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa, ēyaṁ sāhējjasu suppaïṭṭhassa

suggīvassiha rannō atisurayapasaṅgadōsaō jāō

khayavāhī tēṇa imō cēṭṭhaï khaṇajīviyavvotti

ēsōvi surahakumarō santāvaï sayalapayaïvaggaṁ tu

dussīlō ulluṇṭhō asabbhabhāsī akajjaraō

taha ēyassa virattā sāmantamahantamāiyā savvē

rajjasirīē ajōgō, taṁ cēva ya kumara! jōgō si

tujjha puṇa vahaṭṭhāē kaṇagavaīē pabhūyavikkhēvō

paṭṭhaviō tā tumaē rakkhēyavvaṁ niyasarīraṁ

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï sō purisō bhadda! pallināhassa

tāva ya sō vikkhēvō pabhūyarahaturayapāikkō

sahasacciya sampattō samantaō vẹ̄dhiyā imā pallī

aha bhillanivahasahiō nīhariō suppaïṭṭhōvi

bahujaṇasaṁhārakaraṁ laggaṁ āōhaṇaṁ mahāghōraṁ

nihayā bahavō bhillā vijiyā amhē parabalēṇaṁ

gahiūṇa taō sāraṁ savvaṁ ḍahiūṇa sīhaguhamēyaṁ

kāuṁ hayavippahayaṁ viṇiggayaṁ parabalaṁ tattō

ahayampi hu jujjhantō ēyamavatthantaraṁ ihaṁ pattō

dhaṇadēva! nēva jāṇē kiṁ jāyaṁ suppaïṭṭhassa

pañcanamōkārō aha dinnō sammattavayasamēō sē

tēṇavi ya bhāvasāraṁ puṇaruttaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattō

ētthantarammi purisō salilaṁ dhittūṇa āgaō tattha

dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï taō piyasu jalaṁ dēvasamma! imaṁ

aha sō jalaṁ pibantō aïtaṇhāsusiyatāluyattaṇaō

guruvēyaṇāparigaō sahasā pāṇēhiṁ paricattō

dhaṇadēvōvi hu aïgurusōgō ḍahiūṇa tassa taṁ dēhaṁ

savvampi samarabhūmiṁ jōyāvaï niyayapurisēhiṁ

na ya katthaï uvaladdhaṁ karaṅkamēttampi pallināhassa

tattō cintaï ēsō hā! dhī! vihiṇō vilasiyassa

tārisaguṇajuttassavi saralasahāvassa suppaïṭṭhassa

nigghiṇakaṇagavaīē hā! hā! kaha dāruṇaṁ vihiyaṁ?

māindajālasarisaṁ savvaṁ ēyammi handi! saṁsārē

khaṇadiṭṭhanaṭṭharūvaṁ dhaṇapariyaṇajīviyavvāiṁ

na ya najjaï kiṁ jāyaṁ mahāṇubhāvassa suppaïṭṭhassa

kiṁ jīvaï ahava maō saṅgāmē ēttha jujjhantō?

ēmāi cintayantō dhaṇadēvō āgaō nijē satthē

aha kamasō sampattō satthajuō hatthiṇapurammi

tuṭṭhāō jaṇaṇijaṇayā savvē āṇandiyā vayaṁsā sē

sōhaṇadivasē vahuyā pavēsiyā niyayagēhammi

aha puvvasiṇēhēṇaṁ sirikantā sāsuyāiṇunnāyā

niyacēḍijuyā pattā kamalāvaïdēvigēhammi

daṭṭhuṁ puvvavayaṁsiṁ viyasiyamuhapaṅkayā mahādēvī

aïgaruyasiṇēhēṇaṁ uṭṭhiya āliṅgaē ēyaṁ

bhaṇaï ya vayaṁsi! ukkaṇṭhiyāē diṭṭhā pabhūyakālāō

aïsōhaṇaṁ hi jāyaṁ jaṁ sāsurayampi tuhavi ēttha

jaṁ tumaē diṭṭhāē diṭṭhaṁ mannāmi piiharaṁ savvaṁ

iya bhaṇiuṁ dēvīē uciyapavittī kayā tīē

uvaviṭṭhāō dōnnivi kusalapavittī ya sāhiyā savvā

khaṇamēgaṁ sambhāsaṁ kāūṇa bhaṇaï sirikantā

gacchāmi iṇhi gēhē tattō kamalāvaī imaṁ bhaṇaï

païdiyahaṁ aï! tumaē āgantavvaṁ maha samīvē

bhaṇiyaṁ sirikantāē ēvaṁ kāhāmi ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇaṁ

dēvīē aṇunnāyā samāgayā niyayagēhammi

ēvaṁ sirikantāē sasurakulē tattha acchamāṇīē

kamalāvaīdēvīē samayaṁ gurupīijuttāē

dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ samayaṁ visayasuhaṁ sammamaṇuhavantīē

bahuyāō aïkkantā vāsāṇaṁ kōḍikōḍīō

aha annayā kayāivi riuṇhāyā bhattuṇā samaṁ suttā

rayaṇīcarimajāmē sumiṇaṁ pāsittu paḍibuddhā

aha bhaṇaï maē piyayama! sumiṇē candō muhēṇa pavisantō

diṭṭhō, taṁ daṭhṭhūṇaṁ sahasā buddhā taō ahayaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ sundari! puttō bhavissaē tujjha

sayalavaṇivaggapavarō iya ēvaṁ sūyaē sumiṇaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ sirikantāē ēvaṁ piya! hōu vayaṇayaṁ saccaṁ

sāsamadēvīpabhāvā baddhō ēsō maē gaṇṭhī

tīē ciya rayaṇīē tīē kucchiṁsi gabbhasambhūī

jātā kamēṇa jāva ya bōlīṇā dōnni māsā sē

taïyammi puṇō māsē dōhalaō tīē abhayadāṇammi

jāō dhaṇadēvēṇavi siṭṭhē sō pūriō tīē

aha uvaciyagabbhā pūriē dōhalammī pasavaṇasamayammī āgayammī suhēṇa

suhagahanivahammī uccaṭhāṇaṭṭhiyammī suhakaraṇamuhuttē dārayaṁ sā pasūyā

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï sirikantātaṇayapasavaṇō nāma

surasundarināmāē kahāē navamō paricchēō

takkammakusalavilayāsamūhavihiyammi sūikammammi

halluttāvaligihadāsivihiyatakkālakaraṇijjē

saharisapariyaṇavajjariyavajjasuyajammaharisiyamaṇēṇa

dhaṇadhammasēṭṭhiṇā aha vaddhāvaṇayaṁ samāḍhattaṁ

aviya

gahiyakkhavattapavisantanayaranārījaṇōharamaṇīyaṁ

ramaṇīyaṇamuhamaṇḍaṇa- vāvaḍaniyabandhuvaradāraṁ

varadāragganivēsiyavandaṇamālāsaṇāhasiyakalasaṁ

siyakalasahatthapavisantavaṭṭakijjantakalasaddaṁ

kalasaddapaürapāulamaṅgalasaṅgīyaparavapēkkhaṇayaṁ

pēkkhaṇayapikkhakkhittalōyadijjantatambōlaṁ

aviya

ghōsiyajīvā 'ghāō mōyāviyaviulabandini urambō

dijjantavivihadāṇō dīṇāṇāhāisuhajaṇaō

païjiṇamandirakijjantavajjavaramajjaṇāivāvārō

varavatthamāiēhiṁ saṁmāṇiyasāhusandōhō

bhōjiyasayaṇasamūhō saṁmāṇiyavaṇiyanāyaramahalallō

jaṇajaṇiyacamakkārō suyajammamahūsavō vihiō

ēvaṁ kayakāyavvō sampattē bārasammi diyahammi

gahiūṇa darisaṇīyaṁ sampattō rāiṇō mūlaṁ

kayaviṇaō dhaṇadēvō bhaṇaï mahārāya! sēṭṭhivayaṇēṇa

dēvīsahiēṇa tumē bhōttavvaṁ amha gēhammi

hasiūṁ rannā bhaṇiyaṁ na hōi kiṁ sēṭṭhiṇō imaṁ gēhaṁ?

piusarisō jaṁ sēṭṭhī vicintagō sayalarajjassa?

tahavi hu sēṭṭhī jaṁ bhaṇaï kiñci taṁ cēva amha kāyavvaṁ

iya bhaṇiē dhaṇadēvō mahāpasāutti bhaṇiūṇa

niyagēhē gantūṇaṁ takkāluciyaṁ samatthakaraṇīyaṁ

niyapariyaṇēṇa kāraï āṇandiyamāṇasō jāva

dēvīsahiō rāyā karēṇuyāvisaraparigaō tāva

sampattō sēṭṭhigihē bandijaṇugghuṭṭhajayasaddō

kayamaṅgalōvayārō uttariya karēṇuyāi dēvijuō

varamuttāhalaviraïyacaükkasīhāsaṇē pavarē

uvaviṭṭhō dēvijuō tattō ya vilāsiṇīhiṁ pavarāhiṁ

ārattiyāvaraṇapamuhammi vihimmi vihiyammi

bhuttō divvāhāraṁ niyapariyaṇasañjuō jahāvihiṇā

gōsīsavilattaṅgō parihāviyadivvavaravatthō

viṇaya naēṇaṁ tattō dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ imaṁ tu vinnattō

dēvīē piyabhagiṇī vajjaraï imaṁ mahārāya!

pasavanti piuharammī paḍhamaṁ kila sayalavaṇiyajāyāō

kāraṇavasēṇa kēṇavi sañjāyaṁ nēva taṁ majjha

tā dēvidaṁsaṇēṇaṁ ihēva kila piuharanti mannāmi

tā jaï ittiyabhūmiṁ āgacchaï hōi tā laṭṭhaṁ

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiē aha dēvī rāiṇā aṇuṇṇāyā

sirikantāē samīvē sampattā kañcuisamēyā

tattha ya maṇōramāē vilēvaṇāharaṇavatthamāīhiṁ

pūiya bhaṇiyā dēvī suyassa nāmaṁ karēsutti

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvīē taō siṭṭhiṇi! tuha cēva hōi uciyamiṇaṁ

tahavi tumaē bhaṇiyaṁ kāyavvamavassamamhāṇaṁ

gahiūṇa niucchaṅgē taṁ bālaṁ kamalakōmalakarēhiṁ

kamalāvaīē bhaṇiyaṁ sugandhagandhē khivantīē

sirikantāē jaṇiō dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ tu bālaō ēsō

māupiuaddhanāmō siridēvō nāmamēyassa

aïsōhaṇaṁ hi nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ dēvīi iya bhaṇantēṇa

avihavanārigaṇēṇaṁ maṅgalasaddō samugghuṭṭhō

aha taṁ maṇaharadēhaṁ muṭṭhīkayakarajuyaṁ visālacchaṁ

sukumālapāṇipāyaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa vicintaē dēvī

dhannā majjha vayaṁsī jīē suō ērisō samuppannō

jaṇamaṇanayaṇāṇandō maha puṇa ēyampi na hu jāyaṁ

kiṁ majjha jīviēṇaṁ kiṁvā maha vihalagavvarajjēṇa

jā niyataṇayassa muhaṁ picchāmi na mandabhaggatti

ēmāi cintayantī ābhāsittā vayaṁsiyaṁ niyayaṁ

rannā sahiyā dēvī sampattā niyayagēhammi

tattha ya taṁ cintantī suyajammukkaṇṭhiyā sasōillā

paricattadēhaciṭhṭhā uvviggā sayalakajjēsu

mattā va mucchiyā iva suttavva mayavva vigayasattavva

jhāṇagayajōgiṇi iva uvarayanīsēsavāvārā

parihāyantasarīrā gurusōyāyāsa sāmamuhakamalā

rannā kayāi diṭṭhā puṭhṭhā kamalāvaī tāhē

dēvi! tumaṁ kiṁ vimaṇā dubbaladēhā ya dīsasē iṇhiṁ

kiṁ vachiyaṁ na pujjaï sāhīṇē kiṅkarammi maē

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvīē taō aṁsujalāsārāsittasihiṇāē

piyayama! tuha ppasāyā sampajjaï vañchiyaṁ savvaṁ

taṁ natthi kimpi sōkkhaṁ tuha ppasāyāu jaṁ na mē pattaṁ

navaraṁ puttapalōyaṇasōkkhaṁ suiṇēvi nō diṭṭhaṁ

dhannāu tāu nārīō ittha jāō ahō nisiṁ nāha!

niyaya thaṇaṁ dhayantaṁ thaṇandhayaṁ handi! picchanti

pacchā pariṇīyāivi sirikantāē suō samuppannō

tumaē mannāyāē na puṇō maha mandabhāgāē

tā dēva! dēsu puttaṁ aha navi tā natthi jīviyaṁ majjha

tuṭṭaï thaṇōvi aha ēi khīramannā gaī natthi

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ ētthatthē kuṇasu dēvi! mā sōgaṁ

ārāhittā tiyasaṁ pūrēmi maṇōrahē 'vassaṁ

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ rāyā kāuṁ pūyaṁ jiṇindapaḍimāṇaṁ

siyavasaṇadharō ummukkasayalamaṇikañcaṇāharaṇō

pōsahasālaṁ gantuṁ aṭṭhamabhattaṁ pagiṇhiuṁ vihiṇā

kusasattharē nisannō ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō

dēvō va dāṇavō vā jiṇasāsaṇabhattisañjuō kōvi

jaha saṁnihiō siggha āgacchaü vañchiyaṁ dēu

ēvaṁ ca cintayantō ēgantē saṁniruddhajaṇapasarō

niccaladēhō ciṭṭhaï rāyā jā tinni diyahāiṁ

tā rayaṇicarimajāmē viddhaṁsiyasayalatimirasaṅghāyaṁ

bhāsuradēhaṁ purisaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa vicintaē rāyā

nimisanti lōyaṇāiṁ tā kiṁ ēsō na hōi dēvotti

na ya maṇuyāṇa sarīrē jāyaï ēvaṁvihā dittī

tā hōjja imō kō puṇa caraṇāvi mahiṁ phusanti nēyassa

ēvaṁ vigappayantō rāyā ābhāsiō tēṇa

bhō amarakēunaravara! uggatavēṇaṁ kilāmiō si na kiṁ?

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇō sō abbhuṭṭhiya rāiṇā bhaṇiō

kō si tumaṁ kattō vā samāgaō kahasu maha mahābhāga!?

bhaṇiyaṁ surēṇa naravara! kahēmi kōūhalaṁ jaï tē

īsāṇakappavāsī vihuppahō nāma suravarō ahayaṁ

āsannacavaṇasamaō paralōyahiyaṁ samāyariuṁ

titthayaravandaṇatthaṁ vidēhavāsammi āgaō āsi

tattha maē sō bhayavaṁ āpuṭṭhō niyayavuttantaṁ

uppattī kattha mahaṁ cuyassa ēttō bhavissaē bhayavaṁ!?

tattō jiṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bharahammi ya hatthiṇapurammi

jō acchaï puttatthī pōsahasālāi pōsahammi ṭhiō

siriamarakēurāyā tassa tumaṁ hōsi puttotti

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ samāgaō rāya! tuha samīvammi

tā mā kuṇasu kilēsaṁ ahayaṁ hōhāmi tuha puttō

gēṇhasu kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ narinda! ēyaṁ taō u dēvīē

jīē icchasi puttaṁ dāyavvaṁ tīi ābharaṇaṁ

iya bhaṇiuṁ kannāṇaṁ uttāriya kuṇḍalāiṁ divvāiṁ

rannō samappiūṇaṁ dēvō addaṁsaṇībhūō

rannāvi rayaṇiviramē gantuṁ dēvīē viyasiyamuhēṇa

suradaṁsaṇāi savvō vuttantō sāhiō tattō

kuṇḍalajuyalaṁ appiya pabhāyakiccaṁ karittu nīsēsaṁ

paḍilāhiya sāhujaṇaṁ sayaṁ pabhuttō varāhāraṁ

aha annayā ya dēvī riuṇhāyā rayaṇicarimajāmammi

daṭṭhuṁ sumiṇaṁ sahasā paḍibuddhā vēvirasarīrā

bhaṇiyā rannā sundari! kīsa akamhāō kampiyā taṁ si

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama! sampaï sumiṇaṁ maē diṭṭhaṁ

kila kaṇagamaō kalasō majjha muhē pavisiuṁ viṇikkhantō

kēṇāvi bhañjaṇatthaṁ nīō dūraṁ sa kuddhēṇa

puṇaravi bahukālāō kahavi hu laddhō sa khīrapaḍipunnō

siyakusumamāliyāē maēvi sampūiō tattō

ēyaṁ sumiṇaṁ daṭṭhuṁ muhakaḍuyaṁ pariṇaīi sundarayaṁ

jāō bhaēṇa kampō maha dēhē tēṇa naranāha!

taṁ sōūṇa narindō jāō sōgāurō daḍhaṁ hiyaē

vajjaraï dēvi! suviṇaṁ lābhaṁ sūēi taṇayassa

sēsaṁ ca suviṇajāṇagapucchagavihiṇā viyāṇiuṁ tujjha

sāhissaṁ mā kāhisi uvvēgaṁ kiñci hiyayammi

tattō pabhāyasamaē gantuṁ atthāṇamaṇḍavē rāyā

āṇavaï sumiṇasatthatthajāṇaē jhatti vāharaha

tattha niuttanarēhiṁ tahēva sampāḍiyāē āṇāē

sāmantamantipuranāyagēhiṁ punnammi atthāṇē

kayaviṇayā suviṇannū uvaviṭṭhā aha narindaāsannē

dhaṇadēvōvi hu rannō āsannō cēva uvaviṭṭhō

tattō rannā tēsiṁ siṭṭhō suradaṁsaṇāivuttantō

puvvuttō savvōvi hu suviṇagaüvalambhaavasāṇō

sammaṁ viṇicchiūṇaṁ suviṇasarūvaṁ kahēha bhō! tattaṁ

iya bhaṇiyā tē rannā annōnnaṁ jāva cintinti

tāva ya dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ naranāha! dēsu avahāṇaṁ

suviṇaparamatthajāṇaṇahēuṁ nisuṇēsu vuttuntaṁ

taō aha aḍavīē diṭṭhō bhillavaī, tēṇa jaha ya sappēhiṁ

baddhō u cittavēgō vimōiō maṇipabhāvāō

jaha tēṇa niyayacariē siṭṭhē dēvassa āgamō āsi

dēvēṇa kēvalī aha diṭṭhō ya kusagganayarammi

jaha bhāvibhavaṁ puṭṭhō kēvaliṇā jaha ya tassa āiṭṭhaṁ

siriamarakēurannō hōhisi puttō tumaṁ bhadda!

jaṇaṇīi samaṁ tattha ya avahariō puvvavēriyasurēṇa

tā cittavēga! khayarāhivassa gēhammi vaḍ̣dhihisi

ēmāi puvvaüttaṁ savittharaṁ sāhiyaṁ naravaïssa

dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ jāva ya sampattō hatthiṇapurammi

tā dēva! dēviudarē vihuppahō sō surō samuppannō

hōhī, jaō na kēvalivayaṇaṁ iha annahā hōi

puvvaviruddhasurēṇaṁ hariō khayarassa vaḍ̣dhiō gēhē

sāhiyabahuvihavijjō milihī sō niyayajaṇaṇīē

icchiyakannādāṇaṁ mālāē pūyaṇampi mannā si

ēsō naridaṁ! suviṇayaparamatthō phuraï maha hiyaē

ēyaṁ dhaṇadēvassa ō vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa suviṇayannūhiṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ ahō! aüvvaṁ ēyassa u buddhikōsallaṁ

sayayaṁ tallicchēhivi bahusatthaviyakkhaṇēhiṁ amhēhiṁ

tavvihabuddhiviuttēhiṁ sakkiyaṁ nō viṇicchēuṁ

susiliṭṭhō naṇu atthō nirūviō rāya! vaṇiyaüttēṇa

savvēsiṁ amhāṇavi susaṁmaō cēva ēsotti

iya bhaṇiē tē rannā tambōlapayāṇapuvvayaṁ savvē

paṭṭhaviyā taha savvē sāmantamahantamāīyā

tattō rannā bhaṇiyaṁ iṇhiṁ dhaṇadēva! kimiha kāyavvaṁ

dēvīi samaṁ amhaṁ uvaṭṭhiē dusahavirahammi

kiṁ ēttha atthi kōvi hu paḍighāyavihī suduṭṭhasuviṇassa

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ na annahā kēvaligirā ō

tahavi hu ēsa uvāō kīraï mā hōjja tēṇa paḍighāō

mañcayapaḍiyāṇa puṇō tahaṭṭhiyā cēva bhūmitti

pallīvaïṇā taïyā divvamaṇī jō samappiō majjha

sō ēsa aṅgulīyaganivēsiō ciṭṭhaü karammi

ēsō acintasattī aṇēyaṭhāṇēsu diṭṭha māhappō

tā ēyaṁ dēvīē karaṭṭhiyaṁ dēva! kārēha

puvvaviruddhōvi surō haraṇē dēvīi hōjja asamatthō

ēyassa pabhāvāō, aha kahavi karijja avaharaṇaṁ

tahavi hu avagārammī sakkissaï nēva vaṭṭiuṁ vaïrī

nāuṁ imaṁ narēsara! mā sōgaṁ kiñcivi karēha

annaṁ ca

suviṇapaḍighāyaṇatthaṁ kārēsu jiṇālaēsu mahimāō

puēsu samaṇasaṅghaṁ taduciyavatthāsaṇāīhiṁ

dāvēsu abhayadāṇaṁ vivihābhiggahatavēsu ujjamasu

ēvaṁ kayammi naravara! savvampi hu sundaraṁ hōhī

iya bhaṇiuṁ dhaṇadēvō samappiuṁ aṅgulīyayaṁ niyayaṁ

paṇamittā rāyāṇaṁ viṇiggaō rāyabhavaṇāō

rannāvi hu gantūṇaṁ dēvībhavaṇammi sayalavuttantō

siṭṭhō samappiyaṁ taha dēvīē aṅgulīyaṁ taṁ

bhaṇiyā ya dēvī! ēyaṁ khaṇampi hatthāō nēva mōttavvaṁ

ēyassa pabhāvāō pabhavanti na khuddasattāī

jiṇamandirajattāiṁ kāraviyaṁ tāhi rāiṇā savvaṁ

kamalāvaīvi tattō jāyā āvannasattatti

suhasampaḍantahiyaïṭṭhavatthusuviṇīyapariyaṇajuyāē

aha sattamammi māsē jāō dēvīē dōhalaō

lajjāē taṁ kassavi jāhē na kahēi tāva kaïyāvi

parihāyantasarīrā diṭṭhā rannā imaṁ bhaṇiyā

dēvi! tuha kiṁ na pujjaï dīsasi aïdubbalā jaō iṇhiṁ

dēvīē tō bhaṇiyaṁ dōhalaō ēsa mē nāha!

varavāraṇamārụ̄dhā dāṇaṁ dintī ya atthilōyassa

tuhaücchaṅganiviṭṭhā tumaē chattaṁ dharantēṇaṁ

hiṇḍāmi rāya! nayarē pariyariyā sayalabhiccavaggēṇa

rannā bhaṇiyaṁ sundari! kīraï ahuṇā duyaṁ ēyaṁ

aha pavarapaṭṭahatthī siṅgāriya āṇiō niuttēhiṁ

tatthārụ̄dhō rāyā dēvī uṇa tassa ucchaṅgē

uvari dhavalāyavattaṁ muttāhalarēhiraṁ sayaṁ rannā

dhariyaṁ tattō vivihaṁ paḍhantathuipāḍhanivahēṇa

tūrēsu rasantēsuṁ vajjantēsu ya asaṅkhasaṅkhēsu

kalapāṇaēhiṁ vihiē viyambhamāṇē ya saṅgīē

atthijaṇapūriyāsaṁ dāṇaṁ dēntā samatthanayarammi

āṇandanibbharāhiṁ thuvvantā nayaranārīhiṁ

āhiṇḍiūṇa vivihaṁ caükkatiyacaccarēsu icchāē

aha puravarāu bāhiṁ nīhariō kuñjarō kamasō

sahasacciya ummiṭṭhō vicchōlintō samatthajaṇaniyaraṁ

aïvēgēṇa payaṭṭō īsāṇadisāmuhō tāē

rē! lēha lēha dhāvaha ēsa gaō ēsa jāi puraotti

ēmāi vāharantō bhiccajaṇō dhāi paṭṭhīē

rāyāvi hu jāhi kahavi hu dhariuṁ na caēi karivaraṁ taṁ tu

tāhē bhaṇiyā dēvī ēsa gaō tāva ummiṭṭhō

aïvēgaō payaṭṭō cāijjaï kahavi nō niyattēuṁ

tā uttarimō kahavi hu iyaraha aḍavīē pāḍēhī

kamalāvaīē bhaṇiyaṁ ōyariyavvaṁ kahaṁ nu naranāha!

rannā bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu picchasi vaḍapāyavaṁ puraō

ēyassa ya hēṭṭhēṇaṁ jāhī hatthī taō tumē dēvi!

sāhāē laggiavvaṁ sahasā hatthiṁ pamōttūṇa

ēvaṁ ca jāva rāyā dēviṁ ullavaï tāva sō hatthī

aïvēgēṇaṁ pattō vaḍavāyavahiṭṭhabhūbhāgē

dakkhattaṇaō rāyā jhatti vilaggō ya tassa sāhāē

laggasu laggasu dēvi! jhatti ēyaṁ bhaṇēmāṇō

aïvēgaō karissā ( ssa? ) adakkhayāē ya itthibhāvassa

gabbhassa ya garuyattā bhayavēviraō sarīrassa

kayaajjhavasāyāvi hu na sakkiyā jāhi tattha laggēuṁ

tāhē ya karivarō sō jhaḍatti tattō avakkantō

aha gurusōgō rāyā tahaṭṭhiō jā taō palōēi

tā picchaï gayaṇēṇaṁ jantaṁ vēgēṇa taṁ kariṇaṁ

aha vimhiō maṇēṇaṁ cintaï rāyā ahō! mahacchariyaṁ

mōttuṁ bhūmipayāraṁ vaccaï hatthī nahayalēṇa

ahavā

puvvaviruddhasurō sō vilasaï nūṇaṁ imēṇa rūvēṇa

na hu kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyā bhāvā iha annahā honti

ēvaṁ vicintayantassa tassa, hatthī adaṁsaṇībhūō

tāva aṇumaggalaggaṁ rannō sinnaṁ samaṇupattaṁ

aha karivaramaggēṇaṁ samarappiyapamuhasuhaḍasayakaliyaṁ

dēvīgavēsaṇatthaṁ paṭṭhaviuṁ sāhaṇaṁ rāyā

kahakahavi garuyasōō sāmantamahantagāṇa vayaṇēṇa

pattō niyanayarammī sunnō vunnō nirāṇandō

paricattarajjacittō ciṭṭhaï jā kaïvi tattha divasāṇi

kamalāvaïsampāvaṇaāsāē dhariyaniyajīō

tā annadiṇē sinnaṁ samarappiyapamuhamāgayaṁ sahasā

dīṇaṁ vimaṇaṁ khinnaṁ lajjāviṇamantamuhakamalaṁ

aha rannā āpuṭṭhō samarappiō kahasu bhadda! vuttataṁ

kiṁ diṭṭhō duṭṭhakarī dēvīvi vimōiyā tattō?

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ samarappiēṇa suṇa dēva!

karivaradisāpayaṭṭā pattā aḍavīi tā amhē

tattha ya bahuppayāraṁ gavēsamāṇēhiṁ dēva! amhēhiṁ

diṭṭhō na sō karivarō nēva ya dēvī na ya paüttī

avarāvarasavaragaṇaṁ pucchatāṇaṁ sudūrapattāṇaṁ

aha annadiṇē kahiyaṁ kappaḍiyanarēṇa ēkkēṇa

tattō sattamadivasē paümōyaranāmaē saravarammi

gayaṇāu nivaḍamāṇō mahilāsahiō karī diṭṭhō

tattō bhayabhīēṇaṁ dūraṭṭhiyaguvilatarupaviṭṭhēṇa

nārīrahiō puṇaravi palōiō tattha hatthitti

viyaratō saratīrē, iya tassa ō vayaṇayaṁ suṇēūṇa

bhaṇiyaṁ daṁsasu bhaddaya! taṁ sigghaṁ saravaraṁ amha

aha tēṇa daṁsiyaṁ taṁ palōiyaṁ saravaraṁ samaṁ tēṇa

na ya uvaladdhā dēvī niuṇampi gavēsamāṇēhiṁ

saravarajōyaṇamittē viuttapurisēhiṁ pāviō hatthī

taṁ ghittuṁ nirāṇandā ihāgayā dēvamūlammi

tā kiṁ tatthēva sarē gabhīranīrammi uvarayā dēvī

aha tattō uttariuṁ pattā u kahimpi vasimammi?

ahavā sāvayapaürē vaṇammi kēṇavi viṇasiyā hōjja

na ya jāṇāmō kiñcivi narinda! dēvīē vuttantaṁ

ēvaṁ ca jāva jampaï samarappiō patthivassa sē puraō

tāva ya dāraniuttō kayaviṇaō ēvamullavaï

dārammi sumaïnāmō nēmittī ciṭṭhaïti suṇiūṇa

bhaṇiyaṁ rannā kiṁ bhō! sō ēsō sumaïnēmittī?

jassāēsāu tayā dinnā naravāhaṇēṇa maha dēvī?

pāsaṭṭhiēhiṁ siṭṭhaṁ, narinda! ēvanti, aha rannā

bhaṇiyaṁ pavisaü sigdhaṁ pucchāmō jēṇa dēvivuttantaṁ

vayaṇāṇantaramēsō pavēsiō dāravālēṇa

kayaüvayārō rannā uvaviṭṭhō viṇayapuvvayaṁ sumaī

āpuṭṭhō, kiṁ dēvī jīvaï va navatti vajjarasu?

uvaōgaṁ dāūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ aha sumaïṇā jiyaïti

akkhayadēhā sampaï miliyā iva bandhuvaggassa

kaïyā samāgamō maha tīē, kiṁ vā havējja sē gabbhē?

iya puṭṭhō naravaïṇā kayaüvaōgō puṇō bhaṇaï

jaïyā narinda! suviṇē giṇhasi visamaṭṭhiyaṁ kusumamālaṁ

tattō ya māsamittē samāgamō tumha dēvīē

hōhī taṇaō tīē vijujjihī kintu jāyamēttō sō

niyamāūē, naravara! ēvaṁ kila kahaï hu nimittaṁ

puṭṭhō puṇaravi rannā jaṇaṇiviuttō sa jīvihī kiṁ nō?

katthavi vuḍ̣dhi jāhī, kaïyā va samāgamē tēṇa

aha sumaī bhaṇaï puṇō bahukālaṁ jīvihī sa tē puttō

kattha ya vuḍ̣dhiṁ jāhī ēyaṁ puṇa nēva jāṇāmō

kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïyā gayaṇāō kannagā paḍihī

tattō ya sigghamēva hi samāgamō tumha taṇaēṇa

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ gayasōgō pahasiō bhaṇaï rāyā

bhō! bhō! suvannalakkhaṁ sigghaṁ sumaïssa dēhasi

ēyavayaṇāō amhaṁ dēvīvirahammi garuyasōgaggī

pasarantō ōlhaviō samāgamāsājalōhēṇa

aha niyayābharaṇēṇaṁ suvannalakkhēṇa pūiō sumaī

nīhariō rāyāvi hu maṇayaṁ jāō vigayasōgō

aha annayā ya rāyā suttō rayaṇīi pēcchaē sumiṇaṁ

uttaradisāmuhēṇaṁ vayamāṇēṇaṁ maē kūvē

paḍiyā addhamilāṇā dhavalā kusumāṇa māliyā diṭṭhā

gahiyā sahasā jāyā paccaggā surahigandhaḍ̣dhā

daṭhṭhūṇamiṇaṁ sumiṇaṁ paḍibuddhō cintaē imaṁ rāyā

ēyaṁ hi sumaïbhaṇiyaṁ diṭṭhaṁ sumiṇaṁ maē ajja

tā hōhī lahu iṇhiṁ majjha vayantassa uttaradisāē

visamadasāpattāē dēvīē saṅgamō 'vassaṁ

iya cintiūṇa rāyā niyadēsapalōyaṇacchalēṇaṁ tu

gurusēṇāpariyariō nīhariō hatthiṇapurāō

kaïvayapayāṇagāiṁ gantuṁ uttaṅgagirisamāinnē

aïguvilatarusaṇāhē aḍavipaēsammi ēgammi

āvāsiō sasēnnō aha kūvē dīhataṇasamōcchaïē

kahavi hu pamāyavasaō paḍiyā rannō camarahārī

aha rannā āṇattō purisō rajjuppaōgaō tattha

ōinnō santamasē iō taō jāva gavisēi

tā ēgatthaniluṅkkaṁ picchaï juvaïṁ taḍīi agaḍassa

bhayakampantasarīraṁ santamasē tattha accantaṁ

kāsi tumaṁ iha sundari! ii puṭṭhā jā na dēi paḍivayaṇaṁ

tāva ya jalamajjhagayā vilāsiṇī kaṇṭhagayapāṇā

sampattā tēṇa taō ghittūṇaṁ tayaṁ kamēṇa nīhariō

vajjaraï rāya! ētthaṁ annāvi hu acchaē juvaī

ābhaṭṭhāvi na bhāsaï bhaēṇa kampantataṇulayā varaī

ēyaṁ nisamma rannō phuriyaṁ aha dāhiṇaṁ nayaṇaṁ

aha vimhiēṇa rannō vicintiyaṁ kiṁ havijja sā dēvī

ahavā iha aḍavīē dēvīē sambhavō kattha?

ahavā kammavasāṇaṁ sattāṇaṁ navari ēttha saṁsārē

bhaviyavvayāvasēṇaṁ natthi tayaṁ jaṁ na sambhavaī

jaï sā havijja dēvī tā sundaramēva, kāvi aha annā

tahavi hu uttārijjaü karuṇāmūlō jaō dhammō

iya cintiuṇa rannā bhaṇiō purisō tayampi kaḍ̣dhēhi

aha sō rajjūi puṇō purisō kūvammi ōinnō

bhaṇiyā ya suyaṇu! ahayaṁ rannō siriamarakēunāmassa

vayaṇēṇaṁ tuhuttāraṇakajjēṇaṁ puṇaravi paviṭṭhō

tā āruha mañcīē naragāgārāō andhakūvāō

jēṇuttārēmi lahuṁ ēyaṁ ca nisamma sā vayaṇaṁ

ārụ̄dhā mañcīē kamēṇa uttāriyā taō dēvī

dubbaladēhā rannā kahakahavi hu paccabhinnāyā

sāvi ya daṭṭhuṁ rāyaṁ rōvantī ghaggharēṇa saddēṇa

caraṇavilaggā rannā aṁsujalapphunnanayaṇēṇa

nīyā niyayāvāsē dēviṁ daṭhṭhūṇa pariyaṇō savvō

aïgurusōgō rōvaī vivihapalāvēhiṁ dīṇamuhō

aha kayasarīraciṭhṭhā puṭṭhā kamalāvaī narindēṇa

taïyā kariṇā nīyāē kiṁ tumē dēvi! aṇubhūyaṁ?

kaïyā va kahava paḍiyā bhīsaṇakūvammi ēttha aḍavīē?

kamalāvaīi bhaṇiyaṁ suṇasu mahārāya! sāhēmi

vaḍapāyavammi laggē dēvē taṁ vilaggiuṁ asattā haṁ

vēgapahāviyakariṇā hariyā ēgāgiṇī tāva

aha sō girisariyāē visamataḍiṁ pāviūṇa sahasatti

aïvēgabhaṅgabhīuvva nahayalaṁ jhatti uppaïō

tattō bhayabhīyāē vicintiyaṁ hanta! karivarapaviṭṭhō

avahaï kōvi dēvō na jēṇa kariṇō vayanti nahē

iya vimhiyahiyayā haṁ puṇō puṇō jā mahiṁ palōēmi

picchāmi tāva giritarupamuhaṁ samagaṁva vaccantaṁ

aviya

ēgāgiṇī araṇṇē mahilā bīhijja aḍavīmajjhammi

iya kaliuṁva sahāyā taruṇō vēgēṇa dhāvanti

kiḍiyanarasamāiṁ calantamaṇuyāiṁ gāmanayarāiṁ

jalabhariyasaravarāiṁvi ( pi? ) mahinivaḍiyachattasarisāiṁ

dīharavaṇarāīō sappasaricchaō saccavijjanti

pālisāricchā giriō sāraṇisarisāō sariyāō

aha dūramaïgayāē sambhariō aṅgulīyagamaṇī sō

avahatthiya tāhi bhayaṁ pahaō sō tēṇa kumbhayaḍē

aviya maṇisañjuyakarapahaō vajjēṇiva tāḍiō gaïndō sō

mōttuṁ gurucīhāḍiṁ ahōmuhō jhati gayaṇāō

jā nivaḍaï vēgēṇa tāva ya hiṭṭhāmuhaṁ niyantīē

diṭṭhaṁ mahantamēgaṁ sarōvaraṁ bhaṅgurataraṅgaṁ

parihatthamacchapucchacchaḍāhi ucchaliyasalilaüppīlaṁ

mahumattamahuyarīvisararuddhaṁviyasantatāmarasaṁ

aviya phurantamaṇijālayaṁ tarantaṭiṭṭibhālayaṁ

rahaṅgapantimaṇḍiyaṁ vihaṅgasatthavaḍḍayaṁ

bhamantabhūrigōhiyaṁ sarōruhālisōhiyaṁ

aṇēgasāvayāulaṁ jhasōhaluddhasāulaṁ

calantabhīmagāhayaṁ raḍatadadadūrōhayaṁ

marālapantisōhiyaṁ tamālatālarēhiyaṁ

raṇantachappayāliṁyaṁ balāyapantimāliyaṁ

phurantasippisumpuḍaṁ bhamantabhīmadīvaḍaṁ

aha tammi nīrapunnē aṇōrapārammi saravarē hatthī

gayaṇāō nīsahaṅgō paḍiō buḍḍō ya jalamajjhē

aha nīsahē gaïndē buḍḍē gambhīranīramajjhammi

maṇiṇō māhappēṇaṁ jalaüvariṁ cēva thakkā haṁ

āsāiyaphalagāvi ya uttariuṁ saravarassa tīrammi

upaviṭṭhā bhayabhīyā gurusōgā iya vicintanttā

tārisariddhijuyāvi hu khaṇēṇa ēgāgiṇī kahaṁ jāyā

dēsiyajuvaīva ahō! aïguvilō kammapariṇāmō

sō kattha bhiccavaggō sā ya sirī sō viṇīyaparivārō

hōhāmi kahaṁ iṇhiṁ vihiyā ēgāgiṇī vihiṇā?

ēmāi cintayantī uvarimavatthēṇa chāiüṁ vayaṇaṁ

saraṇavihuṇā sōēṇaṁ tattha ahaṁ rōviuṁ laggā

ētthatarammi kēṇavi bhaṇiyā kiṁ suyaṇu! rōyasē karuṇaṁ?

tattō sasambhamāē palōiyaṁ mē taōhuttaṁ

kaïvayapurisasahāō taruṇanarō vēsarīi ārụ̄dhō

kayamuhasandhī puraō diṭṭhō uddhadhūliyaṅgillō

aha sō daṭṭhūṇa mamaṁ vimhiyahiyaüvva vēsarāhintō

uttariya majjha calaṇēsu nivaḍiō bhaṇaï ēvaṁ tu

parijāṇasi bhagiṇi! mamaṁ siridattō haṁ kusagganayarāō

āsi gaō paravisaē vaṇijjabuddhīē satthajuō

bārasamavaccharāō puṇaravi caliō purammi niyayammi

satthēṇa samaṁ iṇhiṁ sampattō iha paēsammi

tā bhagiṇi! kēṇa vihiṇā jāyā ēgāgiṇī tumaṁ ēttha?

iya bhaṇiyā tēṇa ahaṁ vigayabhayā jhatti sañjāyā

tattō ya maē siṭṭhō gayāvahāraïniyayavuttantō

aha dinnavayaṇasōyā bhaṇiyā vaṇiēṇa tēṇāhaṁ

dūrammi hatthiṇapuraṁ sāvayacōrēhiṁ duggamō maggō

āsannaṁ khu kusaggaṁ kiṁ kāyavvaṁ tumē bhagiṇi!?

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ kusagganayarammi vaccimō tāva

pēcchāmi bandhuvaggaṁ pabhūyakālāō siridatta!

aha tēṇa saharisēṇaṁ nīyā satthammi niyayaāvāsē

viṇaōvayārapuvvaṁ ca kāriyā sayaladēhaṭhiiṁ

taṁ dēvadinnakuṇḍalapamuhaṁ savvampi niyayaābharaṇaṁ

mōttūṇa aṅgulīyaṁ samappiyaṁ tassa vaṇiyassa

tattō satthēṇa samaṁ caliyā siridattapariyaṇasamēyā

kijjantavivihaviṇayā vaṇiēṇaṁ, ḍōliyārụ̄dhā

sōvi hu satthō jāva ya lahuyapayāṇēhiṁ vayaï aṇudiyahaṁ

kaïvayapayāṇagāiṁ tā ēgadiṇammi aḍavīē

avasaüṇēṇaṁ thakkō diyahē diyahē na jāyaē saüṇaṁ

jāva ya divaḍḍhamāsē vōlīṇē savvasatthillā

sambalarahiyā tahaïṁ ṭhāumasattā taō samuccaliyā

avaganniya avasaüṇaṁ niyapuragamaṇassa turamāṇā

tattō bīyapayāṇē pabhāyasamayammi tammi satthammi

sahasā annāucciya dinnō bhillēhiṁ ōkkhandō

aha kalayalaṁ nisāmiya satthajaṇē tattha āulībhūē

bhillēhiṁ hammamāṇē lhasijjantē ya sayarāhaṁ

sajjhasabhariyā ahamavi paḍiyā aḍavīi jāva ikkallā

ghēttūṇaṁ ēgadisaṁ naṭṭhā aïguvilatarugahaṇē

khaṇamēgaṁ tatthacchiya vayāmi kila tammi satthaṭhāṇammi

puṇaravi milāmi jēṇaṁ satthassa ahanti cintantī

jāva payaṭṭā gantuṁ tāva na jāṇāmi kattha gantavvaṁ

kattō samāgayā haṁ kāē va disāē sō satthō

bhayakampantasarīrā tāhē ēyaṁ disaṁ gahēūṇa

sañjāyadisāmōhā caliyā tarugahaṇamajjhēṇa

dūraṁ gantūṇa puṇō valiyā vaccāmi piṭṭhaōhuttaṁ

siridattajaṇagavēsaṇaparāyaṇā tattha vaṇagahaṇē

aha bhayataralacchīē iō taō tattha paribhamantīē

ummaggagamaṇabhajjantakaṇṭayāinnacaraṇāē

pahasamasụdhiyāi daḍhaṁ paē paē nīsahaṁ kaṇantīē

vasimannēsaṇahēuṁ caḍiūṇa thalammi ēgammi

jā pulaïyaṁ samantā tāva na dīsaï kahampi vasimanti

viyaranta vālanivahā samantaō bhīsaṇā aḍavī

aviya kattha ya karālakēsariguñjiyasavaṇuttasantasāraṅgā

katthaï mahantajujjhantamattavaṇamahisayāinnā

katthaï garuya pavaṅgamavimukkabōkkārabahiriyadiyantā

kattha ya vaṇadavaḍajjhantajantukayabhīsaṇārāvā

katthaï payaṇḍagaṇḍayakhaṇḍiyaru ruvisararuhirabībhacchā

katthaï sarahapalōyaṇapalāyamāṇōrukarivisarā

aviya viyarantamahādhaṇuhatthalōddhayā sukkamayasirasaṇāhā

jēṭṭhakkamūlakaliyā gurucitārōhiṇīsamēyā

bhaddavayasamaṇasahiyā uṭṭhantavisāhapayaḍamandārā

viyarantabhūririkkhā rēhaï aḍavī nahasirivva

aha taṁ aḍaviṁ suiraṁ palōyayantīi gāḍhatisiyāē

ēkkammi disābhāē diṭṭhaṁ jalabhariyasaramēgaṁ

tattō tattōhuttaṁ caliyā bhayalōlalōyaṇā ahayaṁ

kahakahavi hu sampattā tammi paēsammi kicchēṇa

pīyaṁ ca tattha salilaṁ uvaviṭṭhā taruvarassa hiṭṭhammi

ētthantarammi taraṇī antariō pasariyā rayaṇī

taō phēkkāranti sivāō jaha jaha guñjanti sāvayā vivihaṁ

taha taha bhaēṇa hiyayaṁ kampaē maha tattha rannammi

aha aḍḍharattasamaē jāyā udarammi dūsahā viyaṇā

tavvasaō ya kaṇantī lulāmi bhūmīē jāva ahaṁ

tāva ya migīva rannē aïguru viyaṇāhi pīḍiyasarīrā

sayamēva pasaviyā haṁ mahākilēsēṇa naranāha!

mucchāviramē ya taō lulamāṇaṁ mahiyalammi taṁ bālaṁ

ghittūṇa nijucchaṅgē garuyasiṇēhēṇa tattō ya

gantūṇa jalāsannē ṇhāvittā tāhi niyayavatthāiṁ

pakkhāliya ēgantē uvaviṭṭhā tarulayāgahaṇē

taṁ divvamaṇisaṇāhaṁ uttariya aṅgulīyayaṁ hatthā

kaṇṭhammi maē baddhaṁ suyassa ēvaṁ bhaṇantīē

ēyassa pabhāvāō mā maha taṇayassa kēvi aṅgammi

paharantu bhūyasāvayapisāyaduṭṭhaggahāīyā

vaṇavāsiṇīō! nisuṇaha bhō bhō vaṇadēvayāō! maha vayaṇaṁ

taṇayasamēyā sampaï saraṇaṁ bhavaīṇamallīṇā

kēsarivagghāiṇaṁ maṁsāhāraṇa kūrasattāṇaṁ

bhīsaṇaaḍavīpaḍiyā rakkhēyavvā payattēṇa

jaï putta! imā rayaṇī hontā maha tammi hatthiṇapurammi

tā ēttiyavēlāē rāyā vaddhāviō hontō

sayalassa pariyaṇassa ya purassa sāmantantivaggassa

kassa va na hōjja tōsō puttaya! tuha jammasamayammi

duvvihiyavihivihāṇā paḍiyāē bhīsaṇē ya rannammi

jāō si majjha puttaya! karēmi kiṁ mandabhaggā haṁ?

jāyammi tumē puttaya! rannampi hu sampayaṁ imaṁ vasimaṁ

naṭṭhaṁ bhayaṁ asēsaṁ ucchaṅgagaē tumē vaccha

tuha muhapalōyaṇēṇaṁ sampannamaṇōrahā bhavissāmi

ravikarapahayandhayārē jāyammi diṇammi sakayatthā

ēmāi bhaṇantīē pahasamakhinnāē nīsahaṅgāē

viyaṇāvigamāō tahiṁ samāgayā mē tahiṁ niddā

tattō khaṇantarāō paḍibuddhā jhatti mandabhaggā haṁ

kēṇāvi hu ullaviyaṁ ēyaṁ saddaṁ suṇēūṇaṁ

niuṇaṁ jōyantēṇavi pabhūyakālāō pāva! diṭṭhō si

kāhāmi vaïraantaṁ aṇuhava duvvihiyaphalamiṇhiṁ

ēyaṁ saddaṁ sōccā bhīyā, kō ēsa ēvamullavaï?

iya cintiya jāva ahaṁ niyaücchaṅgaṁ palōēmi

tā natthi tattha puttō vicintiyaṁ tāhi hā! kimēyanti

kiṁ kahavi hōjja paḍiō ahavā kēṇāvi avahariō?

kiṁvā sumiṇaṁ ēyaṁ kiṁvā maïvibbhamō mahaṁ ēsō?

ēmāi cintayantī gavēsiṁu tāhi pāraddhā

iō taō tattha gavēsayantī suyaṁ mahārāya! apāuṇantī

sirammi vajjēṇava tāḍiyā haṁ ghasatti mucchāi vasaṁ gayatti

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï kamalāvaïputtaharaṇanāmotti

surasundarināmāē kahāē dasamō paricchēō

aha laddhacēyaṇā haṁ mucchāvirahammi garuyasōgillā

niyahiyayaṁ kuṭṭintī palaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattā

hā! niddaēṇa kēṇavi aḍavīpaḍiyāē dukkhataviyāē

takkhamēttuppannō puttō hariō ahannāē

kila puttayassa vayaṇaṁ picchissamahaṁ pabhāyasamayammi

navaraṁ hayāsavihiṇā ēyaṁ maha annahā vihiyaṁ

aḍavipavēsāīyaṁ dukkhaṁ dāūṇa dūsahaṁ dēva!

kiṁ ajjavi na hu tuṭṭhō avahariō jēṇa maha puttō?

vaṇadēvayāō! tumhaṁ saraṇammi samāgayāē maha puttō

hariō, tā kiṁ jujjaï ētthavi vēhā karēuṁ jē?

hā putta! kahamaraṇṇē mukkā haṁ saraṇavajjiyā tumaē

hā! kahamucchaṅgagaō sahasā addaṁsaṇībhūō?

nūṇaṁ niṭṭhurarūvaṁ saddaṁ sōūṇa jassa paḍibuddhā

tēṇaṁ ciya avahariō pisāyarūvēṇa kēṇāvi

jassa pabhāvāō tayā sahasā gayaṇāō gayavarō paḍiō

sōvi maṇī akayatthō jāō maha mandabhāgāē

jaṁ kaṇṭhanibaddhēvi hu tammī aṅkaṭṭhiōvi hā putta!

hariō nikkaruṇēṇaṁ kēṇāvi addissarūvēṇa

ēmāi bahuvigappaṁ palavantīē tahiṁ sudīṇāē

maddukkhadukkhiyā iva khīṇā rayaṇīvi sahasatti

aïkaruṇaṁ kandantiṁ daṭṭhuṁva mamaṁ sasōyavayaṇillā

nivaḍantathūlatārayaaṁsūhiṁva ruyaï nahalacchī

ētthantarammi sūrō suyāvahārayanihālaṇatthaṁva

nāsiyaghaṇandhayārō ārụdhō udayagirisiharaṁ

aha addhapaharamēttē diyahē aïdukkhiyā ahaṁ tattha

aïkaruṇaṁ kandantī iō taō jāva viyarāmi

tāva kamaṇḍaluhatthā miuvakkalavasaṇadhāriṇī tattha

pariṇayavayā pasanna samāgayā tāvasī ēgā

daṭṭhuṁ mamaṁ ruyantiṁ vivihapalāvēhiṁ tattha vaṇagahaṇē

sañjāyagaruyakaruṇā samāgayā majjha pāsammi

mahuravayaṇēṇa tīē āpuṭṭhā suyaṇu! kīsa taṁ ruyasi

kattō samāgayā iha bhīsaṇarannammi ikkallā?

kāuṁ tīi paṇāmaṁ tattō viyalantaaṁsuyāē maē

kuñjaraharaṇāīō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō

aha tāvasīē bhaṇiyaṁ imassa jōgā na hōsi taṁ suyaṇu!

tahavi hu kimittha kīraï sakammavasagammi jiyalōē?

sundari! kammavasāṇaṁ sattāṇaṁ iha bhavē vasantāṇaṁ

ēvaṁvihadukkhāiṁ havanti jaṁ ēttha na hu cōjjaṁ

jaṁ kiñci asuhakammaṁ annabhavē sañciyaṁ tumē āsi

tassa vivāgāō imaṁ samāgayaṁ suyaṇu! guruvasaṇaṁ

tā annabhavaviḍhattē dukkhammi samāgayammi kō sōgō?

kiṁ vāvi vilaviēṇaṁ sarīrāyāsabhūēṇaṁ?

ēttō u samāsannē acchaï amhāṇa āsamō rammō

āgaccha suyaṇu! aṇuciyamēyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ jaō tujjha

vāyaï sīyalapavaṇō ēttha ō taṁ abhiṇavapasūyā si

sukumālasarīrāē mā hōjja virūvayaṁ kiñci

iya bhaṇiya tāvasīē nīyā haṁ āsamammi rammammi

paḍijaggiyā ya sammaṁ nikkāraṇavacchalattēṇa

aha kaïvayadivasēhiṁ sañjāyā satthadēhiyā maṇayaṁ

annammi diṇē nīyā tīē haṁ kulavaïsamīvē

tīēvi puvvabhaṇiō vuttantō sāhiō kulavaïssa

karuṇāparēṇa tēṇavi aṇusaṭṭhā mahuravayaṇēhiṁ

vacchē! iha saṁsārē sulahāiṁ ērisāiṁ dukkhāiṁ

akayammi suhanimittē dhammē paralōyabandhummi

jāyanti dūsahāiṁ jēṇaṁ ciya ēttha dusahadukkhāiṁ

tēṇēva cattarajjā vaṇavāsamuvāgayā dhīrā

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇassa u kulavaïṇō tīi tāvasīi ahaṁ

kannē hōuṁ bhaṇiyā bhayavaṁ varanāṇajuttō 'yaṁ

tō puccha icchiyatthaṁ bhaṇiyāē tāhi viṇayapaṇayāē

puṭṭhō maē mahāyasa! kēṇa hiō nandaṇō majjha?

kiṁ jīvaï ahava maō pikkhissamahaṁ kayāivi navatti?

aha bhaṇiyaṁ kulavaïṇā sammaṁ dāūṇa uvaōgaṁ

vacchē! ucchaṅgatthō tuha taṇaō avahiō u dēvēṇa

pāṇaviōyaṇahēuṁ puvvaviruddhēṇa kuddhēṇa

vēyaḍḍhagiriniuñjē nēūṇa silāyalammi viulammi

mukkō chuhābhibhūō kila kicchēṇēsa maraütti

aha kahavi vihivasēṇaṁ samāgaō tattha nahayarō ēkkō

niyabhāriyāsamēṇō tēṇa ya puttotti sō gahiō

khayarassa tassa gēhē vuḍḍiṁ jāhī suhēṇa, tattō ya

sampattajōvvaṇō sō milihī tuha hatthiṇapurammi

ēvaṁ ca tēṇa bhaṇiē paṇaṭṭhasōgā narinda! jāyā haṁ

phalamūlakayāhārā viṇayaparā tāvasijaṇassa

piya! kaïvayadivasāiṁ acchāmi tahiṁ tu āsamē jāva

tā annadiṇē kulavaï mūlē dhammaṁ suṇintīē

bahutāvasisahiyāē sahasā āsēṇa vēgajuttēṇa

avahariō sampattō rāyasuō tattha ēgāgī

aha atihivacchalēhiṁ tāvasakumarēhiṁ vihiyasaṁmāṇō

āgamma vihiyaviṇaō uvaviṭṭhō kulavaï samīvē

kulavaïṇā sō puṭṭhō kō si tumaṁ āgaō kuō bhadda!?

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kahēmi nisuṇēha bhayavaṁ! ti

siddhatthapurē rāyā suggīvō nāma āsi vikkhāō

kaṇagavaī sē dēvī tīē suō surahanāmō haṁ

aïvallahotti piuṇā juvarāyapayammi bālabhāvēvi

ahisittō avamanniya puttaṁ jiṭṭhaṁ tu suppaïṭṭhaṁ

aha annayā kayāivi khayavāhīē mayammi jaṇayammi

tassa paē haṁ rāyā ahisittō mantivaggēṇa

jiṭṭhassa annajaṇaṇītaṇayassa u tassa suppaïṭṭhassa

vijjāharēṇa kēṇavi kayaüvayārēṇa dinnāō

nahagāmiṇipamuhāō vijjāō tappabhāvaō tēṇa

kāūṇa ya saṅgāmaṁ ahiṭṭhiyaṁ appaṇā rajjaṁ

tassa bhaēṇa ahampi hu samāgaō puravarīē campāē

jaṇaṇisamēō pāsē māyāmahakittidhammassa

tēṇavi niyadēsantē dinnaṁ gāmāṇa sahassayaṁ ēgaṁ

tattha ya jaṇaṇīsahiō bhayavaṁ! acchāmi ahayanti

kaïvayadiṇēhiṁ intō imāi aḍavīi vāṇiyagasatthō

maha purisēhiṁ viluttō pattaṁ vittaṁ tahiṁ paüraṁ

annaṁ ca tattha pattā tukkhāraturaṅgamā bahuvihīyā

tāṇāvāhaṇahēuṁ ajjēva pabhāyasamayammi

bāhiṁ nīhariō haṁ kamēṇa turagē ō jāva vāhēmi

tāvikkēṇaṁ sahasā hariō vivarīyasikkhēṇa

aviya jaha jaha ōkkhañcijjaï taha taha vēgaṁ pagiṇhamāṇēṇa

bhayavaṁ! turagaṁmēṇa ihāṇiō āsamē tumha

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï sō surahō kulavaïssa vuttanta

turayamaṇumaggalaggaṁ tāva ya sinnapi sē pattaṁ

aha bhaṇiyaṁ surahēṇaṁ bhayavaṁ! vaccāmi niyayaṭhāṇammi

jaṁ kiñci maē iṇhiṁ kāyavvaṁ taṁ ca āisasu

aha kulavaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ gurujaṇapūyāidhammakaraṇammi

jahasattīi payaṭṭasu saraṇāgayavacchalattē ya

annaṁ ca bhadda! nisuṇasu ēsā rannō ya amarakēussa

dēvī gayaavahariyā acchaī kamalāvaī nāma

dūrē hatthiṇanayaraṁ sāvayapaürā ya duggamā aḍavī

halakiṭṭhamahīē tahā viyaranti na tāvasakumārā

tēṇa na ēsā sakkaï parāṇiuṁ niyapurammi amhēhiṁ

na ya kōvi tahārūvō annō iha āgaō satthō

ēsā sukumālataṇū acchaï kicchēṇa ittha vaṇavāsē

tā jaï tumaṁ parāṇasi saṭṭhāṇaṁ hōi tā laṭṭhaṁ

aha surahēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ! jaṁ bhaṇaha taṁ karēmitti

gantuṁ sayamēva ahaṁ appissaṁ amarakēussa

bhaṇiyāṁ haṁ kulavaïṇā vacchē! surahassa bhāsiyaṁ nisuyaṁ?

tā vaccasu saha imiyā annō puṇa dullahō satthō

aha cintiyaṁ maē kiṁ imēṇa saha hōi gamaṇamamhāṇaṁ

juggaṁ, ahavā jāṇaï bhayavaṁ ciya ēttha jaṁ uciyaṁ

iya cintiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ! jaṁ bhaṇasi taṁ karēmitti

jaï ēvaṁ tā vacchē! payaṭṭa, iha tēṇa bhaṇiyā haṁ

bahu manniya tavvayaṇaṁ tāhē caliyā narinda! tēṇa samaṁ

takkāluciyaṁ kāuṁ tāvasisambhāsaṇāīyaṁ

jāva ya kamēṇa pattā ēttha paēsammi tāva surahō sō

kimpi misaṁ kāuṇaṁ thakkō ētthēṇa raṇṇammi

āvāsiūṇa sinnaṁ diṇē diṇē ēi maha samīvammi

daṁsēi ya bahumāṇaṁ, aha annadiṇammi ēgantē

ghittuṁ āharaṇāiṁ maha pāsē āgaō bhaṇaï ēvaṁ

ēyāiṁ giṇha sundari! na sōhasē taṁ nirābharaṇā

taṁ dēvadinnakuṇḍalapamuhaṁ savvampi niyayaābharaṇaṁ

pariyāṇiūṇa vimhiyahiyāē maē imaṁ bhaṇiō

ēyāiṁ kuō tumaē pattāiṁ suraha! majjha sāhēsu

sō bhaṇaï suṇasu sundari! puvvaṁ maha bhillapurisēhiṁ

iha aḍavīi samiddhō kusaggapurapatthiō vaṇiyasatthō

gahiō tahiṁ ca pattaṁ ēyaṁ tuha jōggamābharaṇaṁ

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ maha santiyamēvamābharaṇamēyaṁ

siridattanāmagassa ō vaṇiyassa samappiyaṁ āsi

harisiyamuhēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jaï ēvaṁ tarihi sundarataranti

tā gēṇha imaṁ sundari! imassa jōggā tumaṁ nannā

aha tassa duṭṭhabhāvaṁ annāūṇaṁ tayaṁ maē gahiyaṁ

tattō ya païdiṇaṁ sō uvayaraï mamaṁ asuhabhāvō

āgacchaï ēgantē parihāsakahāō kahaï maha puraō

saviyāraṁ ca palōyaï daṁsaï aṇurattamappāṇaṁ

aha annadiṇē piyayayama! pāvēṇaṁ tēṇa mayaṇamụ̄dhēṇa

agaṇiya kulamajjāyaṁ ujjhiya lajjaṁ sudūrēṇa

bahu manniya avivēyaṁ bhaṇiyā ēgantasaṇṭhiyā ēvaṁ

vammahapīḍiyadēhō saraṇaṁ tuha suyaṇu! allīṇō

niyaaṅgasaṅgamēṇaṁ sahalaṁ mama kuṇasu jīviyaṁ ajja

tuha āyattā pāṇā savvassavi sāmiṇī taṁ si

tuha suyaṇu! kiṅkarō haṁ āṇākārī ya pariyaṇō savvō

gạ̄dhāṇurāgarattaṁ kiṁ bahuṇā icchasu mamanti

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ sahasā vajjēṇa tāḍiyāva ahaṁ

uppannagaruyadukkhā piyayama! cintāurā jāyā

hā! pāviṭṭhō ēsō balāvi sīlakhaṇḍaṇaṁ kāhī

saraṇavihūṇāi mamaṁ, tā iṇhiṁ kiṁ karēmitti?

nibbhatthāmi girāhiṁ sampaï aïniṭṭhurāhiṁ jaï ēyaṁ

tā ēsa amajjāyō iṇhimpi virūvayaṁ kujjā

tā sampaï mūyattaṁ juttaṁ avalambiuṁ taō pacchā

patthāvaṁ lahiūṇaṁ nāsissamimāō pāvāō

iya cintiya tuṇhikā ahōmuhaṁ kāuṁ tattha khakkā haṁ

sōvi ya daṭhṭhūṇa mamaṁ niruttaraṁ uṭṭhiō tattō

pattāē rayaṇīē nibbharasuttē ya sayalasinnammi

gahiūṇa tamābharaṇaṁ pāsāiṁ palōyaṇamāṇā

nihuyagaīē caliyā bhaēṇa kampantataṇulayā gāḍhaṁ

vañciya pāhariē haṁ nīhariyā tāō sinnāō

ghittūṇa ya ēgadisaṁ caliyā ghaṇataruvaṇassa majjhēṇaṁ

nisuṇantī bahusāvayabhīsaṇasaddē bahuvihī( ha? )ē

pavaṇākampiyapāyavacalantapattāṇa saṇasaṇārāvaṁ

sīhōrālisamāṇaṁ mannantī vēvirasarīrā

vēgēṇa ya gacchantī ghaṇandhayārāē tīē rayaṇīē

dīharaghaṇataṇaōcchāiyāē visamāē bhūmīē

aviyāṇiyaparamatthā jhaḍatti paḍiyā ya ēttha kūvammi

piyayama! kayabahupāvā jīvā iva ghōranarayammi

bhaviyavvayāvasēṇaṁ na mayā gambhīrajalanivuḍḍāvi

agaḍassa taḍiṁ pāviya tattha nilukkā ahaṁ rāya!

maraṇē uvaṭṭhiēvi hu sīlaṁ saṁrakkhiyanti tuṭṭhamaṇā

appāṇaṁ sakayatthaṁ mannantā surahabhayamukkā

gāḍhaṁ chuhābhibhūyā cattāri diṇāṇi ēttha kūvammi

paricattajīviyāsā ṭhiyā ahaṁ saraṇaparihīṇā

ajja puṇa kalayalēṇa sibiraṁ āvāsiyanti nāūṇa

surahāsaṅkāē puṇō samāulā nāha! sañjāyā

tattō kūvapaviṭṭhaṁ tumha naraṁ pāsiūṇa suṭṭhuyaraṁ

bhīyāi pucchiyāivi na uttaraṁ kiñci mē dinnaṁ

puṇaravi ya tumha nāmaṁ sōūṇaṁ vigayaannaāsaṅkā

harisabharanibbharaṅgī uttariyā dēva! kūvāō

ēyaṁ maē 'ṇubhūyaṁ saraṇavihuṇāē tumha virahammi

nisuēṇa jēṇa jāyaï dukkhaṁ pāsaṭṭhiyāṇampi

iya kamalāvaïbhaṇiyaṁ āyanniya amarakēunaranāhō

bāhajalāvilanayaṇō gurusōgō bhaṇiumāḍhattō

kiṁ dēva! ittha kīraï sakammavasayāṇa navari jīvāṇa

jāyanti dūsahāiṁ dukkhāiṁ ēttha saṁsārē

sakayaṁ suhamasuhaṁ vā ikkō aṇuhavaï vivihajōṇīsu

māyā piyā ya bhattā bandhujaṇō vāvi na hu saraṇaṁ

rāgaddōsavasāē asuhaphalaṁ āsi jaṁ kayaṁ kammaṁ

tassa vasāō sundari! sampattā vasaṇariñchōlī

ēvaṁ gaēvi jaṁ dēvi! ēttha kūvammi nivaḍiyā ēvaṁ

sampattā taṁ mannē anannapuṇṇōdaō kōvi

paḍikūḍakāriṇāvi hu vihiṇā vihiyaṁ tu ēttiyaṁ laṭṭhaṁ

jaṁ akkhayadēhāē tumaē saha saṅgamō vihiō

ēmāibahuvigappaṁ dēviṁ āsāsiūṇa sō rāyā

niyasinnēṇa samēō samāgaō gayapuraṁ kamasō

kāriyagaruyapamōō thuvvantō nayaranārinivahēṇa

kamalāvaīsamēō dāṇaṁ dēntō amarakēū

kayamaṅgalōvayārō nāyarajaṇajaṇiyahiyayaāṇandō

niyamandirē paviṭṭhō pakkalapāikkapariyariō

ēvaṁ ca tassa rannō adiṭṭhadukkhassa dēvisahiyassa

bōlīṇāiṁ kaïvi hu varisāṇaṁ sayasahassāiṁ

aha annayā kayāivi atthāṇagayassa rāiṇō tassa

paḍihārāṇunnāō samantabhaddotti nāmēṇa

ujjāṇammi niuttō pattō paṇamittu rāyapayakamalaṁ

sīsanivēsiyakarakamalasampuḍō harisiō bhaṇaï

puvvaṁ dēvēṇaṁ ahaṁ nēmittiyasumaïvayaṇayaṁ sōccā

kusumāyaraüjjāṇassa pālagattē niuttō mhi

taṁ ca tisañjhaṁ niccaṁ palōyamāṇassa ēttiō kālō

vōlīṇō na ya diṭṭhaṁ kiñcivi nēmittiyāiṭṭhaṁ

ajja puṇa appabhāē gayaṇē ujjāṇamajjhayārammi

kusumiyasāhisamūhaṁ iō taō picchamāṇēṇa

ēgammi disābhāē vallaravēllīsaṇāhadumagahaṇē

uttāsiyahaṁsaülō uṭṭhāviō saüṇasandōhō

nisuō vimhayajaṇaō bahiriyaāsannasattasuivivarō

muhariyadisāvibhāgō garuyakhaḍakkārasaṁsaddō

sōūṇa ya taṁ saddaṁ vimhiyaütphullalōyaṇēṇa maē

pulaïya tattōhuttaṁ cintiyamavvō! kimēyanti

kassa puṇa ēsa saddō samuṭṭhiō ēttha vaṇaniguñjammi

iya cintantō kōūhalēṇa tattōmuhō caliō

tāva ya diṭṭhā bhūpaṭṭhisaṇṭhiyā baülapāyavasamīvē

mucchānimīliyacchī adhariyasurasundarīrūvā

ahiṇavajōvvaṇaübbhēyasundarā sayalamaṇaharāvayavā

paümacuyā iva lacchī naravara! varabāliyā ēkkā

nūṇaṁ nahatthalāō nivaḍantīē imīē bhūmīē

juvaīē paḍisaddō samuṭṭhiō ēsa sahasatti

kaha mannē ērisassavi juvaīrayaṇassa ērisā 'vatthā

vibuhajaṇasōyaṇijjā dhī! vihiṇō vilasiyaṁ cittaṁ

iya cintantēṇa maē sīyalajalasīyarēhiṁ saṁsittā

miupavaṇakaraṇavihiṇā aha vihiyā sā samāsatthā

hariṇivva jūhabhaṭṭhā sataralatāraṁ disāō pulayantī

bhaṇiyā maē sumahuraṁ kīsa tumaṁ suyaṇu! bīhēsi?

mā bhaddē! kuṇasu bhayaṁ thēvampi, hu jaṇayanivisēsō haṁ

kā si tumaṁ kattō vā iha paḍiyā majjha sāhēsu?

aviya saggāō nivaḍiyā kiṁ sāvappahayā suraṅgaṇā taṁ si

kiṁ vāvi bhaṭṭhavijjā vijjāharabāliyā suyaṇu!?

tuharūvadaṁsaṇuppannaharaṇabuddhissa nahapayaṭṭassa

vijjāharassa kassavi kiṁvā hatthāō pabbhaṭṭhā?

sāhēsu suyaṇu! ēyaṁ mahantakōūhalaṁ imaṁ majjha

nīsāhārā kaha nahayalāō paḍiyā ihujjāṇē?

iya sā bhaṇiyā bhūnāha! majjha paḍiuttaraṁ adāūṇa

gurudukkhasūyaṇaparaṁ aṁsujalaṁ mōttumāraddhā

aha taṁ tahāvihaṁ pāsiūṇa paricintiyaṁ maē ēyaṁ

taṁ ēyaṁ sañjāyaṁ jaṁ puvvaṁ sumaïṇā bhaṇiyaṁ

kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïyā gayaṇāō kannagā paḍihī

tattō ya sigghamēva hi puttēṇa samāgamō hōhī

tā kiṁ iha puṭṭhāē imāē, tāva sāhēmi

gantuṁ vaïyaramēyaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ cēva naravaïṇō

iya cintiūṇa tattō āsāsittā sumahuravayaṇēhiṁ

āṇīyā niyagēhē samappiyā sā sabhajjāē

niyapariyaṇaṁ ca savaṁ sarīrasaṁvāhaṇāivāvārē

tīē niuïūṇaṁ samāgaṁō dēvapāsammi

ēvaṁ samantabhaddēṇa sāhiyaṁ vaïyaraṁ nisāmittā

vimhiyahiyaō rāyā aha ēvaṁ bhaṇiumāḍhattō

avvō! hu avitahaṁ taṁ picchaha nēmittiyassa sumaïssa

tā puttēṇa samāṇaṁ āsannaṁ daṁsaṇaṁ iṇhiṁ

tā bhō samantabhaddaya! sigghaṁ āṇēha bāliyaṁ tamiha

jīē pabhāvēṇa maē pikkhēyavvō saputtōti

vayaṇāṇantaramēva hi samantabhaddēṇa gantumāṇīyā

sā bāliyā viṇijjiyasurajuvaīrūvasōhaggā

tīē sarīrasōhaṁ picchiya rannā vicintiyaṁ avvō

āgārō ciya sūyaï imīē sukulammi sambhūiṁ

uciyāsaṇōvaviṭṭhā sā kannā amarakēunaravaïṇā

bhaṇiyā hiyayabbhantaragurusōgu vvāyapaṇḍumuhā

vacchē! ujjhasu sōyaṁ cayasu bhayaṁ jaṇayanivisēsassa

sāhijjaü maha ēyaṁ kammi purē taṁ samuppannā?

kassa va dhūyā kaha vā ihāgayā kaha va majjha ujjāṇē

paḍiyā si nahayalāō sāhēsu savittharaṁ ēyaṁ

aha sā ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā gurusōyā sajjhasēṇa abhibhūyā

ummukkadīhasāsā na kiñci paḍiuttaraṁ dēi

aha puṇaruttaṁ rannā puṭṭhāē tīē kahavi saṁlattaṁ

tāya! caēmi na vōttuṁ bahudukhaṁ niyayavuttantaṁ

tahavi hu alandhaṇīyā āṇā tāyassa tēṇa sāhēmi

jambuddīvē bharahē kusagganayarammi nāmēṇa

atthi puraṁ supasiddhaṁ tattha ya naravāhaṇō puhaïnāhō

rayaṇavaī sē dēvī tīē dhūyā ahaṁ tāya!

surasundarittināmā puvviṁ duvvihiyakammapariṇāmā

vēriyasamēṇa kēṇaï pisāyarūvēṇa avahariyā

ēttiyamittaṁ bhaṇiuṁ sōyasamubbhuyagarumannuvasā

thūlaṁsuē muyantī nihuyaṁ rōuṁ pavattā sā

ētthantarammi rannō addhāsaṇasaṅgayāē dēvīē

kamalāvaīē gahiyā rōvantī sā nijucchaṅgē

bhaṇiyā vacchē! mā ruya na hōi dīvantaraṁ imaṁ suyaṇu!

hatthiṇapuraṁ hi ēyaṁ ēsō rāyā amarakēū

kamalāvaī ahampi hu, sahōyarō hōi tuha piyā majjha

vacchē! tumampi amhaṁ suyapuvvā nāmamēttēṇa

bahuvihapaōyaṇēṇaṁ kusagganayarāō jō jaṇō ēntō

sō savvō surasundari! tuha guṇanivahaṁ maha kahintō

ēvaṁ surūvakaliyā ēvaṁ piuṇō ya vacchalā bāḍhaṁ

ēvaṁ kalāsu kusalā ēvaṁ dakkhinnadayajuttā

tā mā kuṇasu visāyaṁ ēyampi ya piuharaṁ nijaṁ tujjha

acchasu vīsatthamaṇā kīḍantī vivihakīḍāhiṁ

ēvavihavayaṇēhiṁ āsāsittā nijuttarīēṇa

aṁsuyadhōyakavōlaṁ tīē muhaṁ sampamajjittā

muhasōyaṁ dāūṇaṁ nīyā dēvīē mandirē niyaē

tatthavi uvviggamaṇā acchaï gurusōyasantattā

nīsasaï dīhadīhaṁ khaṇēṇa thūlaṁsuyāiṁ millēi

mucchijjaī khaṇēṇaṁ khaṇēṇa saṁvaraï appāṇaṁ

vilavaï khaṇēṇa vihasaï rōvaï khaṇēṇa mūyalliyā hōi

gurucintābharavihuriyahiyayā parihāi aṇudiyahaṁ

aha taṁ vigatayāṇandaṁ picchiya kamalāvaī vicintēi

āṇākārī savvōvi pariyaṇō tāva ēīē

taha ya samāṇavayāō siṇēhasārāō rāyakannāō

nāṇāvihacēṭṭhāhiṁ aṇudiyahamimaṁ viṇōēnti

tahavi hu raïṁ na pāvaï ēsā cintāē susaï aṇudiyahaṁ

tā mannē kā cintā jīē ēsā u parihāi

jaï tā māupiūṇaṁ sumaraï tā kiṁ kahēi na hu majjha?

mayaṇaviyārasaricchā nēya viyārā tahiṁ hunti

ēgantaṁ jaha sēvaï vihaḍiyacakkāiṁ jaha ya mēllēi

piyasaṅgamasārāō kahāō jaha suṇaï taccittā

taha mannē pēmmagahō vilasaï ēvaṁvihāhiṁ ciṭṭhāhiṁ

tā jaha ēsā majjhaṁ tahaṭṭhiyaṁ sāhaï sarūvaṁ

tā tassa pāvaṇammivi kōvi uvāōvi labbhaē nūṇaṁ

na ya ēsā vajjarihī puṭṭhāvi jahaṭṭhiyaṁ majjha

vāmasahāvō mayaṇō akkhijjantō na pāyaḍō hōi

najjaï āgārēhiṁ gōvijjantōvi chēēhiṁ

tahavi hu lahāmi kēṇavi handi! uvāēṇa bhāvamēīē

iya cintiya āṇattā niyacēḍī haṁsiyā nāma

surasundarīi uvvēvakāraṇaṁ lahasu haṁsiē! kahavi

tujjha samāṇavayāē sāhissaï hiyayasabbhāvaṁ

jaṁ āṇavēsi sāmiṇi! iya bhaṇiuṁ haṁsiyā gayā jhatti

ēgantaṭṭhiyasurasundarīē pāsammi allīṇā

sabbhāvanēhasūyagēvīsambhakahāhiṁ vivihabhaṇiīhiṁ

uppāiya vīsambhaṁ bhaṇiyā surasundarī tīē

surasundari! tuha cariyassa nisuṇaṇē atthi kōugaṁ majjha

kaha kēṇa kiṁ nimittaṁ avahariyā kiñca aṇubhūyaṁ?

surasundarīē bhaṇiyaṁ tāēṇavi āsi pucchiyā ēva

kiṁ puṇa lajjāē maē na sakkiyaṁ tattha vajjariuṁ

kiñca maha cariyaṁ summantaṁ jaṇēī pāsaṭṭhiyāṇavi dukkhaṁ

tēṇa na vōttuṁ majjhavi gurudukkhasañjaṇagaṁ

tahavi hu tumaē puṭṭhā vayaṁsi! kōūhalēṇa garuēṇa

sāhēmi tēṇa nisuṇasu ēgamaṇā vajjarijjantaṁ

atthi puhaīpayāsaṁ niraggalōdaggavaggiraturaṅgaṁ

vaggiraturaṅgakharakhurukkhayakhēhāinnarikkhapahaṁ

rikkhapahapavaṇakampiradhayavaḍarēhantabhūrisāṇūraṁ

sāṇūragahiravajjiratūraravupphuṇṇādisicakkaṁ

disiccakkagēyasatthāhasatthakijjantavajjavāṇijjaṁ

vāṇijjakalāpattaṭṭhalaṭṭhavāṇiyagaramaṇīyaṁ

ramaṇīyaṇavaravajjiranēurajhaṅkāraruddhasuivivaraṁ

vivarīyarayaviyakkhaṇavilāsiṇīlōyapaḍipunnaṁ

punnukkaḍajaṇavāsaṁ ibbhasahassōvasōhiyaṁ viulaṁ

viularasāyalaparigayaparihāpāyārasōhillaṁ

sōhillatiyacaükkaṁ ukkaḍadappiṭṭhajōhasayakaliyaṁ

nāmēṇa kusaggapuraṁ nayaraṁ diyalōyasāricchaṁ

akkantaguruparakkamaaccantukkaḍapayāvapaḍivakkhō

tatthatthi suvikkhāō rāyā naravāhaṇō nāma

tassa ya rannō mittō kumārabhāvammi kahavi sañjāō

vēyaḍḍhakuñjarāvattacittabhāṇussa aṅgaruhō

nāmēṇa bhāṇuvēgō tēṇa ya pīīthirattaṇanimittaṁ

dinnā niyayā bhagiṇī rayaṇavaī nāma ēyassa

sayalantēurapavarā jāyā sā tassa hiyayavallahiyā

tīi saha visayasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavamāṇassa kālēṇaṁ

ēkkacciya dhūyā haṁ jāyā jammammi majjha tāēṇa

suyajammaṇaabbhahiō nayarammi mahōcchavō vihiō

surasundarisamarūvā ēsā iha cintiūṇa tāēṇa

surasundaritti nāmaṁ païṭṭhiyaṁ uciyasamayammi

kamasō pavaḍḍhamāṇā kumārabhāvammi juvaïjōggāō

gāhāviyā kalāō jāyā ya kamēṇa takkusalā

aviya vittē naṭṭē gīē pattacchējjē ya hatthakaṇḍēsu

vīṇāsaralakakhaṇavañjaṇēsu vāyaraṇatakkēsu

jāyā viyakkhaṇā haṁ buddhīē suragurussa sāricchā

ēkkammi paē laddhē sēsaṁ ūhēmi laddhīē

ambāē tāyassa ya sayalassa ya pariyaṇassa āṇandaṁ

kuṇamāṇā sampattā kamasō haṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ

daṭhṭhūṇa jōvvaṇaṁ maha tāō cintāurō daḍhaṁ jāō

kō aṇurūvō hōhī bhattā iha majjha dhūyāē?

aha annayā ya sumaī nēmittī āgaō tahiṁ rannā

puṭṭhō maha dhūyāē kō hōhī bhadda! bhattārō?

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa naravara! vijāharacakkavaṭṭiṇō ēsā

hōhī sayalantēurapavarā aïvallahā dēvī

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ maṇammi āṇandaēṇa tāēṇa

dāūṇa bhūridavvaṁ paṭṭhaviō sumaïnēmittī

aha annayā ya ahayaṁ pariyariyā bahuvihāhiṁ cēḍīhiṁ

niyasahiyaṇasañjuttā pattā purabāhirujjāṇē

tattha ya vivihapagāraṁ kīḍantīē tadēgadēsammi

diṭṭhā paḍhamavayatthā vijjāharabāliyā ēkkā

parijaviya kiñci mantaṁ uppaïumaṇā pasāraï bhuyāō

ullalaï nahayalammi nivaḍaï dharaṇīi puṇaruttaṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ vimhiyā haṁ sampattā tīi antiyaṁ turiyaṁ

bhaṇiyā ya maē sundari! kā si tumaṁ kiñca kuṇasi imaṁ?

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhaddē! āyannasu, girivarammi vēyaḍ̣dhē

dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīē rayaṇasañcayaṁ atthi varanayaraṁ

vijjāharavaracakkī rāyā tatthatthi cittavēgotti

rāyā ya bhāṇuvēgō atthi purē kuñjarāvattē
