tassa ya dō bhagiṇīō sahōyarāō ya aīva iṭṭhāō

paḍhamā ō bandhudattā rayaṇavaī nāma bīyā u

sā suyaṇu! bandhudattā pariṇīyā cittavēganaravaïṇā

tīē dhūyā ahayaṁ nāmaṁ ca piyaṁvayā majjha

annāvi mahādēvī tāyassa u atthi kaṇagamālatti

tīē ya atthi puttō nāmēṇaṁ mayarakēutti

sō maha aīva iṭṭhō virahaṁ na sahāmi tassa nimisampi

sampaï puṇa tāēṇaṁ dinnāō tassa vijjāō

vijjāṇa sāhaṇatthaṁ pasattakhittammi sō gaō vijaṇē

jahabhaṇiyavihāṇēṇaṁ sāhaï sō tattha vijjāō

vaṭṭaï bīō māsō vijjāō tassa sāhayantassa

ahamavi tassa viōgē tarāmi nō jāva acchēuṁ

tā pucchiūṇa jaṇagaṁ caliyā haṁ tassa darisaṇanimittaṁ

āgamaṇaparissantā ōinnā ittha ujjāṇē

ahiṇavapạdhiyattaṇaō vijjāē kahavi majjha payamēgaṁ

pamhuṭṭhamahannāē tēṇa ya na caēmi uppaïuṁ

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ ēyaṁ sāhiyaṁ suyaṇu! tujjha

vijjāvayassa bhaṁsē saṭṭhāṇaṁ kahaṇu pāvissaṁ?

puṇaruttampi hu pạdhiē sambharaï na majjha taṁ payaṁ kahavi

uttaṭṭhamayasilimbacchi! tēṇamahamāulājāyā

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvaē! atthi tīi vijjāē

ēsō kappō jaṁ kila sāhijjaï handi! annassa!

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē sāhijjaï natthi kōvi dōsotti

jaï ēvaṁ tā sāhasu mā (mē) kahavi payaṁ uvalabhijjā

ēvaṁ ca maē bhaṇiē samāṇasiddhitti tīi bhaṇiūṇa

ṭhāūṇa kannamūlē pạdhiyā saṇiyaṁ tu sā vijjā

tattō citantīē lahumēva maē tayaṁ payaṁ laddhaṁ

lahiūṇa tīē siṭṭhaṁ bhavaï imaṁ kiṁ nu ēvanti?

viyasiyamuhakamalāē tīē bhaṇiyaṁ suṭṭhu uvaladdhaṁ

calaṇēsu nivaḍiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ maha hōsi taṁ guruṇī

jīē vijjhā dinnā, tā maha sāhēsu tujjha kiṁ nāma?

ēttha purammī kassa va dhūyā taṁ sukayapunnassa?

majjha sahīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhaddē! naravāhaṇassa naravaïṇō

rayavaṇaïdēvīē dhūyā surasundarī ēsā

accabbhuyaguṇaniyarā kiṁ na suyā sayalalōyavikkhāyā

vijjāharadhūyāē dhūyā surasundarī bhaddē!?

ēvaṁ tīē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisabāhapuṇṇacchī

gahiūṇa mama kaṇṭhē piyaṁvayā bhaṇiumāḍhattā

ambāē majjha puvviṁ vajjariyaṁ āsi, majjha lahubhagiṇī

bhūmicaramittassa u rannō maha bhāuṇā dinnā

tā māusiyādhūyā bhagiṇī taṁ hōsi majjhaṁ candamuhi!

iya jampiūṇa dinnaṁ tīē maha sāiyaṁ garuyaṁ

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ āgacchasu bhagiṇi! majjha gēhammi

bandhujaṇavacchalāē ambāē daṁsaṇaṁ kuṇasu

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē pikkhissaṁ māusiṁ paḍiniyattā

kāraṇavasēṇa sampaï gacchissaṁ bhāuyasamīvaṁ

itthatthē nibbandhaṁ mā kāhisi ucchugā ahaṁ iṇhiṁ

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvanti ya kintu pucchāmi

kiñcivi, taṁ maha sāhasu, tīē bhaṇiyaṁ tu puccha, sāhēmi

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē bhaddē! kakkhāē gōviē ēttha?

cittapaḍē kiṁ acchaï lihiyaṁ, cittammi kōugaṁ majjha

tā daṁsijjaü ēyaṁ jaï jōggaṁ daṁsiuṁ bhagiṇi!

viyasiyamuhāi tīē pasāriuṁ daṁsiō paḍō amha

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tīi isō maē sahatthēṇa lihiutti

tattha ya paḍammi lihiyaṁ daṭhṭhūṇamaṇaṅgasaṁnibhaṁ taruṇaṁ

amaēṇava sittā haṁ jāō hiyayassa āṇandō

cirapariciyavva diṭṭhō diṭṭhī āṇandabāhapaḍihatthā

jāyā savvasarīrē samuṭṭhiō bahalarōmañcō

phuraphuriyaṁ aharēṇaṁ ullasiyaṁ bhuyalayāhiṁ sahasatti

ūsasiyaṁ ca thaṇēṇaṁ tharahariyaṁ ūrujuyalēṇaṁ

suttāva mucchiyā iva mattā iva vigayacēyaṇā jāyā

sōhaggamandiraṁ taṁ daṭhṭhūṇaṁ cittalihiyampi

nāūṇa majjha bhāvaṁ vasantiyāē sahīi saṁlattaṁ

kō ēsa taē lihiō piyaṁvaē! lōyaṇāṇandō?

bhaṇiyamaha kumuiṇīē vasantiē! kiṁ tuhittha pucchāē?

kāmiṇihiyayāṇandō lihiō raïvirahiō mayaṇō

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō sirimaïyāē sahīē saṁlattaṁ

ēttiyakālaṁ raïvirahiō imō āsi pañcasarō

sampaï raīē sahiō ēsō mayaṇotti kiṁ na pulaēsi?

payaḍā raīvi ēsā āsannā cēva ēyassa

taṁ sōuṁ savvāhiṁ sahatthatālaṁ tu pahasiuṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

ēvaṁ ēyaṁ sirimaï! sammaṁ hi viṇicchiyaṁ tumaē

aha laddhacēyaṇāē vinnāyā hanti jāyalajjāē

āgāraṁ viṇigūhiya sakōvamēvaṁ maē bhaṇiyaṁ

hambhō! aliyapalāviṇi! daṁsaṇamittampi natthi ēēṇa

kattō āsannattaṁ jēṇa kayā haṁ raī tumaē?

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ mā sahi! rūsasu, diṭṭhammi jēṇa ēyammi

cittammi raī jāyā tēṇa raī taṁ maē bhaṇiyā

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē kiṁvā asamañjasabhāsiṇīhiṁ ēyāhiṁ

tāva ya, piyaṁvaē! kahasu ēsa kō vā taē lihiō?

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē bhāyā maha ēsa mayarakēutti

rūvēṇa jō aṇaṅgō sūrō cāī kalākusalō

kaïyāvi cittaphalaē kaïyāvi paḍammi tassa paḍirūvaṁ

lihiūṇa maē appā viṇōiō ēttiyaṁ kālaṁ

sampaï puṇa asamatthā sahiuṁ virahaṁ imassa caliyā haṁ

tā bhagiṇi! muñca vaccāmi jēṇa pāsammi tassēva

bhaṇiyaṁ ca sirimaīē ēvaṁ jō garuyaguṇagaṇāvāsō

sō tuha bhāyā

cittagaēṇavi tāva ya āṇandō sahijaṇassa sañjaṇiō

iṇhiṁ paccakkhampi hu daṁsijjaō amayabhūō sō

vihasiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē bhaṇiyaṁ mā sahi

aviya jaï tāva kāvi hu ahaṁ tā 'vassaṁ tassa saṅgamēṇa suhaṁ

kāyavvaṁ bhagiṇīē aṇukūlō jaï vihī hōhī

bhaṇiyaṁ ca maē tāva ya ēyāō havantu aliyabhaṇirīō

piyasahi! tumampi sampaï asamañjasabhāsiṇī jāyā

aïniuṇaṁ kilaṁ citta amhē kōūhalēṇa pulaēmō

tumhē saḍhahiyayāō annaha savvaṁ viyappēha

aha kumuiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti natthi sandēhō

tā sahi! tumampi ēvaṁ cittaṁ lihiuṁ samabbhasasu

appēsu paḍaṁ ēyaṁ piyaṁvaē! jēṇa cittamabbhasaï

tuha bhagiṇī, aha tīē samappiō kumuiṇīi paḍō

sambhāsiuṁ tāhiṁ piyaṁvayā sā taō mamaṁ uppaïyā nahaggē

sahīhi juttā bahukēliyāhiṁ ahampi pattā niyamandirammi

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï piyaṁvayādaṁsaṇotti nāmēṇa

surasundarīkahāē ēkkārasamō paricchēō

aha tattha suvitthinnē pasatthavatthōhavihiyaüllōcē

gantuṁ niyavāsagihē pāsuttā pavarasayaṇīē

bhaṇiyāō ya sahīō vaccaha savvāō niyayagēhēsu

maha kuṇakuṇāi sīsaṁ sīyanti ya savvaaṅgāiṁ

jaragahiṁyava sarīraṁ tā sōvissaṁ khaṇantaraṁ ēgaṁ

tattō ya kumuiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ karēsutti

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō vajjariyaṁ sirimaīē kiṁ bhagiṇi!

sahasā jāyamasatthaṁ tuha dēhaṁ, kāraṇaṁ bhaṇasu?

bhaṇiyaṁ vasantiyāē sirimaï! taṁ cēva vēccayaṁ muṇasi

tā cintēsu sayaṁ ciya rōgassa nidāṇamēyassa

aha sirimaīi majjhaṁ saṁ dhāṇāiṁ niēva sāsūyaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ na kimpi tāva ya lakkhijjaï bajjhavittīē

aviya duvihā saṅkhēvēṇaṁ sārīrā ' 'gantuyā ya rōgatti

aha vāyapittasimbhubbhavā ya, iha ādimā nēyā

tāṇaṁ maṅkhaṇalaṅghaṇanivāyasēvāiyā cigicchāō

vējjayasatthuddiṭṭhā purisaṁ kālaṁ na nāūṇa

bhūyagahacakkhusāgiṇidōsā āgantuyā muṇēyavvā

balihōmamantatantāiyā hu vivihā cigicchā siṁ

sārīriyarōgāṇaṁ na lakkhaṇaṁ kiñci dīsaï imīē

tā nūṇaṁ āgantuyadōsō takkijjaī nannō

uttārijjaü lōṇaṁ hakkārijjantu vivihagāruḍiyā

sarisavaghāō dijjaü bajjaü taha rakkhapōṭṭaliyā

aha laliyāē bhaṇiyaṁ tā kiṁ sigghaṁ na kīraē ēyaṁ

vāhī uvikkhiō jaṁ na hōi iha sundarō bhaddē!

tō sirimaïē bhaṇiyaṁ lakkhēmō amhi kēvalaṁ vāhiṁ

na uṇō paüṇīkāuṁ sattā aha māhavī bhaṇaï

lakkhaï jō kira vāhiṁ paüṇampi hu sō karissaē pattaṁ

jēṇiha diṭṭhā cōrā paharayamavi dēha sō nūṇaṁ

nihuyaṁ hasiūṇa taō savvāhivi saharisaṁ samullaviyaṁ

sirimaï! iṇhi na chuṭṭasi amha sahiṁ jaṇasu paüṇanti

annaṁ, sa tujjha jaṇaō suprasiddhō mantajāṇaō suyaṇu!

tā vāhiūṇa mantaṁ paüṇaṁ surasundariṁ kuṇasu

aha sirimaīi bhaṇiyaṁ jaï maha jaṇaō viyāṇaī mantē

tā kiṁ maha, jaï miṭṭhaṁ khīraṁ tā kiṁ nu chāṇassa?

kimpuṇa bhaṇāmi ikkaṁ jaï maha ēsā na rūsaē sahiyā

ēsa aüvvō vāhī na phiṭṭaē mantamēttēṇa

aha kumuiṇīē bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ puṇa kōvassa kāraṇaṁ ēttha?

sāhēsu nivvisaṅkā vigamō vāhīē jaï hōi

tō sirimaīē bhaṇiyaṁ jō sō cittammi vilihiō diṭṭhō

sō jaï navaraṁ vējjō vāhiṁ avaṇijja ēiē

aha cittapaḍaṁ sahasā pasāriyaṁ pūiūṇa tō bhaṇaï

kumuiṇiyā! jaï ēvaṁ, tā ēyaṁ handi! vinnavaha

īsiṁ hasiūṇa taō savvahivi saharisaṁ samullaviyaṁ

ēvanti, pañjaliuḍā bhaṇiuṁ ēyaṁ samāḍhattā

dakkhinnanihi! mahāyasa! cittaṭṭhiya! suṇasu amha viṇṇattiṁ

tuha daṁsaṇāō ēsā amha sahī āurā jāyā

tā taha karēsu sundara! jaha ēsā hōi vigayavāhīyā

guru mayaṇāmayasampīḍiyāṇa mahilāṇaṁ taṁ vijjō

huṅkāraṁ mōttūṇaṁ tāhiṁ sakōvaṁ maē imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ

māē! gahagahiyā iva kimasambaddhaṁ samullavaha?

kiṁ vāvi acittēṇaṁ vinnaviēṇaṁ guṇō imēṇaṁ tu

cittagaō nahi katthavi kōvi hu uppāyaē vāhiṁ

aha sirimaīē bhaṇiyaṁ tuha cittagaō imō hu jēṇēva

tēṇēva ya accittā vihiyā surasundari! tumanti

dīhaṁ nīsasiūṇaṁ tāhē saṇiyaṁ maē samullaviyaṁ

jaï ēyampi viyāṇasi tā kiṁ na sampāḍasi jhati?

iya bhaṇiūya ahōmuhavayaṇā vilihāmi jāva mahivaṭṭhaṁ

tāva ya sahatthatālaṁ hasiuṁ tīē samullaviuṁ

sabbhāvasāhagēṇaṁ imēṇa vayaṇēṇaṁ rañjiyā suyaṇu!

tā taha karēmi sampaï jaha savvaṁ sōhaṇaṁ hōi

iya bhaṇiuṁ cittapaḍaṁ gahiuṁ pāsammi sā gayā jhatti

maha jaṇaṇīē tattō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō

cittapaḍavilihiō sō aṇaṅgarūvō payaṁsiō taruṇō

tīēvi gantuṁ rannō siṭṭhō savvōvi vuttantō

aha tāō taṁ cittaṁ palōiüṁ harisiō imaṁ bhaṇaï

sōhaṇaṭhāṇē rāgō sañjāō majjha dhūyāē

ahavā na rāyahaṁsa mōttuṁ annattha ramaï varahaṁsī

tassēva varissāmō sāhiyavijjassa niyadhūyaṁ

taha bhāṇuvēgakhayarō amha samīvammi ēi aṇavarayaṁ

tēṇēva varissāmō niyadhūyaṁ amarakēussa

iya naravaïṇā bhaṇiē pahasiyavayaṇāē majjha jaṇaṇīē

bhaṇiyā sirimaī gantuṁ sāhijjaü majjha dhūyāē

mā surasundari! iṇhiṁ uvvēvaṁ kuṇasu niyayacittammi

siddhaṁ samīhiyaṁ tuha iya bhaṇiyā sirimaī tāhē

majjha samīvē pattā siṭṭhō savvōvi puvvavuttantō

ahayampi harisiyamaṇā maṇayaṁ jāyā samāsatthā

cintēmi kahaya hōhī taṁ diyahaṁ jattha sō maē sakkhā

daṭṭhavvō nayaṇucchavabhūō maṇavallahō lōō?

tassaṅgamaāsāē sāhārantīē māṇasaṁ niyayaṁ

taṁ cēva cittakammaṁ ālihamāṇā ya aṇudiyahaṁ

susiṇiddhasahijaṇēṇaṁ tappāvaṇasūyagēhiṁ vayaṇēhiṁ

jāva ya kaïvi diṇāī ṭhiyā ahaṁ saṇṭhavijjantā

tāvannammi diṇammī parihiyavaraṇāō camariyāhatthā

kayagōrōyaṇatilayā nāhiyasatthēsu nimmāyā

parivāiyā u ēgā āsīvāyaṁ karēttu amhāṇaṁ

puraō uvavisiūṇaṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiṁu samāḍhattā

jaharuiyaṁ uvabhujjaï iṭṭhaṁ rāmijjaē imaṁ sāraṁ

jamhā na kiñci vijjaï annaṁ ihalōgavaïrittaṁ

siratuṇḍamuṇḍaṇāiṁ paralōgatthaṁ kuṇantu jē kēvi

tē varayā varadhuttēhi vañciyā visayasōkkhāṇaṁ

jamhā jīvapayatthō vijjaï annō na dēhavaïrittō

paccakkhapamāṇēṇaṁ aggahaṇā kharavisāṇaṁva

paccakkhaṁ mōttūṇaṁ na ya annaṁ atthi iha pamāṇaṁ tu

santēvi pamāṇattē na sijjhaï tēṇa jīvotti

paccakkhapuvvagaṁ jaṁ aṇumāṇaṁ iha, na tēṇa taggahaṇaṁ

na ya vijjaï taggahaṇē liṅgampi aṇindiyattaṇaō

lōyapavañcaṇahēuṁ dhuttēhiṁ kayāṇi vivihasatthāṇi

na pamāṇaṁ vibuhāṇaṁ kaha tēhiṁ bhavijja tassiddhī?

tā pañcabhūyasamudayarūvō jīvō na tēsiṁ vigamammi

tassābhāvammi kuō paralōgō jēṇa ya tadatthaṁ

kīraï aïduddharayaṁ bambhavvayasīlapālaṇāīyaṁ

mụ̄dhēhiṁ sayaṁ naṭṭhēhiṁ taha paraṁ nāsayantēhiṁ

gammāgammavibhāgaṁ mōttuṁ visayāṇa sēvaṇaṁ kuṇaha

bhakkhaha sarasaṁ maṁsaṁ piyaha suraṁ vigayaāsaṅkā

iya tīē buddhilāē vayaṇaṁ sōūṇa kugaïsañjaṇagaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ maē ahammē! mā mā ēvaṁ samullavasu

vibuhajaṇanindaṇijjaṁ aviyāriyasundaraṁ ajuttīyaṁ

kō va sakannō ēyaṁ tuha bhaṇiyaṁ saddahējjāvi?

jaṁ bhaṇasi natthi jīō annō dēhāō, aṇuvaṁlabhāō

tamasaṅgayamaccatthaṁ, jamhā jīvassa aggahaṇaṁ

kiṁ tuha paccakkhēṇaṁ uyāhu nīsēsapurisavisaēṇaṁ?

na ya tāva paḍhamapakkhō vissābhāvappasaṅgāō

jaṁ jaṁ tumaṁ na picchasi taṁ taṁ jaï natthi tā phuḍaṁ muddhē!

dēsantarakālantarabhāvāṇamabhāvayā pattā

aha sayaladēsakālubbhavā narā nēya taṁ palōinti

ēyaṁ ca kaha ṇu najjaï durahigayā annacittā jaṁ?

kiñca jo cciya imaṁ vigappaï tuha dēhē handi! natthi jīvotti

sōvi ya jīvō paralōgagāmiō nāṇaliṅgotti

paccakkhamēva ēgaṁ jaṁ ca pamāṇaṁ, na juttamēyampi

paccakkhaparōkkhāiṁ dunnēva jaō pamāṇāiṁ

lōyapayāraṇahēuṁ iccāiṁ jamuttamahalamēyampi

rāgaddōsavimukkā savvannū savvalōgahiyā

tēhi paṇīyaṁ satthaṁ tēsiṁ āṇāi jaṁ ca annēhiṁ

kaha taṁ dhuttapaṇīyattaṇēṇa hōjjāpamāṇanti?

tammi ya bhaṇiō jīvō annabhavō tassa hōi paralōgō

tā pañcabhūyasamudayarūvō jīvō kahaṁ muddhē!?

siddhammi ya paralōgō bambhavvayapālaṇāiṁ savvampi

tabbhaṇiyaṁ tā juttaṁ kāuṁ savvaṁ hiyatthīṇaṁ

gammāgammavibhāgaṁ iccāiṁ jamuttamahalamēyampi

jiṇavayaṇanisiddhattā paralōē dukkhahēuttā

ēmāivivihajuttīhiṁ sā kayā takkhaṇaṁ niruttariyā

jāyā vilakkhavayaṇā asamatthā uttaraṁ dāuṁ

aha pāsavattiṇīhiṁ avahasiyā sahīhiṁ sōluṇṭhaṁ

ṭakkaraṭumbayamuhamakkaḍāhiṁ bāḍhaṁ abhiddaviyā

amha sahīē saddhiṁ ajjavi vāyaṁ karēsi dussīlē!

tā vaccasu saṭṭhāṇaṁ diṭṭhaṁ paṇḍiccayaṁ tujjha

iya hasiyā sā ruṭṭhā phurantaaharā viṇiggayā tattō

ahamavi sahijaṇajuttā suhēṇa jā tattha acchēmi

tā annadiṇē rāyā samāgaō majjha māugēhammi

bhaṇiō ambāē kiṁ dīsaha cintāurā tubbhē?

tāēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ sammaṁ hi viyāṇiyaṁ tumē dēvi!

nisuṇēsu kahijjantaṁ gurucintākāraṇaṁ jamiha

surasundarīē vuddhilanāmā parivāiyā jiyā vāē

jā puvvaṁ kila tīē paüṭṭhacitāē ālihiyaṁ

surasundarīi rūvaṁ cittapaḍē tāhi taṁ gahēūṇaṁ

ujjēṇīē pattā sattuñjayanaravaïsamīvē

taṁ daṁsiya naravaïṇō vajjariya tīē duṭṭhahiyayāē

naravara! amhē puhaïṁ hiṇḍāmō tumha kajjēṇa

jaṁ rayaṇaṁ puhaīē picchāmō taṁ ca tumha sāhēmō

kannārayaṇaṁ ēyaṁ kusagganayarē maē diṭṭhaṁ

naravāhaṇassa rannā dhūyā surasundarī imā kannā

kō tīē niravasēsaṁ lihiuṁ sakkijja taṇurūvaṁ?

aviya

savvaṁ ciya sō thērō jēṇēsā nimmiyā payāvaïṇā

kahamannahā na vihiyā suhakhāṇī attaṇō bhajjā?

ēyaṁ viṇimmiuṁ laḍaharūvatāruṇṇacārusōhaggaṁ

nūṇaṁ aïbahumāṇō viriciṇō āsi attāṇē

dhaṇuhāyaḍḍhaṇakhinnaṁ mayaṇaṁ nāūṇa hiyayabhēyakarā

mannē vihiṇā vihiyā ēsā naṇu hatthabhallivva

annaṁ ca jō imīē pāṇiggahaṇaṁ karissaī purisō

sō bharahaddhanarīsō hōhī purisō na sandēhō

iya aïsayanāṇīhiṁ āiṭṭhaṁ tīi jammasamayammi

tā naravara! tuha jōggā sā kannā na uṇa annassa

aha bahudaviṇaṁ dāuṁ pahaṭṭhavayaṇēṇa tēṇa sā rannā

bhaṇiyā bhayavaï! siṭṭhā jaṁ kannā sōhaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ

ēyaṁ ca majjha sundari! siṭṭhaṁ savvampi cārapurisēhiṁ

aha tēṇa majjha pāsē paṭṭhaviō rayaṇacūḍotti

nāmēṇa niyayamantī tēṇa ya āgamma maggiō ahayaṁ

sattuñjayanaravaïṇō dijjaü surasundarī kannā

bhaṇiyō ya maē ēsō nēmittiyasumaïvayaṇaō bhadda!

hōhī khayarassa piyā tassēva ya tēṇa dāyavvā

annaṁ, sō tuha sāmī thērō tā kintha tassa kannāē?

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mā ēvaṁ bhaṇasu naranāha!

guruāyarēṇa ahayaṁ paṭṭhaviō tēṇa dēsu niyadhūyaṁ

ēīē adāṇēṇaṁ picchāmi na sundaraṁ tumha

tattō ya maē gāḍhaṁ kuddhēṇaṁ ērisaṁ samullaviyaṁ

tāva ya na dēmi dhūyaṁ jaṁ ruccaï taṁ kuṇējjāsu

tā gacchasu niyapahuṇō sāhijja jahaṭṭhiyaṁ imaṁ vayaṇaṁ

gihamāgayassa kō puṇa tuha daṇḍō kīraü iṇhiṁ?

aha tēṇa tattha gantuṁ kahiē sō niyabalēṇa gāraviō

ujjēṇīō caliō amhāṇaṁ uvari jattāē

aviya

bahubhaḍanarindasandaṇapakkalapāikkacakkapariyariō

kharakhurakhayakhōṇīyalaasaṅkhatōkkhāralakkhajuō

dappiyapayaṇḍaparahatthisatthavittāsaṇikkarasiēhiṁ

gurugirigaruyāgārēhiṁ saṅgaō bahugaïndēhiṁ

sō sattuñjayarāyā gururōsō bhūrisinnasañjuttō

cārapurisēhiṁ siṭṭhaṁ sampattō amha dēsētti

tā dēvi! nimittēṇaṁ imēṇa cintāurō ahaṁ jāō

ambāē taō bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama! kiṁ ēttha cintāē

surasundariti bhaṇiuṁ dhūyā kaṇagāvalīē mayalēhā

dijjaü kayasaṁmāṇō saṭṭhāṇaṁ jēṇa sō jāi

iharā pabhūyasēnnō appabalāṇaṁ sa amha dēsassa

kāhī garuyamuvaddavamiya bhaṇiē rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ

mantīhivi dēvī! imaṁ vimantiyaṁ āsi navari mantissa

maïsāgarassa ēsō na sundarō bhāviō mantō

jaṁ tēṇa imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ āgacchaü tāva sō kusaggammi

iha āgayassa jamhā maraṇaṁ sē sumaïṇā siṭṭhaṁ

annaṁ ca tassa rannō niggamaṇē āsi maṅgulā saüṇā

ajayāvahā ya savvē saṇiccharāī gahā dhaṇiyaṁ

iha āgayammi tammī vijaō amhaṁ parājaō tassa

tā dēva! nivvisaṅkā acchaha kiṁ annamantēṇa?

rōhagasañjuttī uṇa kīraü gāmāvi tassa jē maggē

tē uvvasantu khippaṁ tiṇaghāsāī ya ujjhantu

ḍhakkijjaü kūvāī kujalāiṁ sarōvarāiṁ kīrantu

pasaranivāraṇahēuṁ sasāhaṇaṁ tattha vayaütti

iya dēvi! mantivayaṇaṁ kāriya savvampi āgaō ēttha

pabalattaṇaō sattussa tahavi cintāurō jāō

aha haṁsiṇi! jā kaïvi hu suhēṇa vaccati tattha divasāiṁ

tā annadiṇē nayaraṁ pavẹ̄dhiyaṁ sattusinnāē

taō pihiāiṁ gōurāiṁ jalēṇa paripūriyāō parihāō

saṁnaddhabaddhakavayā païkavisīsaṁ ṭhiyā jōhā

saṁvā(cā) rimajantāiṁ paüṇīkīranti, vivihasatthāiṁ

tikkhalijjanti tahā kīraï suhaḍāṇa sammāṇō

padadiyahaṁ dijjanti ya ukkālā sattusinnamaïgamma

nivaḍanti suhaḍakarisurayanaravarā ubhayapakkhēvi

saṁsaïyā sāmantā nāyarayā āulā daḍhaṁ jāyā

kiṅkāyavvavimụ̄dhā jāyā taha mantiṇō amha

bhīyā kāyarapurisā saṅgarakaraṇammiuddhurā suhaḍā

sāhasadhaṇō ya tāō sandhīraï sumaïvayaṇēṇa

ēvaṁ haṁsiṇi! jāē samantaō āulammi nayarammi

aha annadiṇē ahayaṁ pāsuttā hammiyatalammi

rayaṇīē kēṇāvi hu hīrantaṁ appayaṁ pulōittā

paḍibuddhā bhayabhīyā vilaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattā

hā ammi! tāya! kōvi hu dēvō vā nahayarō va maṁ haraï

dhāvaha dhāvaha suhaḍā! imāō mēllāvaha mamanti

ēmāiṁ vilavamāṇā bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa suyaṇu! mā bhāhi

nō tujjha kiñci virūvaṁ karēmi pāṇappiyā taṁ si

tuha rūvadaṁsaṇuppannagaruyaaṇurāyaparavasēṇa maē

hariyā si kīsa sundari! bhayabhīyā ēvamullavasi?

vēyaḍḍhanaganivāsī khayarō haṁ suyaṇu! mayarakēutti

bhuñjihisi maē saddhiṁ bhōē kiṁ ruyasi uvviggā?

ēyaṁ ca tassa vayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisiyā ahaṁ cittē

kiṁ nāma majjha daïō ēsō sō mayarakēutti?

bhāyā piyaṁvayāē jassa tayā cittavilēhiyaṁ rūvaṁ

daṭhṭhūṇa mayaṇavasagā jāyā ummattiyā ahavā

sō ajjavi vijjāō sāhaï tā āgamō kaha ṇu tassa?

kaha maha ittiyapunnā jaṁ sō dīsijja paccakkhaṁ?

ēmāiṁ cintayantī nīyā haṁ tēṇa katthavi paēsē

ōinnā bhūmīē mukkā haṁ kayaligahaṇammi

ētthantarammi rayaṇī khayaṁ gayā sāhiuṁva paramatthaṁ

sammaṁ niyaccha vacchē! na hōi sō vallahō ēsa

jāē pabhāyasamaē diṭṭhō sō sāmalēṇa dēhēṇa

tattō gurusōgāē vicintiyaṁ hā! na sō ēsō

sō tattakañcaṇanibhō rūvēṇa aṇaṅgarūvasāricchō

cittagaēṇa imassa jō sāricchaṁ natthi thēvampi

tā kiṁ karēmi iṇhiṁ saraṇavihūṇā paravvasā ahayaṁ

iya cintatīē tayā bhaēṇa kampō samuppannō

aha sō daṭṭhūṇa mamaṁ aṁsujalāsārasittagaṇḍayalaṁ

bhayabhīyaṁ kampantiṁ ēvaṁ bhaṇiuṁ samāḍhattō

kiṁ suyaṇu! tumaṁ bīhasi bhūyapisāuttisaṅkirī majjha

nisuṇasu jō haṁ jēṇa va hariyā kajjēṇa ya mayacchi!

vēyaḍ̣dhē varanayaraṁ gaṅgāvattanti atthi suprasiddhaṁ

tattha ya rāyā sirigandhavāhaṇō āsi vikkhāō

mayaṇāvalīdēvīē taṇaō nahavāhaṇotti sē āsi

bīō ya mayarakēū taïō puṇa mēhanāutti

nahavāhaṇōvi sāhiyavijjō aha jōvvaṇaṁ tu sampattō

variyā ya tannimittaṁ varakannā kaṇagamālatti

sā uṇa vivāhasamaē vijjāharacittavēganāmēṇa

avahariuṁ pariṇīyā ruṭṭhō ēsō taō tassa

aṇumaggaṁ gantūṇaṁ baddhō sō nāgiṇīē vijjāē

gahiūṇa kaṇagamālaṁ samāgaō niyayanayarammi

tattō vijjācchēō jāō nahavāhaṇassa jēṇēsō

mahilāsamēyavijjāharassa jāō 'vagāritti

cirapariciyadēvēṇaṁ dinnāō cittavēgakhayarassa

vijjāō tēṇa jāō vijjāharacakkavaṭṭī sē

sayamēva nahayarindā savvēvi hu paṇaïmuvagayā tasya

iya muṇiuṁ maha jaṇaō saṁviggō bhaṇiumāḍhattō

picchaha bhō! maṇuyāṇaṁ maṇōrahā annahā visaḍḍhanti

vihiṇō vasēṇa navaraṁ annaha kajjāṇa pariṇāmō

kira niyataṇayaṁ kāuṁ vijjāharacakkavaṭṭiṇaṁ, karihī

kayakiccō pavvajjaṁ kēvalijaṇayassa pāsammi

taṁ puṇa annaha jāyaṁ tā kiṁ kajjaṁ imēṇa rajjēṇaṁ

narayāinimittēṇaṁ, sēvāmō tāyapayajuyalaṁ

jaō

saṁsārō hu asārō ghōrā aïdāruṇā ya narayammi!

dusahāō viyaṇāō cittō kammāṇa pariṇāmō

cavalō indiyagāmō rāgaddōsā ya dujjayā lōē

aṇavaṭṭhiyaṁ ca cittaṁ kimpāgaphalōvamā visayā

aïdusahō piyavirahō bammahalaliyaṁ vivāyakaḍuyanti

narayapuravattiṇīō sēvijjantāō juvaīō

kusasūivisamasaṇṭhiyapavaṇāhayasalilacañcalaṁ jīyaṁ

sāmannaṁ savvēsiṁ maraṇaṁ sattāṇaṁ saṁsārē

vañcaṇaparā ya jīvā duṭṭhakasāēhiṁ tāviō lōō

asuhaphalō gharavāsō maṇuyattaṁ taha ya nō sulahaṁ

dulahā dhammammi maī bahuvigghasamāulaṁ ahōrattaṁ

payaīē calā lacchī pēmmaṁ suviṇōvamaṁ lōē

āriyakhēttāīyā aïdulahā sampayā ya jiyalōē

aïdāruṇamannāṇaṁ jīvā micchattavāmụ̄dhā

parihāyantā bhāvā dhammē aïnindiō pamāutti

khijjaï taṇusāmatthaṁ āuyamavi thōvayaṁ hōi

kiṁ bahuṇā?

nārayatiriyanarā 'maragaīsu gurudusahadukkhataviyāṇa

mōttūṇaṁ jiṇadhammaṁ jiyāṇa saraṇaṁ jaō nannaṁ

tamhā tāyasamīvaṁ gantuṁ sahalīkarēmi maṇuyattaṁ

nahavāhaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ahamavi tāyamaṇugamissaṁ

jaō

sāmittaṁ kāūṇaṁ āṇāniddēsakāragassāvi

kaha sēvaṁ kāhāmō sampaï bhiccassa niyayassa?

bhaṇiyaṁ tāēṇa taō kāyavvamimaṁ vivēyajuttāṇaṁ

tattō niyasuyasahiō takkāluciyaṁ karēūṇa

suravāhaṇakēvaliṇō mūlē kāūṇa nimmalacarittaṁ

niṭṭhaviyaaṭṭhakammō antagaḍō kēvalī jāō

aha cittavēgakhayarāhivēṇa tatthēva niyayanayarammi

dāuṁ sadēsakhaṇḍaṁ ahisittō khayararāyā haṁ

ēvaṁ ca ṭhiē kāraṇavasēṇa kēṇaï pabhāyasamayammi

niyanayarā ēgāgī caliō haṁ rayaṇadīvammi

nahapaṭṭhiēṇa diṭṭhā sundari! hammiyatalammi pāsuttā

taṁ si taō avahariyā mēttalasarasalliēṇa maē

tā mā rōvasu sundari! pāṇāṇavi sāmiṇī tumaṁ majjha

bhuñjihisi maē saddhiṁ bhōē vēyaḍḍhasēlammi

tavvayaṇaṁ sōuṇaṁ vajjēṇava tāḍiyā sudukkhattā

iya cintiuṁ payattā hāhā! maha pāvapasarassa

majjha kaēṇaṁ tāō pāraddhō garuyasattuṇā tāva

ahamavi imēṇa hariyā annattha nibaddharāgāvi

dhā! maha! jīēṇaṁ na tāyaāsāsaṇaṁ na piyalābhō

sattuñjayadinnāē hōjja suhī tāva tāōvi

maṇavallahassa tassa u lābhēṇa havijja ahava suhiyā haṁ

maha pāvapariṇaīē ēttō ēkkampi nō jāyaṁ

ēvaṁ vicintayantī bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa tāva ētthēva

ciṭṭhaü tumaṁ jāva ahaṁ āsannē vaṁsigahaṇāmmi

gantūṇaṁ vijjāē pannattīē lahuṁ payacchāmi

jāvasahassamēttaṁ pārambhiyapuvvasēvāē

iya bhaṇiūṇa gaō sō ahamavi gurusōyatāviyā tattha

kiṅkāyavvamụ̄dhā saraṇavihūṇā bhayuppitthā

hariṇivva jūhabhaṭṭhā sataralatāraṁ disāō pulayantī

aṁsujalapunnanayaṇā ruyamāṇī jāva ciṭṭhāmi

tāva ya tatthāsannaṁ picchāmi visālasālasōhillaṁ

pavaṇākampiyaphalabharavinamiyaguñjōhasaṅkinnaṁ

maṇahariphalaṁ pasarantaparimalaṁ bahalapattalacchāyaṁ

tapphalabhakkhaṇanivaḍantajantusantāṇakayasadda

nivaḍantasasantataḍapphaḍantamayavihagakaliyabhūvīḍhaṁ

taruyaramuccaṁ maccuṁ jantusantāṇanāsayaraṁ

taṁ daṭṭhuṁ visarukkhaṁ vicintiyaṁ garuyadukkhataviyāē

piyasahi! haṁsiṇi! taïyā maraṇammi nibaddhacittāē

kiṁ kāhāmi ahannā rahiyā piyabandhujaṇaṇijaṇaēhiṁ

vihiṇā viḍambiyā haṁ jīvantī iya vicintēntī

gantuṁ tassa samīvē gahiūṇa phalaṁ muhammi pakkhittaṁ

mā maha havijja ērisaviḍambaṇā annajammēvi

iya bhaṇiūṇa sasōyaṁ khaṇantaraṁ jāva tattha acchāmi

tāva ya guruvisaviyaṇāē vibbhalā mahiyalē paḍiyā

taō bhamiyaṁva vaṇatarūhiṁ uvvattiyayaṁva sayalavasuhāē

sandhīhiṁ vihaḍiyaṁ piva visīiyaṁ savvaaṅgēhiṁ

tattō ya akahaṇīyaṁ pāviyavatthantaraṁ tayā bhaddē!

jāṇāmi nēva kiñcivi taduttaraṁ jaṁ mahaṁ jāyaṁ

kēvalamucchaṅgagayaṁ kassavi taruṇassa amayabhūyassa

visanivvavaṇasamatthaṁ maṇisalilaṁ pāyayantassa

khaṇamēttaṁ tēna ciya majjha sarīraṁ pasiñcamāṇassa

sayamaṅgāiṁ kōmalakarēhiṁ parimaddayantassa

jalasittatālavēṇṭayahatthāē vihiyasisiravāyāē

ciradiṭṭhaṁ piyasahīē piyaṁvayāē kahijjantaṁ

sayalaṁ maha vuttantaṁ cittapaḍālōyaṇāipajjantaṁ

harisabharapulaïyaṅgaṁ khaṇantaraṁ nisuṇamāṇassa

appāṇaṁ pāsittā paṇaṭṭhavisavēyaṇā samāsatthā

sumiṇaṁva mannamāṇā paḍibuddhā haṁsiē! taïyā

ummīliyanayaṇajuyā tāva ya pēcchāmi mayaṇapaḍirūvaṁ

mahahiyayaniggayaṁ piva taruṇanaraṁ cittasaṁvāiṁ

taṁ daṭṭhu cintiyaṁ mē kiṁ mannē indajālamēyanti?

kiṁ vāvi annajammō uyāhu kiṁ suviṇayaṁ ēyaṁ?

kiṁvā maïsaṁmōhō kiṁvāvi hu saccamēva ēyanti?

ahavā nahi nahi ēyaṁ kattō maha ittiyā punnā?

jaṁ sō maṇavallahaō dīsijja jaṇō imēhiṁ nayaṇēhiṁ

jaṁ sē ucchaṅgagayā imassa puṇa sambhavō kattha?

ēvaṁ vicintayantī piyaṁvayāē imaṁ samullaviyā

surasundari! kiṁ ajjavi uvvuṇṇamuhivva pulaēsi?

ēsō hu rayaṇadīvō bhagiṇī ya piyaṁvayā ahaṁ tujjha

sāhiyavijjō ēsō maha bhāyā mayarakēutti

ēvaṁ ca tīē bhaṇiē ēsōcciya sotti harisiyā cittē

sajjhasavēviradēhā saṅkinnarasantaraṁ pattā

uṭṭhēttu tadaṅkāō piyaṁvayāē samīvamallīṇā

addhacchipēcchiēhiṁ pēcchittā taṁ apēcchantaṁ

ētthantarammi ēgō khayarō āgamma bhaṇaï kayaviṇaō

jiṇapūyāē vēlā samaïcchaï kumara! uṭṭhēha

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ piyaṁvayaṁ ṭhāviuṇa maha pāsē

kaïvayapurisamēō jiṇabhavaṇaṁ pāviō ēsō

tāva ya piyaṁvayāē puṭṭhā kaha suyaṇu! ēttha taṁ pattā

bhūmīcaramaṇuyāṇaṁ suduggamē rayaṇadīvammi?

kīsa va visamuvabhuñjiya appā vasaṇammi pāḍiō bhīmē?

tattō ya maē tīē puvvuttaṁ sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

aha sāvi maē puṭṭhā cittapaḍaṁ appiūṇamamhāṇaṁ

taïyā kattha gayā taṁ kiṁvā aṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ tumaē?

kaha vā uvabhuttavisā bhīmaarannammi pāviyā ahayaṁ?

kaha vā duṭṭhampi visaṁ khaṇēṇa dēhāō avaṇīyaṁ?

bhaṇiyaṁ piyaṁvayāē cittapaḍaṁ appiūṇa tumhāṇa

vēgēṇa ahaṁ pattā imammi vararayaṇadīvammi

diṭṭhō ya mayarakēū kaïvayaniyapariyaṇēṇa sañjuttō

bhāusiṇēhēṇa ṭhiyā kaïvayadivasāṇi ahamēttha

ētthāgayatāēṇaṁ bhaṇiyā haṁ putti! ciṭṭhasu ihēva

hōsu paḍicārigā iha tāva tumaṁ mayarakēussa

jaṁ āṇavēi tāutti jampiyaṁ tāhē ēttha dīvammi

vijjapasāhaṇujjayabhāusamīvē ṭhiyā suyaṇu!

nāuṁ vijjāsiddhiṁ bahuvihakhayarēhiṁ sañjuō tāō

aṭṭhāhiyānimittaṁ samāgaō ēttha dīvammi

mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ jiṇindamahimaṁ karēttu vijjāō

sampūiya jahavihiṇā saṁmāṇiya māṇaṇijjajaṇaṁ

pūittu pūyaṇīē dāṇaṁ dāūṇa khayaralōyassa

varanaṭṭagīyavāiyakaliyaṁ aṭṭhāhiyaṁ kāuṁ

ajjēva nisāviramē sampattō rayaṇasañcayaṁ tāō

kāyavvasēsakiccō ṭhiō ihaṁ mayarakēūvi

kāuṁ pabhāyakiccaṁ sarīracintāē niggaō ajja

vaṁsikuḍaṅgāsannē diṭṭhaṁ ca pahāṇakaravālaṁ

gahiūṇa kōugēṇaṁ jamajīhāsacchahaṁ tayaṁ khaggaṁ

taruṇatamāladalābhaṁ phurantadhārāsuduppicchaṁ

āsannakuḍaṅgīē chēyaparicchākaēṇa sahasatti

dāuṁ ēgapahāraṁ chinnā sā vaṁsajālitti

aha thūlamuttiyāvalipariyattaṇakhaṇiyavāmahatthassa

vijjāparijavaṇaniruddhanāsiyānimiyanayaṇassa

tammajjhadēsaparisaṇṭhiyassa vijjāpasāhaṇarayassa

vijjāharassa kassavi maṇikuṇḍalabhūsiyakavōlaṁ

sahasatti uttimaṅgaṁ nivaḍantaṁ picchiūṇa mahivaḍ̣dhē

sañjāyasajjhasēṇaṁ nirūviyaṁ hā! kimēyanti?

pulayantēṇa ya nāyaṁ ēsō sō mayarakēunāmotti

sāmī gaṅgāvattassa gandhavāhaṇanarindasuō

avvō! pamāyavasaō kaha varaō māriō niravarāhō?

dhī! dhī! annāṇassa u niratthayaṁ pāvamāyariyaṁ

ēmāi cintayantō puṇō puṇō appayaṁ ca nindantō

jā vayaï thōvabhūmiṁ tā phuriyaṁ dāhiṇaṁ nayaṇaṁ

kiṁ mannē maha sūyaï sunimittamimanti cintaï jāva

tāva visarukkhamūlē diṭṭhā taṁ nivaḍiyā suyaṇu!

maṇaharasayalāvayavaṁ miyaṅkalēhavva jaṇamaṇāṇandaṁ

daṭhṭhūṇa tumaṁ sundari! sittō amaēṇava kumārō

avvō! kaha ṇu mayāvi hu āṇandaṁ dēi majjha hiyayassa?

piyapaṇayiṇivva ēsā juvaī navajōvvaṇārambhā

tā kiṁ imā mayacciya kiṁvā sajiyatti jāva pulaēi

tāva ya tuhamuhasaṇṭhiyavisaphalakhaṇḍēṇa vinnāyaṁ

aïtivvavisaviyārā jāyā ō acēyaṇā imā bālā

tō nēūṇa saṭṭhāṇaṁ karēmi ēīi tēgicchaṁ

iya cintiya surasundari! gahiūṇa tumaṁ samāgaō ēttha

siṭṭhō puvvuddiṭṭhō vuttantō tēṇa maha savvō

bhaṇiyā ya ahamimēṇaṁ ̣dhōēsuṁ tamaṅgulīyayaṁ sigghaṁ

vijjāpayāṇasamaē tāēṇa samappiyaṁ jaṁ tu

taṁ divvamaṇisaṇāhaṁ nivāraṇaṁ sayaladōsapasarassa

uvaladdhapaccayaṁ puṇa visēsaō visasamūhammi

bhaṇiyā khayarakumārā pūyāsāmaggiyaṁ lahuṁ kuṇaha

ēyaṁ paüṇīkāuṁ jiṇapūyaṁ tāhi kāūṇa

kāhāmi santikammaṁ vigdhajayaṭṭhā ya mantajāvaṁ ca

vijjāharavāyāyaṇapāvavisuddhiṁ samicchantō

ētthantarammi ya maē samappiyaṁ aṅgulīyayaṁ tassa

tassalilapāṇavihiṇā kayā pasatthā tumaṁ suyaṇu!

jāva ya imassa puraō cittapaḍālōyaṇāivuttantaṁ

sāhēmi tāva sundari! uvaladdhā cēyaṇā tumaē

taṁ jaṁ tumaē puṭṭhaṁ taṁ savvaṁ sāhiyaṁ maē ēyaṁ

tā surasundari! siddhaṁ samīhiyaṁ tujjha savvampi

ahavā

dīvantaraṭhiyampi hu jalanihimajjhāō dūradēsāō

āṇittu ghaḍēi vihī aṇukūlō iṭṭhalōyanti

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu nisuṇēsu

majjha kaēṇaṁ tāō acchaï gurusattupāraddhō

piyadaṁsaṇēvi jāē ajjavi sōgāuraṁ daḍhaṁ hiyayaṁ

piyasahi! maha santāvō tēṇajjavi bāhaē dēhaṁ

sattuñjayapāraddhō vaṭṭaï pāṇāṇa saṁsaē tāō

tā kaha aṇukūlattaṁ vihiṇō maha mandabhāgāē?

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ haṁsiṇi! sōgāvēgāō rōumāraddhā

tāva ya kayakāyavvō samāgaō tīē sō bhāyā

bhaṇiyā ya tēṇa kimiyaṁ piyaṁvaē! ruyaï tujjha piyabhagiṇī

tīēvi savvaṁ sōyassa kāraṇaṁ tassa akkhāyaṁ

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sundari! mā rūya avassamajjēva

gantuṁ kayantavayaṇaṁ nayāmi tuha jaṇayapaḍivakkhaṁ

jīvantē maï sundari! kō tuha jaṇayaṁ parābhavējjati?

tā gacchissaṁ sampaï bāhusahāō ahaṁ tattha

ētthēva paḍhamajinavarabhavaṇammi piyaṁvayāsamēyāē

acchēyavvaṁ tumaē jahāsuhaṁ sōyarahiyāē

jāvāgacchāmi ahaṁ hantuṁ sattuñjayaṁ durāyāraṁ

iya bhaṇiūṇuppaïō gayaṇaṁ vasunandakhaggakarō

sahiyā piyaṁvayāē tatthēva ṭhiyā ahampi taddivasaṁ

cintēntī tassēva ya samāgamaṁ garuyaaṇurāyā

kiṁ ajjavi maṇadaïō sahasā hantūṇa taṁ durāyāraṁ

vijjāpayāvakaliōvi āgaō nēya sō jhatti

vōlīṇammi ya divasē rayaṇiṁ savvampi bhagiṇisahiyā haṁ

kiṁ puṇa na āgaō sotti jāva ciṭṭhāmi uvviggā

tāva ya kharapharusagiraṁ tajjitō bhīsaṇō sarūvēṇa

niddhūmasihisihāvalipiṅgaladhammillavikarālō

jiyadasaṇacchayadasaṇō karagganarasirapaṇaccaṇikkaraō

marukūvavivarasarisā ' 'piṅgalalōyaṇasuduppicchō

galatalavilaïyakhalakhalakhalintanaramuṇḍamāliyākaliō

taḍipuñjujjalacañcalanillāliyadīhajīhālō

bhīmaṭṭahāsapaḍiravaüttāsiyasayalasattasaṅghāō

kasiṇō vigarālamuhō vēyālō āgaō tattha

ā pāvē! jaṁ taïyā parapurisāsattamāṇasāē tumē

parajuvaïlōluēṇaṁ tēṇa ya pāviṭṭhapurisēṇa

maha vihiyaṁ gurudukkhaṁ tassa phalaṁ tēṇa pāviyaṁ tāva

iṇhiṁ tumampi pāvasu niyaciṭṭhiyasacchahaṁ phalanti

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇō sō haṁsiṇi! ghittuṁ mamaṁ bhayuppitthaṁ

uppaïō gayaṇēṇaṁ niṭṭharavayaṇēhiṁ tajjētō

maha aṇumaggavilaggaṁ akkōsintiṁ piyaṁvayaṁ sahasā

kāuṁ gayajīviyaṁ piva bhīsaṇahuṅkārakaraṇēṇaṁ

nēūṇa dūradēsaṁ mukkā gayaṇāō tēṇa pāvēṇa

sañcunniyaṅguvaṅgā nūṇaṁ maraütti buddhīē

daïvavasēṇa ya paḍiyā layāviyāṇammi tammi ujjāṇē

diṭṭhā samantabhaddēṇa tāhi puṭṭhā ya vuttantaṁ

kiṁ indayālamēyaṁ kiṁvā sumiṇanti kattha vā pattā

kattha gaō vēyālō piyaṁvayāē ya kiṁ jāyaṁ?

maṇavallahassa imiṇā havējja vihiyaṁ asōhaṇaṁ kiñci

mannē tēṇēva lahuṁ na āgaō tammi sō dīvē

kiṁvā majjha nimittaṁ samāgaēṇaṁ havijja vihiyaṁ tu

sattuñjayanaravaïṇā thōvabalassēha tāyassa?

ēmāi cintayantīi tāhiṁ gurusōyatāviyāē maē

pucchantassavi siṭṭhaṁ samantabhaddassa nō kiñci

tattō ya āṇiyā haṁ bhūvaïpuraō samantabhaddēṇa

sajjhasasōēhiṁ tahimpi tārisaṁ kiñci nō kahiyaṁ

iya payaḍiyaṁ gujjhaṁ nēhasārāi tujjhaṁ niyacariyamēvaṁ haṁsiē! savvamēyaṁ

aïgaruyasiṇēhā sāhiyaṁ vittharēṇaṁ paṇayaparavasāē pucchiyaṁ jaṁ taïtti

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisahapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï surasundariharaṇavannaṇō nāma

surasundarīkahāē bārasamō varaparicchēō

aha haṁsiyāē bhaṇiyaṁ avvō! aïdūsahaṁ samaṇubhūyaṁ

jaṁ kila nisuṇantāṇavi uppajjaï garuyaüvvēvō

ēvaṁvihadukkhāṇaṁ na ya uciyā hōsi piyasahi! tumanti

kiṁ puṇa kīraï vihiṇō vicittacariyassa lōyammi?

niccaṁ suhōciyampi hu bahuvihadukkhāṇa kuṇaï āvāsaṁ

addiṭṭhaïṭṭhavirahampi virahiyaṁ kuṇaï daïēṇa

iya surasundari! vihiṇō vicittayaṁ jāṇiūṇa uvvēvaṁ

thēvampi hu mā kāhisi, kō ṇu guṇō tassa karaṇēvi

annaṁ ca jārisāiṁ tuha dēhē lakkhaṇāiṁ dīsanti

taha hōyavvaṁ tumaē vijjāhararāyapattīē

annaṁ ca maēvi suyaṁ kusagganayarāō āgayanarēṇa

kamalāvaïdēvīē puraō ēvaṁ kahijjantaṁ

sattuñjayanaravaïṇā ruddhē nayarammi āulē lōē

nahavāhaṇanaranāhē saṁsaïbhūē sasāmantē

ghāsindhaṇahāṇīē kicchēṇacchantayammi puralōē

jantavimukkamahōvalanihāyanivaḍantapāyārē

paṭaüḍivivarasaṇṭhiyakōddāligakhayapaḍantakhaṇḍīsu

dhaṇusu(mu)haviṇiggayāṇēyapattipacchāiyanahaggē

iya nayarammi kusaggē nivaḍantabhaḍōharuhiracikkhallē

sahasā phurantakhaggō samāgaō khēyarō ēgō

tēṇa ya gaïndaparisaṇṭhiyassa sattuñjayassa khaggēṇa

sahasā sīsaṁ chinnaṁ phurantarōsāruṇacchēṇa

hantūṇa ya taṁ sattuṁ rannō naravāhaṇassa pāsammi

āgamma tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nihaō sattū tuha narinda!

vijjāharahariyāē rayaṇaddīvē ṭhiyāē dhūyāē

tujjha surasundarīē vayaṇāō āgaō ahayaṁ

siricittavēgataṇaō khayarō haṁ mayarakēunāmotti

pāsē piyaṁvayāē tuha dhūyā acchaï suhēṇa

iya bhaṇiūṇa gaō sō rannā uṇa harisiēṇa niggantuṁ

sabalēṇa sattusinnē palāyamāṇammi pahurahiē

gayarahaturaṅgamāiṁ gahiyaṁ savvampi davvasāraṁ sē

tā surasundari! piyasahi! tatthatthē kuṇasu mā cintaṁ

jamhā sō tuha jaṇaō tujjha piēṇēva nibbhaō vihiō

ahiṇavasāhiyavijjassa tassa kiṁ kāhii pisāō?

jāyaṁ havijja aha kāraṇantaraṁ kimpi tujjha daïyassa

tavvasaō sō piyasahi! na āgaō jhatti taṁ dīvaṁ

ēmāiniuṇavayaṇēhiṁ tīē āsāsiyā narindasuyā

jāyā vimukkagurusōgavēgiyā ' 'ṇandapaḍihatthā

aha haṁsiyāē savvaṁ gantuṁ kamalāvaīē dēvīē

siṭṭhaṁ tīēvi rannō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

surasundarīē ēvaṁ piubhagiṇinikēyaṇē vasantīē

antēuravilayāṇaṁ alamāṇandaṁ jaṇantīē

vaccanti vāsarāiṁ suhēṇa jā kaïvi, tāva annadiṇē

abbhintaraparisāē kaïvayaniyapurisasahiyassa

surasundarisahiyāē dēvīē saṅgayassa naravaïṇō

paḍihāraaṇunnāō rannō aïvallahō vaṇiō

bhāsurarayaṇasupūriyathālakarō āgaō kayapaṇāmō

dhaṇadēvō nāmēṇaṁ uvaviṭṭhō rāiṇō puraō

uvaṇīyadarisaṇīyō sasambhamēṇēva rāiṇā bhaṇiō

bhō bhō dhaṇadēva! tumaṁ āsi gaō siṁhaladdīvaṁ

tā kaha ṇu lahu niyattō kusalaṁ pōyassa kiñci nō jāyaṁ

jāyaṁ vigghaṁ jēṇiha samāgaō māsamēttēṇa?

bahudivasapāvaṇijjē tammi gaō siṁhalammi dīvammi

sigghaṁ jaṁ si niyattō mahantamacchērayaṁ ēyaṁ

bhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ āyannasu naravarinda! vuttantaṁ

jaha tattha gaō sigghaṁ samāgaō ēttha nayarammi

siṅghaladīvāgayavāṇiēhiṁ pōcchāhiō iō tāva

caliō taduciyabhaṇḍaṁ ghittūṇa bahuppagāramahaṁ

tumhāṇa pāyajuyalaṁ paṇamiya bahusayaḍasatthasañjuttō

gambhīranāmayaṁ taṁ pattō vēlāulaṁ viulaṁ

aviya nāviyajaṇapaḍipunnaṁ paüṇīkīrantajāṇavattō haṁ

pūgaphalanāliērāirāsirēhantarāyapahaṁ

gayadantapālikaliyaṁ gayavaïvayaṇaṁva katthaï vibhāi

katthaï kappūrāgurucandaṇasahiyaṁ suragirivva

muttāhāravirāiyamahīvīḍhaṁ puṇḍarīyasiharaṁva

katthaï jāiphalēlākaliyaṁ taṁ kāmuyamuhaṁva

nāṇādēsasamāgayabhūrikaraniruddhasayaladisipakkhaṁ

pavisantabhūribhaṇḍaṁ naravaïbhavaṇaṁva taṁ diṭṭhaṁ

dāuṁ taduciyasuṅkaṁ bhaṇḍaṁ nīyaṁ samuddatīrammi

naïnāhagamaṇadacchaṁ bōhitthaṁ bhāḍiyaṁ viyaḍaṁ

kamasō ya sayalabhaṇḍaṁ caḍāviyaṁ jāhi tattha bōhitthē

tāhē suhatihirikkhē naïnāhē pūiē vihiṇā

kāuṁ jiṇindapūyaṁ dāṇaṁ dāūṇa samaṇasaṅghassa

āpucchiya suhinivahaṁ sambhāsiya sayalaparivāraṁ

kīrantamaṅgalaravē samucchalantē ya tūranigghōsē

paḍumāgahasandōhē jayajayasaddaṁ paüñjantē

pihupattāsayamayalaṁ guṇaniyaranibaddhaphalahasaṅghāyaṁ

sañjamiyasayajōgaṁ bōhitthaṁ muṇivarasaricchaṁ

ārụ̄dhō haṁ tattō vēlāē samāgayāē gahirāē

pavaṇapaḍipunnasiyavaḍavasēṇaṁ gantuṁ payaṭṭaṁ taṁ

parihatthamacchapuñchacchaḍaacchōḍaṇapōcchalantasalilōhaṁ

salilōhasamucchāiyaphurantagirigaḍayabhīsaṇayaṁ

bhīsaṇamagarōvaggiyabhuyagagasijjantagōhiyānivahaṁ

nivahaparisaṇṭhiyuṭṭhiyatimiṅgilāḍhattaāvattaṁ

āvattasamuvvattiyasattasamāḍhattabhīsaṇārāvaṁ

ārāvavasavisaṇṭhulajalayaraparisaraṇaghōrajalaṁ

ghōrajalaghaṇaghaṇāravamuhariyadisicakkamukkaḍataraṅgaṁ

raṅgantaviddumāsiyasappasamuppitthamīṇaülaṁ

aviya

bahusattakayāhāraṁ nivaḍantamahanta āvayānivahaṁ

appattapayāvāsaṁ duggapurisaṁva naïnāiṁ

calamāṇamīṇamayaraṁ phurantaghaṇatimiraruddhapēranta

kasiṇanisāgāsaṁ piva apattapērantasīmāṇaṁ

ēvaṁvihaṁ samuddaṁ majjhaṁmajjhēṇa jāṇavattaṁ taṁ

jā vaccaï kaïvi hu jōyaṇāṇi vēgēṇa naranāha!

tāva ya annammi diṇē kūvayakhambhaggasaṁniviṭṭhēṇa

nijjāmaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ picchaha acchērayaṁ purisā!

kōvi hu mahāṇubhāvō adīṇavayaṇō surindasamarūvō

bāhāhiṁ kaha samuddaṁ aṇōrapāraṁ imaṁ taraī?

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ paḍibēḍayasaṅgayā maē rāyā

tappāsē paṭṭhaviyā pattaṭṭhā kōliyakumārā

gantūṇa tēhiṁ bhaṇiō sō purisō bhadda! ittha āruhasu

dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ vaṇiēṇaṁ tujjha pāsammi paṭṭhaviyā

iya bhaṇiyō ārụ̄dhō samāgaō tāhi amha bōhitthē

diṭṭhō ya maē naravara! taruṇanarō sō mahābhāgō

nijjiyaaṇaṅgarūvō punnimamayalañchaṇōvva aïsōmō

varakaṇayanihasagōrō ahiṇavaüṭṭhintamuharōmō

kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ aṇuharaē naravarinda! sō tumha

diṭṭhammi tammi diṭṭhī amhaṁ sittavva amaēṇa

avvō! mahāṇubhāvō ēsō aṇuharaï mayarakēussa

tā hōjja kiṁ nu ēsō jō taïyā aḍavipaḍiyāē

kamalāvaïdēvīē aṅkāō jāyamittaō hariō

puvvaviruddhasurēṇaṁ kēṇavi addiṭṭharūvēṇa?

ahavā kiṁ maha imiṇā vicintaēṇēha tāva pucchāmi

kō kattha kaha va ēsō paḍiō ya samuddamajjhammi?

iya cintiūṇa ya maē abbhaṅguvvaṭṭaṇāiyaṁ tassa

paramāyarēṇa kāriya bhuñjāviya paramaviṇaēṇa

puṭṭhō suhāsaṇagaō kaha ṇu tumaṁ dhīra! ēttha bhīmammi

rayaṇāyarammi paḍiō kattha va tumhāṇa āvāsō?

tattō ya tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu dhaṇadēva! vajjarijjantaṁ

ēgaggamaṇō hōuṁ ētthatthē kōugaṁ jaï tē

dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīyapurē vēyaḍ̣dhē rayaṇasañcaē atthi

pavaṇagaïkhayaraputtō baülavaī kucchisambhūō

khayarindacakkavaṭṭī vikkhāō cittavēganāmotti

amiyagaïkhayaradhūyā bhajjā sē kaṇagamālatti

tīē ya ahaṁ puttō maṇadaïō mayarakēunāmotti

kamasō ya vaḍḍhamāṇō pattō haṁ jōvvaṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ

ēttō ya atthi nayaraṁ vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarāē sẹ̄dhīē

savvōuyataruvaṇasaṇḍamaṇḍiyaṁ camaracañcanti

bhāṇugaïkhayaraputtō cittagaī tattha khayaravararāyā

sō maha piuṇō mittaṁ ahampi aïvallahō tassa

aha annayā kayāivi pattassa purammi camaracañcammi

pīīi cittagaïṇā dinnā maha rōhiṇī vijjā

sā sattahiṁ māsēhiṁ tatthēṇa ṭhiēṇa sāhiyā vijjā

jahabhaṇiyavihāṇēṇaṁ vihīsiyāṇaṁ abhīēṇaṁ

tattō sāhiyavijjō sampattō niyapurē ahaṁ piuṇā

paramāṇandiyahiyaēṇa saṁsiō khayaramajjhammi

picchaha kaha bālēṇavi raüddarūvāvi rōhiṇī vijjā

akkhuhiyamāṇasēṇaṁ sāhiyā majjha taṇaēṇaṁ?

ajjavi vijjāō kila sāhiumasamatthaō imō bālō

iya cintāē na dinnā vijjāō imassa addēhiṁ

tā jaï imēṇa paḍhamaṁ raüddaruvāvi sāhiyā ēsā

kā gaṇaṇā annāsimpi sāhaṇē hōjja ēyassa?

aha sōhaṇammi diyahē kāuṇaṭṭhāhiyaṁ mahāmahimaṁ

siddhāyayaṇaṭhiyāṇaṁ jiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ pamōēṇa

bhaṇiuṁ samāṇasiddhiṁ dinnāō majjha sayalavijjāō

sōhaṇavihīvi savvō uvaïṭṭhō tāṇa tāēṇa

gantūṇa rayaṇadīvē phurantakiraṇōharayaṇavicchuriē

vijjāharavaranimmiyajugāijiṇamandirē rammē

tattha ya pasatthakhittē viyaṇē vipphuriyakiraṇajālēsu

vijjāpasāhaṇujjayakhayarōciyavivihabhavaṇēsu

sāhasu vijjāniyaraṁ parimiyapiyapariyaṇēṇa pariyariō

kayajiṇavandaṇapūō parihariyāsēsavāvārō

jōyaṇamēttē khittē hiṁsā pañcindiyāṇa sattāṇa

appaparajōgajaṇiyā jattēṇa ya vajjaṇīyatti

jamhā pamāyaōvi hu jāyāi imāi jāyaē vigdhaṁ

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ piuṇā samappiyaṁ majjha aṅguliyaṁ

ēyampi bandhasu karē nivāraṇaṁ sayaladōsapasassa

puttaya! iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ paṭṭhaviō pariyaṇasamēō

gantūṇa rayaṇadīvē pāraddhō sāhiuṁ jahāvihiṇā

bahurūviṇipamuhāō nāṇārūvāō vijjāō

aviya

bahurūvā pannattī gōrīgandhārimōhaṇuppayaṇī

āgarisaṇi ummōyaṇi uccāḍaṇi taha vasīyaraṇī

ēmāibahuvihāō sāhēmāṇassa majjha vijjāō

chammāsā vōlīṇā ūṇā divasēhiṁ thōvēhiṁ

ētthantarammi rayaṇīi carimajāmammi jāvapajjantē

tharahariyaṁ dharaṇīē dhaṇiyaṁva disāgaïndēhiṁ

pajjaliyaṁ gayaṇēṇa hasiyaṁva pabhūyabhūyanivahēṇa

ḍhaṇiyaṁva pavvaēhiṁ varisiyamiva uvalavarisēṇaṁ

tayaṇantaraṁ samīrō sugandhagandhō ya vāiō maüō

paviralaphusiyaṁ gandhōdagaṁ ca paḍiyaṁ tahiṁ divvaṁ

divvā ya kusumavuṭṭhī dasaddhavannā samantaō paḍiyā

payaḍībhūyāō taō vivihālaṅkārakaliyāō

niyaniyanāmaṅkēhiṁ kaliyāō vicittacindhanivahēhiṁ

cittavaravāhaṇāō nāṇānēvatthakaliyāō

annōnnavannābhāsurasarūvarūvāō vivihavilayāō

bhaṇiyaṁ ca tāhiṁ amhē vijjāō tujjha siddhāō

tavvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ harisiyacittēṇa pūyaṇaṁ vihiyaṁ

agghāīyaṁ tāsiṁ pattēyaṁ jīi jaṁ uciyaṁ

vijjāsiddhiṁ nāuṁ mahayā bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa sañjutō

āujjagīyavāyaṇanaṭṭavihiṁ bahuvihaṁ ghēttuṁ

aṭṭhāhiānimittaṁ pūyāuvagaraṇayaṁ gahēūṇa

vēyaḍ̣dhāō tāva ya tāōvi samāgaō tattha

kāūṇa mahāmahimaṁ jugāijiṇamandirammi bhattīē

sampūjiya jahavihiṇā vijjāniyaraṁ payattēṇa

nimmalapavittatitthōdaēhiṁ paḍimāō jiṇavarindāṇaṁ

nhaviūṇa mahādāṇaṁ dāuṁ vijjāharōssa

pūēttu pūyaṇijjē saṁmāṇiya māṇaṇijjajaṇaniyaraṁ

varagīyanaṭṭavāiyasañjuyamaṭṭhāhiyaṁ kāuṁ

paḍupaḍahabhēribhambhādunduhisaddōhapūriyadiyantaṁ

sundaranahayarasundaripēkkhaṇayakkhittakhayarōhaṁ

nimmalajiṇaguṇakittaṇapaḍiṭṭhapaḍumāgahōhasaṅkinnaṁ

vajjantavaṁsavīṇākalasaddāṇandiyajaṇōhaṁ

pēcchāgayasurakinnaracittacamukkārakārayaṁ rammaṁ

kāuṁ jiṇindabhavaṇē jāgaramurupāvaviddavaṇaṁ

sayalaparivārasahiō pattō vēyaḍḍhapavvayaṁ tāō

kāyavvasēsakiccō tatthēva avaṭṭhiō ahayaṁ

kāuṁ jiṇassa pūyaṁ vihiṇā jiṇavandaṇaṁ ca kāūṇa

uiē ravimmi ahayaṁ sarīracintāē nīhariō

kāuṁ sarīracintaṁ kayasōō dīhiyāi līlāi

vaccāmi jāva thōvaṁ bhūbhāgaṁ tāva picchāmi

vaṁsikuḍaṅgāsannē khaggaṁ bhūpaṭṭhisaṇṭhiyaṁ pavaraṁ

ghittūṇa cavalayāē jhaḍatti chinnā kuḍaṅgī sā

tattha ya puvvapaviṭṭhō āsī khayarō u mayarakēutti

sāmī gaṅgāvattassa gaṅghavāhaṇanarindasuō

chinnāē kuḍaṅgīē chinnaṁ mahivaṭṭhasaṇṭhiyaṁ diṭṭhaṁ

sahasā sīsaṁ tassa ō jhaṁratayaṁ ruhirapabbhāraṁ

taṁ daṭṭhūṇa sasambhamacalantapihulōlalōyaṇajuēṇa

hā hā! ahō! akajjaṁ kayanti paridēviyaṁ bahuhā

avvō! pamāyavasaō vihiyā hiṁsā maē imā jāō

tattō ya kimpi hōhī viggha maha mandabhaggassa?

ahavā saṁsiddhāō vijjāō vigghasambhavō natthi

tahavi hu vigghajayaṭhṭhā juttaṁ maha jāvapūyāiṁ

iya cintiya caliō haṁ aha phuriyaṁ dāhiṇēṇa nayaṇēṇa

kiṁ mannē maha sūyaï sunimittamimanti cintintō

kaïvi hu payāṇi jāva ya vayāmi dhaṇadēva! tattha vaṇagahaṇē

picchāmiṁ tāva kimpāgasāhiṇō hiṭṭhabhūbhāgē

suttaṁva mucchiyaṁ piva sarīrasōhāē sūiyaṁ tivvaṁ

niyakulalacchimaüvvaṁ amaēṇava nimmiyaṁ juvaïṁ

aviya dīharakasiṇasukōmalakuntalabhārēṇa sahaï akkantaṁ

āyaḍ̣dhiyabhamaraülaṁ tīē kamalaṁva varasīsaṁ

kannantapattalōyaṇanāsāvaṁsōvasōhiō ruirō

uvahasaïva muhacandō tīi sasaṅkaṁ asampunnaṁ

kambunnayasukumālā gīvā jaḍasaṅgavajjiyā tīē

kharakaṇṭayakaliyāiṁ uvahasaï muṇālanālāiṁ

ghaṇavakkalapīṇunnayathaṇajuyalaṁ sayalalōyamaṇahāri

kaha uvamijjaü tīai surindagayakumbhajuyalēṇa?

tāva ya vivēyarahiyaṁ thaṇajuyalaṁ kāmuē daḍhaṁ dahaü

pattasavaṇāṇa tumhaṁ nayaṇāṇa na hōi juttamiṇaṁ

iya bhaṇamāṇaṁ mannē jhīṇaṁ majjhaṁ tu tīi bālāē

ahavā aviṇīyajaṇē uvaēsō lahuyayaṁ kuṇaï

garuō sihiṇāṇa bharō vōḍhavvō kaha maïtti cintāē

jhīṇaṁ tīē majjhaṁ dāliddiyadhūyajaṇaüvva

maṇahārisugambhīrā payāhiṇāvattanābhiyā tīē

mayaraddhayamajjaṇakūviyavva vihiṇā viṇimmaviyā

maṁsalasūmālēṇaṁ viyaḍaniyambacchalēṇa sā kuṇaï

ālōiyamittēṇavi samittalaṁ taruṇajaṇahiyayaṁ

rambhāgabbhasukōmalamurujuyaṁ tīi rēhaē rammaṁ

mayaṇagharadāradēsē ujjhiyamiva tōraṇaṁ vihiṇā

kummunnayacalaṇajuyalaṁ saṁhayamiumaṁsalaṅgulisaṇāhaṁ

aṇurāillaṁ tīē bhaṇa kassa na cōraē cittaṁ?

iya taṁ sahasā daṭṭhuṁ diṭṭhī āṇandiyā daḍhaṁ majjha

ciyapariciyaṁva daṭṭhuṁ jāō hiyayassa āṇandō

piyapaṇaïṇivva tāhē nirūviyā sā maē vigayaciṭṭhā

muhanīharantaphēṇā sanīladēhacchavī bālā

niyaaṅguliṁ khivittā tīē vayaṇaṁ nirūviyaṁ jāva

kimpāgaphalaṁ tāva ya uvaladdhaṁ addhacavviyayaṁ

ēyaphalaviyārāō jāyā ō acēyaṇā imā nūṇaṁ

tā nēuṁ saṭṭhāṇaṁ karēmi ēīi parikammaṁ

vijjāharassa kassavi dhūyā ēsā havijja iha pattā

nivvēēṇaṁ kēṇavi visaphalamasiyanti mannāmi

bhūmicaramaṇuyāṇaṁ suduggamō ēsa rayaṇadīvō jaṁ

tēṇēva bhūmīgōcara-dhūyā ēsā kahaṁ hōjjā?

ērisanēvatthāō kannā ēsatti nicchaō ēsa

jaṁ puṇa acchipphuraṇaṁ maha hōhī bhāriyā tēṇa

daṭṭhūṇaṁ vivihāō vijjāharabāliyāō aṇurāō

na ya āsi majjha puvviṁ daṭhṭhūṇa imaṁ jahā jāō

tā nūṇaṁ bhaviyavvaṁ imāē sutaṇūē majjha daïyāē

ēmāiṁ vicintēntō gahiṁu niyabāhuucchaṅgē

tīē sukōmalamaṇaharataṇuphāsasuhētinivvuyasarīrō

niyaṭhāṇaṁ sampattō jugāijiṇamandirāsannē

aha āsi tattha bhagiṇī piyaṁvayā aṇṇajaṇaṇī dhūyā mē

puvvuddiṭṭhaṁ kahiyaṁ vuttantaṁ tāhi sē bhaṇiyā

nimmalajalēṇa sahiyaṁ appēsu tamaṅgulīyagaṁ sigghaṁ

vijjāpayāṇasamaē tāēṇa samappiyaṁ jaṁ tu

taṁ divvamaṇisaṇāhaṁ nivāraṇaṁ sayaladōsapasarassa

uvaladdhapaccayaṁ puṇa visēsaō visasamūhammi

tassalilaṁ pāintō tīē aṅgāiṁ tahaya siñcantō

bhaṇiō piyaṁvayāē ēsā maha hōi bhagiṇitti

bhaṇiyaṁ maē kahaṁ puṇa katthavi diṭṭhā imā taē puvviṁ?

bhaṇiyaṁ piyavayāē māūē majjha lahubhagiṇī

rayaṇavaī u kusaggē daïyā naravāhaṇassa naravaïṇō

tīē ēsā dhūyā kannā surasundarī nāma

vēyaḍ̣dhāō puvviṁ āgacchantī imammi dīvammi

khinnā avaïnnā haṁ kusaggapurabāhirujjāṇē

tattha ya diṭṭhā ēsā vijjāē payaṁ tahiṁ ca vīsariyaṁ

paḍupannāē imīē sāhiyamēttāē uvaladdhaṁ

taha cittapaḍē lihiyaṁ rūvaṁ daṭṭhūṇa tumha ēyāē

āhūō aṇurāō garuō ummāyavaḍḍhaṇaō

aviya aïsundarotti mudiyaṁ daïō hōjjatti khijjiyaṁ bahuhā

jaï tāva daṁsaṇampi hu hōjja kayatthatti nīsasiṁya

jaï tāva kāvi hu ahaṁ tā 'vassaṁ tassa saṅgamēṇa suhaṁ

kāyavvaṁ bhagiṇīē iya bhaṇiyā ahaṁ ihaṁ pattā

ēmāi jāva sāhaï piyaṁvayā tīi puvvavuttantō

tāva visavēgavigamāō cēyaṇā tīi uvaladdhā

uvaladdhacēyaṇamahaṁ satthasarīraṁ piyaṁvayāpāsē

mōttūṇa gatō risahassa pūyaō vigghajayahēuṁ

kāuṁ jiṇindapūyaṁ vihiṇā jiṇavandaṇaṁ karēūṇa

taha santidēvayāē mantaṁ javiūṇa uvaüttō

tīē thuiṁ pạdhittā ussaggaṁ kariya taha saüssāsaṁ

vijjāharavāvāyaṇavigghassa vighāyaṇaṭṭhāē

jāva ya samāgaō haṁ puṇaravi ya piyaṁvayā pāsammi

tāva ya sōyavasāgayavāhajalōhaliyagaṇḍayalā

rūyamāṇī sā diṭṭhā puṭṭhā ya piyaṁvayā mayā tāhē

kīsa imā kamalacchī rōyaï gurusōgatattavva?

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēīi kāraṇē garuyasattusaṁruddhō

acchaï imīi jaṇaō tēṇa imā ruyaï sōgēṇa

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyā sāhīṇē kiṅkarammi ēyammi

kō tuha piyaraṁ sundari! sakkēi parābhavēuṁ jē?

vasunandayakhaggakarō ēgāgī cēva taṁ durāyāraṁ

gantuṁ haṇāmi sattuñjayārimahamēva kiṁ bahuṇā?

ētthēva paḍhamajiṇavarabhavaṇammi piyaṁvayāsamēyāē

acchēyavvaṁ tumaē jahāsuhaṁ sōyarahiyāē

jāvā gacchāmi ahaṁ hantuṁ sattuñjayaṁ durācāraṁ

iya bhaṇiūṇuppaïō tamāladalasāmalaṁ gayaṇaṁ

pattō ya kusaggapuraṁ ubbhaḍabhaḍaruddhaviyaḍapāyāraṁ

antōvahantabahujantavattapāsāṇabhīsaṇayaṁ

aṭṭālayaraïyadhayaṁ sayagghisaṅghāyaruddhakavisīsaṁ

vaḍḍhantabahalakalayalagajjantubbhaḍabhaḍāḍōvaṁ

aha kōūhalavasaō gayaṇatthō pēcchiuṁ payattō haṁ

tāva purabhañjaṇatthaṁ samuṭṭhiyaṁ mālavāṇīyaṁ

aviya appēha majjha kasiyaṁ kavayaṁ maha dēha sundaraṁ vapharaṁ

iya sattuñjayasinnē summanti bhaḍāṇa ullāvā

̣dhukkantu vaḍaïlāō jantāiṁ vahantu saraü paṭṭaüḍī

aha khuppaü nīsēṇīṁ pāyārē ghaḍaü sūyariyā

dahaha tamaṅgāvaraṇaṁ chuhēha parihāsu pattharē paürē

aṭṭālayavikasiyāhiṁ khaṇaha sattuñjaī bhaṇaï

musumūriūṇa gurupattharēhiṁ cuḍulīhiṁ sataṇanivahāhiṁ

ujjhanti tamaṅgantaraṭhiēhiṁ jōhēhiṁ sūyariyā

pāyāranimiyanisēṇisaṇṭhiyāpuranarindajōhēhiṁ

kuntaggalacchijjantā paḍanti parihāsu aripurisā

aṭṭālayajantāgayapattharaniyarēṇa vaḍaïlāniyarō

umacchijjaï kattalavihuriyabhaḍahatthadhariōvi

pakkhahatamaṅgasaṇṭhiyadhāṇukkavimukkabāṇanibbhinnā

kalayalacaḍulaniyattā kasiyāittā vivajjanti

pāyālamūlaparisakkirāṇa khurudukkhiyāṇa jōhēhiṁ

sīsāiṁ dalasayāiṁ kīranti sayagdhipayarēhiṁ

pāyāramapattāō paṭṭaüḍīōvi tillasittēhiṁ

ḍajjhanti sasaṅkajaliyarūvagurukaṭṭhanivahēhiṁ

kavisīsantarasaṇṭhiyapakkaladhāṇukkabāṇasañchannaṁ

jāyaṁ siridhariyāraṇanipphandamarāiṇō sinnaṁ

tāva ca rōsavasuṭṭhiyaaṇēyasāmantasuhaḍanivahēṇa

āsāsiya niyasinnaṁ ̣dhukkijjaï sālasaṁmuhayaṁ

ubbhaḍapasaṇḍimaṇḍiyapayaṇḍakōdaṇḍakaṇḍanibbhinnō

pāyārō kayapurapakkhaṇōvva rōmañcamuvvahaï

tō pūriūṇa parihāō sattujōhēhiṁ dīhavaṁsēhiṁ

pajjāliya pērantaṁ palīviyaṁ sayalamāvaraṇaṁ

laggantajantapattharapaḍantapāyārasiharaparituṭṭhaṁ

rahasavasuṭṭhiyahalabōlamuhuriyaṁ hōi sattubalaṁ

aha paḍiyā kōṭṭaṭṭālayāvi gurupihulapattharasubaddhā

jantēhiṁ suraṅgāhi ya kasiyāhi ya viddavijjantā

iya paribalēṇa sahasā parāiē picchiūṇa purasuhaḍē

rōsavasadaṭṭhaüṭṭhō uggīriya maṇḍalaggō haṁ

pattō gaïndaparisaṇṭhiyassa sattuñjayassa āsannē

bhaṇiō ya imō rē! rē! diṭṭhō taṁ ajja kālēṇa

jō maha daïyājaṇayassa paribhavaṁ kuṇasi akayavērassa

ahavā viṇāsasamaē hōi phalaṁ vaṁsaviḍavassa

purisō bhavasu iyāṇiṁ jaï saccaṁ suhaḍavāyamuvvahasi

ghittūṇa tayaṁ kēsēsu jhatti aha matthayaṁ chinnaṁ

aha luyasīsaṁ daṭhṭhūṇa sāmiyaṁ paribalaṁ sasambhantaṁ

valiūṇa bāṇaniyarēṇa ghāiüṁ maṁ samāḍhattaṁ

aha taṁ sutikkhasaraniyara dhōraṇiṁ vañciuṁ payattēṇa

pattō sasōyanaravāhaṇassa atthāṇabhūmīē

sattuñjayassa sīsaṁ puraō mōttūṇa kayapaṇāmēṇa

dhaṇadēva! puvvavuttō vuttantō sāhiō tassa

tā accha niruvviggō ahayaṁ puṇa jāmi rayaṇadīvāō

āṇēttu tumha dhūyaṁ jēṇa samappēmi sigghanti

iya bhaṇiūṇuppaïō daïyāmuhadaṁsaṇussuō jāva

pattō imaṁ paēsaṁ tāva ya sahasā maē diṭṭhō

tālatarūdīhajandhō masimūsāmahisakālagasarīrō

asiliṭṭhalambabāhū niggayadasaṇō palambōṭṭhō

khajjōyadittacakkhū nillaliyajamalajuyalajīhālō

aïvīṇaciviḍhanāsō vēyālō tāvasañjaṇaō

apphōḍantō bahusō abhigajjantō tahaṭṭahāsēhiṁ

palayaghaṇanīsaṇēhiṁ kuṇamāṇō nahayalaṁ muhalaṁ

rē! rē! taïyā jaṁ dinnamāsi daïyāvahāraō dukkhaṁ

vaïrassa tassa antaṁ karēmi, diṭṭhō kahiṁ jāsi?

rē vaïriya! bālattē jīvantō tāva kahava chuṭṭō si?

iṇhi nō puṇa chuṭṭasi chụdhō bhīmammi jalahimmi

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ sahasā pattō addaṁsaṇaṁ sa vēyālō

ahamavi gayaṇāhintō dhasatti paḍiō jalanihimmi

puṇaruttajavijjantī jāva na sā vahaï nahagamā vijjā

tāhē nāyaṁ nūṇaṁ hariyāō majjha vijjāō

kōvi hu ēsa payaṇḍō vaïrī asurotti cintayantēṇa

dhaṇadēva! tāva bāhāhiṁ jalanihiṁ tariumāraddhō

ēvaṁ narinda! sāhaï jāva ya sō majjha niyayavuttantaṁ

nijjāmaēṇa tāva ya sabhayaṁ ēvaṁ samullaviyaṁ

bhō bhō nāviyapurisā! sakannadhārā samujjayā hōha

dīsaï kayantavayaṇaṁva bhīmamuppāiyaṁ jēṇa

suppappamāṇamubbhūyamabbhavaddalayamuaha nahamaggē

khalasaṅgayaṁva jaṁ kuṇaï saṅkhayaṁ jhatti vaḍḍhantaṁ

ērisaṭhāṇē jāyaṁ ēyaṁ uppāiyaṁ mahādhōraṁ

aïrā sabhaḍanāviyanāvāiviṇāsaṇaṁ kuṇaï

ēyaṁ nisamma vayaṇaṁ kūvayakhambhaggasaṇṭhiyanarassa

pavahaṇapurisasamūhō saṅkhuddhō vigayajīyāsō

taō

muccaï naṅgaranivahō kūvayakhambhō tiricchaō vihiō

nāvāvi siyavaḍēṇaṁ ghaṇēṇa pacchāiyā savvā

ētthantarammi pacchāiyaṁ nahaṁ kasiṇamēhanivahēṇa

saṅkhōhiyasalilanihī pavāiō māruō caṇḍō

jamajīhavva camakkaï taḍicchaḍāsantataṁ samantēṇa

dhārāharāvi gajjanti bhīsaṇaṁ maccusuhaḍavva

kharapavaṇuddhuyasāyarataraṅgavēgēhiṁ hīraē nāvā

gurukallōlavasuṭṭhiyanaṅgaraniyarēṇa dhariyāvi

aṇavarayataraṅgēhiṁ uppayanivayaṁ kuṇantiyā vahaï

tandūsayassa līlaṁ kōṭṭimakarahammamāṇassa

tāva ya khaṇantarāō kharamāruyakhañcaṇēṇa jajjariyā

karakarakarassa tuṭṭanti naṅgarā vīivēgēhi

pavaraturaṅgamataruṇivva tāhiṁ ummukkabandhaṇā nāvā

vīīnōlijjantā pahāviyā garuyavēgēṇa

katthaï susiddhavijjā khayarivva nahaṅgaṇēṇa uppayaï

vijjāvigamē katthaï nivaḍaï khayarivva gayaṇāō

ḍaṇḍāhayā bhuyaṅgivva jāi katthaï taraṅgaraṅgatā

mahajaṇasaduttatthavva dhāvaē katthaï aīva

katthaï jhāṇōvagayā jhāyaï sā jōgiṇivva nikkampā

katthaï kantāragayā thērī iva mandayaṁ vayaï

katthaï gurujaṇadiṭṭhā varāhakulabāliyavva lajjāē

ghummaï vēviradēhā sā nāvā jalahimajjhammi

kallōlajalapalāviyaphalayagalantōrubinduaṁsūhiṁ

ruyaïvva samassiyajaṇōhaparirakkhaṇā 'sattā

vihaḍiyabandhaṇaphalahōhamukkagurusaddavippalāvēhiṁ

āsannabhaṅgabhīyavva vilavaī saraṇaparihīṇā

ummattiyavva tattō iō taō sāyarammi bhamamāṇā

avavarayaṁ vidalantā jalagayamāmayasarāvuvva

uvvunnakannadhārā āulavilavantakōliyakulōhā

uttatthavaṇiyasatthā uddhayakandantakammayarā

kacchōṭṭantaragōviyasuvannakhaṇḍammi jaṇasamūhammi

niyataṇusandāmiyaphalayakhaṇḍadakkhammi vaṇiniyarē

niyakuladēvayaniyaraṁ ōvāyatē samatthalōyammi

nāviyajaṇē ya bhaṇḍaṁ pavikkhirantē samuddammi

jalacchāiyapērantaṁ ēkkaṁ āsāiūṇa girigaḍayaṁ

vidalantaphalayaniyarā phuṭṭā sahasatti sā nāvā

ahamavi tattō naravara! āsāiyaphalahayammi saṁlaggō

antēṇṇivēllinōlijjamāṇalahumacchavicchuriō

katthaï asaṅkhasaṅkhōhakhōhiō jalanihimmi buḍḍantō

katthaï gāhagasijjantagōhiyāmuhaviṇimmukkō

katthaï nakkukkattiyasippipuḍupphiḍiyamottiyāinnō

katthaï taraṅgavēviraviddumagahaṇēṇa rujjhantō

avarāvaragurulaharītaraṅgavēgēhiṁ hīramāṇō haṁ

diṇapañcagēṇa naranāha! pāviō nīrapērantaṁ

ravikarasampāyapaṇaṭṭhapaürajaḍḍō taō samuttariuṁ

kāuṁ supakkakayalīphalāiṇā pāṇavittimahaṁ

parisusiyanāliēruggaēṇa tillēṇa kāumabbhaṅgaṁ

ṇhāūṇa sarōtīrē candaṇatarupallavarasēṇa

kappūramīsiēṇaṁ kāūṇa vilēvaṇaṁ payattēṇa

jāiphalēlāsahiyaṁ samāṇiya pavaratambōlaṁ

vararayaṇasilāvaṭṭhē uvaviṭṭhō cintiuṁ payattō haṁ

avvō! kaha ṇu akaṇḍē jāō dhaṇapariyaṇaviṇāsō?

kaha sō mahāṇubhāvō hōhī bhaggammi jāṇavattammi?

āsāiyaphalaō jaï samuttarējjā bhavē laṭṭhaṁ

ēmāi cintayantō kaïvi hu divasāṇi jāva acchāmi

tā annadiṇē kēṇavi ullaviyaṁ vayaṇamēyanti

bhō dhaṇadēva! mahāyasa! uvviggō kīsa acchasē ēvaṁ?

tattō tattōhuttaṁ jāva palōēmi sambhantō

tāva ya diṭṭhō bhāsurasarīradhārī pahaṭṭhamuhakamalō

parihiyasakhiṅkhiṇīpañcavannavaravatthasōhillō

uttaṁsaṭṭhiyabhāsurasappaphaṇāgāraciñcaïō

aïpicchaṇijjarūvō kōvi hu dēvō mahābhāgō

aha kayaabbhuṭṭhāṇō avagụ̄dhō tēṇa sāyaraṁ ahayaṁ

bhaṇiō ya mamaṁ parijāṇasīha kiṁvā na taṁ bhadda!

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ajjavi sammaṁ na yāṇimō dēva!

tā sāhijjaü amhaṁ kō si tumaṁ kattha diṭṭhō vā?

bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa taō āsi taē hatthiṇāurē nayarē

diṭṭhō maṇōramujjāṇasaṇṭhiō dēvasammotti

lakkhaṁ dāūṇa tayā jōgiyahatthāō supaïṭṭhasuō

jayasēṇō nāmēṇaṁ vimōiō jassa vayaṇēṇa

jō ya tayā aḍavīē satthavilōvammi suppaïṭṭhassa

pallīvaïṇō pāsē bālaggāhō taē diṭṭhō

taha ya kusaggapurāō niyattamāṇēṇa daḍḍhapallīē

sīhaguhāē bāhiṁ karaṅkamajjhaṭṭhiō diṭṭhō

palicchinnacalaṇajuyalō gurupaharaṇaghāyajajjariyadēhō

gāḍhaṁ tisābhibhūō jō taïyā kaṇṭhagayapāṇō

parahiyaraēṇa tumaē arahaṁ dēvō susāhuṇō guruṇō

iya accantaṁ dāuṁ sammattaṁ niyamasañjuttaṁ

tattō ya namōkkārō dinnō saṁsārasāgaruttārō

jassāsi taē taïyā sō haṁ bhō! dēvasammajiō

navakārapabhāvāō vēlandharanāgarāyamajjhammi

jāō sivaō nāmaṁ sāmāṇiyapaṇayapayakamalō

tattō ya maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ēyanti kintu pucchami

ṭhāṇammi kammi acchaï tumhē sāhēha maha ēyaṁ

aha suravarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nisuṇasu mērussa dakkhiṇadisāē

bāyālīsasahassāhiṁ jōyaṇāṇaṁ aṇūṇāiṁ

lavaṇasamuddaṁ ōgāhiūṇa atthittha pavvaō rammō

sattarasasaya ēgavīsē uḍḍhaṁ uccattaṇaṁ jassa

addhaṭṭhajōyaṇāiṁ samantaō niyayakantipasarēṇa

lavaṇōhissa salilaṁ payāsaī aṅkarayaṇamaō

nāmēṇa daübhāsō tassa ya siharammi atthi varabhavaṇaṁ

bāvaṭṭhijōyaṇuccaṁ rammaṁ vararayaṇaciñcaïyaṁ

tattha ya vasāmi ahayaṁ sāmāṇiyadasasahassa pariyariō

paliōvamaṭṭhiīō sivaō vēlandharāhivaī

lavaṇasamuddē annāvi atthi sivayā ō rāyahāṇī mē

jōyaṇasahassabārasavitthiṇṇā sā samantēṇa

sivayāi tīi bahusō acchāmi ahaṁ aṇēyadēvīhiṁ

pariyariō divvasuhaṁ bhuñjantō taha daübhāsē

tā bhadda! tuha pasāyāō ērisī pāviyā maē riddhī

kallammi daübhāsammi āgaō pavvaē ahayaṁ

ōhinnāṇēṇa tumaṁ pattaṁ daṭhṭhuṇa rayaṇadīvammi

āyāō tuhadaṁsaṇakaṅkhī, bhaṇa jaṁ maē kiccaṁ?

avvō! jiṇindadhammassa ērisaṁ ēttiyassavi phalanti

tā kīsa na gēṇhāmō jiṇadikkhaṁ iya vicintēntō

bhaṇiō puṇōvi dēvēṇa hōi dēvāṇa daṁsaṇamamōhaṁ

tō bhava paüṇō jēṇāhamajja bahurayaṇasañjuttaṁ

divvavimāṇārūḍhaṁ nēmi tumaṁ hatthiṇāurē nayarē

tattha ya gayassa hiyaïcchiyampi hōhī mahābhāga!

ēvanti maē bhaṇiē divvavimāṇaṁ viuvviyaṁ sahasā

bhūrirayaṇōhasahiō caḍāviō tammi tēṇāhaṁ

raṇayanivahaṁ taddīvatthaṁ aṇēyapayārayaṁ naravara! varaṁ ghēttuṁ majjhaṁ samappiya sāyaraṁ

sivagapahuṇā sammaṁ divvē vimāṇavarē ṭhiō gayapurapuraṁ tēṇāṇīō khaṇēṇa taō ahaṁ

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï gayapurapaccāgamotti nāmēṇa

surasundarīkahāē tērasamō iha paricchēō

ēvaṁ ca jāva sāhaï dhaṇadēvō naravaïssa vuttantaṁ

ētthantarammi surasundarīvi gurusōyasantattā

hā! maha imassa dukkhāgarassa hiyayassa vajjaghaḍiyassa

assōyavvaṁ sōccāvi phuṭṭaē jaṁ na saïkhaṇḍaṁ

kiṁ dhariēhiṁ iṇhiṁ imēhiṁ pāṇēhiṁ dukkhanilaēhiṁ?

maṇavallaïssa jāyammi maṅgulē jāṇabhaṅgammi

saï daṁsaṇēvi nēhassa pagarisō daṁsiō taē nāha!

sattuñjaēṇa ruddhō vimōiō jēṇa tāotti

avahariyā jēṇāhaṁ surēṇa tēṇēva chinnavaravijjō

kaha hōhisi nāha! tumaṁ jāṇavivattīē jalahimmi?

hā! kaha sasaṅkakaranimmalaṁ muhaṁ nāha! tuha palōissaṁ

ēvaṁvihammi vihiē vihiṇā hayabhāgadhēyā haṁ?

calanēhāō mahilāō honti saccō jaṇappavāō 'yaṁ

jaṁ ērisēva nisuē ajjavi jīvāmi pāvā haṁ

ēmāi vicintēntī sōgāvēgāō vigayacēyannā

pāsaṭṭhiyadēvīē paḍiyā mucchāē ucchaṅgē

kamalāvaīvi dēvī sambhāviyasuyaviōgasōgattā

bāhajalāvilanayaṇā vilaviumēvaṁ samāḍhattā

hā! puttaya! aḍavīē taïyā maha jāyamittaō hariō

iṇhimpi akayadaṁsaṇa! kattha gaō maha aünnāē?

dhannā ēsā jīē tāva ya tuha putta! pulaïyaṁ vayaṇaṁ

hā! hā! ahaṁ ahannā jāē jāōvi na hu diṭṭhō

jaṁ taïyā kulavaïṇā āiṭṭhaṁ, hōjja kiṁ nu taṁ aliyaṁ

sampattajōvvaṇō sō milihī kila hatthiṇapurammi?

rāyāvi amarakēū karayalapalhatthavayaṇavicchāō

suyasōyavihuriyaṅgō bāhajalaṁ mōttumāraddhō

dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ ētthantarammi surasundariṁ pavīyantī

puṭṭhā vilāsiṇī haṁsiyā u sañjāyasaṅkēṇa

mucchānimīliyacchī kā ēsā kannagā aüvvatti

ujjāṇanivaḍaṇāiṁ tīivi sē sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

sambhariyasumaïvayaṇō dhaṇadēvō tāhi ēvamullavaï

kīsa visannō naravara! vilavasi kiṁvā tumaṁ dēvi!

kiṁ taṁ visumariyaṁ bhē nēmittiyasumaïṇā jamāiṭṭhaṁ

kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïyā kira kannagā paḍihī

tattō sigghaṁ hōhī samāgamō tumha niyayaputtēṇa

tā mā tūraha sampaï milihī sō natthi sandēhō

jaṁ sō jahatthavāī sumaī uvaladdhapaccaō bahusō

tā mā kuṇaha visāyaṁ jāēvi hu jāṇabhaṅgammi

ēvaṁ ca samāsāsaï dhaṇadēvō jāva niuṇavayaṇēhiṁ

ētthantarammi sahasā dunduhisaddō samucchaliō

gayaṇāō ōyarantā dēvā dīsanti nayarabāhimmi

summaï jayajayasaddō surakāmiṇigīyasaṁvaliō

kiṁ kiṁ imanti jampanti jāva atthāṇasaṇṭhiyā lōyā

tāva ya samantabhaddō samāgatō harisapaḍihatthō

bhaṇaï ya kayappaṇāmō purassa puvvuttarē disābhāē

kusumāyaraüjjāṇē jaïjaṇajōggammi bhūmīē

samaṇagaṇasamparivuḍō samatthasatthatthavittharavihinnū

paravāivāravāraṇanivāraṇē kēsarisaricchō

vivihatavōvihiniraō visuddhacārittasañjamujjuttō

parahiyakaraṇēkkaraō sūrī supaïṭṭhanāmotti

ajjēva samōsariō tassa ya niddaḍḍhaghāikammassa

sampaï appaḍivāī uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ

kēvalimahimākaraṇatthamittha tiyasā samāgayā dēva!

taṁ sōūṇa narindō sāṇandō vandiuṁ caliō

dēvi! tumampi hu paüṇā sahiyā surasundarīē hōhitti

vandittā bhagavantaṁ puccha tumaṁ puttavutantaṁ

ṇhāyavilittō rāyā mahayā bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa sañjuttō

pavaragaïndārụ̄dhō pattō kusumāyarujjāṇaṁ

sayalaparivārasahiō kāuṁ tipayakkhiṇaṁ muṇivarassa

payajuyalaṁ paṇamittā uvaviṭaṭhō uciyadēsammi

aha kayakēvalimahimō sadēvamaṇuyāsurāiparisāē

gambhīrabhāraīē sūrī vajjariumāraddhō

nārayatiriyanarāmaragaīsu sattēhiṁ dukkhataviēhiṁ

kahakahavi māṇusattaṁ pāvijjaï ēttha saṁsārē

laddhūṇavi taṁ dulahaṁ micchattāīhiṁ mōhiyā bahavē

na kuṇanti parattha hiyaṁ visayāmisalōluyā jīvā

jiṇavayaṇasuivihīṇā kajjākajjāiṁ nēva jāṇanti

bhakkhēyābhakkhēyaṁ pēyāpēyaṁ na lakkhēnti

gammāgammavibhāgaṁ giddhā na gaṇanti vigayamajjāyā

dhammiyahiyalōēṇaṁ vārijjantā iya bhaṇanti

mụ̄dhā tumhē dhuttēhiṁ vañciyā natthi kōvi jaṁ jīvō

jō paralōyaṁ gacchaï suhaduhabhōttā amuttō vā

tassābhāvē pāvaṁ hiṁsāikayaṁ havijja kassēha?

tā pañcabhūyasamudayamittaṁ nannaṁ jaē kiñci

ēvaṁvihapariṇāmā nigghiṇahiyayā kuṇanti jiyaghāyaṁ

aliyaṁ vayanti, giṇhantadattayaṁ, jati paradāraṁ

bhūripariggahanirayā rāgaddōsēhiṁ mōhiyamaīyā

nisibhōyaṇamaṁsāsī giddhā mahumajjapāṇammi

kōhamayamāyalōbhēhiṁ vidduyā saṅkiliṭṭhapariṇāmā

avirayamicchaddiṭṭhī kiliṭṭhakammaṁ samajjanti

tavvasagā puṇa kālaṁ kāuṁ nivaḍanti ghōranaraēsu

niccaṁ ghaṇandhayārēsu tivvasīuṇhakaliēsu

tattha ya tē uvavannā paramāhammiyasurēhiṁ virasantā

chijjanti nisiyakaravattadittaparasūhiṁ sayahūttaṁ

gurutikkhakaṇṭayāinnasimbalīniviḍasāhamajjhammi

ārōviuṇa bahusō ākāḍ̣dhijjanti rajjūhiṁ

kaḍhakaḍhakạdhēntakumbhīsu tēhiṁ paccanti niddayamaṇēhiṁ

pāījjanti jalantaṁ tambaṁ tisiyatti jampantā

sasarīrasamukkattiyamaṁsaṁ chuhiyāṇa aggisaṅkāsaṁ

kāuṁ chubbhaï vayaṇē nēraïyāṇaṁ anāhāṇaṁ

pūivasaruhirapunnaṁ vēyaraṇiṁ nimmayaṁ viuvvittā

vōlijjanti rasantā hā! hā! māyatti jampantā

chāyatthā sampattā asipattavaṇammi nisiyapattēhiṁ

chijjanti vilavamāṇā asitōmarakuntarūvēhiṁ

tattha kayacchijjantā rakkhaha saraṇāgayatti jampantā

sumarāviyapuvvabhavā gāḍhayaraṁ tēhiṁ hammanti

kiṁ bahuṇā acchinimīliyamittaṁ natthi suhaṁ dukkhamēṁva santattaṁ

naraē nēraīyāṇaṁ ahōnisiṁ paccamāṇāṇaṁ

ēvaṁ pabhūyakālaṁ aṇuhaviuṁ dāruṇāiṁ dukkhāiṁ

kahavi hu uvvaṭṭittā jāyanti tirikkhajōṇīsu

tatthavi chuhāpivāsuṇhasīyavahabandharōyaviyaṇāhiṁ

bhārarōvaṇanatthaṇadamaṇaṅkusatōttayāīhiṁ

avarōpparabhakkhaṇatāḍaṇāidukkhāiṁ viviharuvāiṁ

paccaṇubhavanti bahusō puṇō puṇō vivihajōṇīsu

tattō lahanti jaï kahavi dullahaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ jīvā

tatthavi jāyaï dukkhaṁ sārīraṁ māṇasaṁ vivihaṁ

dāriddagaruyamōggaranivāyaduhiyā karēnti annēsiṁ

nīyāṇavi āṇattiṁ kadannalavapāvaṇicchāē

na gaṇinti rāidiyahaṁ vaccanti sudūravisamadēsampi

pavisanti visamavivaraṁ laṅghati ya jalanihiṁ dīṇā

dhaṇapāvaṇavañchāē dukkhaṁ na gaṇinti lōhagahagahiyā

dippantakuntapaürē pavisanti ya bhīmasaṅgāmē

iṭṭhajaṇaviyōgāō aṇiṭhṭhasampāvaṇē ya jaṁ dukkhaṁ

vivihāvayāhi ya tahā kō puṇa taṁ vanniuṁ taraï?

bahuviharōgāyaṅkēhi pīḍiyā nivvuiṁ na pāvinti

ghippanti jarāi taō marēnti tattō sunivvinnā

jaï kaïvi hu dēvattaṁ pāvinti tahimpi jāyaē dukkhaṁ

īsāvisāyabhayasōyalōhasantattacittāṇa

parariddhiṁ pēcchantā bhiccā viva sāmiēṇa āṇattā

jāyanti cavaṇasamaē dēvāvi hu dukkhiyā dhaṇiyaṁ

culasīijōṇilakkhēkkasaṅkulē iha bhavē bhamantēhiṁ

taṁ natthi kimpi ṭhāṇaṁ aṇantukhattō na jaṁ ēntaṁ

savvatthavi dukkhattā jāyanti jiṇindadhammaparihīṇā

tā bhō dēvāṇupiyā! karēha jiṇadēsiyaṁ dhammaṁ

sō duvigappō bhaṇiō jaïdhammō taha gihatthadhammō ya

duvihassavi vinnēyaṁ sammattaṁ guṇagaṇāvāsaṁ

tattatthasaddahāṇaṁ suhāyapariṇāmarūvayaṁ taṁ tu

jīvāiṇō payatthā tattaṁ puṇa hōi vinnēyaṁ

jīvā 'jīvāpunnaṁ pāvāsavasaṁvarā ya nijjaraṇā

bandhō mukkhō ya tahā tattāṇi imāṇi nava honti

suhumā bāyara bēindiyā ya tēindiyā ya caürindī

sannī assannī khalu cōddasa pajjatta 'pajjattā

dhammā 'dhammā ' 'gāsā tiyatiyabhēyā ya tahēva kālō ya

khandhā dēsapaēsā paramāṇū ajīva cōddasahā

sāyaṁ uccāgōyaṁ sattatīsaṁ ca nāmapagaīō

tiṇṇi ya āuṇi tahā bāyālaṁ punnapagaḍīō

nāṇantarāyadasagaṁ daṁsaṇa nava mōhapagaïchavvīsaṁ

nāmassa caüttīsaṁ tiṇha ya ēkkikka pāvāu

indiya kasāya avvaya kiriṇā paṇa caüra paṇa ya paṇavīsā

jōgā tinnēva bhavē bāyālaṁ āsavō bhaṇiō

samiī guttī dhammō aṇuppēhaparīsahā carittaṁ ca

sattāvannaṁ bhēyā paṇatiyabhēyāi saṁvaraṇē

aṇasaṇabhēyāi tavō bārasahā tēṇa nijjarā bhaṇiyā

kaṇagāvalibhēyāō ahava tavō 'ṇēgahā hōi

payaïṭhiīaṇubhāgapaēsabhēyā caüvvihō bandhō

aṭṭhavihakammavigamō mōkkhō puṇa sāsaō bhaṇiō

ēēsiṁ saddahāṇē arihaṁ dēvō susāhuṇō guruṇō

iya paḍivattinimittaṁ sammattaṁ hōi vinnēyaṁ

sāvajjajōgaparivajjaṇaṁ tu maṇavayaṇakāyajōgēhiṁ

ēsō jaīṇa dhammō duraṇucarō mandasattāṇaṁ

kāyavvā jēṇa dayā chaṇhavi puḍhavāiyāṇa jīvāṇa

savvōvāhivisuddhaṁ bhaṇiyavvaṁ saccayaṁ vayaṇaṁ

tiṇamittampi adinnaṁ na ya ghittavvaṁ asuddhacittēṇa

dhārēyavvaṁ ca sayā nava guttisaṇāhabambhavayaṁ

dhammōvagaraṇavajjō thēvōvi pariggahō na kāyavvō

āhāracaükkampi hu rayaṇīē nēva bhōttavvaṁ

samiīu pañca guttīu tinni niccaṁ ca sēviyavvāō

jēyavvā taha uiyā bābīsaparīsahā sammaṁ

kāyavvaṁ sattīē vēyavaccaṁ ca sūripamuhāṇa

naratiridēvōhakayā uvasaggā taha ya sahiyavvā

saddāisu visaēsuṁ rāgaddōsā na cēva kāyavvā

bāyāladōsasuddhō bhōttavvō kāraṇē piṇḍō

vēyaṇavēyāvaccē īriyaṭṭhāē ya sañjamaṭṭhāē

taha pāvavattiyāē chaṭhṭhaṁ puṇa dhammacintāē

kāyavvō sajjhāō parihariyavvāō savvavikahāō

ujjamiyavvaṁ sayayaṁ sabbhintarabāhiratavammi

mōttūṇa aṭṭaruddē jhāēyavvāṇi dhammasukkāṇi

bhavēyavvō ya aṇiccayāivarabhāvaṇānivahō

abbhasiyavvō viṇaō pāvā sacchandayā na kāyavvā

niccampi aṇuṭṭhēō dasappayārōvi jaïdhammō

khantī maddava ajjava muttī tavasañjamē ya bōddhabvē

saccaṁ sōyaṁ ākiñcaṇaṁ ca bambhaṁ jaïdhammō

vasiyavvaṁ muṇimajjhē nō kāyavvā kusīlasaṁsaggī

pañcavihōvi pamāō parihariyavvō payattēṇa

majjaṁ visayakasāyā niddā vigahā ya pañcamī bhaṇiyā

iyaṁ pañcavihapamāō jīvaṁ pāḍēi saṁsārē

kiṁ bahuṇā dhīdubbalamaṇatāvakarō u jāvajīvāē

bōḍhavvō aṭṭhārasasīlaṅgasahassapabbhārō

kīrantō jaïdhammō khippaṁ mōkkhammi nēi naranāha!

dīharakālēṇaṁ puṇa sāvagadhammōvi taṁ savvaṁ

pañca ya aṇuvvayāiṁ guṇavvayāiṁ ca honti tinnēva

sikkhāvayāiṁ caürō sāvagadhammō duvālasahā

ēmāivittharēṇaṁ duvihēvi hu sāhiyammi dhammammi

patthāvaṁ nāūṇaṁ rannā sūrī imaṁ puṭṭhō

kamalāvaīi puttō aḍavīē jayamēttaō kēṇa

avahariō, puvvakayaṁ kiṁvā vēraṁ sarantēṇa?

vuḍ̣dhiṅgaō sa kattha va bhayavaṁ! kaïyā va amha sō milihī?

ēyaṁ savittharēṇaṁ sāhēha aṇuggahaṁ kāuṁ

nāūṇa ya uvagāraṁ kahijjamāṇē pabhūyalōyassa

aha kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ kahimō āyannasu narinda!

dhāyaïsaṇḍē dīvē puracchimaddhammi bharahakhittammi

atthi purī pōrāṇā nāmēṇaṁ avarakaṅkatti

tīē ambaḍavaṇiṇō mahilā nāmēṇa atthi acchuttā

tīē kamēṇa jāyā vararūvā tinni puttāō

maṇḍaṇamalhaṇacandaṇanāmā, tēsiṁ ca tinni mahilāō

lacchisarassaïsampayanāmāō pavararūvāō

payaīi taṇukasāyā annōnnaṁ pavarapīisañjuttā

dāṇarayā santuṭṭhā suhēṇa acchanti tē vaṇiṇō

aha annayā kayāivi lacchī vaṇṭhēṇa ninnanāmēṇa

diṭṭhā, abbhuvavannō sō tīē ruvalāvannē

patthēi ya taṁ bahusō sā puṇa taṁ nēcchaī maṇēṇāvi

aha annayā talāē tōyanimittaṁ gayā lacchī

turayārụdhō aha ninnaōvi pattō 'ṇumaggaō tīē

viyaṇē gahiyā maḍḍāi rōviyā turayapaṭṭhīē

vilavantī vēgapahāviēṇa turaēṇa pāḍiyā aḍaviṁ

bhillēhiṁ samaṁ jujjhammi māriō ninnaō rannē

gahiyābharaṇā lacchī mukkā bhillēhiṁ tattha aḍavīē

hiṇḍantī tattha mūḍhadisā asiyā sīhēṇa chuhiēṇa

aha sā malhaṇapattī sarassatī mōhilēṇa vaṇiēṇa

patthijjantī païṇō sāhēi jahaṭṭhiyaṁ savvaṁ

aha malhaṇēṇa rannō gantuṁ siṭṭhammi tammi vuttantē

uddāliyadaviṇō mōhilōvi nivvāsiō rannā

puvvasayasahassāiṁ bahūṇi parivāliūṇa niyamāuṁ

tinnivi kālaṁ kāuṁ nibaddhamaṇuyāuyā tattō

jambuddīvē ētthaṁ atthi purī mēhalāvatī nāma

ēravaē varakhēttē āriyadēsammi vitthinnā

bhīmarahō tatthāsī rāyā kusumāvalī u sē dēvī

tīē puttatāē uvavannō maṇḍaṇō tāva

jāō ya uciyasamaē dēvakumārōvamō visālacchō

kaṇagarahō sē nāmaṁ vihiyaṁ uciyammi samayammi

kamasō jōvvaṇapattō visuddhavaṁsāṇa rāyakannāṇa

rāyasirīpamuhāṇaṁ pavarāṇaṁ gāhiō pāṇiṁ

juvarāya paē ṭhaviō bhujaï māṇussaē pavarabhōē

antēuramajjhagaō dēvō viva dēvalōgammi

tīi nayarīi ibbhā sahōyara dōnni āsi satthāhā

sāgaradattō ya tahā samuddadattō ya supasiddhā

aha sō ninnayavaṇṭhō nihaō bhillēhiṁ tattha aḍavīē

kaïvayabhavagahaṇāiṁ hiṇḍittā tiriyajāīsu

uvvaṭṭiūṇa puttō sāgaradattassa satthavāhassa

dhannāē bhāriyāē subandhunāmō samuppannō

sōvi hu malhaṇajīvō kālaṁ kāūṇa āupajjantē

jāō sudaṁsaṇāē bhajjāē samuddadattassa

puttō dhaṇavaïnāmō suruvajuttō kalāsu pattaṭṭhō

ēttō ya atthi nayarī vijayā tatthēva ēravaē

tīē samiddhijuttō dhaṇabhūī nāma āsi satthāhō

mahilā sundarināmā puttō ya sudhammanāmotti

aha candaṇōvi vaṇiō mariuṇa taō sudhammanāmassa

ēgōyarō kaṇiṭṭhō jāō dhaṇavāhaṇō nāma

tatthēva ya ēravaē supaïṭṭhapurammi āsi haridattō

ibbhō tassa ya mahilā viṇayavaī viṇayasañjuttā

puttō uṇa vasudattō aha sā lacchī tayā ō aḍavīē

sīhahayā mariūṇaṁ bhabhiūṇa tirikkhajōṇīsu

viṇayavaīē dhūyā jāyā ō sulōyaṇatti nāmēṇa

vasuddattassa kaṇiṭṭhā suruvaruvā suruvahuvva

sāvi hu candaṇabhajjā kālaṁ kāūṇa sampayā tattō

jāyā sulōyaṇāē kaṇiṭṭhabhagiṇī aṇaṅgavaī

ētthantarammi malhāṇabhajjāvi sarassaī mayā santī

tāṇaṁ dōṇhavi lahuī vasumaïnāmā samuppannā

ēvaṁ ca tāō tinnivi vasēṇa bhaviyavvāyāi ēgattha

jāyāō bhagiṇīō avarōpparanēhakaliyāō

jōvvaṇamaṇupattāō samāṇajāīṇa rūvajuttāṇa

aṇurūvāṇa varāṇaṁ māyāvittēhiṁ variyāō

aviya jēṭṭhā sulōyaṇā sā pariṇīyā ninnavaṇṭhajīvēṇa

sāgaradattasuēṇaṁ subandhunāmēṇa vaṇiēṇa

bīyā aṇaṅgavaïyā dhaṇabhūisuēṇa vijayanayarīē

dhaṇavāhaṇanāmēṇaṁ pariṇīyā puvvadaïēṇa

taïyā vasumaïnāmā malhaṇajīvēṇa puvvadaïēṇa

dhaṇavaïṇā pariṇīyā taṇaēṇa samuddadattassa

jiṭhṭhaṁ sulōyaṇaṁ vajjiūṇa bhaviyavvayāniōēṇa

puvvabhavavallahēhiṁ juttāō nēhakaliēhiṁ

puvvabhavabbhāsāō sulōyaṇā vallahā subandhussa

tīē uṇa sō na tahā, ēvaṁ vaccanti divasāiṁ

aha annayā kayāivi kaṇayarahō turayavāhaṇanimittaṁ

bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa sahiō niggacchaï rāyamaggēṇa

tāva ya nāyariyāō niyaniyahammiyatalēsu caḍiūṇa

kumaraṁ niggacchantaṁ pulaïumēvaṁ payattāō

ēkkā vilāsapaüraṁ kumaraṁ daṭṭhuṁ aṇaṅgapaḍirūvaṁ

kayaünnā sā jīē ēsō daïotti cintēi

annā kumarapalōyaṇataggayacittā vimukkavāvārā

nipphandalōyaṇajuyā suravahūlīlaṁ samuvvahaï

annā uṇa karasaṇṭhiyamuttāhalatārahāriyā sahaï

phalihakkhamālavāvaḍajhāṇaṭṭhiyajōgiṇisaricchā

kōugarahasapayaṭṭā gurujaṇasaṅkāi taha nittantī

rēhaï dōlārūḍhavva kāvi kumarassa niggamaṇē

līlācalantalōyaṇakumarapalōyaṇavimukkanīsāsā

mayaṇasarasalliyaṅgivva najjaē caürasahiyāhiṁ

kāvi hu cumbaï bālaṁ annā sahiyāi laggaē galaē

annā karēi gīyaṁ kāvi hu uccaṁ samullavaï

līlācalantagīvō jattō jattō niyacchaï kumārō

sōhaggamahō vaḍḍhaï tahiṁ tahiṁ nayaranārīṇaṁ

ēvaṁ ca samayaṇāhiṁ pulaïjjantō sa nayaranārīhiṁ

pattō kamēṇa sāgaradattagihāsannabhūbhāgē

diṭṭhō sulōyaṇāē avalōyaṇasaṇṭhiyāi tēṇāvi

diṭṭhā imā sakajjalasiṇiddhapihunayaṇasōhillā

puvvabhavabbhāsāō avarōpparadaṁsaṇāō sañjāō

aïguruō aṇurāō takkhaṇamēttēṇa dōṇhampi

aha niggaō turantō turaṅgamārūḍhaviggahō kumarō

dēhēṇa na cittēṇaṁ sulōyaṇārūvahayahiyaō

puṭṭhō aṇēṇa sumaī bālavayaṁsō vayasaṁ! kassēsā

dappaṇavāvaḍahatthā avalōyaṇasaṇṭhiyā juvaī?

ēsā kumara! sulōyaṇanāmā daïyā subandhuvaṇiyassa

sāgaradattasuyassa ō iya bhaṇiē sumaïṇā kamasō

āvāhiūṇa turaē samāgaō niyagihammi kaṇagarahō

mayaṇasaravihuriyaṅgō cinttaï tappāvaṇōvāyaṁ

kiṁ majjha vibhūīē kiṁvā antaürēṇa rajjēṇa?

jō tīē muhakamalē chappayalīlaṁ na pāvēmi

jaïvi hu lōyaviruddhaṁ sukuluppannāṇa ērisaṁ kajjaṁ

tahavi hu tīē viuttō sattō dhariuṁ na jīyampi

nāūṇa tīē bhāvaṁ dūīsampēsaṇēṇa cittagayaṁ

jaï tāva sāvi icchaï khivāmi antēurē niyaē

iya cintiūṇa tēṇaṁ paḍuyā pavvāiyā samāṇattā

taha kuṇasu tumaṁ bhayavaï! jaha sā maē paṇaïṇī hōi

tīēvi gantu viyaṇē taha sā ābhāsiyā suniuṇāē

jaha payaḍiyasabbhāvā hiyayagayaṁ jhatti ullavaï

uvviggā viva dīsasi kīsa tumaṁ putti! kēṇa bhē kajjaṁ?

āṇēmi jēṇa aïdullahampi niyamantasattīē

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaï! maha hiyayaṁ dullahaṁ jaṇaṁ mahaï

nibbhaggarōrapurisōvva bhōyaṇaṁ cakkavaṭṭissa

jaha kāvi sāramēī icchaï sīhēṇa saṅgamamalajjā

taha cēva ahaṁ bhayavaï! saṅgaṁ icchāmi kumarēṇa

tīē bhaṇiyaṁ idampi putti! āṇēmi mantasattīē

kittiyamēttaṁ ēyaṁ maha mantō jattha vipphuraï

mā putti! kuṇa visāyaṁ jāvaṁ mantassa taha payacchissaṁ

ajjavi ya kumārēṇaṁ jaha saṅgō jāyaē tujjha

taha kāyavvaṁ bhayavaï! na hōi jaha majjha lāghavaṁ lōē

iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ tīē dinnā muttāvalī niyayā

pavvāiyāē tattō gantuṁ kumarassa sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ

harisiyamaṇēṇa tēṇavi āṇāviya niyayapurisēhiṁ

antēurammi khittā sulōyaṇā rāgamōhiyamaṇēṇa

agaṇiya jaṇāvavāyaṁ ullaṅghiyaniyayamajjāyaṁ

vinnāyavaïrēhiṁ ca sāhiyaṁ nāyarēhiṁ naravaïṇō

tēṇavi bahuppagāraṁ sikkhaviō mahuravayaṇēhiṁ

na ya icchaï taṁ mōttuṁ tāhē nāūṇa tassa nibbandhaṁ

rannā paürā bhaṇiyā asamatthā amhē kumarassa

sāmēṇa tā na muñcaï daṇḍō kumarammi tīraï na kāuṁ

tā khamaha ēkkamēyaṁ avarāhaṁ amha kumarassa

ēyaṁ naravaïvayaṇaṁ sōūṇaṁ nāyarāvi dīṇamuhā

vicchāyanirāṇandā jahāgayaṁ paḍigayā savvē

kaṇagarahōvi hu tīē surayasuhāsattamāṇasō niccaṁ

kamasō sēsantēuraparibhōgaparammuhō jāō

cintēi na rajjaṭhiiṁ na nīi bāhiṁ na dēi atthāṇaṁ

sahiō sulōyaṇāē acchaï vivihāhiṁ kīlāhiṁ

ēvaṁ pabhūyakālō vōlīṇō tassa rāyataṇayassa

tīē ahiṇavajōvvaṇasuhaphāsapasattacittassa

aha annayā kayāivi paribhūyā hanti jāyakōvāē

puvviṁ tassiṭṭhāē dēvīē rāyasiriyāē

paricariyaparivvāiyavidinnaümmāyakāraō cunnō

ēgantapasuttāṇaṁ dōṇhavi sirammi pakkhittō

tassa ya vasēṇa dōnnivi sahasā ummattayāṇi jāyāṇi

gāyanti hasanti samullavanti asamañjasaṁ bahuhā

bhīmarahēṇavi tattō vāhariyā mantatantiyā bahavē

tēvi hu karinti kiriyaṁ bhūyavigārotti mannantā

aviya kāuṁ sarīrarakkhaṁ gāḍhaṁ gahiūṇa kēvi muddāsu

pahaṇanti gurucavēḍāghāēhiṁ kasappahārēhiṁ

ālihiya mañja 'lēsuṁ kēvi hu viṇivēsiūṇa uvaüttā

ahimantiya siddhatthayaghāēhiṁ haṇanti puṇaruttaṁ

kēvi hu virālatannayapurīsamīsēhiṁ guggulāīhiṁ

uvvariyammī khivittā uddhūvaṇiyaṁ payacchanti

vāyassa vigārasaṅkirēhiṁ vējjēhiṁ vivihakiriyāō

pāraddhāō na uṇō kōvi guṇō tāṇa sañjāō

ummattayarūvēṇaṁ paṇaṭṭhacittāṇa vaccaē kālō

aha annayā pasuttē pāhariyajaṇammi rayaṇīē

bhañjittā niyalāiṁ nihuyaṁ ciya niggayāiṁ nayarīō

dōnnivi bhamanti sīuṇhavāyabahudukkhataviyāiṁ

iya naravara! saṁsārē suhiō hōūṇa jāyaē duhiō

rāyāvi bhamaï bhikkhaṁ suvaï mahīē nirāvaraṇō

pavarāhāravilēvaṇaāharaṇavibhūsiyāiṁ hōūṇa

hiṇḍanti tāiṁ bhikkhaṁ gihē gihē dukkhataviyāiṁ

dhūlīdhūsariyāiṁ bālōhahasējjamāṇacēṭṭhāiṁ

hiṇḍanti sudīṇāiṁ nivasiyajaradaṇḍikhaṇḍāiṁ

bālōhapēcchaṇijjaṁ buhajaṇasaṁsōyaṇijjamaccatthaṁ

picchasu naravara! jāyaṁ taṁ mihuṇaṁ kammadōsēṇaṁ

ēyaṁ ca tāva ēvaṁ, ēttō u purīē vijayanāmāē

rattō 'ṇaṅgavaīē bhuñjaï ghaṇavāhaṇō bhōē

paḍibōhiō suhammēṇa sūriṇā jiṭṭhabhāuṇā ēsō

sahiō 'ṇaṅgavaīē pavvaïō sūripāsammi

ēttō ya dhaṇavaīvi hu vasumaïyāē siṇēhajuttāē

sahiō pañcapayārē bhuñjaï māṇussaē bhōē

jaha sō mōhilavaṇiō rannā nivvāsiō sadēsāō

kāūṇa tahāruvaṁ suhaphalayaṁ kimpaṇuṭṭhāṇaṁ

uvavannō vēyaḍ̣dhē uttarasẹ̄dhīē vējayantapurē

cittaṅgayassa puttō puhavīi sumaṅgalō nāma

sāhiyabahuvihavijjō aha sō gayaṇaṅgaṇēṇa hiṇḍantō

kaïyāvi mēhalāvaïpurīē līlāē sampattō

hammiyatalamārụdhā ṇhāyantī tēṇa vasumaī diṭṭhā

puvvabhavabbhāsāō rattō sō tīi ruvammi

kāuṁ dhaṇavaïrūvaṁ uvabhuttā tēṇa vasumaī muddhā

tīē surayapasattō dhaṇavaïrūvī ṭhiō tattha

sō puṇa dhaṇavaïvaṇiō puvvabhavōvattakammadōsēṇa

avahariya tēṇa mukkō ihēva bharahē viṇīyāē

sō tattha risahajiṇavaravaṁsapasūyassa daṇḍavīriyassa

kēvaliṇō payamūlē pavvaïō jāyanivvēō

puvvasayasahassāiṁ tīsaṁ kāūṇa uggatavacaraṇaṁ

uvavaṇṇō īsāṇē dēvō candajjuṇō nāma

paradārapasattō sō sumaṅgalō tēṇa chinnavaravijjō

mukkō paraō māṇūsanagassa dēvēṇa kuddhēṇa

paḍibōhiyā u dēvēṇa vasumaī jāyativvasaṁvēgā

sūrisuhammapavattiṇipayamūlē ajjiyā jātā

ēvaṁ ca aṇaṅgavaī vasumaïajjāi saṁyuyā tattha

mayaharicandajasāē payamūlē kuṇaï uggatavaṁ

aha annayā kayāivi viyārabhūmiṁ gayāhiṁ ēyāhiṁ

diṭṭhaṁ taṁ ummattaṁ mihuṇaṁ bahuḍimbhapariyariyaṁ

uggāyantaṁ bahuhā naccantaṁ dhūlidhūsarasarīraṁ

taṁ daṭṭhumaṇaṅgavaī savisāyā ēvamullavaï

ajjē! vasumaï! ēsā bhagiṇīi sulōyaṇāi aṇuharaï

jaradaṇḍikhaṇḍavasaṇā gahagahiyanarassa pāsatthā

bhaṇiyaṁ ca vasumaīē suiraṁ nijjhāiūṇa savisāyaṁ

ēsō sō kaṇagarahō ēsāvi sulōyaṇā nūṇaṁ

tattō gantuṁ dōhivi mahuraṁ ābhāsiyaṁ tayaṁ juyalaṁ

uggāyaï hasaï naccaï bōllaï asamañjasaṁ bahuyaṁ

tāhē dōvi jaṇāiṁ suhammasūrissa pāyamūlammi

karuṇāparāhiṁ ajjāhiṁ tāhiṁ nīyāiṁ savisāyaṁ

aïsayanāṇī ya guru puṭṭhō ummāyakāraṇaṁ tāhiṁ

guruṇāvi tāṇa siṭṭhō puvvuttō sayalavuttantō

bhaṇiō ajjāhiṁ guru bhayavaṁ! jaï atthi kōvi paḍijōgō

tā ēyāṇa paüñjaha jaï picchaha kiñciṁ uvagāraṁ

tattō guruṇā tēsiṁ dinnō ummāyanāsaṇapaḍiṭṭhō

paḍijōgō jāyāiṁ dōnnivi aha satthacittāiṁ

aha tāṇa vasumaīē siṭṭhō savvōvi puvvavuttantō

ēyassa gurupabhāvā naṭṭhō tumhāṇa ummāō

iya sōūṇaṁ dōnnivi suhammasūrissa paramaviṇaēṇa

vandanti caraṇajuyalaṁ aha sūrī bhaṇiumāḍhattō

bhōgasuhalālasāṇaṁ paradārarayappiyāṇa purisāṇa

bahuvihaviḍambaṇāō iha paralōē ya jāyanti

pāvanti visayatisiyā vahabandhaṇamāraṇāidukkhāiṁ

nāūṇa kumara! ēvaṁ bhōgapivāsaṁ pariccayasu

paradārapasattēṇaṁ jaṁ pāvaṁ cikkaṇaṁ taē baddhaṁ

pupphasarisō vivāgō rajjabbhaṁsāiō tassa

ēttōvi aṇantaguṇaṁ kaḍuyavivāgaṁ phalaṁ tu paralōē

pāvijjaï duvvisahaṁ nārayatiriyāisaṁsaraṇē

ēmāidēsaṇāē āvibbhūyammi caraṇapariṇāmē

pavvāviyaïṁ guruṇā dōnnivi nivvinnacittāiṁ

mayahariyāē pāsē bhagiṇījuyalēṇa sañjuyā tattō

sammaṁ guruviṇayarayā sulōyaṇā kuṇaï vivihatavaṁ

ēvaṁ candajasāē payamūlē tāṇa acchamāṇīṇaṁ

tiṇhampi hu bhagiṇīṇaṁ gayāṇi bahupuvvalakkhāṇi

muṇiṇō kaṇagarahassavi ghaṇavāhaṇasāhuṇā samēyassa

vōlīṇāō bahuyā varisāṇaṁ kōḍikōḍīō

aha aṇasaṇēṇa sūri kālaṁ kāūṇa bīyakappammi

jāō sasippahasurō vimāṇacandajjuṇāhivaī

ghaṇavāhaṇōvi mariuṁ jāō sāmāṇiō surō tassa

vijjuppahotti iyarā dēvī sē candarēhatti

vasumaïajjāvi tahā puvvuvannassa tattha dēvassa

candajjuṇassa jāyā dēvī candappahā nāma

ēttō ya sō subandhū daïyāi guruvirahasōyasaṁsattō

haṭṭagharakāṇaṇāīsu katthavi ya dhiiṁ apāvintō

kaṇagarahassa paüṭṭhō cintēntō vivihamāraṇōvāyaṁ

rōddajjhāṇōvagaō vilavantō dīṇavayaṇillō

rayaramiyahasiyajampiyasaharisaavaguhaṇāiṁ daïyāē

puṇaruttaṁ sumarantō jāō sō gahagahiuvva

taō niyayagharammi na ciṭṭhaï hiṇḍaï ujjāṇakāṇaṇaïsu

kattha gayā kēṇa hiyā kīsa nilukkā si jampantō

kaha ruṭṭhā maha sundari! jēṇa na daṁsēsi appayaṁ sigghaṁ

huṁ huṁ diṭṭhā diṭṭhā pasīya maha dēsu paḍivayaṇaṁ

jaṁ jaṁ picchaï lōyaṁ taṁ taṁ pucchaï, taē piyā diṭṭhā?

ēmāiṁ vilavamāṇō nīhariō tāō nayarīō

ummattayarūvēṇaṁ hiḍantō vivihagāmanayarēsu

duhiō dīṇō viyaṇō chuhāpivāsāhiṁ santattō

kaïyāvi hu sampattō aṇēyatāvasajaṇāurē rammē

nāṇādumasayagahaṇāmmi āsamē vivihaphalapaürē

tattha ya sē kulavaïṇā maṇayaṁ sañjāyasatthacittassa

niyadhammō parikahiō tassavi sō pariṇaō tāhē

giṇhiya tāvasadikkhaṁ daïyāguruvirahajāyavēraggō

kayakandaphalāhārō ghōratavaṁ cariumāraddhō

dōmāsiyatēmāsiyacaümmāsāiyaṁ tavaṁ vivihaṁ

kāuṁ pabhūyakālaṁ atuṭṭavērāṇubandhō sō

mariūṇa ya uvavannō paramāhammiyasurēsu ambarisī

uvavannamēttaō sō puvvabhavālōyaṇaṁ kuṇaï

nāūṇa puvvavaïraṁ vihaṅganāṇēṇa āsuruttō sō

cintēi kattha vaïrī sā vā maha duṭṭhamahilatti?

dussīlā sā pāvā aṇurattaṁ taha mamaṁ pariccaïya

āsattā kaṇagarahē sacciya tā vaïriṇī paḍhamaṁ

tārisadukkhaṁ dinnaṁ taïyā maha jēhiṁ duṭṭhasīlēhiṁ

iṇhiṁ gantuṁ dōnnivi hantavvāiṁ maē tāiṁ

iya cintiūṇa vēgēṇa āgaō rōsaphuraphurantō sō

saṁlēhaṇasusiyaṅgō jatthacchaï kaṇagarahasāhū

dhammajjhāṇōvagayassa tassa paḍimāgayassa rayaṇīē

piuvaṇaṭhiyassa muṇiṇō ghōruvasaggē kuṇaï pāvō

kāuṁ pisāyarūvaṁ ukkattaï nisiyakattiyāhatthō

maṁsāiṁ saruhirāiṁ sambhāriyapuvvakayavaïrō

bhīmaṭṭahāsapuvvaṁ uḍḍhaṁ ukkhiviya khivaï khōṇīē

duvvisahagurukasāghāyatāḍaṇaṁ kuṇaï puṇaruttaṁ

muñcaï dhūlīvarisaṁ khaṇēṇa uvalōhapūriyaṁ kuṇaī

jalaṇavarisēṇa varisaï chindaï khaṇēṇa aṅgāiṁ

kāūṇa hatthirūvaṁ sutikkhadantēhiṁ dēī vēhāiṁ

niyakāiyāē siñcaï lōlaï calaṇēhiṁ bhūmīē

kiṁ bahuṇā bhaṇiēṇaṁ nigghiṇahiyaēṇa tēṇa asurēṇa

muṇidēhē duvvisahā vihiyānaraōvamā viyaṇā

tīi viyaṇāi sāhū acaliyacittō pasatthasuhalēsō

dhammajjhāṇōvagaō nindantō niyayaduccariyaṁ

kayaaṇasaṇō mahappā kālaṁ kāūṇa bīyakappammi

candajjuṇammi jāō vihuppahō nāma dēvotti

ambarisī muṇidēhaṁ pāṇavimukkampi garuyarōsēṇaṁ

chindiya sayahā pattō sulōyaṇajjāsamīvammi

sāvi hu pabhāyasamaē kāussaggē ṭhiyā suhajjhāṇē

sāhuṇimajjhōvagayā sumarāviyapuvvaduccariyā

lōhamayapurisapaḍimaṁ phuliṅgajālāulaṁ viuvviya

pāvē! parapurisapiē! avagūhasu vallahaṁ ēyaṁ

iya bhaṇiya tēṇa samayaṁ gāḍhaṁ bandhitu jaliyadaṇḍēhiṁ

haṇiūṇa takkhaṇēṇaṁ sāvi taō māriyā tēṇa

avicaliyasuddhabhāvā kālaṁ kāuṁ vihuppahasurassa

uppannā piyadēvī sayampabhā nāma tatthēva

iya bhō naravara! daṭṭhuṁ rāgaddōsāṇa dāruṇavivāgaṁ

dūrēṇa cayasu saṅgaṁ rāgaddōsēhiṁ pāvēhiṁ

vahaṁ vihāyā ' 'su pahiṭhṭhamāṇasō muṇīṇa sō ambarisī surāhamō

kayatthamappāṇa maṇē gaṇantō jahāgayaṁ tāhi gaō saṭhāṇayaṁ

sāhudhaṇēsaraviraïyasubōhagāhāsamūharammāē

rāgaggidōsavisaharapasamaṇajalamantabhūyāē

ēsōvi parisamappaï sulōyaṇākaṇagarahavahō nāma

surasundarīkahāē cōddasamō iha paricchēō

aha sō kayasamaṇavahō aṁvarisī muiyamāṇasō tattha

niccaṁ nēraïyāṇaṁ kayatthaṇājāyagurutōsō

bandhitu pāvakammaṁ taō cuō vihavapaṁsulīgabbhē

uvvannō sō tīē bahuvihakaḍukhārapāṇēhiṁ

sāḍiyadēhō rōddaṁ jhāṇaṁ āūriūṇa narayammi

mariūṇa sattapaliō uvavannō paḍhamapuḍhavīē

aṇuhaviya tivvadukkhaṁ niyaāukkhaē taōvi uvvaṭṭō

iha bharahē vippasuō uvavannō duggaō nāma

dāriddadukkhataviō dikkhaṁ parivāyayāṇa ghittūṇa

kāuṁ annaṇatavaṁ ukkaḍarōsō maō tattō

dharaṇindassa u jāō sāhiyapaliyāuō mahārāō

nāmēṇa kālabāṇō divvamahāriddhisampannō

tatthavi sumariyavaïrō uvaōgaṁ dēi tāṇa dōṇhampi

ṭhāṇaviyāṇaṇahēuṁ vibhaṅganāṇēṇa sakasāō

tattiyanāṇābhāvāu bīyakappaṭṭhiyāṇi ēyāṇi

diṭṭhāṇi na tēṇa tahiṁ puṇaruttakaōvaōgēvi

ēvaṁ vaccaï kālō narinda! sēsāuyassa aha tassa

bhuñjittu divvamōē thōvūṇayaaṭṭhapaliyāiṁ

īsāṇakappavāsī vihuppahō sō surō taō caviuṁ

tuha puttō uvavannō kamalāvaïdēvikucchīē

dōhalapūraṇahēuṁ paribbhamantī purammi hatthigayā

sattamamāsē naravara! dēvī kamalāvaī ēsā

ētthantarammi diṭṭhā kaōvaōgēṇa kālabāṇēṇa

gavvaṭṭhiyaniyavaïriyadaṁsaṇasañjāyarōsēṇa

āgamma taō turiyaṁ ahiṭṭhiō tēṇa kuñjarō sahasā

vicchōlintō lōyaṁ vēgēṇa pahāviō tēṇa

vaḍapāyavasāhālaggaṇēṇa naravara! tumammi uttariē

gayaṇēṇa samuppaïō tēṇēva ahiṭṭhiō hatthī

maṇisañjuyadēvikarapahāraparivihuriō gayaṁ mōttuṁ

jaṇaṇīsamayaṁ marihī gayaṇāō nivaḍiō vaïrī

iya cintēntō naravara! kayakiccō sō surō gaō ṭhāṇaṁ

dēvīvi kuñjaragayā paḍiyā gayaṇāō saratīrē

uttariūṇa ya tattō miliyā siridattasatthavāhassa

caliyā satthēṇa samaṁ kusagganayarammi naranāha!

satthavilōvē jāē aḍavīpaḍiyāē tattha dēvīē

jāō puttō diṭṭhō kaōvaōgēṇa dēvēṇa

aha puṇaravi sō dēvō vaïraṁ sariūṇa nigghiṇasahāvō

sampattō vēgēṇaṁ dēvīpāsammi gururōsō

niuṇaṁ jōyantēṇavi pabhūyakālāō pāva! diṭṭhō si

kāhāmi vaïraantaṁ aṇuhava duvvihiyaphalamiṇhiṁ

ēvaṁ bhaṇamāṇēṇaṁ pasuttakamalāvaīē aṅkāō

naravara! sō tuha puttō hariō surakālabāṇēṇa

gahiūṇa ya taṁ bālaṁ cintēi surō kiliṭṭhapariṇāmō

mārēmi imaṁ sattuṁ iṇhiṁ maliūṇa hatthēhiṁ

khaṇḍāṇi ahaṁ kāuṁ karēmi kiṁvā disābaliṁ ahavā

acchōḍēmi silāē tilaṁ tilaṁ kiṁ nu chindāmi?

ēvaṁ hi kaē ahavā na hōjja viyaṇā pabhūyakālīyā

maraṇāu takkhaṇēṇaṁ imassa avvattacittassa

tā gantūṇaṁ katthavi muñcāmi amāṇūsammi ṭhāṇammi

taṇhāchuhābhibhūō marihī sayamēva dukkhēṇa

iya cintiūṇa mukkō vēyaḍḍhasilāyalammi viyaṇammi

sō tuha puttō naravara! surōvi pattō niyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

naravara! acchaü ēyaṁ kahēmi annaṁ kahantaraṁ tāva

īsāṇāō caviō vijjuppahō ēttha vēyaḍ̣dhē

dakkhiṇasẹ̄dhīi purē ramaṇīē rayaṇasañcaē pavarē

pavaṇagaïkhayaraputtō uvavannō baülavaïyāē

nāmēṇa cittavēgō ēttō dēvīvi candarēhā sā

caviūṇa ya uppannā nayarē sirikuñjarāvattē

khayarassa amiyagaïṇō piyāi bhajjāi cittamālāē

aïvallahā u dhūyā nāmēṇaṁ kaṇagamālatti

ēttō ya puvvabhaṇiō sulōyaṇāiṇa āsi jō māyā

vasudattō nāmēṇaṁ sōvi hu bhamiūṇa saṁsārē

uppannō vēyaḍ̣dhē gaṅgāvattammi khayararāyassa

sirigandhavāhaṇassa u puttō mayaṇāvalīē ō

nahavāhaṇotti nāmaṁ variyā aha tassa kaṇagamālā sā

hariūṇa ya pariṇīyā chalēṇa sā cittavēgēṇa

nahavāhaṇēṇa baddhō sō khayarō nāgiṇīi vijjāē

āṇīyā niranayarē vilavantī kaṇagamālāvi

pariyāyantarapattaṁ aṇicchamāṇimpi icchaē ramiuṁ

bhagiṇimpi piccha naravara! ēsō annāṇadōsēṇa

iya naravara! saṁsārē annāṇandhēhiṁ ēttha jīvēhiṁ

bhagiṇīvi ahilasijjaï dhūyā suṇhā va jaṇaṇī vā

bhagiṇīvi hōi bhajjā, piyāvi puttō, suyāvi jaṇaṇitti

bhajjāvi jattha māyā dhiratthu saṁsāravāsassa
